 pratyaya parīkṣā nāma prathamam prakaraṇam āryamañju śriye kumāra bhūtāya namaḥ yaḥ  anta dvaya āvāsa vidhūta vāsaḥ saṃbuddha dhī sāgara labdha janmā saddharma toyasya gabhīra bhāvam yathā anubuddham kṛpayā jagāda yasya darśana tejāṃsi paravādi mata indhanam dahanti adya api lokasya mānasāni tamāṃsi ca yasya asama jñāna vacaḥ śara oghā nighnanti niḥśeṣa bhava ari senām tri dhātu rājya śriyam ādadhānā vineya lokasya sa devakasya nāgārjunāya praṇipatya tasmai tad kārikāṇām vivṛtim kariṣye uttāna sat prakriya vākya naddhām tarka anila avyākulitām prasannām tatra   ityādi vakṣyamāṇam śāstram tasya kāni saṃbandha abhidhāna prayojanāni iti praśne madhyamaka avatāra vihita vidhinā advaya jñāna alaṃkṛtam mahā karuṇa upāya puraḥsaram prathama citta utpādam tathāgata jñāna utpatti hetum ādim kṛtvā yāvat ācārya nāgārjunasya vidita aviparīta prajñāpāramitā ānīteḥ karuṇayā para avabodha artham śāstra praṇayanam iti eṣa tāvat śāstrasya saṃbandhaḥ yad śāsti vaḥ kleśa ripūn aśeṣān saṃtrāyate durgatitaḥ  bhavāt ca tad śāsanāt trāṇa guṇāt ca śāstram eta t vayam ca anya mateṣu na asti iti svayam eva ca ācāryaḥ  vakṣyamāṇa sakala śāstra abhidheya artha sa prayojanam upadarśayan tad aviparīta saṃprakāśa tvena māhātmyam udbhāvya tad svabhāva avyatireka vartine parama gurave tathāgatāya śāstra praṇayana nimittakam praṇāmam kartu kāma āha anirodham anutpādam anucchedam aśāśvatam aneka artha manāna artham anāgamam anirgamam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam ityādi tad atra anirodhādi aṣṭa viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ śāstra abhidheya arthaḥ sarva prapañca upaśama śiva lakṣaṇam nirvāṇam śāstrasya prayojanam nirdiṣṭam tam vande vadatām varam iti anena praṇāmaḥ iti eṣa tāvat śoka dvayasya samudāya arthaḥ avayava arthaḥ tu vibhajyate tatra niruddhiḥ nirodhaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ  nirodha iti ucyate utpādanam utpādaḥ ātma bhāva unmajjanam iti arthaḥ ucchittiḥ ucchedaḥ prabandha vid chittiḥ iti arthaḥ śāśvataḥ  nityaḥ sarva kāle sthāṇuḥ iti arthaḥ ekaḥ ca asau  arthaḥ ca iti eka arthaḥ  abhinna arthaḥ na pṛthak iti arthaḥ nānā arthaḥ  bhinna arthaḥ pṛthak iti arthaḥ āgatiḥ āgamaḥ viprakṛṣṭa deśa avasthitānām saṃnikṛṣṭa deśa āgamanam nirgatiḥ nirgamaḥ saṃnikṛṣṭa deśa avasthitānām viprakṛṣṭa deśa gamanam etiḥ gati arthaḥ pratiḥ prāpti arthaḥ upasarga vaśena dhātu artha vipariṇāmāt upasargeṇa dhātu arthaḥ  balāt anyatra nīyate gaṅgā salila mādhuryam sāgareṇa yathā ambhasā pratītya śabdaḥ  atra lyabantaḥ prāptau  apekṣāyām vartate samutpūrvaḥ padiḥ prādurbhāva artha  iti samutpāda śabdaḥ prādurbhāve vartate tatas ca hetu pratyaya apekṣaḥ  bhāvānām utpādaḥ pratītyasamutpāda arthaḥ apare tu bruvate itiḥ gamanam vināśaḥ itau sādhava ityāḥ pratirvīpsā arthaḥ iti evam tad hita antam iti aśabdam vyutpādya prati prati iti ānām vināśinām samutpāda iti varṇayanti teṣām  pratītya samutpādam vaḥ  bhikṣavaḥ  deśayiṣyāmi   yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam paśyati sa dharma paśyati  iti evamādau viṣaye vīpsā arthasya saṃbhavāt  samāsasadbhāvāt ca syāt jyāyasī vyutpattiḥ iha tu  cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpāṇi ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam  iti evamādau viṣaye sākṣāt aṅgīkṛtārtha viśeṣe cakṣuḥ pratītyā iti pratītya śabda eka cakṣuḥ indriya hetukāyām api eka vijñāna utpattau  abhīṣṭāyām kutaḥ vīpsā artha tā prāpti arthaḥ tu anaṅgīkṛtārtha viśeṣe api pratītya śabde saṃbhavati prāpya saṃbhavaḥ pratītya samutpāda iti aṅgīkṛtārtha viśeṣe api saṃbhavati cakṣuḥ pratītya cakṣuḥ prāpya cakṣū rūpam ca apekṣya iti vyākhyānāt  tad hita ante ca iti aśabde  cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpāṇi ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam  iti atra pratītya śabdasya avyayatva abhāvāt samāsa asadbhāvāt ca vibhakti śrutau satyām cakṣuḥ pratītya vijñānam rūpāṇi ca iti nipātaḥ syāt  na ca etad evam iti avyayasya eva lyabantasya vyutpattiḥ abhyupeyā yaḥ tu  vīpsā artha tvāt pratyupasargasya eteḥ prāpti artha tvāt samutpāda śabdasya ca saṃbhava artha tvāt  tān  tān pratyayān pratītya samutpādaḥ prāpya saṃbhava iti eke prati prati vināśinām utpādaḥ pratītyasamutpāda iti anye  iti para vyākhyānam anūdya dūṣaṇam abhidhatte tasya para pakṣa anuvādā kauśala tvam eva tāvat saṃbhāvyate kim kāraṇam yaḥ  hi prāpti artham pratītya śabdam vyācaṣṭe na asau pratiṃ vīpsā artham vyācaṣṭe na apyetim prāpti artham kim tarhi pratiṃ prāpti artham samuditam ca pratītya śabdam prāptau  eva varṇayati tena idānīm prāpya saṃbhavaḥ pratītyasamutpāda iti evam vyutpāditena pratītyasamutpāda śabdena yadi niravaśeṣa saṃbhavi padārtha parāmarśaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ tadā tām tām hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm prāpya saṃbhava pratītya samutpāda iti vīpsā saṃbandhaḥ kriyate atha viśeṣa parāmarśaḥ tadā cakṣuḥ prāpya rūpāṇi ca iti na vīpsāyāḥ saṃbandha iti evam tāvat anuvāda akauśalam ācāryasya etad vā ayuktam kim ca ayuktam etad   cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpāṇi ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam  iti atra artha dvaya asaṃbhavāt iti yad uktam dūṣaṇam tad api na upapadyate kim kāraṇam katham anena eva tad prāpteḥ saṃbhava iti yukti anupādānena pratijñā mātra tvāt  atha ayam abhiprāyaḥ syāt  arūpi tvā dvijñānasya cakṣuṣā prāptiḥ na asti rūpiṇām eva tad prāpti darśanāt iti etad api na yuktam   iti atra api prāpti abhyupagamāt prāpya śabdasya ca apekṣya śabda paryāya tvāt prāpti arthasya eva ācārya ārya nāgārjunena pratītya śabdasya tad tad prāpya yad utpannam na utpannam tad svabhāvataḥ iti abhyupagamāt  tatas  dūṣaṇam api na upapadyate iti apare yad ca api sva matam vyavasthāpitam  kim tarhi asmin sati idam bhavati asya utpādāt idam utpadyate iti idaṃpratyaya tā arthaḥ pratītyasamutpāda artha  iti  tad api na upapadyate pratītyasamutpāda śabdayoḥ pratyekam artha viśeṣān abhidhānāt tad vyutpādasya ca vivakṣita tvāt  atha api rūḍhi śabdam pratītyasamutpāda śabdam abhyupetya araṇyetilaka ādi vadevam ucyate tad api na upapannam avayava artha anugatasya eva pratītyasamutpādasya ācāryeṇa tad tad prāpya yad utpannam na utpannam tad svabhāvataḥ iti abhyupagamāt  atha asmin sati idam bhavati hrasve dīrgham yathā sati iti vyākhyāyamānena nanu tad eva abhyupagatam bhavati hrasvam pratītya hrasvam prāpya hrasvam apekṣya dīrgham bhavati iti tatas ca yad eva dūṣyate tad eva abhyupagamyate iti na yujyate iti alam prasaṅgena tad evam hetu pratyaya apekṣam bhāvānām utpādam paridīpayatā bhagavatā ahetu eka hetu viṣama hetu saṃbhūta tvam sva para ubhaya kṛta tvam ca bhāvānām niṣiddham bhavati tad niṣedhāt ca sāṃvṛtānām padārthānām yathā avasthitam sāṃvṛtam sva rūpam udbhāvitam bhavati sa eva idānīm sāṃvṛtaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ svabhāvena anutpanna tvāt  ārya jñāna apekṣayā na asmin nirodhaḥ  vidyate yāvat na asmin nirgamaḥ  vidyate iti anirodha ādibhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ viśe ṣaṇaiḥ viśiṣyate yathā ca nirodhāt ayaḥ  na santi pratītyasamutpādasya tathā sakala śāstreṇa pratipādayiṣyati ananta viśeṣaṇa saṃbhave api pratītyasamutpādasya aṣṭānām eva upādānam eṣām prādhānyena vivāda aṅga bhūta tvāt yathā avasthita pratītya samutpāda darśane sati āryāṇām abhidheya ādi lakṣaṇasya prapañcasya sarvathā uparamāt  prapañcānām upaśamaḥ  asmin  iti sa eva pratītyasamutpādaḥ prapaḥca upaśama iti ucyate citta caittānām ca tasmin  apravṛttau jḥāna jḥeya vyavahāra nivṛttau jāti jarā maraṇa ādi niravaśeṣa upadrava rahita tvāt  śivaḥ yathā abhihita viśeṣaṇasya pratītyasamutpādasya deśanā kriyayā īpsitatama tvāt  karmaṇā nirdeśaḥ anirodham anutpādam anucchedam aśāśvatam aneka artha manāna artham anāgamam anirgamam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam prapañca upaśamam śivam deśayāmāsa saṃbuddhaḥ tam vande vadatām varam yathā upavarṇita pratītyasamutpādau  agamāt ca tathāgatasya eva ekasya aviparīta artha vādi tvam paśyan sarva para pravādān  ca bāla pralāpān ivāvetya atīva prasāda anugata ācāryaḥ  bhūyaḥ bhagavantam viśeṣayati vadatām varam iti atra ca nirodhasya pūrvam prativedhaḥ utpāda nirodhayoḥ paurvāparya avasthāyāḥ siddhaya bhāvam dyotayitum vakṣyati hi pūrvam jātiḥ yadi bhavet jarā maraṇam uttaram nirjara amaraṇā jātiḥ bhavet jāyeta ca amṛtaḥ iti tasmāt na ayam niyamaḥ  yad  pūrvam utpādena bhavitavyam paścāt nirodhena iti idānīm anirodha ādi viśiṣṭa pratītya samutpāda pratipipādayiṣayā utpāda pratiṣedhena nirodha ādi pratiṣedha saukarya manyamāna ācāryaḥ prathamam eva utpāda prativedham ārabhate utpādaḥ  hi paraiḥ parikalpyamānaḥ svatas  vā parikalpyeta paratas  ubhayatas  ahetutaḥ  vā parikalpyeta sarvathā ca na upapadyata iti niścitya āha na svatas  na api paratas  na dvābhyām na api ahetutaḥ utpannā jātu vidyante bhāvāḥ kvacana kecana tatra jātu iti kadācid iti arthaḥ kvacana śabda ādhāra vacanaḥ kvacid śabda paryāyaḥ kecana śabda ādheya vacanaḥ kecid śabda paryāyaḥ tatas ca evam saṃbandhaḥ na eva svata utpannā jātu vidyante bhāvāḥ kvacana kecana evam pratijñā trayam api yojyam nanu ca na eva svata utpannā iti avadhāryamāṇe parata utpannā iti aniṣṭam prāpnoti na prāpnoti prasajya pratiṣedhasya vivakṣita tvāt  paratas  api utpādasya pratiṣetsyamāna tvāt  yayā ca upapattyā svata utpādaḥ  na saṃbhavati sā tasmāt hi tasya bhavane na guṇa u asti kaścid  jātasya janma punar eva ca na eva yuktam ityādinā madhyamaka avatāra ādi dvāreṇa avaseyā ācārya buddha pālitaḥ tu āha na svata utpadyante bhāvāḥ tad utpāda vaiyarthyāt  atiprasaṅga doṣāt ca na hi sva ātmanā vidyamānānām padārthānām punar utpāde prayojanam asti atha san  api jāyeta na kadācid na jāyeta iti atra eke dūṣaṇam āhuḥ tad ayuktam hetu dṛṣṭānta anabhidhānāt para ukta doṣa aparihārāt ca prasaṅga vākya tvāt ca prakṛta artha viparyayeṇa viparīta artha sādhya tad dharma vyaktau parasmāt utpanna abhāva ajanma sāphalyāt  janma niraḥ  baḥ dhāt ca iti kṛtānta virodhaḥ syāt  sarvam etad dūṣaṇam ayujyamānam vayam paśyāmaḥ katham kṛtvā tatra yad tāvat uktam hetu dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānāt iti tad ayuktam kim kāraṇam yasmāt paraḥ svata utpattim abhyupagacchan pṛcchayate svata iti hetu tvena tad eva ca utpadyate iti na ca vidyamānasya punarutpattau prayojanam paśyāmaḥ anavasthām ca paśyāmaḥ na ca tvayā utpannasya punar utpāda iṣyate anavasthā ca api aniṣṭā iti tasmāt nirupapattika eva tvad vādaḥ sva abhyupagama virodhaḥ ca iti kim iti codite parona abhyupaiti yatas  hetu dṛṣṭānta upāda ānasāphalyam syāt  atha sva abhyupagama virodha codanayā api paraḥ  na nivartate tadā nirlajja tayā hetu dṛṣṭāntābhyām api na eva nivarteta na ca unmattakena saha asmākam vivāda iti tasmāt sarvathā priya anumāna tām eva ātmanaḥ ācāryaḥ prakaṭayati asthāne api anumānam praveśayan na ca mādhyamikasya sataḥ svatantram anumānam kartum yuktam pakṣa antara abhyupagama abhāvāt tathā uktam ārya devena sat asat sadasat ca iti yasya pakṣaḥ  na vidyate upālambhaḥ cireṇa api tasya vaktum na śakyate vigraha vyāvartanyām ca uktam yadi kācana pratijñā syāt me tatas  eva me bhavet doṣaḥ na asti ca mama pratijñā tasmāt na eva asti me doṣaḥ yadi kiṃcid upala meyam pravartayeyam nivartayeyam vā pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ arthaiḥ tad abhāvāt me anupālambhaḥ iti yadā ca evam svatantra anumāna anabhidhāyi tvam mādhyamikasya tadā kutas   nādhya ātmikāni āyatanāni svata utpannāni  iti svatantrā pratijñā yasyām sāṃkhyāḥ pratyavasthāpyante kaḥ  arya pratijña arthaḥ kim kārya ātmaka tvāt svata uta kāraṇa ātmaka tvāt iti kim ca atas  kārya ātmakāt ced  siddha sādhanam kāraṇa ātmakāt ced  viruddha artha tā kāraṇa ātmanā vidyamānasya eva sarvasya utpattimata utpādāt iti kutaḥ asmākam vidyamāna tvāt iti hetuḥ yasya siddha sādhanam viruddha artha tā vā syāt  yasya siddha sādhanasya yasyāḥ ca viruddha artha tāyāḥ parihāra artham yatnam kariṣyāmaḥ tasmāt para ukta doṣa aprasaṅgāt eva tad parihāraḥ ācārya buddha pālitena na varṇanīyaḥ atha api syāt  mādhyamikānām pakṣa hetu dṛṣṭāntānām asiddheḥ svatantra anumāna anabhidhāyi tvāt svata utpatti pratiṣedha pratijñāta artha sādhanam mā bhūt ubhaya siddhena vā anumānena para pratijñā nirākaraṇam para pratijñāya astu svata eva anumāna virodha codanayā svata eva pakṣa hetu dṛṣṭānta doṣa rahitaiḥ pakṣa ādibhiḥ bhavitavyam tatas ca tad anabhidhānāt tad doṣa aparihārāt ca sa eva doṣa iti ucyate na etad evam kim kāraṇam yasmāt  yaḥ  hi yam artham pratijānīte tena sva niścayavat anyeṣām niścaya utpādana icchayā yayā upapattyā asau  arthaḥ  adhigataḥ sā eva upapattiḥ parasmai upadeṣṭavyā tasmāt eṣa tāvat nyāyaḥ yad pareṇa eva sva abhyupagata pratijñāta artha sādhanam upādeyam na ca ayam ca anena param prati hetu dṛṣṭānta asaṃbhavāt pratijñā anusāra tayā eva kevalam sva pratijñāta artha sādhanam upādatta iti nirupapattika pakṣa abhyupagamāt sva ātmānam eva ayam kevalam visaṃvādayan na śaknoti pareṣām niścayam ādhātum iti idam eva asya spaṣṭataram dūṣaṇam yad uta sva pratijñāta artha sādhana āsāmarthyam iti kim atra anumāna bādha udbhāvanayā prayojanam atha api avaśyam svatas  anumāna virodha doṣa udbhāvanīyaḥ saḥ  api udbhāvita eva ācārya buddha pālitena katham iti ced  na svata utpadyante bhāvāḥ tad utpāda vaiyarthyāt iti vacanāt  atra hi tad iti anena sva ātmanā vidyamānasya parāmarśaḥ kasmāt iti ced  tathā hi tasya saṃgraheṇa ukta vākyasya etad vivaraṇa vākyam na hi sva ātmanā vidyamānānām punar utpāde prayojanam iti anena ca vākyena sādhya sādhana dharma anugatasya para prasiddhasya sādharmya dṛṣṭāntasya upādānam tatra sva ātmanā vidyamānasya iti anena hetu parāmarśaḥ utpāda vayarthyāt ityanena sādhya dharma parāmarśaḥ tatra yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt  kṛtaka tvam anityam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ tasmāt kṛtaka tvāt anitya iti kṛtaka tvam atra upanaya abhivyaktaḥ  hetuḥ evam iha api na svata utpadyante bhāvāḥ sva ātmanā vidyamānānām punar utpāda vaiyarthyāt  iha hi sva ātmanā vidyamānam puraḥ avasthitam ghaṭa ādikam punar utpāda anapekṣam dṛṣṭam tathā ca mṛd piṇḍa ādi avasthāyām api yadi sva ātmanā vidyamānam ghaṭa ādikam iti manyase tadā api tasya sva ātmanā vidyamānasya na asti utpāda iti evam sva ātmanā vidyamāna tvena upanaya abhivyaktena punar utpāda pratiṣedha avyabhicāriṇā hetunā svata eva sāṃkhyasya anumāna virodha udbhāvanam anuṣṭhitam eva iti tad kim ucyate tad ayuktam hetu dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānāt iti na ca kevalam hetu dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānam na saṃbhavati para ukta doṣa aparihāra doṣaḥ  na saṃbhavati katham kṛtvā sāṃkhyā hi na eva abhivyakta rūpasya puraḥ avasthitasya ghaṭasya punar abhivyaktim icchanti tasya eva ca iha dṛṣṭānta tvena upādānam siddha rūpa tvāt  anabhivyakta rūpasya ca śakti rūpāpannasya utpatti pratiṣedha viśiṣṭa sādhya tvāt  kutas  siddha sādhana pakṣa doṣa āśaṅkā kutaḥ vā hetoḥ viruddha artha tā śaṅkā iti tasmāt svatas  anumāna virodha codanāyām api yathā upavarṇita doṣa abhāvāt para ukta doṣa aparihāra asaṃbhava eva iti asaṃbaddham eva etad dūṣaṇam iti vijñeyam ghaṭa ādikam iti ādi śabdena niravaśeṣa utpitsu padārtha saṃgrahasya vivakṣita tvāt anaikāntika tā api paiṭādibhiḥ na eva saṃbhavati athavā ayam anyaḥ prayoga mārgaḥ puruṣa vyatiriktāḥ padārthāḥ svata utpatti vādinaḥ tatas  eva na svata utpadyante sva ātmanā vidyamāna tvāt  puruṣavat  iti idam udāharaṇam udāhāryam yadi api ca abhivyakti vādina utpāda pratiṣedhaḥ  na bādhakaḥ tathā api abhivyaktau  utpāda śabdam nipātya pūrvam paścāt ca anupalabdhi upalabdhi sādharmyeṇa utpāda śabdena abhivyakteḥ eva abhidhāna āt ayam pratiṣedhaḥ  na abādhakaḥ katham punar ayam yathā ukta artha abhidhānam vinā vyasta vicāraḥ  labhyata iti ced  tad ucyate atha vākyāni kṛtāni tāni mahārtha tvāt yathā uditam artham saṃgṛhya pravṛttāni tāni ca vyākhyāyamānāni yathoktam artha ātmānam prasūyanta iti na atra kiṃcid anupāttam saṃbhāvyate prasaṅga viparītena ca arthena parasya eva saṃbandhaḥ  na asmākam sva pratijñāyā abhāvāt  tatas ca siddhānta virodha asaṃbhavaḥ parasya ca yāvat bahavaḥ  doṣāḥ prasaṅga viparīta āpattyā āpadyante tāvat asmābhiḥ abhīṣyata eva iti kutaḥ nu khalu aviparīta ācārya nāgārjuna mata anusāriṇaḥ ācārya buddha pālitasya sa avakāśa vacana abhidhāyi tvam yatas  asya paraḥ  avakāśam labheta niḥsvabhāva bhāva vādinā sa svabhāva bhāva vādinaḥ prasaṅge āpa pā dyamāne kutas  prasaṅga viparīta artha prasaṅgi tā na hi śabdāḥ dāṇḍapāśikā iva vaktāram asvatantrayanti kim tarhi satyām śaktau vaktuḥ vivakṣām anuvidhīyante tatas ca para pratijñā pratiṣedha mātra phala tvāt prasaṅga āpādanasya na asti prasaṅga viparīta arthāpattiḥ tathā ca ācāryaḥ  bhūyasā prasaṅga āpatti mukhena eva para pakṣam nirākaroti sma tad yathā na ākāśam vidyate kiṃcid pūrvam ākāśa lakṣaṇāt  alakṣaṇam prasajyeta syāt pūrvam yadi lakṣaṇāt  rūpa kāraṇa nirmukte rūpe rūpam prasajyate āhetukam na ca asti arthaḥ kaścid āhetukaḥ kvacid  bhāvaḥ tāvat na nirvāṇam jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇam prasajyeta asti bhāvaḥ hi na jarā maraṇam vinā ityādinā atha artha vākya tvāt ācārya vākyānām mahārtha tve sati aneka prayoniṣpatti hetu tvam parikalpyate ācārya buddha pālita vyākhyānāni api kim iti na tathā eva parikalpyante atha syāt  vṛtti kārāṇām eṣa nyāyaḥ yad prayoga vākya vistara abhidhānam kartavyam iti etad api na asti vigraha vyāvartanyā vṛttim kurvatā api ācāryeṇa prayoga vākya anabhidhānāt api ca ātmanaḥ tarka śāstra ati kauśala mātram āviścikīrṣayā aṅgīkṛta madhyamaka darśanasya api yad svatantra prayoga vākya abhidhānam tad atitarām aneka doṣa samudāya āspadam asya tārkikasya upalakṣyate katham kṛtvā tatra yad tāvat evam uktam atra prayoga vākyam bhavati na paramārthataḥ ādhyātmikāni āyatanāni svata utpannāni vidyamāna tvāt  caitanyavat iti kimartha punar atra paramārtha ta iti viśeṣaṇam upādīyate loka saṃvṛtya abhyupagatasya utpādasya apratiṣidhyamāna tvāt  pratiṣedhe ca abhyupeta bādha aprasaṅgāt iti ced  na etad yuktam saṃvṛtya api svata utpatti anabhyupagamāt yathā uktam sūtre  sa ca ayam bīja hetukaḥ aṅkura utpadyamānaḥ  na svayaṃkṛtaḥ  na para kṛtaḥ  na ubhaya kṛtaḥ  na api ahetu samutpannaḥ  niśvara kāla aṇu prakṛti svabhāva saṃbhūtaḥ  iti tathā bījasya sataḥ  yathā aṅkuraḥ  na ca yaḥ  bīju sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas  na ca eva tad evam anucchedaa śāśvata dharma tā iha api vakṣyati pratītya yad yad bhavati na hi tāvat tad eva tad  na ca anyat api tad tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam iti parama ta apekṣam viśeṣaṇam iti ced  tad ayuktam saṃvṛtya api tadīya vyavasthā anabhyupagamāt satya dvaya aviparīta darśana paribhraṣṭā eva hi tīrthikā yāvat ubhayathā api niṣidhyante tāvat  guṇa eva saṃbhāvyata iti evam parama tāpekṣam api viśeṣaṇa abhidhānam na yujyate na ca api lokaḥ svatautpattim pratipannaḥ yatas tad apekṣayā api viśeṣaṇa sāphalyam syāt  lokaḥ  hi svatas  parata iti evamādikam vicāram anavatārya kāraṇāt kāryam utpadyate iti etāvat mātram pratipannaḥ evam ācāryaḥ  api vyavasthāpayāmāsa iti sarvathā viśeṣaṇa vaiphalyam eva niścīyate api ca yadi saṃvṛtyā utpatti pratiṣedha nirāci kīrṣuṇā viśeṣaṇam etad upādīyate tadā svatas  asiddha ādhāre pakṣa doṣaḥ āśraya asiddhau vā hetu doṣaḥ syāt  paramārthataḥ svatas cakṣuḥ ādi āyatanānām anabhyupagamāt  saṃvṛtyā cakṣuḥ ādi sadbhāvāt adoṣa  iti ced  paramārtha ta iti etad tarhi kasya viśeṣaṇam sāṃvṛtānām cakṣuḥ ādīnām paramārtha ta utpatti pratiṣedhāt  utpatti pratiṣedha viśeṣaṇe parama artha grahaṇam iti ced  evam tarhi evam eva vaktavyam syāt  sāṃvṛtānām cakṣuḥ ādīnām paramārtha taḥ  na asti utpattiḥ iti na ca evam ucyate ucyamāne api paraiḥ vastu satām eva cakṣuḥ ādīnām abhyupagamāt  prajñapti satām anabhyupagamāt  paratas  asiddha ādhāraḥ pakṣa doṣaḥ syāt iti na yuktam etad  atha syāt  yathā anityaḥ śabda iti dharma dharmi sāmānyam eva gṛhyate na viśeṣaḥ viśeṣa grahaṇe hi sati anumāna anumeya vyavahāra abhāvaḥ syāt  tathā hi yadi cāturmahābhautikaḥ śabdaḥ  gṛhyate sa parasya asiddhaḥ atha ākāśa guṇa u gṛhyate sa bauddhasya svatas  asiddhaḥ tathā vaiśeṣikasya śabda anitya tām pratijānānasya yadi kāryaḥ śabdaḥ  gṛhyate sa paratas  asiddhaḥ atha vyaṅgayaḥ sa svatas  asiddhaḥ evam yathāsaṃbhavam vināśaḥ  api yadi sa hetukaḥ sa bauddhasya svatas  asiddhaḥ atha nirhetukaḥ sa parasya asiddha iti tasmāt  yathā atra dharma dharmi sāmānya mātram eva gṛhyate evam iha api dharmi mātram utsṛṣṭa viśeṣaṇam grahīṣyata iti ced  na etad evam yasmāt  yadā eva utpāda pratiṣedhaḥ  atra sādhya dharmaḥ  abhipretaḥ tadā eva dharmiṇaḥ tad ādhārasya viparyāsa mātra āsādita ātma bhāvasya pracyutiḥ svayam eva anena aṅgīkṛtā bhinnau hi viparyāsa aviparyāsau tad yadā viparyāsena asat sattvena gṛhyate taimirikeṇa iva keśa ādi tadā kutas  sat bhūta padārtha leśasya api upalabdhiḥ yadā ca aviparyāsāt abhūtam na adhyāropitam vitaimirikeṇa iva keśa ādi tadā kutaḥ asat bhūta padārtha leśasya api upalabdhiḥ yena tadānīm saṃvṛtiḥ syāt  ata eva uktam ācārya pādaiḥ yadi kiṃcid upala meyam pravartayeyam nivartayeyam vā pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ arthaiḥ tad abhāvāt me anupālambhaḥ iti yatas ca evam bhinnau viparyāsa aviparyāsau atas  viduṣām aviparīta avasthāyām viparītasya asaṃbhavāt kutas  sāṃvṛtam cakṣuḥ yasya dharmi tvam syāt  iti na vyāvartate asiddha ādhāre pakṣa doṣaḥ āśraya asiddhaḥ  vā hetu doṣaḥ iti aparihāra eva ayam nidarśanasya api na asti sāmyam tatra hi śabda sāmānyam anitya tā sāmānyam ca avivakṣita viśeṣam dvayoḥ api saṃvidyate na tu evam cakṣuḥ sāmānyam śūnyatā śūnya tāvādibhyām saṃvṛtyā aṅgīkṛtam na api paramārthataḥ iti na asti nidarśanasya sāmyam yaḥ ca ayam asiddha ādhāra pakṣa doṣa udbhāvane vidhiḥ eṣa eva sattva ādityasya hetoḥ asiddhārtha tā udbhāvane api yojyaḥ ittham ca etad evam yad svayam aṣyanena ayam yathā uktaḥ  arthaḥ  abhyupagataḥ tārkikeṇa santi eva adhyātmika āyatana utpādakā hetu ādayaḥ tathā tathāgatena nirdeśāt  yad hi yathā tathāgatena asti nirdiṣṭam tad tathā tad yathā śāntam nirvāṇam iti asya para upakṣiptasya sādhanasya idam dūṣaṇam abhihitam anena kaḥ  hi bhavatām abhipretaḥ  atra hetu arthaḥ saṃvṛtyā tathā tathāgatena nirdeśāt  uta paramārtha ta iti saṃvṛtyā ced  svatas  hetoḥ asiddhārtha tā paramārthataḥ ced  na san  āsanna sat asat dharmaḥ  nirvartate yadā sat asat ubhaya ātmaka kārya pratyayatva nirākaraṇāt  tadā katham nirvartakaḥ  hetuḥ evam sati hi yujyate na eva asau nirvartakaḥ  hetuḥ iti vākya arthaḥ tatas ca paramārtha taḥ  nirvartya nirvartakatva asiddheḥ asiddhārtha tā viruddha artha tā vā hetoḥ iti yatas ca evam svayam eva amunā nyāyena hetoḥ asiddhiḥ aṅgīkṛta anena tasmāt sarveṣu eva anumāneṣu vastu dharma upanyasta hetukeṣu svata evam hetu ādīnām asiddha tvāt sarvāṇi eva sādhanāni vyāhanyante tad yathā na paramārthataḥ parebhyaḥ tad pratyayebhyaḥ ādhyātmika āyatana janma paratvāt  tad yathā paṭasya athavā na pare parama arthena vivakṣitāḥ cakṣuḥ ādi ādhyātmika āyatana nirvartakāḥ pratyayā iti pratīyante paratvāt  tad yathā tantu ādaya iti paratva ādikam atra svata eva asiddham yathā ca anena utpannā eva ādhyātmikā bhāvāḥ tad viṣayi viśiṣṭa vyavahāra karaṇāt iti asya para abhihitasya hetoḥ asiddha artha tām udbhāvayiṣuṇā idam uktam atha samāhitasya yoginaḥ prajñācakṣuṣā bhāva yāthātmyam paśyataḥ utpāda gati ādayaḥ santi paramārtha ta iti sādhyate tadā tad viṣayi viśiṣṭa vyavahāra karaṇāt iti hetoḥ asiddhārtha tā gateḥ api utpāda niṣedhāt eva niṣedhāt iti evam sva kṛta sādhane api paramārtha taḥ  agatam na eva gamyate adhva tvāt  gatādhvavat iti adhvatva hetoḥ svata eva asiddha artha tā yojyā na paramārthataḥ sabhāgam cakṣū rūpam paśyati cakṣuḥ indriya tvāt  tad yathā tad sa bhāgam tathā na cakṣuḥ prekṣate rūpam bhautika tvāt  rūpavat  khara svabhāvā na mahī bhūta tvāt  tad yathā nirlaḥ ityādiṣu hetu ādi asiddhiḥ svata eva yojyā sattvāt iti ca ayam hetuḥ paratas  anaikāntikaḥ kim sattvāt  caitanyavat na ādhyātmikāni āyatanāni svata utpadyantām uta ahaḥ ghaṭa ādivat  svata utpadyantām iti ghaṭa ādīnām sādhya sama tvāt na anaikāntika tā iti ced  na etad evam tathā anabhidhānāt  nanu ca yathā parakīyeṣu anumāneṣu dūṣaṇam uktam evam sva anumāneṣu api yathā ukta dūṣaṇa prasaṅge sati sa eva asiddha ādhārā siddha hetu ādi doṣaḥ prāpnoti tatas ca yaḥ ubhayoḥ doṣaḥ na tena ekaḥ ca udyaḥ  bhavati iti sarvam etad dūṣaṇam ayuktam jāyata iti ucyate svatantram anumānam bruvata āmayam doṣaḥ  jāyate na vayam svatantram anumānam prayuñjma mahe para pratijñā niṣedha phala tvāt asmad anumānānām tathā hi paraḥ cakṣuḥ paśyati iti pratipannaḥ sa tad prasiddhena eva anumānena nirākriyate cakṣuṣaḥ sva ātma adarśana dharmam icchasi para darśana dharma avinābhāvi tvam ca aṅgīkṛtam tasmāt  yatra yatra sva ātma adarśanam tatra tatra para darśanam api na asti tad yathā ghaṭe asti ca cakṣuṣaḥ sva ātma adarśanam tasmāt  para darśanam api asya na eva asti tatas ca sva ātma adarśana viruddham nīla ādi para darśanam sva prasiddhena eva anumānena virudhyata iti etāvat mātram asmadanūmānaiḥ udbhāvyata iti kutaḥ asmad pakṣe yathā ukta doṣa avatāraḥ yatas  samāna doṣa tā syāt  kim punar  anyatara prasiddhena api anumānena asti anumāna bādhā asti sā ca sva prasiddhena eva hetunā na para prasiddhena lokata evam dṛṣṭa tvāt  kadācid hi loke arthi pratyarthibhyām pramāṇīkṛtasya sākṣiṇaḥ  vacanena jayaḥ  bhavati parājayaḥ vā kadācid  sva vacanena para vacanena tu na jayaḥ  na api parājayaḥ yathā ca loke tathā nyāye api laukikasya eva vyavahārasya nyāya śāstre prastuta tvāt  ata eva kaiścid uktam na paratas  prasiddhi balāt anumāna bādhā para prasiddheḥ eva nirācikīrṣita tvāt iti yaḥ tu manyate ya eva ubhaya niścita vādī sa pramāṇam dūṣaṇam vā na anyatara prasiddha saṃdigdha vācī iti tena api laukikīm vyavasthām anurudhyamānena anumāne yathā ukta eva nyāyaḥ  abhyupeyaḥ tathā hi na ubhaya prasiddhena vā āgamena bādhā kim tarhi sva prasiddhena api sva artha anumāne tu sarvatra sva prasiddhiḥ eva garīyasī na ubhaya prasiddhiḥ ata eva tarka lakṣaṇa abhidhānam niṣprayojanam yathāsva prasiddhayā upapattyā buddhaiḥ tad anabhijña vineya jana anugrahāt iti alam prasaṅgena prakṛtam eva vyākhyāsyāmaḥ paratas  api na utpadyante bhāvāḥ parābhāvāt eva etad ca na hi svabhāvaḥ  bhāvānām pratyaya ādiṣu vidyate iti atra pratipādayiṣyati tatas ca parābhāvāt eva na api parata utpadyante api ca anyat pratītya yadi nāma paraḥ  abhaviṣya jjāyeta tarhi bahulaḥ śikhinaḥ  andhakāraḥ sarvasya janma ca bhavet khalu sarvatas ca tulyam paratvam akhile ajanake api yasmāt  ityādinā [madhyamaka avatārāt] parata utpatti pratiṣedhaḥ  avaseyaḥ ācārya buddha pālitaḥ tu vyācaṣṭe na parata utpadyante bhāvāḥ sarvatas  sarva saṃbhava prasaṅgāt  ācārya bhāva vivekaḥ  dūṣaṇam āha tad atra prasaṅga vākya tvāt  sādhya sādhana viparyayam kṛtvā svatas  ubhayatas  ahetutaḥ  vā utpadyante bhāvāḥ kutaścid kasyacid utpatteḥ iti prāk pakṣa virodhaḥ anyathā sarvatas  sarva saṃbhava prasaṅgāt  iti asya sādhana dūṣaṇa anantaḥpāti tvāt asaṃgata artham etad  [iti] etad api asaṃgata artham pūrvam eva pratipādita tvāt  dūṣaṇa antar pāti tvāt ca para pratijñāta artha dūṣaṇena iti yad kiṃcid etad iti na punar yatna āsthīyate dvābhyām api na upajāyante bhāvāḥ ubhaya pakṣa abhihita doṣa prasaṅgāt  pratyekam utpāda asāmarthyāt ca vakṣyati hi syāt ubhābhyām kṛtam duḥkham syāt ekaika kṛtam yadi iti ahetutaḥ  api na utpadyante hetau  asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca na vidyate iti vakṣyamāṇa doṣa prasaṅgāt  gṛhyeta na eva ca jagat yadi hetu śūnyam syāt yadvat eva gaganotpala varṇa gandhau ityādi doṣa prasaṅgāt ca ācārya buddha pālitaḥ tu āha ahetutaḥ  na utpadyante bhāvāḥ sadā ca sarvatas ca sarva saṃbhava prasaṅgāt  atra ācārya bhāva vivekaḥ  dūṣaṇam āha atra api prasaṅga vākya tvāt  yadi viparīta sādhya sādhana vyakti vākya artha iṣyate tadā etad uktam bhavati hetuta utpadyante bhāvāḥ kadācid  kutaścid  kasyacid utpatteḥ ārambha sāphalyāt ca sā iyam vyākhyā na yuktā prāc ukta doṣāt iti tad etad ayuktam pūrva udita parihārāt iti apare yad ca api īśvara ādīnām upasaṃgraha artham tadā api na yuktam īśvara ādīnām sva para ubhaya pakṣeṣu yathā abhyupagamam antarbhāvāt iti tasmāt  prasādhitam etad na asti utpāda iti utpāda asaṃbhavāt ca siddhaḥ  anutpāda ādi viśiṣṭa pratītyasamutpāda iti atra āha yadi evam anutpāda ādi viśiṣṭaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ  vyavasthitaḥ  bhavadbhiḥ yad tarhi bhagavatā uktam avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārā avidyā nirodhāt saṃskāra nirodha iti tathā anityāḥ ca te bata saṃskārā utpāda vyaya dharmiṇaḥ utpadya hi nirudhyante teṣām vyupaśamaḥ sukhaḥ tathā utpādāt vā tathāgatānām anutpādāt vā tathāgatānām sthitā eva eṣā dharmāṇām dharmatā ekaḥ  dharmaḥ sattva sthitaye yad uta catvāra āhārāḥ dvau dharmau lokam pālayataḥ  hrīḥ ca apatrāpyam ca ityādi tathā para lokāt iha āgamanam ihalokāt ca para loka gamanam iti evam nirodha ādi viśiṣṭaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ  deśitaḥ  bhagavatā sa katham na ni vi rudhyata iti yata evam nirodha ādayaḥ pratītyasamutpādasya upalabhyante ata eva idam madhyamaka śāstram praṇītam ācāryeṇa na iya nīta artha sūtra anta vibhāga upadarśana artham tatra ya ete pratītyasamutpādasya utpāda ādaya uktāḥ na te vigata avidyā timirān āsrava viṣaya svabhāva apekṣayā kim tarhi avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana jñāna viṣaya apekṣayā tattva darśana apekṣayā tu uktam bhagavatā etad hi bhikṣavaḥ paramam satyam yad uta amoṣa dharma nirvāṇam sarva saṃskārāḥ ca mṛṣā moṣa dharmāṇaḥ iti tathā na asti atra tathatā vā avitatha tā vā moṣa dharmaka mapi etad  pralopa dharmakam api etad mṛṣā api etad māyā iyam bāla lāpinī iti tathā phena piṇḍa upamam rūpam vedanā budbuda upamā marīci sadṛśī saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ kadalī nibhāḥ māyā upamam ca vijñānam uktam āditya bandhunā iti evam dharmān vīkṣamāṇaḥ  bhikṣuḥ ārabdha vīryavān divā vā yadi vā rātrau saṃprajānan pratismṛtaḥ pratividhyet padam śāntam saṃskāra upaśamam śivam iti nirātmaka tvāt ca dharmāṇām ityādi yasya evam deśanābhiprāya anabhijña tayā saṃdehaḥ syāt  kā hi atra deśanā tattva arthā kā nu khalu ābhiprāyikī iti yaḥ ca api manda buddhi tayā neyārthām deśanām nīta arthām avagacchati tayoḥ ubhayoḥ api vineya janayoḥ ācāryaḥ  yukti āgamābhyām saṃśaya mithyā jñāna apākaraṇa artham śāstram idam ārabdhavān tatra ana svataḥ  ityādinā yuktiḥ upavarṇitā tad mṛṣā moṣa dharma yad bhagavān iti abhāṣata sarve ca moṣa dharmāṇaḥ saṃskārāḥ tena te mṛṣā pūrvā prajñāyate koṭiḥ na iti uvāca mahā muniḥ saṃsāraḥ  anavara agraḥ  hi na asti ādiḥ na api paścimam kātyāyana avavāde ca asti na asti iti ca ubhayam pratiṣiddham bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvinā ityādinā āgamaḥ  varṇitaḥ uktam ca ārya akṣayam atisūtre katame sūtrāntā neyārthāḥ katame nīta arthāḥ ye sūtrāntā mārgava tārāya nirdiṣṭāḥ ima ucyanteḥ neyārthāḥ ye sūtrāntāḥ phala avatārāya nirdiṣṭāḥ ima ucyante neyārthāḥ yāvat  ye sūtrāntāḥ śūnyatā nimitta apraṇihita anabhisaṃskāra ajāta anutpāda abhāva nirātmaniḥ sattva nirjīvaniḥ pudgalā svāmika vimokṣa mukhā nirdiṣṭāḥ ta ucyante nīta arthāḥ iyam ucyate bhadanta śāradvatī putra nīta artha sūtra anta pratiśaraṇa tā na neyārtha sūtra anta pratiśaraṇa tā iti tathā ca ārya samādhi rāja sūtre nīta artha sūtra anta viśeṣa jānati yathā upadiṣṭā sugatena śūnyatā yasmin punar  pudgala sattva pūruṣā neyārthataḥ  jānati sarva dharmān tasmāt utpāda ādi deśanām mṛṣā arthām pratipādayitum pratītyasamutpāda anudarśanam ārabdhavān ācāryaḥ nanu ca utpāda ādīnām abhāve sati yadi sarva dharmāṇām mṛṣātva pratipādana artham idam ārabdhavān ācāryaḥ nanu evam sati yad mṛṣā na tad asti iti na santi akuśalāni karmāṇi tad abhāvāt na santi durgatayaḥ na santi kuśalāni karmāṇi tad abhāvāt na santi sugatayaḥ sugati durgati asaṃbhavāt ca na asti saṃsāraḥ iti sarva ārambha vaiyarthyam eva sthāt  ucyate saṃvṛti satya vyapekṣayā lokasya idaṃsatyā abhiniveśasya pratipakṣa bhāvena mṛṣā artha tā bhāvānām pratipādyate asmābhiḥ na eva tu āryāḥ kṛta kāryāḥ kiṃcid upalabhante yad mṛṣā amṛṣā vā syāt iti api ca yena hi sarva dharmāṇām mṛṣā tvam parijñātam kim tasya karmāṇi santi saṃsāraḥ  vā asti na ca api asau kasyacid dharma ssya astitvam na astitvam vā upalabhate yathā uktam bhagavatā ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre cittam hi kāśyapa parigaveṣyamāṇam na labhyate yad na labhyate tad na upalabhyate yad na upalabhyate tad na eva atītam na anāgatam na pratyutpannam yad na eva atītam na anā gatam na pratyutpannam tasya na asti svabhāvaḥ yasya na asti svabhāvaḥ tasya na asti utpādaḥ yasya na asti utpādaḥ tasya na asti nirodhaḥ iti vistaraḥ yaḥ tu viparyāsa anugamāt mṛṣā tvam na avagacchati pratītya bhāvānā svabhāvam abhiniviśate sa dharmeṣu idaṃsatyā abhiniveśāt abhiniviṣṭaḥ san karmāṇi api karoti saṃsāre api saṃsarati viparyāsa avasthita tvāt na bhavyaḥ  nirvāṇam adhigantum kim punar  mṛṣā svabhāvā api padārthāḥ saṃkleśa vyavadāna nibandhanam bhavanti tad yathā māyā āyuvatiḥ tad svabhāva anabhijñānām tathāgata nirmitaḥ ca upacita kuśala mūlānām uktam hi dṛḍha adhyāśaya paripṛcchā sūtre tad yathā kula putra māyākāra nāṭake pratyupasthite māyā kāra nirmitām striyam dṛṣṭvā kaścid rāga parīta cittāḥ parṣad śāradya bhayena utthāya āsanāt apakrāmet  saḥ  apakramya tām eva striyam aśubha taḥ  manasikuryāt  anityataḥ  duḥkhataḥ śūnyataḥ  anātmataḥ  manasikuryāt  iti vistaraḥ vinaye ca yantra kāra kāri tā yantra yuvatiḥ sadbhūta yuvati śūnyā sadbhūta yuvati rūpeṇa pratibhāsate tasya ca citrakārasya kāma rāga āspadībhūtā tathā mṛṣā svabhāvā api bhāvā bālānām saṃkleśa vyavadāna nibandhanam bhavanti tathā ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre atha khalu tāni pañca mātrāṇi bhikṣu śatāni bhagavataḥ  dharma deśa nāmanavataranti anavagāhamānāni anadhimucyamānāni utthāya āsanebhyaḥ prakrāntāni atha bhagavān [tasyām velāyāṃ] yena mārgeṇa ete bhikṣavaḥ  gacchanti sma tasmin mārge dvau bhikṣū nirmimīte sma atha tāni pañca bhikṣu śatāni yena [mārgeṇa] tau dvau bhikṣū [nirmitakau] tena upasaṃkrāmanti sma upasaṃkramya tau  avocan kutra āyuṣmantau gamiṣyathaḥ nirmitakau  avocatām gamiṣyāva āvām araṇya āyataneṣu tatra dhyāna sukha sparśa vihāraiḥ vihariṣyāvaḥ yam hi bhagavān dharmam deśayati tam āvām na avatarāvaḥ  na avagāhāvahe na adhimucyāmahe uttrasyāvaḥ saṃtrāsam āpadyāvahe atha tāni pañca bhikṣu śatāni etad avocan vayam api āyuṣmantaḥ  bhagavataḥ  dharma deśanām na avatarāmaḥ  na avagāhāmahe na adhimucyāmahe uttrasyāmaḥ saṃtrasyāmaḥ saṃtrāsam āpadyāmahe tena vayam araṇya āyataneṣu dhyāna sukha sparśa vihāraiḥ vihariṣyāmaḥ nirmitakau  avocatām tena hi āyuṣmantaḥ saṃgāsyāmaḥ  na vivadiṣyāmaḥ avivāda paramā hi śramaṇasya dharmāḥ kasya āyuṣmantaḥ prahāṇāya pratipannāḥ tāni avocan rāga dveṣa mohānām prahāṇāya vayam pratipannāḥ nirmitakau  avocatām kim punar āyuṣmatām saṃvidyante rāga dveṣa mohā yān kṣapayiṣyatha tāni avocan na te adhyātmam na bahirdhā na ubhayam antareṇa upalabhyante na api te aparikalpitā utpadyante nirmitakau  avocatām tena hi āyuṣmantaḥ  mā kalpayata [mā vikalpayata] yadā ca āyuṣmantaḥ  na kalpayiṣyatha na vikalpayiṣyatha tadā na raṃkṣyatha na viraṃkṣyatha yaḥ ca na raktaḥ  na viraktaḥ sa śānta iti ucyate śīlam āyuṣmantaḥ  na saṃsarati na parinirvāti samādhiḥ prajñā vimuktiḥ vimukti jñāna darśanam āyuṣmantaḥ  na saṃsarati na parinirvāti ebhiḥ ca āyuṣmantaḥ  dharmaiḥ nirvāṇam sūcyate ete ca dharmāḥ śūnyāḥ prakṛti viviktāḥ prajahīta etām āyuṣmantaḥ saṃjñām yad uta parinirvāṇam iti mā ca saṃjñāyām saṃjñā kārṣṭa mā ca saṃjñāyām saṃjñām parijñāsiṣṭa yaḥ  hi saṃjñāyām saṃjñām parijānāti saṃjñā bandhanam eva asya tad bhavati saṃjñā vedayita nirodha samāpattim āyuṣmantaḥ samāpadyadhvam saṃjñā vedayita nirodha samāpatti samāpannasya bhikṣoḥ na asti uttarīkaraṇīyam iti vadāvaḥ atha teṣām pañcānām bhikṣu śatānām anupādāya āśravebhyaḥ cittāni vimuktāni abhūvan tāni vimukta cittāni yena bhagavān  tena upasaṃkrāntāni upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā abhivandya ekānte nyasīdan atha āyuṣmān subhūtiḥ tān bhikṣūn etad avocat  kutra āyuṣmantaḥ  gatāḥ kutaḥ vāgatāḥ te avocan na kvacid gamanāya na kutaścid āgamanāya bhadanta subhūte bhagavatā dharmaḥ  deśitaḥ āha kaḥ  nāma āyuṣmatām śāstā āhuḥ yaḥ  na utpannaḥ  na parinirvāsyati āha katham yuṣmābhiḥ dharmaḥ śrutaḥ āhuḥ na bandhanāya na mokṣāya āha kena yūyam vinītāḥ āhuḥ yasya na kāyaḥ  na cittam āha katham yūyam prayuktāḥ āhuḥ na avidyā prahāṇāya na vidyā utpādanāya āha kasya yūyam śrāvakāḥ āhuḥ yena na prāptam nābhisaṃbuddham āha ke yuṣmākam sabrahmacāriṇaḥ āhuḥ ye traidhātuke na upavicaranti āha kiyat cireṇa āyuṣmantaḥ parinirvāsyanti āhuḥ yadā tathāgata nirmitāḥ parinirvāsyanti āha kṛtam yuṣmābhiḥ karaṇīyam āhuḥ aham kāramamakāra parijñānataḥ āha kṣīṇā yuṣmākam kleśāḥ āhuḥ atyanta kṣayāt sarva dharmāṇām āha dharṣitaḥ  yuṣmābhiḥ māraḥ āhuḥ skandha māra an upalambhāt  āha dharṣitaḥ  yuṣmābhiḥ māraḥ āhuḥ skandha māra an upalambhāt  āha paricaritaḥ  yuṣmābhiḥ śāstā āhuḥ na kāyena na vācā na manasā āha viśodhitā yuṣmābhiḥ dakṣiṇīya bhūmiḥ āhuḥ agrāhataḥ  apratigrāhataḥ āha uttīrṇaḥ  yuṣmābhiḥ saṃsāraḥ āhuḥ anucchedataḥ  aśāśvatatas  āha pratipannā yuṣmābhiḥ dakṣiṇīya bhūmiḥ āhuḥ sarva grāha vinirmuktitaḥ āha kiṃgāmina āyuṣmantaḥ āhuḥ yaṃgāminaḥ tathāgata nirmitāḥ iti hi āyuṣmataḥ subhūteḥ paripṛcchataḥ teṣām bhikṣūṇām prativisarjayatām tasyām parṣadi aṣṭānām bhikṣu śatānām anupādāya āśravebhyaḥ cittāni vimuktāni dvātriṃśataḥ ca prāṇi sahasrāṇām virajaḥ  vigata m alam dharma cakṣuḥ viśuddham iti iti evam mṛṣā svabhāvābhyām tathāgata nirmitābhyām bhikṣubhyām pañcānām bhikṣu śatānām vyavadāna nibandhanam kṛtam iti uktam ca ārya vajramaṇḍāyām dhāraṇyām tad yathā mañjuśrīḥ kāṇḍam ca pratītya mathanīm ca pratītya puruṣasya hasta vyāyāmam ca pratītya dhūmaḥ prādurbhavati iti agniḥ abhinirvartate sa ca agni saṃtāpaḥ  na kāṇḍa saṃniśritaḥ  na mathanī saṃniśritaḥ  na puruṣa hasta vyāyāma saṃniśritaḥ evam eva mañjuśrīḥ asat viparyāsa mohitasya puruṣa pudgalasya utpadyate rāga paridāhaḥ  dveṣa paridāhaḥ  moha paridāhaḥ sa ca paridāhaḥ  na adhyātmam na bahirdhā na ubhayam antareṇa sthitaḥ api tu mañjuśrīḥ yad ucyate moha iti tad kena kāraṇena ucyate moha iti atyanta muktaḥ  hi mañjuśrīḥ sarva dharmaiḥ mohaḥ tena ucyate moha iti tathā naraka mukhā mañjuśrīḥ sarva dharmā idam dhāraṇī padam āha katham bhagavan  idam dhāraṇī padam āha narakā mañjuśrīḥ bāla pṛgtha janaiḥ asa dviparyāsa viṭhapitāḥ sva vikalpa saṃbhūtāḥ āha kutra bhagavat narakāḥ samavasaranti bhagavān āha ākāśa samavasaraṇā mañjuśrīḥ narakāḥ tad kim manyase mañjuśrīḥ sva vikalpa saṃbhūtā narakā uta svabhāva saṃbhūtāḥ āha sva vikalpena eva bhagavan sarva bāla pṛthagjanān naraka tiryagyoni yama lokam saṃjānanti te ca asat samāropeṇa duḥkhām vedanām vedayanti duḥkham anubhavanti triṣu api apāyeṣu yathā ca aham bhagavan narakān paśyāmi tathā nārakam duḥkham tad yathā bhagavan kaścid eva puruṣaḥ suptaḥ svapna antara gataḥ  naraka gatam ātmānam saṃjānīte sa tatra kvathitāyām saṃprajvalitāyām aneka pauruṣāyām loha kumbhyām prakṣiptam ātmānam saṃjānŌṣyāt  sa tatra kharām kaṭukām tŌṣu rām duḥkhām vedanām vedayet  sa tatra mānasam paridāham saṃjānŌṣyāt  uttraset  saṃtrāsam āpadyeta sa tatra pratibuddhaḥ samānaḥ ahaḥ duḥkham ahaḥ duḥkham iti krandet  śocet  paridevet  atha tasya mitra jñāti sa ālohitāḥ paripṛccheyuḥ kena tad te duḥkham iti sa tān mitra jñāti sa ālohitān evam vadet  nairayikam duḥkham anubhūtam sa tān ākrośet  paribhāṣet  aham ca nāma nairayikam duḥkham anubhavāmi yūyam ca me uttari paripṛcchatha kena etad tava duḥkham iti atha te mitra jñāti sa ālohitāḥ tam puruṣam evam vadeyuḥ mā bhairmoḥ puruṣa suptaḥ  hi tvam na tu am itas  gṛhāt  kvacid nirgataḥ tasya punar api smṛti rutpadyate suptaḥ  aham abhūvam vitatham etad mayā parikalpitam iti sa punar api saumanasyam pratilabhate tad yathā bhagavan sa puruṣaḥ  asat samāropeṇa suptaḥ svapna antara gataḥ  naraka gatam ātmānam saṃjānīyāt  evam eva bhagavan sarva bāla pṛthagjanā asat bhāga paryavanaddhāḥ strī nimittam kalpayanti te strī nimittam kalpayitvā tābhiḥ sārdham ramamāṇam ātmānam saṃjānanti tasya bāla pṛtha janasya evam bhavati aham puruṣaḥ iyam strī mama eṣā strī tasya tena cchanda rāga paryavasthitena cittena bhoga paryeṣṭim cittam krāmayanti sa tatonidānam kalaha vigraha vivādam saṃjanayati tasya praduṣṭa indriyasya vairam saṃjāyate sa tena saṃjñā viparyāsena kālagataḥ samānaḥ  bahūni kalpa sahasrāṇi narakeṣu duḥkhām vedanām vedayamānam ātmānam saṃjānāti tad yathā bhagavan tasya puruṣasya mitra jñāti sa ālohitā evam vadanti mā bhaiḥ mā bhaiḥ bhaḥ puruṣa suptaḥ  hi tvam na tu am itas  gṛhyat  kutaścid nirgataḥ iti evam eva buddhā bhagavantaḥ catur viparyāsa viparyastānām sattvānām evam dharmam deśayanti na atra strī na puruṣaḥ  na sattvaḥ  na jīvaḥ  na puruṣaḥ  na pudgalaḥ vitathā ime sarva dharmāḥ asanta ime sarva dharmāḥ viṭhapitā ime sarva dharmāḥ māyā upamā ime sarva dharmāḥ svapna upamā ime sarva dharmāḥ nirmitā upamā ime sarva dharmāḥ udaka candra upamā ime sarva dharmāḥ iti vistaraḥ te imām tathāgatasya dharma deśanām śrutvā vigata rāgān sarva dharmān paśyanti vigata mohān sarva dharmān paśyanti asvabhāvān anāvaraṇān te ākāśa sthitena cetasā kālam kurvanti te kālagatāḥ samānā nirupadhi śeṣe nirvāṇa dhātau parinirvānti evam aham bhagavan narakān paśyāmi iti uktam ca ārya upāli paripṛcchāyām bhaya darśita nairayikam me sattva sahasra sa vejita na eke na ca vidyati kaściha sattva yaḥ  cyutu gacchati ghoram apāyam na ca kāraku kāraṇa santi yehi kṛtā asi tomara śastrāḥ kalpa vaśena tu paśyati tatra kāyi patanti apāyita śastrāḥ citra manorama sajjita puṣpāḥ svarṇa vimāna jalanti manojñāḥ teṣu api kāraku na astiha kaści te api ca sthāpita kalpa vaśena kalpa vaśena vikalpitu lokaḥ saṃjña gaheṇa vikalpitu bālaḥ saḥ  ca gahaḥ  agahaḥ asa bhūtaḥ  māya marīci samā hi vikalpāḥ tad evam ete asvabhāvā bhāvāḥ sva viparyāsa viṭhapitā bālānām saṃkleśa hetavaḥ  bhavanti saṃsāre iti sthitam yathā ca mṛṣā svabhāvānām padārthānām saṃkleśa vyavadāna hetu tvam tathā madhyamaka avatārāt vistareṇa avaseyam atra āha yadi svatas  paratas  ubhayatas  ahetutaḥ ca na asti bhāvānām utpādaḥ tatra katham avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārā iti uktam bhagavatā ucyate saṃvṛtiḥ eva na tattvam kim saṃvṛteḥ vyavasthānam vaktavyam idaṃpratyaya tā mātreṇa saṃvṛteḥ siddhiḥ abhyupagamyate na tu pakṣa catuṣṭaya abhyupagamena sa svabhāva vāda prasaṅgāt  tasya ca ayukta tvāt  idaṃpratyaya tā mātra abhyupagame hi sati hetu phalayoḥ anyonya apekṣa tvāt na asti svābhāvikī siddhiḥ iti na asti sa svabhāva vādaḥ ata eva uktam svayam kṛtam para kṛtam dvābhyām kṛtam ahetukam tārkikaiḥ iṣyate duḥkham tvayā tu uktam pratītyajam iha api vakṣyati pratītya kārakaḥ karma tam pratītya ca kārakam karma pravartate na anyat paśyāmaḥ siddhi kāraṇam iti bhagavatā api etāvat mātram eva uktam tatra ayam dharma saṃketaḥ  yad uta asmin sati idam bhavati asya utpādāt idam utpadyate yad uta avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃskāra pratyayam vijñānam ityādi atra kecid paricodayanti anutpannā bhāvā iti kim ayam pramāṇa jaḥ  niścaya uta apramāṇa jaḥ tatra yadi pramāṇa ja iṣyate tadā idam vaktavyam kati pramāṇāni kiṃlakṣaṇāni kiṃviṣayāṇi kim svata utpannāni kim parata ubhayatas  ahetutaḥ  vā iti atha apramāṇa jaḥ sa na yuktaḥ pramāṇa adhīna tvāt prameya adhigamasya anadhigataḥ  hi arthaḥ  na vinā pramāṇaiḥ adhigantum śakyata iti pramāṇa abhāvāt artha adhigama abhāve sati kutaḥ ayam samyak niḥ caya iti na yuktam etad aniṣpannā bhāvā iti yatas  vāyam niścayaḥ  bhavataḥ  anutpannā bhāvā iti bhaviṣyati tatas  eva mama api sarva bhāvāḥ santi iti yathā ca ayam te niścayaḥ anutpannāḥ sarva dharmā iti tathā eva mama api sarva bhāva utpattiḥ bhaviṣyati atha te na asti niścayaḥ  anutpannāḥ sarva bhāvā iti tadā svayam aniścitasya para pratyāyana asaṃbhavāt śāstra ārambha vaiyarthyam eva iti santi apratiṣiddhāḥ sarva bhāvā iti ucyate yadi kaścid niścayaḥ  nāma asmākam syāt  sa pramāṇa jaḥ  vā syāt apramāṇa jaḥ  vā na tu asti kim kāraṇam iha aniścaya saṃbhave sati syāt tad pratipakṣaḥ tad apekṣaḥ  niścayaḥ yadā tu aniścaya eva tāvat asmākam na asti tadā kutas tad viruddha aviruddhaḥ  niścayaḥ syāt  saṃbandhi antara nirapekṣa tvāt khara viṣāṇasya hrasva dīrgha tāvat  yadā ca evam niścayasya abhāvaḥ tadā kasya prasiddhayartham pramāṇāni parikalpayiṣyāmaḥ kutaḥ vā eṣām saṃkhyā lakṣaṇam viṣayaḥ  vā bhaviṣyati svatas  parata ubhayatas  ahetutaḥ  vā samutpattiḥ iti sarvam etad na vaktavyam asmābhiḥ yadi evam niścayaḥ  na asti sarvatas  katham punar idam niścita rūpam vākyam upalabhyate bhavatām na svatas  na api paratas  na dvābhyām na api ahetutaḥ bhāvā bhavanti iti ucyate niścitam idam vākyam lokasya sva prasiddhayā eva upapattyā nāryāṇām kim khalu āryāṇām upapattiḥ na asti kena etad uktam asti vā na asti vā iti parama arthaḥ  hi āryāṇām tūṣṇīṃbhāvaḥ tatas  kutas tatra prapañca saṃbhavaḥ  yad upapattiḥ anupapattiḥ vā syāt  yadi hi āryā upapattim na varṇayanti kena khalu idānīm parama artham lokam bodhayiṣyanti na khalu āryā loka saṃvyavahāreṇa upapattim varṇayanti kim tu lokata eva yā prasiddha upapattiḥ tām para avabodha artham abhyupetya tayā eva lokam bodhayanti yathā eva hi vidyamānām api śarīra aśucitām viparyāsa anugatā rāgiṇaḥ  na upalabhante śubha ākāram ca abhūtam adhya āropya parikliśyante teṣām vairāgya artham tathāgata nirmitaḥ  devaḥ  vā śubha saṃjñayā prāk  pracchāditān kāya doṣān upavarṇayet  santi asmin kāye keśā ityādinā te ca tasyāḥ śubha saṃjñāyāḥ  vimuktā vairāgyam āsādayeyuḥ evam iha api āryaiḥ sarvathā api anupalabhyamāna ātmakam bhāvānām avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā viparītam svabhāvam adhyāropya kvacid ca kaṃcid viśeṣam atitarām parikliśyanti pṛthagjanāḥ tān idānīm āryāḥ tad prasiddhayā eva upapattyā paribodhayanti yathā vidyamānasya ghaṭasya na mṛd ādibhya utpāda iti abhyupetam evam utpādāt pūrvam vidyamānasya vidyamāna tvāt na asti utpāda iti avasīyatām yathā ca para bhūtebhyaḥ  jvālā aṅgāra ādibhyaḥ  aṅkurasya utpattiḥ na asti iti abhyupetam evam vivakṣitebhyaḥ  api bīja ādibhyaḥ  na asti iti avasīyatām atha api syāt  anubhava eṣaḥ  asmākam iti etad api uktam yasmāt anubhava eṣa mṛṣā anubhava tvāt  taimirika dvi candra ādi anubhavavat iti tatas ca anubhavasya api sādhya sama tvāt tena pratyavasthānam na yuktam iti tasmāt anutpannā bhāvā iti evam tāvat viparīta svarūpa adhyāra upapratipakṣeṇa prathama prakaraṇa ārambhaḥ idānīm kvacid yaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ  adhyāropitaḥ tad viśeṣa apākaraṇa artham śeṣa prakaraṇa ārambhaḥ gantṛ gantavya gamana ādikaḥ  api niravaśeṣaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  na asti pratītyasamutpādasya iti pratipādana artham atha syāt  eṣa eva pramāṇa premeya vyavahāraḥ  laukikaḥ  asmābhiḥ śāstreṇa anuvarṇita iti tad anuvarṇanasya tarhi phalam vācyam ku tārkikaiḥ sa nāśitaḥ  viparīta lakṣaṇa abhidhānena tasya asmābhiḥ samyak lakṣaṇam uktam iti ced  etad api ayuktam yadi hi ku tārkikaiḥ viparīta lakṣaṇa praṇayanāt kṛtam lakṣya vaiparītyam lokasya syāt  tad artham prayatna sāphalyam syāt  na ca etad evam iti vyartha eva ārya prayatna iti api ca yadi pramāṇa adhīnaḥ prameya adhigamaḥ tāni pramāṇāni kena paricchidyanta ityādinā vigraha vyāvartanyām vihitaḥ  doṣaḥ tad aparihārāt samyak lakṣaṇa dyotaka tvam api na asti kim ca yadi sva sāmānya lakṣaṇa dvaya anurodhena pramāṇa dvayam uktam yasya tad lakṣaṇa dvayam kim tad lakṣyam asti atha na asti yadi asti tadā tad aparam prameyam asti iti katham pramāṇa dvayam atha na asti lakṣyam tadā lakṣaṇam api nirāśrayam na asti iti katham pramāṇa dvayam vakṣyati hi lakṣaṇa asaṃpravṛttau ca na lakṣyam upapadyate lakṣyasya anupapattau ca lakṣaṇasya api asaṃbhavaḥ iti atha syāt  na lakṣyate anena iti lakṣaṇam kim tarhi akṛtyalyuṭaḥ  bahulam  iti karmaṇi lyuṭam kṛtvā lakṣyate tad iti lakṣaṇam evam api tena etasya lakṣyamāṇatva asaṃbhava ādyena etad lakṣyate tasya karaṇasya karmaṇaḥ  artha antara tvāt  sa eva doṣaḥ atha syāt  jñānasya karaṇa tvāt tasya ca sva lakṣaṇa antarbhāvāt ayam adoṣa iti ucyate iha bhāvānām anyāsa ādhāraṇam ātmīyam yad svarūpam tad sva lakṣaṇam tad yathā pṛthivyāḥ kāṭhinyam vedanāyāḥ  viṣaya anubhavaḥ  vijñānasya viṣaya prativijñaptiḥ tena hi tad lakṣyata iti kṛtvā prasiddha anugatām ca vyutpattim avadhūya karma sādhanam abhyupagacchati vijñānasya ca karaṇa bhāvam pratipadyamānena iti uktam bhavati sva lakṣaṇasya eva karma tā sva lakṣaṇa antarasya karaṇa bhāvaḥ ca iti tatra yadi vijñāna sva lakṣaṇam karaṇam tasya vyatiriktena karmaṇā bhavitavyam iti sa eva doṣaḥ atha syāt  yad pṛthivī ādi gatam kāṭhinya ādikam vijñāna gamyam tad tasya karma asti eva tad ca sva lakṣaṇa avyatiriktam iti evam tarhi vijñāna sva lakṣaṇasya karmatva abhāvāt prameya tvam na syāt  karma rūpasya eva sva lakṣaṇasya prameya tvāt  tatas ca dvividham prameyam sva lakṣaṇam sāmānya lakṣaṇam ca iti etad viśeṣya vaktavyam kiṃcid sva lakṣaṇam prameyam yad lakṣyata iti evam vyapadiśyate kiṃcid aprameyam yad lakṣyate anena iti vyapadiśyata iti atha tad api karma sādhanam tadā tasya anyena karaṇena bhavitavyam jñāna antarasya karaṇa bhāva parikalpanāyām anavasthā doṣaḥ ca āpadyate atha manyase sva saṃvittiḥ asti tatas tayā sva saṃvityā grahaṇāt karmatāyāḥ  satyām asti eva prameya antar bhāva iti ucyate vistareṇa madhyamaka avatāre sva saṃvitti niṣedhāt  sva lakṣaṇam sva lakṣaṇa antareṇa lakṣyate tad api sva saṃvittyā iti na yujyate api ca tad api nāma jñānam sva lakṣaṇa vyatirekeṇa asiddheḥ asaṃbhavāt lakṣya abhāve nirāśraya lakṣaṇa pravṛtti asaṃbhavāt  sarvathā na asti iti kutas  sva saṃvittiḥ tathā ca uktam ārya ratna cūḍa paripṛcchāyām sa cittam asam anupaśyan citta dhārām paryeṣate kutaścittasya utpattiḥ iti tasya evam bhavati ālambane sati cittam utpadyate tad kim anyat ālambanam anyat cittam atha yad eva ālambanam tad eva cittam yadi tāvat anyat ālambanam anyat cittam tadā dvi citta tā bhaviṣyati atha yad eva ālambanam tad eva cittam tad katham cittena cittam samanupaśyati na ca cittam cittam samanupaśyati tad yathā api nāma tayā eva asidhārayā sā eva asi dhārā na śakyate chettum na tena eva aṅgulī agreṇa tad eva aṅguli agram śakyate spraṣṭum evam eva na tena eva cittena tad eva cittam śakyam draṣṭum tasya evam yoniśas  prayuktasya yā cittasya anavasthāna tā anuccheda aśāśvata tā na kūṭastha tā na ahetukī na pratyaya viruddhā na tatas  na anyatas  na sā eva na anyā tām citta dhārām citta latām citta dharmatām citta an avasthita tām citta apracāra tām citta adṛśyatām citta sva lakṣaṇa tām tathā jānāti tathā paśyati yathā tathatām na ca nirodhayati tām ca citta viveka tām tathā prajānāti tathā paśyati iyam kula putra [bodhisattvasya] citte citta anupaśyanā smṛti upasthānam iti tad evam na asti sva saṃvittiḥ tad abhāvāt kim kena lakṣyate kim ca bhedena vā tad lakṣaṇam lakṣyāt syāt abhedena vā tatra yadi tāvat  bhedena tadā lakṣyāt  bhinna tvāt alakṣaṇavat lakṣaṇam api na lakṣaṇam lakṣaṇāt ca bhinna tvāt alakṣyavat lakṣyam api na lakṣyam tathā lakṣyāt bhinna tvāt lakṣaṇasya lakṣaṇa nirapekṣam lakṣyam syāt  tatas ca na tad lakṣyam lakṣaṇa nirapekṣa tvāt  kha puṣpavat  atha abhinne lakṣya lakṣaṇe tadā lakṣaṇāt avyatiriktattvāt lakṣaṇa sva ātmavat vihīyate lakṣyasya lakṣyatā lakṣyāt ca avyatirikta tvāt lakṣya sva ātmavat lakṣaṇam api na lakṣaṇa svabhāvam yathā ca uktam lakṣyāt lakṣaṇam anyat ced syāt tad lakṣyam alakṣaṇam tayoḥ abhāvaḥ  ananya tve vispaṣṭam kathitam tvayā iti na ca vinā tattva anya tvena lakṣya lakṣaṇa siddhau anyā gatiḥ asti tathā ca vakṣyati ekībhāvena vā siddhiḥ nānā bhāvena vā yayoḥ na vidyate tayoḥ siddhiḥ katham nu khalu vidyate iti athavā ucyate avācya tayā siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced  na etad evam avācya tā hi nāma paraspara vibhāga parijñāna abhāve sati bhavati yatra ca vibhāga parijñānam na asti tatra idam lakṣaṇam idam lakṣyam iti viśeṣataḥ pariccheda asaṃbhave sati dvayoḥ api abhāva eva iti tasmāt avācya tayā api na asti siddhiḥ api ca yadi jñānam karaṇam viṣayasya paricchede kaḥ kartā na ca kartāram antareṇa asti karaṇa ādīnām saṃbhavaḥ chidi kriyāyām iva atha cittasya tatra kartṛ tvam parikalpyate tad api na yuktam yasmāt artha mātra darśanam cittasya vyāpāraḥ artha viśeṣa darśanam caitasānām tatra artha dṛṣṭiḥ vijñānam tad viśeṣe tu caitasāḥ iti abhyupagamāt  ekasyām hi pradhāna kriyāyām sādhyāyām yathāsvam guṇa kriyā nirvṛtti dvāreṇa aṅgībhāva upagamāt karaṇa ādīnām karaṇa ādi tvam na ca iha jñāna vijñānayoḥ ekā pradhāna kriyā kim tarhi artha mātra paricchittiḥ vijñānasya pradhāna kriyā jñānasya tu artha viśeṣa pariccheda iti na asti jñānasya karaṇa tvam na api cittasya kartṛ tvam tatas ca sa eva doṣaḥ atha syāt  anātmānaḥ sarva dharmā iti āgamāt  kartuḥ sarvathā bhāvāt  kartāram antareṇa api vidyata eva kriyā ādi vya vahāra iti etad api na asti āgamasya samyak artha anavadhāraṇāt etad eva uktam madhyamaka avatāre atha api syāt  yathā śilāputrakasya śarīram rāhoḥ śiraḥ iti śarīra śiraḥ vyatirikta viśeṣaṇā saṃbhave api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ  asti evam pṛthivyāḥ sva lakṣaṇam iti sva lakṣaṇa vyatirikta pṛthivī asaṃbhave api bhaviṣyati iti na etad evam atulya tvāt  śarīra śiraḥ śabdayohi buddhayā ādi pāṇi ādivat sahabhāvi padārtha antara sā apekṣatā pravṛttau śarīraśiraḥ śabda mātra ālambanaḥ buddhayupajananaḥ sahacāri padārtha antara sā ākāṅkṣa eva vartate kasya śarīram kasya śira iti itaraḥ  api viśeṣaṇa antaraḥ saṃbandha nirācikīrṣayā śilā putra karāhu viśeṣaṇa dhvaninā laukika saṃketa anuvidhāyinā pratikartuḥ kāṅkṣām apahanti iti yuktam iha tu kāṭhinya ādi vyatirikta pṛthivī ādi asaṃbhave sati na yuktaḥ  viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ tīrthikaiḥ vyatirikta lakṣya abhyupagamāt tad anurodhena viśeṣaṇa abhidhānam aduṣṭam iti ced  na etad evam na hi tīrthika parikalpitā yukti vidhurāḥ padārthāḥ sva samaye abhyupagantum nyāyyāḥ pramāṇa antara ādeḥ api abhyugama prasaṅgāt  api ca pudgala ādi prajñaptivat  sa śarīra upādānasya śilā putrakasya upādātuḥ laukika vyavahāra aṅga bhūtasya viśeṣaṇasya avicāra prasiddhasya sadbhāvāt  śiraupādānasya ca rāhoḥ upādātuḥ sadbhāvāt ayuktam etad nidarśanam śarīra śiraḥ vyatiriktasya artha antarasya asiddheḥ tanmātrasya upalambhāt  siddham eva nidarśanam iti ced  na etad evam laukike vyavahāre ittham vicāra apravṛtteḥ avicārataḥ ca laukika padārthānām astitvāt yathā eva hi rūpa ādi vyatirekeṇa vicāryamāṇa  ātmā na saṃbhavati api ca loka saṃvṛtyā skandhān upādāya asya astitvam evam rāhu śilā putrakayoḥ api iti na asti nidarśana siddhiḥ evam pṛthivī ādīnām yadi api kāṭhinya ādi vyatiriktam vicāryamāṇam lakṣyam na asti lakṣya vyatirekeṇa ca lakṣaṇam nirāśrayam tathā api saṃvṛtiḥ eva iti paraspara apekṣayā tayoḥ siddhayā siddhim vyavasthāpayāṃbabhūvuḥ ācāryāḥ avaśyam ca etad evam abhyupeyam anyathā hi saṃvṛtiḥ upapattyā na viyujyeta tad eva tattvam eva syāt na saṃvṛtiḥ na ca upapattyā vicāryamāṇānām śilā putraka ādīm eva asaṃbhavaḥ kim tarhi vakṣyamāṇayā yuktyā rūpa vedanā ādīnām api na asti saṃbhava iti teṣām api saṃvṛtyā śilā putraka ādivat na astitvam āstheyam syāt  na ca etad evam iti asat etad  atha syāt  kim anayā sūkṣma īkṣikayā na eva hi vayam sarva pramāṇa prameya vyavahāram satyam iti ācakṣmahe kim tu loka prasiddhiḥ eṣā amunā nyāyena vyavasthāpyata iti ucyate vayam api evam brūmaḥ kim anayā sūkṣma īkṣikayā laukika vyavahāre avatārika ta yā tiṣṭhatu tāvat eṣā viparyāsa mātra āsādita ātma bhāva sattākā saṃvṛtiḥ mumukṣūṇām mokṣa āvāhaka kuśala mūla upacaya hetuḥ yāvat na tattva adhigama iti bhavān  tu etām saṃvṛti parama artha satya vibhāga durvidagdha buddhi tayā kvacid upapattim avatārya anyāyataḥ  nāśayati saḥ  aham saṃvṛti satya vyavasthāvaicakṣaṇyāt laukika eva pakṣe sthitvā saṃvṛti eka deśa nirākaraṇa upakṣipta upapatti antaram upapatti antareṇa vinivartayan loka vṛddha iva loka cārāt paribhraśyamānam bhavantam eva nivartayāmi na tu saṃvṛtim tasmāt  yadi laukikaḥ  vyavahāraḥ tadā avaśyam lakṣaṇavat lakṣyeṇa api bhavitavyam tatas ca sa eva doṣaḥ atha parama arthaḥ tadā lakṣya abhāvāt lakṣaṇa dvayam api na asti iti kutas  pramāṇa dvayam atha śabdānām evam kriyā kāraka saṃbandha pūrvikā vyutpattiḥ na aṅgīkriyate tad idam ati kaṣṭam taiḥ eva kriyā kāraka saṃbandha pravṛttaiḥ śabdaiḥ bhavān vyavaharati śabda artham kriyā karaṇa ādikam ca na icchati iti ahaḥ vata icchā mātra pratibaddha pravṛttitaḥ  vṛttiḥ bhavataḥ yadā ca evam prameya dvayam avyavasthitam tadā sva sāmānya lakṣaṇa aviṣaya tvena āgama ādīnām pramāṇa antara tvam kim ca ghaṭaḥ pratyakṣa iti evam ādikasya laukika vyavahārasya asaṃgrahāt anārya vyavahāra abhyupagamāt ca avyāpitā lakṣaṇasya iti na yuktam etad  atha syāt  ghaṭa upādāna nīla ādayaḥ pratyakṣāḥ pratyakṣa pramāṇa paricchedya tvāt  tatas ca yathā eva kāraṇe kārya upacāram kṛtvā buddhānām sukha utpāda iti vyapadiśyate evam pratyakṣa nīla ādi nimittakaḥ  api ghaṭaḥ kārye kāraṇa upacāram kṛtvā pratyakṣa iti vyapadiśyate na evaṃviṣaye upacāraḥ  yuktaḥ utpādaḥ  hi loke sukha vyatirekeṇa upalabdhaḥ sa ca saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa svabhāva tvāt aneka duṣkara śata hetu tvāt asukha eva sa sukha iti vyapadiśyamānaḥ asaṃbaddha eva iti evaṃviṣaye yukta upacāraḥ ghaṭaḥ pratyakṣa iti atra tu na hi ghaṭaḥ  nāma kaścid yaḥ apratyakṣaḥ pṛthak upalabdhaḥ  yasya upacārāt pratyakṣa tvam syāt  nīla ādi vyatiriktasya ghaṭasya abhāvāt aupacārikam pratyakṣa tvam iti ced  evam api sutarām upacāraḥ  na yuktaḥ upacaryamāṇasya āśrayasya abhāvāt  na hi khara viṣāṇe taikṣṇyam upacaryate api ca loka vyavahāra aṅga bhūtaḥ  ghaṭaḥ  yadi nīla ādi vyatiriktaḥ  na asti iti kṛtvā tasya aupacārikam pratyakṣa tvam parikalpyate nanu evam sati pṛthivī ādi vyatirekeṇa nīla ādikam api na asti iti nīla ādeḥ asi aupacārikam pratyakṣa tvam kalpyatām yathā uktam rūpa ādi vyatirekeṇa yathā kumbhaḥ  na vidyate vāyu ādi vyatirekeṇa tathā rūpam na vidyate iti tasmāt evam ādikasya loka vyavahārasya lakṣaṇena asaṃgrahāt avyāpitā eva lakṣaṇasya iti tattva vid apekṣayā hi pratyakṣa tvam ghaṭa ādīnām nīla ādīnām ca na iṣyate loka saṃvṛtyā tu abhyupagantavyam eva pratyakṣa tvam ghaṭa ādīnām yathā uktam śatake sarva eva ghaṭaḥ  adṛṣṭaḥ  rūpe dṛṣṭe hi jāyate brūyāt kaḥ tattva vid nāma ghaṭaḥ pratyakṣa iti api etena eva vicāreṇa sugandhi madhuram mṛdu pratiṣedhayitavyāni sarvāṇi uttama buddhinā iti api ca aparokṣa artha vāci tvāt pratyakṣa śabdasya sākṣāt abhimukhaḥ  arthaḥ pratyakṣaḥ pratigatam akṣam asmin  iti kṛtvā ghaṭa nīla ādīnām aparokṣāṇām pratyakṣa tvam siddham bhavati tad paricchedakasya jñānasya tṛṇa tuṣa agnivat  pratyakṣa kāraṇa tvāt  pratyakṣa tvam vyapadiśyate yaḥ tu akṣam akṣam prati vartata iti pratyakṣa śabdam vyutpādayati tasya jñānasya indriya aviṣaya tvāt  viṣaya viṣaya tvāt ca na yuktā vyutpattiḥ prativiṣayam tu syāt  pratyartham iti vā atha syāt  yathā ubhaya adhīnāyām api vijñāna pravṛtau āśrayasya paṭu mandatā anuvidhānāt  vijñānānām tad vikāra vikāri tvāt āśrayeṇa eva vyapadeśaḥ  bhavati cakṣuḥ vijñānam iti evam yadi api artham artha prati vartate tathā api akṣam akṣam āśritya vartamānam vijñānam āśrayeṇa vyapadeśāt  pratyakṣam iti bhaviṣyati dṛṣṭaḥ  hi asādhāraṇena vyapadeśaḥ  bherī śabdaḥ  yava aṅkura iti na etad pūrveṇa tulyam tatra hi viṣayeṇa vijñāne vyapadiśyamāne rūpa vijñānam iti evamādinā vijñāna ṣaṭkasya bhedaḥ  na upadarśitaḥ syāt  manaḥ vijñānasya cakṣuḥ ādi vijñānaiḥ saha eka viṣaya pravṛtta tvāt  tathā hi nīla ādi vijñāna ṣaṭke vijñānam iti ukte sa ākāṅkṣa eva pratyayāt jāyate kim etad rūpi indriya jam vijñānam āhosvit mānasam iti āśrayeṇa tu vyapadeśe manaḥ vijñānasya cakṣuḥ ādi vijñāna viṣaye pravṛtti saṃbhave api paraspara bhedaḥ siddhaḥ  bhavati iha tu pramāṇa lakṣaṇa vivakṣayā kalpanā apoḍha mātrasya pratyakṣatva abhyupagame sati vikalpāt eva tad viśeṣatva abhimata tvāt asādhāraṇa kāraṇena vyapadeśe sati na kiṃcid  prayojanam upalakṣyate prameya paratantrāyām ca pramāṇa saṃkhyā pravṛttau prameya ākāra anukāritā mātra tayā ca samāsādita ātma bhāva sattākayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ svarūpasya vyavasthāpanāt na indriyeṇa vyapadeśaḥ kiṃcid upakaroti iti sarvathā viṣayeṇa eva vyapadeśaḥ  nyāyyaḥ loke pratyakṣa śabdasya prasiddha tvāt vivakṣite arthe pratyartha śabdasya aprasiddha tvāt āśrayeṇa eva vyutpattiḥ āśrīyata iti ced  ucyate asti ayam pratyakṣa śabdaḥ  loke prasiddhaḥ sa tu yathā loke tathā asmābhirucyata eva yathā sthita laukika padārtha tiraskāreṇa tu tadvayutpāde kriyamāṇe prasiddha śabda tiraskāraḥ prasiddhaḥ syāt  tatas ca pratyakṣam iti evam na syāt  ekasya ca cakṣuḥ vijñānasya eka indriya kṣaṇa āśrayasya pratyakṣa tvam na syāt  vīpsā artha abhāvāt ekaikasya ca pratyakṣatva abhāve bahūnām api na syāt  kalpanā apoḍhasya eva ca jñānasya pratyakṣatva abhyupagamāt tena ca lokasya saṃvyavahāra abhāvāt laukikasya ca pramāṇa prameya vyavahārasya vyākhyātum iṣṭa tvāt  vyarthā eva pratyakṣa pramāṇa kalpanā saṃjāyate cakṣuḥ vijñāna sāmaṅgī nīlam jānāti naḥ tu nīlam iti ca āgamasya pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa abhidhāna arthasya aprastuta tvāt  pañcānām indriya vijñānānām jaḍatva pratipādaka tvāt ca na āgamāt api kalpanā apoḍhasya eva vijñānasya pratyakṣa tvam iti na yuktam etad  tasmāt loke yadi lakṣyam yadi vā sva lakṣaṇam sāmānya lakṣaṇam vā sarvam eva sākṣāt upalabhyamāna tvāt aparokṣam atas  pratyakṣam vyavasthāpyate tad viṣayeṇa jñānena saha dvi candra ādīnām tu ataimirika jñāna apekṣayā apratyakṣa tvam taimirika ādi apekṣayā tu pratyakṣa tvam eva parokṣa viṣayam tu jñānam sādhya avyabhicāri liṅga utpannam anumānam sākṣāt atīndriya artha vidāma āptānām yad vacanam sa āgamaḥ sādṛśyāt ananubhūta arthadhigama upamānam gauḥ iva gavaya iti yathā tad evam pramāṇa catuṣṭayāt lokasya artha adhigamaḥ  vyavasthāpyate tāni ca paraspara apekṣayā sidhyanti satsu pramāṇeṣu prameya arthāḥ satsu prameyeṣu artheṣu pramāṇāni naḥ tu khalu svābhāvikī pramāṇa prameyayoḥ siddhiḥ iti tasmāt laukikam eva astu yathādṛṣṭam iti alam prasaṅgena prastutam eva vyākhyāsyāmaḥ laukika eva darśane sthitvā buddhānām bhagavatām dharma deśanā atra āhuḥ sva yūthyāḥ yad idam uktam na svata utpadyante bhāvā iti tad yuktam svata utpatti vaiyarthyāt  yad ca uktam na dvābhyām iti tad api yuktam eka aṃśa vaikalyāt  ahetupakṣaḥ tu ekānta nikṛṣṭa iti tad pratiṣedhaḥ  api yuktaḥ yad tu khalu idam ucyate na api parata iti tad ayuktam yasmāt parabhūtā eva bhagavatā bhāvānām utpādakā nirdiṣṭāḥ catvāraḥ pratyayā hetuḥ ca ālambanam anantaram tathā eva ādhipateyam ca pratyayaḥ na asti pañcamaḥ tatra nirvartakaḥ  hetuḥ iti lakṣaṇāt  yaḥ  hi yasya nirvartakaḥ  bīja bhāvena avasthitaḥ sa tasya hetu pratyayaḥ utpadyamānaḥ  dharmaḥ  yena ālambanena utpadyate sa tasya ālambana pratyayaḥ kāraṇasya anantaraḥ  nirodhaḥ kāryasya utpatti pratyayaḥ tad yathā bījasya anantaraḥ  nirodhaḥ  aṅkurasya utpāda pratyayaḥ yasmin sati yad bhavati tad tasya ādhipateyam iti ta ete catvāraḥ pratyayāḥ ye ca anye puras jāta saha jāta paścāt jāta ādayaḥ te eteṣu eva antarbhūtāḥ īśvara ādayaḥ tu pratyayā eva na saṃbhavanti iti ata eva avadhārayati pratyayaḥ na asti pañcama iti tasmāt ebhyaḥ para bhūtebhyaḥ  bhāvānām utpattiḥ asti parata utpattiḥ iti atra ucyate na eva hi bhāvānām para bhūtebhyaḥ pratyayebhya utpattiḥ iti yasmāt  na hi svabhāvaḥ  bhāvānām pratyaya ādiṣu vidyate avidyamāne svabhāve para bhāvaḥ  na vidyate iti yadi hi hetu ādiṣu parabhuteṣu pratyayeṣu samasteṣu vyasteṣu vyasta samasteṣu hetu pratyaya sāmagyā anyatra vā kvacid  bhāvānām kāryāṇām utpādāt pūrvam sattvam syāt  syāt tebhya utpādaḥ na ca evam yad utpādāt pūrvam saṃbhavaḥ syāt  yadi syāt  gṛhyeta ca utpāda vaiyarthyam ca syāt  tasmāt nam ca asti bhāvānām pratyaya ādiṣu svabhāvaḥ avidyamāne ca svabhāve na asti para bhāvaḥ bhavanam bhāva utpādaḥ parebhya utpādaḥ para bhāvaḥ sa na vidyate tasmāt ayuktam etad  para bhūtebhyaḥ  bhāvānā mutpattiḥ iti athavā bhāvānām kāryāṇām aṅkura ādīnām vīja ādiṣu pratyayeṣu satsu vikṛta rūpeṣu na asti svabhāvaḥ  nirhetukatva prasaṅgāt  tad kim apekṣam para tvam pratyaya ādīnām vidyamānayoḥ eva hi maitra upagrāhakayoḥ paraspara apekṣam paratvam na ca evam bīja aṅkurayoḥ yaugapadyam tasmāt avidyamāne svabhāve kāryāṇām para bhāvaḥ para tvam bīja ādīnām na asti iti para vyapadeśa abhāvāt eva na parata utpāda iti tasmāt āgama abhiprāya anabhijña tā eva parasya na hi tathāgatā yukti viruddham vākyam udāharanti āgamasya ca abhiprāyaḥ prāk eva upavarṇitaḥ tad evam pratyayebhya utpāda vādini pratiṣiddhe kriyāta utpāda vādī manyate na cakṣū rūpa ādayaḥ pratyayāḥ sākṣāt vijñānam janayanti vijñāna jani kriyā niṣpādaka tvāt tu pratyayā ucyante sā ca kriyā vijñānam janayati tasmāt pratyayavatī vijñāna jani kriyā vijñāna janikā na pratyayāḥ yathā pacikriyā odanasya iti ucyate kriyā na pratyayavatī yadi kriyā kācid  syāt  sā cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ pratyayaiḥ pratyayavatī vijñānam janayet  na tu asti katham kṛtvā iha kriyā iyam iṣyamāṇā jāte vā vijñāne iṣyate ajāte vā jāyamāne vā tatra jāte na yuktā kriyā hi bhāva niṣpādikā bhāvaḥ ced niṣpannaḥ kim asya kriyayā jātasya janma punar eva ca na eva yuktam ityādinā ca madhyamaka avatāre pratipāditam etad  ajāte api na yuktā kartrā vinā janiḥ iyam na ca yukta rūpā ityādi vacanāt  jāyamāne api bhāve kriyā na saṃbhavati jāta ajāta vyatirekeṇa jāyamāna abhāvāt yathā uktam jāyamāna artha jāta tvāt jāyamānaḥ  na jāyate atha vā jāyamāna tvam sarvasya eva prasajyate iti yatas ca evam triṣu kāleṣu jani kriyāyāḥ  asaṃbhavaḥ tasmāt na asti sā ata eva āha kriyā na pratyayavatī iti viśeṣaṇam na asti vinā viśeṣam ityādinā pratipāditam etad madhyamaka avatāre na hi vandhyā putraḥ  gomān iti ucyate yadi evam apratyayavatī tarhi bhaviṣyati iti etad api ayuktam iti āha na apratyayavatī kriyā yadā pratyayavatī na asti tadā katham apratyayavatī nirhetukā syāt  na hi tantu mayaḥ paṭaḥ na yukta iti vīraṇam ayaḥ  abhyupagamyate tasmāt kriyā na bhāva janikā atra āha yadi evam kriyāyāḥ  asaṃbhavaḥ pratyayāḥ tarhi janakā bhaviṣyanti bhāvānām iti ucyate pratyayā na akriyāvantaḥ yadā kriyā na asti tadā kriyā rahitā akriyāvantaḥ  nirhetukāḥ pratyayāḥ katham janakāḥ atha kriyāvanta eva janakā iti ucyate kriyāvantaḥ ca santi uta na iti prakṛtena abhisaṃbandhaḥ uta śabdaḥ  avadhāraṇe tatra kriyāyāḥ  abhāva uktaḥ katham kriyāvat tvam pratyayānām iti yathā ca vijñāna jani kriyā uktā evam parikriyā dayaḥ  api bhāvā uktā veditavyā iti na asti kriyātaḥ api samutpattiḥ bhāvānām iti bhavati utpāda abhidhānam artha śūnyam atra āha kim na etena kriyāvantaḥ pratyayā ityādi vicāreṇa yasmāt cakṣuḥ ādīn pratītya pratyayān vijñānāt ayaḥ  bhāvā jāyante tasmāt cakṣuḥ ādīnām pratyaya tvam tebhyaḥ ca utpādaḥ  vijñāna ādīnām iti etad api ayuktam iti āha utpadyate pratītyemān itīme pratyayāḥ kila yāvat na utpadyata ime tāvat na apratyayāḥ katham yadi cakṣuḥ ādīn pratyayān pratītya vijñānam utpadyate iti asya ime pratyayā ucyante nanu yāvat tad vijñāna ākhyam kāryam na utpadyate tāvat ime cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ katham na apratyayāḥ apratyayā eva iti abhiprāyaḥ na ca apratyayebhya utpattiḥ sikatābhya iva tailasya atha matam pūrvam apratyayāḥ santaḥ kiṃcid anyam pratyayam apekṣya pratyaya tvam pratipadyanta iti etad api ayuktam yad  tad  pratyaya antaram apratyayasya tasya pratyaya tvena kalpyate tad api pratyaya tve sati asya pratyayaḥ bhavati tatra api eṣā eva cintana iti na yuktam etad  kim ca iha ime cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ vijñānasya pratyayāḥ kalpyamānāḥ sataḥ  vā asya kalpyeran asataḥ  vā sarvathā ca na yujyate iti āha na eva asataḥ  na eva sataḥ pratyayaḥ arthasya yujyate kasmāt iti āha asataḥ pratyayaḥ kasya sataḥ ca pratyayena kim asataḥ  hi arthasya avidyamānasya katham pratyayaḥ syāt  bhaviṣyatā vyapadeśaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti ced  na evam bhaviṣyatā ced vaya padeśa iṣṭaḥ śaktim vinā na asti hi bhāvitāsya ityādinā ukta doṣa tvāt sataḥ  api vidyamānasya labdha janmanaḥ  niṣphalā eva pratyaya kalpanā evam samastānām pratyayānām kārya utpādana asāmarthyena apratyaya tvam udbhāvya atas  param vyastānām apratyaya tvam pratipādyate atra āha yadi api evam pratyayānām asaṃbhavaḥ tathā api asti eva lakṣaṇa upadeśāt pratyaya prasiddhiḥ tatra nirvartakaḥ  hetuḥ iti lakṣaṇam ucyate hetu pratyayasya na ca avidyamānasya lakṣaṇa upadeśaḥ  yuktaḥ  bandhyā sutasya iva iti ucyate syāt hetu pratyayaḥ yadi tasya lakṣaṇam syāt  yasmāt  na san  āsanna sat asan dharmaḥ  nirvartate yadā katham nirvartakaḥ  hetuḥ evam sati hi yujyate tatra nirvartaka utpādakaḥ yadi nirvartyaḥ  dharmaḥ  nirvarteta tam utpādakaḥ  hetuḥ utpādayet  na tu nirvartate sat asat ubhaya rūpasya nirvartyasya abhāvāt  tatra sanna nirvartate vidyamāna tvāt  asan  api avidyamāna tvāt  sadasan  api paraspara viruddhasya eka arthasya abhāvāt  ubhaya pakṣa abhihita doṣa tvāt ca yata evam kāryasya utpattiḥ na asti hetu pratyayaḥ api atas  na asti tatas ca yad uktam lakṣaṇa saṃbhavāt vidyate hetu pratyaya iti tad evam sati na yujyate idānīm ālambana pratyaya niṣedha artham āha anālambana eva ayam san dharma upadiśyate atha anālambane dharme kuta ālambanam punar  iha sa ālambana dharmāḥ katame sarva citta caittā iti āgamāt  citta caittā yena ālambanena utpadyante yathāyogam rūpa ādinā sa teṣām ālambana pratyayaḥ ayam ca vidyamānānām vā parikalpyeta avidyamānānām vā tatra vidyamānānām na arthaḥ tad ālambana pratyayena dharmasya hi utpatti artham ālambanam parikalpyate sa ca ālambanāt pūrvam vidyamāna eva iti atha evam anālambane dharme sva ātmanā prasiddhe kim asya ālambana yogena parikalpitena iti anālambana eva ayam san vidyamānaḥ  dharmaḥ citta ādikaḥ kevalam sa ālambana iti ucyate bhavadbhiḥ sva manīṣikayā na tu asya ālambanena kaścid saṃbandhaḥ  asti atha avidyamānasya ālambanam parikalpyate tad api na yuktam anālambana eva ayam ityādi avidyamānasya hi na asti ālambanena yogaḥ anālambana eva ayam san dharma upadiśyate bhavadbhiḥ sa ālambana iti vākya śeṣaḥ atha anālambane dharme kuta ālambanam punar  atha śabdaḥ praśne kuta iti hetau tena ayam arthaḥ atha evam anālambane dharme asati avidyamāne bhūyas  kuta ālambanam ālambanaka abhāvāt ālambanasya api abhāva iti abhiprāyaḥ katham tarhi sa ālambanāḥ citta caittāḥ sāṃvṛtam etad lakṣaṇam na pārama arthi kam ityadoṣaḥ idānīm samanantara pratyaya niṣedha artham āha anutpanneṣu dharmeṣu nirodhaḥ  na upapadyate na anantaramatas  yuktam niruddhe pratyayaḥ ca kaḥ tatra paścime ślokasya ardhe pādavyatyayaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ caśabdaḥ ca bhinna kramaḥ  niruddhe ca iti tena evam pāṭhaḥ niruddhe ca pratyayaḥ kaḥ na anantaramatas  yuktam iti śloka bandha artham tu evam uktam tatra kāraṇasya anantaraḥ  nirodhaḥ kāryasya utpāda pratyayaḥ samanantara pratyaya lakṣaṇam atra vicāryate anutpanneṣu dharmeṣu kārya bhūteṣu aṅkura ādiṣu nirodhaḥ  na upapadyate kāraṇasya bīja ādeḥ yadā etad evam tadā kāraṇasya nirodha abhāvāt aṅkurasya kaḥ samanantara pratyayaḥ atha anutpanne api kārye bīja nirodha iṣyate evam sati niruddha bīje abhāvībhūte aṅkurasya kaḥ pratyayaḥ kaḥ  vā bīja nirodhasya pratyaya iti ubhayam etad ahetukam iti āha niruddhe ca kaḥ pratyaya iti caśabdaḥ  anutpanna śabda apekṣaḥ tena anutpanne ca aṅkure bīja ādīnām nirodhe iṣyamāṇe api ubhayam etad ahetukam apadyata iti na anantaramatas  yuktam atha vā na svatas  na api parata ityādinā utpādaḥ  niṣiddhaḥ tam abhisaṃdhāya āha anutpanneṣu dharmeṣu nirodhaḥ  na upapadyate na anantaramatas  yuktam iti api ca niruddhe pratyayaḥ ca kaḥ iti atra pūrvakam eva vyākhyānam idānīm adhipati pratyaya svarūpa niṣedha artham āha bīja ādīnām bhāvānām niḥsvabhāvānām na sattā vidyate yatas  sati idam asmin bhavati iti etad na eva upapadyate iha yasmin sati yad bhavati tad tasya ādhipateyam iti adhipati pratyaya lakṣaṇam bhāvānām ca pratītyasamutpanna tvāt  svabhāva abhāve kutas tada yad asmin  iti kāraṇa tvena vyapadiśyate kutas tad  yad idam iti kāryatvena tasmāt na asti lakṣaṇataḥ  api pratyaya siddhiḥ atra āha tantu ādibhyaḥ paṭa ādikam upalabhya paṭa ādeḥ tantu ādayaḥ pratyayā iti ucyate paṭa ādi phala pravṛttiḥ eva svarūpataḥ  na asti kutas  pratyayānām pratyaya tvam setsyati yathā ca paṭa ādi phala pravṛttiḥ asatī tathā pratipādayan  āha na ca vyasta samasteṣu pratyayeṣu asti tad phalam pratyayebhyaḥ katham tad ca bhavet na pratyayeṣu yad  tatra vyasteṣu tantu turī vemata sara śalāka ādiṣu pratyayeṣu paṭaḥ na asti tatra anupalabhyamāna tvāt  kāraṇa bahu tvāt ca kārya bahutva prasaṅgāt  samuditeṣu api tantu ādiṣu na asti paṭaḥ pratyekam avayaveṣu avidyamāna tvāt  ekasya kāryasya khaṇḍaśa utpatti prasaṅgāt  tasmāt phala abhāvāt na santi pratyayāḥ svabhāvata iti atha asat api tad tebhyaḥ pratyayebhyaḥ pravartate iti abhiprāyaḥ syāt  apratyayebhyaḥ  api kasmāt phalam na abhipravartate apratyayeṣu api na asti phalam iti apratyayebhyaḥ  api vīraṇa ādibhyaḥ kasmāt na abhipravartate paṭa iti na asti phala pravṛttiḥ svarūpataḥ atra āha yadi anyat  phalam syāt anye ca pratyayāḥ tadā kim pratyayeṣu phalam asti na asti iti cintā syāt  na asti tu vyatiriktam phalam kim tarhi pratyaya mayam eva iti ucyate phalam ca pratyaya mayam pratyayāḥ ca asvayaṃmayāḥ phalam asvamayebhyaḥ  yad tad pratyaya mayam katham yadi pratyaya mayam pratyaya vikāraḥ phalam iti vyavasthāpyate tad ayuktam yasmāt te api pratyayā asvayaṃmayā apratyaya svabhāvā iti arthaḥ tantum ayaḥ  hi paṭa iti ucyate syāt  paṭaḥ yadi tantava eva svabhāva siddhāḥ syuḥ te hi aṃśumayā aṃśu vikārā na svabhāva siddhāḥ tatas ca tebhyaḥ  asvayaṃmayebhyaḥ  asvabhāvebhyaḥ  yad phalam paṭa ākhyam tad katham tantu mayam bhaviṣyati yathā uktam paṭaḥ kāraṇataḥ siddhaḥ siddham kāraṇam anyatas  siddhiḥ yasya svatas  na astaḥ  tad anyat janayet katham iti tasmāt na pratyaya mayam phalam saṃvidyate apratyaya mayam tarhi astu na apratyaya mayam phalam saṃvidyate iti tantum ayaḥ  yadā paṭaḥ na asti tadā katham vīraṇa mayaḥ syā atra āha mā bhūt phalam pratyaya apratyaya niyamaḥ tu vidyate tathā ca bhavān bravīti yadi asat  phalam pratyayebhyaḥ pravartate apratyayebhyaḥ  api kasmāt na abhipravartate iti na ca asati phale paṭakaṭākhye tantu vīraṇānām pratyayānām pratyaya tvam yuktam atas  phalam api asti iti ucyate syāt phalam yadi pratyaya apratyayā eva syuḥ sati hi phale ime asya pratyayā ime apratyayā iti syāt  tad ca vicāryamāṇam na asti iti phala abhāvāt pratyaya apratyayāḥ kutas  pratyayāḥ ca apratyayāḥ ca iti samāsaḥ tasmāt na asti bhāvānām svabhāvataḥ samutpattiḥ iti yathā uktam ārya ratnākara sūtre śūnya vidya na hi vidyate kvaci antarīkṣi śakunasya vā padam yaḥ  na vidyati sa bhāvataḥ kvaci saḥ  na jātu para hetu bheṣyati yasya na eva hi sabhāvu labhyati saḥ  asvabhā  u para paccayaḥ katham asvabhā  u paru kim janīṣyati eṣa hetu sugatena deśitaḥ sarva dharma acalā dṛḍham sthitā nirvikāra nirupadravāḥ śivāḥ antarīkṣa patha tulya ajānakā tatra muhyati jagam ajānakam śailaparvata yathā akampiyā evam dharma avikampiyāḥ sadā naḥ cyavati na pi ca upapadyayu evam dharmata jinena deśitā ityādi tathā yaḥ  na pi jāyati nā cupapadyī naḥ cyavate na pi jīryati dharmaḥ tam jinu deśayatī narasiṃhaḥ tatra niveśayi sattva śatāni yasya sabhāvu na vidyati kaści naḥ para bhāvatu kenaci labdhaḥ na antarataḥ na pi bāhiratas  vā labhyati tatra niveśayi nāthaḥ śānta gatī kathitā sugatena naḥ ca gati upalabhyati kāci tatra ca voharasī gati muktaḥ  mukta ku mocayamī bahu sattvān iti vistaraḥ iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau pratyaya parīkṣā nāma prathamam prakaraṇam gatāgata parīkṣā dvitīyam prakaraṇam atra āha yadi api utpāda pratiṣedhāt pratītya samutpādasya anirodha ādi viśeṣaṇa siddhiḥ tathā api anāgama nirgama pratītyasamutpāda siddhaye loka prasiddha gamana āgamana kriyā pratiṣedha artham kiṃcid upapatti antaram ucyatām iti ucyate yadi gamanam nāma syāt niyatam tad gate vā adhva jāte parikalpyeta agate gamyamāne vā sarvathā ca na yujyate iti āha gatam na gamyate tāvat agatam na eva gamyate gatāgata vinirmuktam gamyamānam na gamyate tatra uparata gami kriyam adhvajātam gatam iti ucyate āviśyamānam gami kriyayā vartamānam gamyata iti ucyate yad gatam uparata gami kriyam tad vartamāna gami kriyā yoga vācinā gamyate iti anena śabdena ucyamānam asaṃbaddham iti kṛtvā gatam tāvat  gamyata iti na yujyate tāvat śabdena ca pratiṣedha kramam darśayati agatam api na gamyate agatam hi anupajāta gami kriyam anāgatam ucyate gamyata iti ca vartamānam atas  anāgata vartamānayoḥ atyanta bhedāt agatam api gamyata iti na yujyate yadi agatam katham gamyate atha gamyate na tad agatam iti gamyamāne api na asti gamanam yasmāt  gatāgata vinirmuktam gamyamānam na gamyate iha hi gantā yam deśam atikrāntaḥ sa tasya deśaḥ  gataḥ yam ca na atikrāntaḥ saḥ  asya anāgataḥ na ca gatāgata vyatirekeṇa tṛtīyam aparama dhvajātam paśyāmaḥ  gamyamānam nāma yatas ca evam gamyamānam na gamyate gamyata iti na prajñāyate tasmāt na asti gamyamānam atas  na tad  gami kriyayā āviśyate na gamyata iti na asti gamyamāne api gamanam atha syāt  gantuḥ gacchataḥ  yaḥ caraṇa ākrāntaḥ  deśaḥ sa gamyamānaḥ syāt iti na evam caraṇayoḥ api paramāṇu sāṃghāta tvāt  aṅguli agra avasthitasya paramāṇoḥ yaḥ pūrvaḥ deśaḥ sa tasya gate antargataḥ pārṣṇi avasthitasya caram aparamāṇoḥ ya uttaraḥ  deśaḥ sa tasya agate antargataḥ na ca paramāṇu vyatirekeṇa caraṇam asti tasmāt na asti gatāgata vyatirekeṇa gamyamānam yathā ca evam caraṇe vicāraḥ evam paramāṇūnām api pūrva apara diś bhāga saṃbandhena vicāraḥ kārya iti atha ardha gatam gamyamānam uktam uttaram jāyamāna vicāreṇa tasmāt gamyamānam na gamyate iti siddham tatra āha gamyata eva gamyamānam iha hi ceṣṭā yatra gatiḥ tatra gamyamāne ca sā yatas  na gate na āgate ceṣṭā gamyamāne gatiḥ tatas  tatra ceṣṭā caraṇa utkṣepa parikṣepa lakṣaṇā yatas  vrajataḥ  gantuḥ yatra deśe ceṣṭā gatiḥ tatra eva deśe sā ca ceṣṭā na gate adhvani saṃbhavati na api agate kim tu gamyamāna eva tatas ca gamyamāne gatiḥ yatra hi gatiḥ upalabhyate tad gamyamānam tad ca gami kriyayā āviśyate tasmāt  gamyamānam eva gamyate iti ekaḥ  atra gamiḥ jñāna arthaḥ aparaḥ ca deśa antara saṃprāpti artha iti evam api parikalpyamāne gamyamānam na gamyata iti āha gamyamānasya gamanam katham nāma upapatsyate gamyamāne dvi gamanam yadā na eva upapadyate iha hi gami kriyā yogāt eva gamyamāna vyapadeśam icchati bhavān tad ca iti gamyata bravīti ekā ca atra gami kriyā tayā gamyamāna vyapadeśaḥ  bhavatu kāmam adhvanaḥ gamyata iti bhūyas  kriyā saṃbandhaḥ  gamyamānasya na yujyata iti gamyamānasya gamanam katham nāma upapatsyate kāraṇam āha gamyamāne dvi gamanam yadā na eva upapadyate iti gamyamānam iti gamyata iti arthaḥ dvi gatam gamanam dvi gamanam ekasya gami kriyāyāḥ  gamyamānam iti atra upayukta tvāt  dvitīyāyāḥ  abhāvāt ca gamyata iti ayam vyapadeśaḥ  vinā gamanena yadā na eva upapadyate tadā gamyamānam gamyata iti paripūrṇaḥ  vākya arthaḥ  na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ gamyamānam iti etāvat mātram eva saṃbhavati dvitīya kriyā bhāvāt na tu gamyata iti atha gamyate iti atra eva gami kriyā saṃbandha iṣyate evam sati gamyamāna vyapadeśe na asti kriyā saṃbandha iti na paripūrṇa tā vākya arthasya iti āha gamyamānasya gamanam yasya tasya prasajyate ṛte gateḥ gamyamānam gamyamānam hi gamyate yasya vādinaḥ  gamyamānasya gamanam iti pakṣaḥ gamyamāne saṃjñā bhūte gami kriyā śūnye yaḥ  gamikriyām ādheya bhūtām icchati tasya pakṣe ṛte gateḥ gamyamānam iti prasajyate gati rahitam gamanam syāt  yasmāt asya gamyamānam hi gamyate hi śabdaḥ  yasmāt arthe yasmāt  gati rahitam eva gamyamānam sat  tasya vādinaḥ  gamyate gamyata iti atra kriyā upayogāt  tasmāt  gati rahitam gamanam prasajyate atha ubhayatra api kriyā saṃbandha iṣyate gamyamāne gamyate iti atra ca evam api gamyamānasya gamane prasaktam gamana dvayam yena tad gamyamānam ca yad ca atra gamanam punar  yena gamanena yogāt gamyamāna vyapadeśam pratilabhate adhvā tad ekam gamanam tatra gamyamāne adhikaraṇa bhute dvitīyam gamanam yena saḥ  adhvā gamyate etad gamana dvayam gamyamānasya gamane sati prasaktam bhavatu gamana dvayam kaḥ  doṣa iti ced  ayam doṣaḥ yasmāt  dvau gantārau prasajyete prasakte gamana dvaye kim punar  kāraṇam gantṛ dvaya prasaṅge iti āha gantāram hi tiraskṛtya gamanam na upapadyate yasmāt avaśyam kriyā sva sādhanam apekṣate karma kartāram vā gami kriyā ca evam kartari avasthitā atas  gantāram apekṣate na asti ca ekasmin  eva gacchati devadatte dvitīyaḥ kartā iti atas  kartṛ dvaya abhāvāt na asti gamana dvayam tatas ca gamyamānam gamyata iti na upapadyate atha syāt  yadā ayam devadattaḥ sthitaḥ sa na bhāṣate paśyati na tadā ekaḥ aneka kriyaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ evam ekasmin gantari kriyā dvayam bhaviṣyati iti na evam śaktiḥ hi kārakaḥ  na dravyam kriyā bhedāt ca tad sādhanasya api śakteḥ siddha eva bhedaḥ na hi sthiti kriyayā vaktā syāt  dravyam ekam iti ced  bhavatu evam na tu dravyam kārakaḥ kim tarhi śaktiḥ sā ca bhidyata eva api ca sadṛśa kriyā dvaya kāraka tvam na eka deśikasya dṛṣṭam atas  na ekasya gantuḥ gamana dvayam atra āha yadi api evam tathā api gantari devadatte gamanam upalabhyate devadattaḥ  gacchati iti vyapadeśāt  tatas ca vidyata eva gamanam gamana āśraya gantṛ sadbhāvāt ucyate syāt evam yadi gamana āśrayaḥ  gantā syāt  na tu asti katham iti āha gantāram cetiraskṛtya gamanam na upapadyate gamane asati gantātha kuta eva bhaviṣyati gantāram antareṇa nirāśrayam gamanam asat iti uktam tatas ca gantāram cetiraskṛtya pratyākhyāya gamanam na asti asati gamane kutaḥ nirhetukaḥ  gantā atas  na asti gamanam atra āha vidyata eva gamanam tadvataḥ tena vyapadeśāt  iha gantā gamanena yuktaḥ tad yogāt ca gacchati yadi gamanam na syāt  gamanavataḥ  devadattasya gacchati iti vyapadeśaḥ  na syāt  daṇḍa abhāve daṇḍi vyapadeśa abhāvavat  ucyate syāt gamanam yadi gacchati iti evam vyapadeśaḥ syāt  yasmāt  gantā na gacchati tāvat agantā na eva gacchati anyaḥ  gantuḥ agantuḥ ca kaḥ tṛtīyaḥ  hi gacchati iha gacchati iti gantā sa tāvat na gacchati yathā ca na gacchati tathā uttareṇa śloka trayeṇa pratipādayiṣyati agantā api na gacchati agantā hi nāma yaḥ  gami kriyā rahitaḥ gacchati iti ca gami kriyā yoga pravṛttaḥ śabdaḥ yadi asā avagantā katham gacchati atha gacchati na asau agantā iti tad ubhaya vyatiriktaḥ  gacchati iti ced na evam kaḥ  hi gantuḥ agantuḥ vinirmuktaḥ tṛtīyaḥ  asti yaḥ  gacchati iti kalpyeta tasmāt na asti gamanam atra āha na āgantā gacchati na api ubhaya rahitaḥ kim tarhi gantā eva gacchati iti etad api asat kim kāraṇam yasmāt  gantā tāvat gacchati iti katham eva upapatsyate gamanena vinā gantā yadā na eva upapadyate gantā gacchati iti atra vākye ekā eva gami kriyā tayā ca gacchati iti vyapadiśyate gantā iti tu vyapadeśe na asti dvitīyā gami kriyā iti gamanena vinā gantā
