agacchan gantā iti yadā na saṃbhavati tadā gantā gacchati iti na yujyate kāmam gacchati iti astu gantā iti tu na saṃbhavati iti tad ayuktam atha gati yogāt sa gatika eva gantā tathā api dvitīya gami kriyā abhāvat gacchati iti vyapadeśaḥ  na syāt iti āha pakṣaḥ  gantā gacchati iti yasya tasya prasajyate gamanena vinā gantā gantuḥ gamanam icchataḥ yasya vādinaḥ  gami kriyā yogāt eva gantā iti pakṣaḥ tasya gantuḥ gamanam icchataḥ sa gamana gantṛ vyapadeśāt gamanena vinā gantā gacchati iti syāt  dvitīya gami kriyā bhāvāt  atas  gantā gacchati iti na yujyate gacchati iti etasya arthe gantā iti śabdaḥ  gamanena vinā gantā iti atra vākye atha ubhayatra api gati yoga iṣyate gantā gacchati iti evam api gamane dve prasajyete gantā yadi uta gacchati gantā iti ca ucyate yena gantā san yad ca gacchati yena gamanena yogāt  gantā iti ucyate vyapadiśyate tad ekam gamanam gantā bhavan yad ca gacchati yām ca gati kriyām karoti tad etad gamana dvayam prasaktam atas  gantṛ dvaya prasaṅga iti pūrvavat  dūṣaṇam vaktavyam tasmāt na asti gacchati iti vyapadeśaḥ atra āha yadi api evam tathā api devadattaḥ  gacchati iti vyapadeśa sadbhāvāt gamanasti iti na evam yasmāt devadatta āśraya eva eṣā cintā kim asau gantā san gacchati uta agantā gacchati tad vayatiriktaḥ  vā iti sarvathā ca na upapadyata iti yad kiṃcid etad  atra āha vidyata eva gamanam tad ārambha sadbhāvāt iha devadattaḥ sthiti upamardena gamanam ārabhate na ca avidyamāna kūrma roma prāvāra ādikam ārabhate ucyate syāt gamanam yadi tad āramme eva syāt  yasmāt  gate na ārabhyate gantum gatam na ārabhyate agate na ārabhyate gamyamāne gantum ārabhyate kuha yadi gamana ārambhaḥ  bhavet  tad  gate vā adhvanyāramyeta agate vā gamyamāne vā tatra gate gamanam na ārabhyate tad hi nāma uparata gami kriyam yadi tatra gamanam ārabhyeta tad  gatam iti evam na syāt  atīta vartamānayoḥ virodhāt  agate api gamanam na ārabhyate anāgata vartamānayoḥ virodhāt  na api gamyamāne tad abhāvāt kriyā dvaya prasaṅgāt  kartṛ dvaya prasaṅgāt ca tad evam sarvatra gamana ārambham apaśyan  āha gantum ārabhyate kuha iti yathā ca gamanam na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha na pūrvam gamana ārambhāt gamyamānam na vā gatam yatra ārabhyeta gamanam agate gamanam kutas  iha devadattaḥ  yadā avasthita āste sa tadā gamanam na ārabhate tasya gamana ārambhāt pūrvam na gamyamānam adhu ajātam asti na ca gatam yatra gamanam ārabhyeta tasmāt  gata gamyamāna abhāvāḥ t enayoḥ na gamana ārambhaḥ atha syāt  yadi api gamana ārambhāt pūrvam na gatam na gamyamānam tathā api agatam asti tatra gamana ārambhaḥ syāt iti ucyate agate gamanam kutas  anupajāta gami kriyam anārabdha gami kriyama gatam tatra gamana ārambha iti asaṃbaddham etad iti āha agate gamanam kutas  iti yadi api gatāgata gamyamāneṣu gamana ārambhaḥ  na asti gatāgata gamyamānāni tu santi na ca asati gamane etāni yujyanta iti ucyate syāt  gamanam yadi etāni eva syuḥ sati hi gami kriyā prārambhe yatra uparatā gami kriyā tad  gatam iti parikalpyeta yatra vartamānā tad  gamyamānam yatra ajātā tad agatam iti yadā tu gami kriyā prārambha eva na asti tadā gatam kim gamyamanam kim agatam kim vikalpyate adṛśyamāna ārambhe gamanasya eva sarvathā prārambhe anupalabhyamāne kim mithyā adhva trayam parikalpyate kutaḥ vā tadvayapadeśa kāraṇam gamanam iti ayuktam etad  atra āha vidyata eva gamanam tad pratipakṣa sadbhāvāt yasya ca pratipakṣaḥ  asti tad asti āloka andhakāravat pārāvāravat  saṃśaya niścayavat ca asti ca gamanasya pratipakṣaḥ sthānam iti ucyate syāt  gamanam yadi tad pratipakṣaḥ sthānam syāt  katham iha idam sthānam gantuḥ agantuḥ tad anyasya vā parikalpyeta sarvathā ca na yujyata iti āha gantā na tiṣṭhati tāvat agantā na eva tiṣṭhati anyaḥ  gantuḥ agantuḥ ca kaḥ tṛtīyaḥ  atha tiṣṭhati yathā gantā na tiṣṭhati tathā uttareṇa ślokena ākhyāsyati agantā api na tiṣṭhati sa hi tiṣṭhati eva tasya kim aparayā sthityā prayojanam agantā api na tiṣṭhati sa hi tiṣṭhati eva tasya kim aparayā sthityā prayojanam ekayā sthityā agantā aparayā tiṣṭhati iti sthiti dvaya prasaṅgāt  sthātṛ dvaya prasaṅga iti pūrvavat doṣaḥ gantra gantṛ rahitaḥ ca anyaḥ  na asti atra āha na āgantā tiṣṭhati na api gantuḥ agantuḥ ca anyaḥ kim tarhi gantā eva tiṣṭhati iti na evam yasmāt  gantā tāvat tiṣṭhati iti katham eva upapatsyate gamanena vinā gantā yadā na eva upapadyate yadā ayam tiṣṭhati iti ucyate tadā sthiti virodhi gamanam asya na asti vinā ca gamanam gantṛ vyapadeśaḥ  na asti atas  gantā tiṣṭhati iti na upapadyate atra āha vidyata eva gamanam tad nivṛtti sadbhāvāt iha gateḥ nivartamānaḥ sthitim ārabhate gamana abhāve tu na tatas  nivarteta ucyate syāt  gamanam yadi tad nivṛttiḥ eva syāt  [na tvasti] yasmāt  na tiṣṭhati gamyamānān na gatāt na āgatāt api tatra gantā gatāt adhvanaḥ  na nivartate gati abhāvāt  agatāt api gati abhāvāt eva gamyamānāt api na nivartate tad anupalabdheḥ gami kriyā bhāvāt ca tasmāt na gati nivṛttiḥ atra āha yadi gamana pratidvan dvi sthiti abhāvāt gatiḥ asatī evam tarhi gamana prasiddhaye sthiti sādhayāmaḥ tad siddhau gamana siddhiḥ tasmāt vidyata eva sthānam pratidvandvi sadbhāvāt  sthiteḥ hi pratidvandvi gamanam tad asti tatas ca sthitiḥ api pratidvandvi sadbhāvāt  etad api ayuktam yasmāt  gamanam saṃpravṛttiḥ ca nivṛttiḥ ca gateḥ samā atra hi yad gamanam sthiti siddhaye varṇitam tad gatyā samam gati dūṣaṇena tulyam iti arthaḥ yathā gantā na tiṣṭhati tāvat ityādinā gati prasiddhaye sthiteḥ hetu tvena upāttāyā dūṣaṇam uktam evam iha api sthiti prasiddhaye gamanasya hetu tvena upāttasya sthātā na gacchati tāvat ityādinā śloka dvaya pāṭha parivartena dūṣaṇam vaktavyam iti na asti gamanam tad abhāvāt pratidvandvinī sthitiḥ api iti evam tāvat  gamanam gatyā tulyam pratyākhyeyam atha syāt  vidyata eva sthānam tad ārambha sadbhāvāt iha gati upamardena sthānam ārabhyate katham tad na syāt  ucyate saṃpravṛttiḥ ca gateḥ samā vācyā tatra yathā pūrvam gate na ārabhyate gantum ityādinā gamana ārambhaḥ  niṣiddhaḥ evam iha api sthite na ārabhyate sthātum sthātum na ārabhyate asthite na ārabhyate sthīyamāne sthātum ārabhyate kuha ityādinā śloka traya parivartena sthāna saṃpravṛttiḥ api gateḥ samā sthāna nivṛttiḥ api gati nivṛttyā samā pratyākhyeyā yathā gati niṣedhe na tiṣṭhati gamyamānān na gatāt na āgatāt api iti gateḥ dūṣaṇam uktam evam sthiti niṣedhe api na gacchati sthīyamānān na sthita anna āsthitāt api iti gatyā tulyam dūṣaṇam iti na asti sthitiḥ tad abhāvāt kutaḥ gati pratipakṣa sthiti sadbhāva vādinām gateḥ siddhiḥ iti api ca yadi gamanam syāt  gantṛ vyatirekeṇa vā syāt avyatirekeṇa vā sarvathā ca vicāryamāṇam na saṃbhavati iti āha yad eva gamanam gantā sa eva iti na yujyate anya eva punar gantā gateḥ iti na yujyate katham punar na yujyata iti āha yad eva gamanam gantā sa eva hi bhavet yadi ekībhāvaḥ prasajyeta kartuḥ karmaṇa eva ca yā iyam gami kriyā sā yadi gantuḥ avyatiriktā na anyā syāt  tadā kartuḥ kriyāyāḥ ca eka tvam syāt  tatas ca iyam kriyā ayam kartā iti viśeṣaḥ  na syāt  na ca chidi kriyāyāḥ chettuḥ ca eka tvam atas  yad eva gamanam sa eva gantā iti na yujyate anyatram api gantṛ gamanayoḥ yathā na asti tathā pratipādayan  āha anya eva punar gantā gateḥ yadi vikalpyate gamanam syāt ṛte gantuḥ gantā syāt gamanāt ṛte yadi hi gantṛ gamanayoḥ anya tvam syāt  tadā gamana nirapekṣaḥ  gantā syāt  gantṛ nirapekṣam ca gamanam gṛhyeta pṛthak  siddham ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ na ca gantuḥ pṛthak siddham gamanam gṛhyata iti anya eva punar gantā gateḥ iti na yujyate iti prasādhitam etad  tad evam ekībhāvena vā siddhiḥ nānā bhāvena vā yayoḥ na vidyate tayoḥ siddhiḥ katham nu khalu vidyate yayoḥ gantṛ gamanayoḥ yathā udita nyāyena ekībhāvena vā nānā bhāvena vā na asti siddhiḥ tayoḥ idānīm kena anyena prakāreṇa siddhiḥ astu ata āha tayoḥ siddhiḥ katham nu khalu vidyata iti na asti gantṛ gamanayoḥ siddhiḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ atra āha iha devadattaḥ  gantā gacchati iti loka prasiddham tatra yathā vaktā vācam bhāṣate kartā kriyām karoti iti prasiddham evam yayā gatyā gantā iti abhivyajyate tām gacchati iti na yathā ukta doṣaḥ tad api asat yasmāt  gatyā yayā ucyate gantā gatim tām sa na gacchati yayā gatyā devadattaḥ  gantā iti abhivyajate sa gantā san tām tāvat na gacchati na prāpnoti yadi vā na karoti iti arthaḥ yasmāt na gati pūrvaḥ asti gateḥ pūrvaḥ gati pūrvaḥ yadi gantā gateḥ pūrvam siddhaḥ syāt  sa tām gacchet  katham yasmāt  kaścid kiṃcid hi gacchati kaścid devadattaḥ kiṃcid artha antara bhūtam grāmam nagaram vā gacchati iti dṛṣṭam na ca evam yayā gatyā gantā iti ucyate tasyāḥ pūrvam siddha rūpaḥ  gati nirapekṣaḥ  gantā nāma asti yaḥ tām gacchet  atha manyase yayā gatyā gantā iti abhivyajyate tām eva asau na gacchati kim tahi tatas  anyām iti etad api asat yasmāt  gatyā yayā ucyate gantā tatas  anyām sa na gacchati gatī dve na upapadyete yasmāt eke pragacchati yayā gatyā gantā abhivyajyate tatas  anyām api sa gantā san na gacchati gati dvaya prasaṅgāt  yayā gatyā gantā abhivyajyate gantā san yām ca aparām gacchati iti etad  gati dvayam prasaktam na ca ekasmin gantari gati dvayam iti uktam etad  etena vaktā vācam bhāṣate kartā kriyām karoti iti pratyuktam tad evam sadbhūtaḥ  gamanam gantā tri prakāram na gacchati na asat bhūtaḥ  api gamanam tri prakāram sa gacchati gamanam sat asat bhūtaḥ tri prakāram na gacchati tatra gamyata iti gamanam iha ucyate tatra sadbhūtaḥ  gantā yaḥ  gami kriyā yuktaḥ asat bhūtaḥ  gantā yaḥ  gami kriyā rahitaḥ sat asat bhūtaḥ  ya ubhaya pakṣīya rūpaḥ evam gamanam api tri prakāram gami kriyā saṃbandhena veditavyam tatra sadbhūtaḥ  gantā sat bhūtam asat bhūtam sat asat bhūtam tri prakāram gamanam na gacchati etad ca karma kāraka parīkṣāyām ākhyāsyate evam asat bhūtaḥ  api gantā tri prakāram gamanam na gacchati sat asat bhūtaḥ  api iti tatra eva pratipādayiṣyati yatas ca evam gantṛ gantavya gamanāni vicāryamāṇāni na santi tasmāt gatiḥ ca gantā ca gantavyam ca na vidyate yathā uktam āryā kṣayam ati nirdeśa sūtre agatiḥ iti bhadanta śāradvatī putra saṃkarṣaṇa padam etad  gatiḥ iti bhadanta śāradvatī putra niṣkarṣaṇa padam etad  yatra na saṃkarṣaṇa padam na niṣkarṣaṇa padam tad ā āryāṇām padam apada yogena anāgatiḥ agatiḥ cāryāṇām gatiḥ iti yadi bījam eva aṅkure saṃkramati bījam eva tad syāt na yad aṅkuraḥ śāśvata doṣa prasaṅgaḥ ca atha aṅkuraḥ  anyata āgacchati ahetuka doṣa prasaṅgaḥ syāt  na ca ahetukasya utpattiḥ khara viṣāṇasya iva ata eva āha bhagavān bījasya sataḥ  yathā aṅkuraḥ  na ca yaḥ  bīju sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas  na ca eva tad evam anuccheda aśāśvata dharmatā iti mudrāt pratimudra dṛśyate mudra saṃkrānti na ca upalabhyate na ca tatra na ca eva sa anyatas  evam saṃskāra nuccheda śāśvatāḥ iti ca tathā ādarśa pṛṣṭhe tatha taila pātre nirīkṣate nārimukham alaṃkṛtam saḥ  tatra rāgam janayitva bālaḥ  pradhāvitaḥ  kāmi gaveṣamāṇaḥ  mukhasya saṃkrānti yadā na vidyate bimbe mukham na eva kadāci labhyate mūḍhaḥ  yathā saḥ  janayeta rāgam tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān tathā [ārya samādhi rāja sūtre api] tahi kāli saḥ  daśa balaḥ  anaghaḥ jinu bhāṣate imu samādhi varam su pinā upamā bhagavatī sakalā na hi kaści jāyati na ca u mriyate na ca sattvu labhyati na jīvu naraḥ  imi dharma phena kadalī sadṛśāḥ māyā upamā gagana vidyu samā daka candra saṃnibha marīci samāḥ na ca asmi loki mṛtu kaści naraḥ  para loke  saṃkramati gacchati vā na ca karma naśyati kadāci kṛtam phalu deti kṛṣṇa śubha saṃsarataḥ  na ca śāśvatam na ca uccheda punaḥ na ca karma saṃcayu na ca api sthitiḥ na ca saḥ  api kṛtva punar ā aspṛśati na ca anyu kṛtva puna vedayate na ca saṃkramaḥ  na ca punā āgamanam na ca sarvam asti na ca na asti punar  na ca dṛṣṭa sthāna gati śuddhiḥ iha u na ca satva cāra supaśānta gati supina upamam hi tri bhavam vaśikam laghu bhagnam anityena māya samam na ca āgatam na ca iha upagatam śūnya animitta sada saṃtatiyaḥ  anutpāda śānta animitta padam sugatāna gocara jināna guṇā bala dhāraṇī daśa balāna balam buddhāna iyam vṛṣabhitā paramā vara śukla dharma guṇa saṃnicayaḥ  guṇa jñāna dhāraṇi balam paramam ṛddhī vikurvaṇa vidhiḥ paramaḥ  vara pañcabhijña pratilābha nayaḥ iti vistaraḥ iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau gatāgata parīkṣā nāma dvitīyam prakaraṇam cakṣuḥ ādi indriya parīkṣā tṛtīyam prakaraṇam atra āha yadi api gatiḥ ca gantā ca gantavyam ca na vidyate tathā api pravacana siddha yapekṣayā draṣṭṭa draṣṭavya darśana ādīnām astitvam āstheyam tathā ca abhidharme ucyate darśanam śravaṇam ghrāṇam rasanam sparśanam manaḥ indriyāṇi ṣaṭ eteṣām draṣṭavī ādīni gocaraḥ tasmāt santi darśana ādīni svabhāvata iti ucyate na santi iha hi paśyati iti darśanam cakṣuḥ tasya ca rūpam viṣaya tvena upadiśyate yathā darśanam rūpam na paśyati tathā pratipādayan  āha svam ātmānam darśanam hi tad tam eva na paśyati na paśyati yadā ātmānam katham drakṣyati tad parān tatra tad eva darśanam sva ātmānam na paśyati sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt tatas ca sva ātma adarśanāt śrotra ādivat nīla ādikam na paśyati tasmāt na asti darśanam yadi api sva ātmānam darśanam na paśyati tathā aṣi agnivat  parān drakṣyati tathā hi agniḥ para ātmānam eva dahati na sva ātmānam evam darśanam parān eva drakṣyati na sva ātmānam iti etad ati ayuktam yasmāt  na paryāptaḥ  agni dṛṣṭāntaḥ  darśanasya prasiddhaye yaḥ  ayam agni dṛṣṭāntaḥ  darśanasya prasiddhaye bhavatā upanyastaḥ sa na paryāptaḥ  na alam na samarthaḥ  na yujyata iti arthaḥ yasmāt  sa darśanaḥ sa pratyuktaḥ  gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ saha darśanena vartata iti sa darśanaḥ yaḥ  ayam agni dṛṣṭāntaḥ  darśana prasiddhaye bhavatā upanyastaḥ saḥ  api saha darśanena dārṣṭa antika arthena pratyuktaḥ  dūṣitaḥ kena punar iti āha gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ yathā gatam na gamyate na āgatam na gamyamānam evam agninā api dagdham na dahyate na adagdham dahyata ityādinā samam vācyam yathā ca na gatam na āgatam na gamyamānam gamyate evam na dṛṣṭam dṛśyate tāvat adṛṣṭam na eva dṛśyate dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa vinirmuktam dṛśyamānam na dṛśyate ityādi vācyam yathā ca gantā na gacchati tāvat iti ādi uktam evam na dagdhā dahati tāvat ityādi vācyam evam na draṣṭā paśyati tāvat ityādinā agni dṛṣṭāntena saha gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ yasmāt samam dūṣaṇam atas  agnivat  darśana siddhiḥ iti na yujyate tatas ca siddham etad  sva ātmavat  darśanam parān api na paśyati iti yadā evam tadā na apaśyamānam bhavati yadā kiṃcana darśanam darśanam paśyati iti evam katham etad tu yujyate yadā ca evam apaśyat   kiṃcid darśanam bhavati tadānīm apaśyataḥ  darśana ātvā ayogāt stambha ādivat  paśyati iti darśanam iti vyapadeśaḥ  na yujyate yadi api darśana śabdāt anantaram śloka bandha anurodhena darśana paśyati iti pāṭhaḥ tathā api vyākhyāna kāle paśyati iti darśanam iti evam katham etad tu yujyate iti paṭhitavyam kim ca anyat  iha paśyati iti darśanam iti ucyamāne darśana kriyayā darśana svabhāvasya vā cakṣuṣaḥ saṃbandhaḥ parikalpyeta adarśana svabhāvasya vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha paśyati darśanam na eva na eva paśyati adarśanam darśana svabhāvasya tāvat  dṛśi kriyā yuktasya bhūyas  paśyati ityādinā saṃbandhaḥ  na upapadyate dṛśi kriyā dvaya prasaṅgāt  darśana dvaya prasaṅgāt ca adarśanam api na paśyati darśana kriyā rahita tvāt aṅgūlī agravadityā abhiprāyaḥ yadā paśyati darśanam na eva na eva paśyati adarśanam tadā darśanam paśyati iti evam katham etad tu yujyate iti anena eva saṃbandhaḥ ye tu manyante nirvyāpāram hi idam dharma mātram utpadyamānam utpadyate iti na eva kiṃcid  kaścid viṣayam paśyati kriyāyāḥ  abhāvāt  tasmāt darśanam na paśyati iti siddham etad prasādhyata iti atra ucyate yadi kriyā vyavahāra aṅga bhūtā na syāt  tadā dharma mātram api na syāt  kriyā virahita tvāt kha puṣpavat iti kutas  kriyā rahitam dharma mātram bhaviṣyati tasmāt yadi vyavahāra satyam dharma mātravat  kriyā api abhyupagamyatām atha tattva cintā tadā kriyāvat  dharma mātram api na asti iti bhavatā abhyupagamyatām yathā uktam śatake kriyāvān śāśvataḥ  na asti na asti sarva gate kriyā niṣkriyaḥ  nāstinā tulyaḥ  nairātmyam kim na te priyam iti tasmāt na ayam vidhiḥ bādhakaḥ parasya na api asmākam siddha sādhana doṣaḥ atra āha na eva hi paśyati iti darśanam iti kartṛ sādhanam abhyupagamyate kim tarhi paśyati anena itī darśanam iti karaṇa sādhanam tatas ca ukta doṣa aprasaṅgaḥ yaḥ ca anena darśanena karaṇa bhūtena paśyati sa draṣṭā eṣa ca vidyate vijñānam ātmā vā kartṛ sadbhāvāt ca darśanam api siddham iti ucyate vyākhyātaḥ  darśanena eva draṣṭā ca api upagamyatām yathā svam ātmānam darśanam hi ityādinā dūṣaṇam uktam evam draṣṭuḥ api darśanavat dūṣaṇam veditavyam tad yathā svam ātmānam na eva draṣṭā darśanena vipaśyati na paśyati yadā ātmānam katham drakṣyati tad parān ityādi vācyam tasmāt darśanavat  draṣṭā api na asti iti siddham atra āha vidyata eva draṣṭā tad karma karaṇa sadbhāvāt iha yad na asti iti na tasya karma karaṇe vidyete tad yathā vandhyā sūnoḥ asti ca draṣṭuḥ karaṇam darśanam draṣṭavyam ca karma tasmāt chettṛvat vidyamāna karma karaṇaḥ  vidyata eva draṣṭā iti ucyate na eva hi draṣṭavya darśane vidyete tad kutaḥ draṣṭā syāt  draṣṭu sāpekṣe hi draṣṭavya darśane sa ca nirūttyamāṇaḥ tiraskṛtya draṣṭā na asti atiraskṛtya ca darśanam iha draṣṭā nāma yadi kaścid syāt  sa darśana sa apekṣaḥ  vā syāt nirapekṣaḥ  vā tatra yadi darśana sa apekṣaḥ  atiraskṛtya darśanam iṣyate tadā siddhasya vā darśana apekṣā syāt asiddhasya vā tatra siddhaḥ  draṣṭā na hi darśanam apekṣate kim siddhasya sataḥ  draṣṭuḥ punar darśana apek ṣā kuryāt  na hi siddham punar api sādhyata iti atha asiddhaḥ  apekṣeta asiddha tvāt vandhyā sutavat darśanam na apekṣate evam tāvat atiraskṛtya darśanam apekṣya draṣṭā na asti tiraskṛtya api darśana nirapekṣa tvāt  iti uktam prāk  tad evam tiraskṛtya atiraskṛtya vā darśanam yadā draṣṭā na asti tadā draṣṭavyam darśanam ca eva draṣṭari asati te kutas  draṣṭari asati nirhetuke draṣṭavya darśane na saṃbhavataḥ iti kutas tad sadbhāvāt  draṣṭā prasetsyati atra āha vidyete eva draṣṭavya darśane tad kārya sadbhāvāt tatra pratītya mātā pitarau yathā uktaḥ putra saṃbhavaḥ cakṣū rūpe pratītyā evam uktaḥ  vijñāna saṃbhavaḥ iti draṣṭavyam darśanam ca pratītya vijñānam utpadyate trayāṇām saṃnipātāt sa āsrava sparśaḥ sparśa sahajā vedanā tad pratyayā tṛṣṇā iti evam catvāri api bhava aṅgāni draṣṭavya darśana hetukāni vidyante tasmāt kārya sadbhāvāt  draṣṭavya darśane vidyete iti ucyate syātām ete yadi vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam eva syāt  yasmāt  draṣṭavya darśana abhāvāt vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam na asti iti iha draṣṭuḥ abhāvāt  draṣṭavya darśane api na sta iti uktam atas  kutaḥ vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam vijñāna sparśa vedanā tṛṣṇā ākhyam tasmāt na santi vijñāna ādīni atra āha santi evatāni tad kārya sadbhāvāt iha tṛṣṇā pratyayam upādānam ityādinā upādāna bhava jāti jarā maraṇa ādikam vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayāt utpadyate tasmāt santi vijñāna ādīni tad kārya sadbhāvāt ucyate syuḥ upādāna ādīni yadi vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam eva syāt  yadā tu draṣṭavya darśana abhāvāt vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam na eva asti tadā upādāna ādīni bhaviṣyanti punar  katham na santi upādāna ādīni iti arthaḥ idānīm darśanavat śeṣa āyatana vyākhyāna atideśa artham āha vyākhyātam śravaṇam ghrāṇam rasanam sparśanam manaḥ darśanena eva jānīyāt śrotṛ śrotavyaka ādi ca iti uktam hi bhagavatā na cakṣuḥ prekṣate rūpam manaḥ  dharmān na vetti ca etad ta paramam satyam yatra lokaḥ  na gāhate sāmagryā darśanam yatra prakāśayati nāyakaḥ prāha upacāra bhūmim tām parama arthasya buddhimān iti tathā cakṣuḥ ca pratītya rūpataḥ cakṣu vijñānam iha upajāyate naḥ cakṣuṣi rūpa niśritam rūpa saṃkrānti na ca eva cakṣuṣi nairātmya aśubhāḥ ca dharmime teṣu ātmā iti śubhāḥ ca kalpitāḥ viparītam asat vikalpitam cakṣu vijñāna tatas  api jāyate vijñāna nirodha saṃbhavam vijñāna aupāda vayam vipaśyati na kahiṃci gatam na ca āgatam śūnya māyā upama yogi paśyati tathā ācārya upāli pṛcchāyām sarva sa yogi tu paśyati cakṣuḥ tatra na paśyati pratyaya hīnam na eva ca cakṣu prapaśyati rūpam tena sa yoga viyoga vikalpaḥ āloka samāśrita paśyati cakṣū rūpa manorama citra viśiṣṭam yena ca yoga samāśrita cakṣuḥ tena na paśyati cakṣu kadāci yaḥ  api ca śrūyati śabdu manojñaḥ saḥ  api ca na antari jātu praviṣṭaḥ saṃkramaṇam na ca labhyati tasya kalpa vaśāt tu samucchritu śabdaḥ iti tathā gītam na nṛtyam api vādya rutam na grāhyam svapna upamā hi ratayaḥ abudha mohanāḥ ca saṃkalpa lālasa gatā abudhā atra nāśam kim kleśa dāsa iva bāla janaḥ  bhavāmi iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau cakṣuḥ ādi indriya parīkṣā nāma tṛtīyam prakaraṇam skandha parīkṣā caturtha  prakaraṇam atra āha yadi evam cakṣuḥ ādīni indriyāṇi na santi na skandhāḥ apratiṣedhāt  tad antargatāni ca indriyāṇi atas tāni api bhaviṣyanti iti ucyate syuḥ eva yadi skandhāḥ syuḥ tatra rūpa skandham adhikṛtya āha rūpa kāraṇa nirmuktam na rūpam upalabhyate rūpeṇa api na nirmuktam dṛśyate rūpa kāraṇam tatra rūpam bhautikam tasya kāraṇam catvāri mahābhūtāni tadvayatiriktam pṛthak bhūtam rūpam rūpa śabda gandha rasa spraṣṭavya ākhyam na upalabhyate ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ rūpeṇa api na nirmuktam rūpāt pṛthak bhūtam rūpa kāraṇam upalabhyate tad etad pratijñā dvayam prasādhayitu kāma āha rūpa kāraṇa nirmukte rūpe rūpam prasajyate āhetukam na ca asti arthaḥ kaścid āhetukaḥ kvacid  yathā ghaṭāt artha antara bhūtaḥ paṭaḥ na ghaṭa hetukaḥ evam rūpa kāraṇa catur mahābhūta vyatirikta bhautikam rūpam iṣyamāṇam na bhūta hetukam syāt  na ca asti arthaḥ kaścid āhetukaḥ kvacid  tasmāt ahetukatva doṣa prasaṅgāt na rūpa kāraṇa nirmuktam rūpam abhyupetavyam iti idānīm rūpeṇa api vinirmuktam yathā rūpa kāraṇam na asti tathā pratipādayan  āha rūpeṇa tu vinirmuktam yadi syāt rūpa kāraṇam yadi kārya rūpa vinirmuktam rūpa kāraṇam syāt  tadā yathā ghaṭāt kuṇḍam pṛthak siddham ghaṭa hetukam na bhavati evam kāryāt pṛthak bhūtam kāraṇam iṣyamāṇam akārya kam kāraṇam syāt  nirhetukam syāt  kāraṇasya hi kāraṇa tve kārya pravṛttiḥ hetuḥ kārya nirapekṣāt ca kāraṇāt  pṛthak siddhā na asti kārya pravṛttiḥ yad ca akāryakam kāraṇam tad nirhetuka tvāt nara uraga turaga viṣāṇavat na asti eva iti āha na asti akāryam ca kāraṇam iti atha ca idam rūpasya kāraṇam iṣyamāṇam sati vā rūpe kāraṇa tvena iṣyate asati vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyata iti āha rūpe sati eva rūpasya kāraṇam na upapadyate rūpe asati eva rūpasya kāraṇam na upapadyate sati vā saṃvidyamāne rūpe kim rūpa kāraṇena prayojanam asati asaṃvidyamāne rūpe kim kim rūpa kāraṇena prayojanam kasya vā tad kāraṇam parikalpyate tasmāt asati api rūpe rūpa kāraṇam na upapadyate atha syāt  yadi api evam rūpa kāraṇam na saṃbhavati tathā api kāryam rūpam saṃvidyate sadbhāvāt  kāraṇam api bhaviṣyati iti syāt evam yadi kāryam rūpam syāt  na tu asti ysmāt  niṣkāraṇam punā rūpam na eva na eva upapadyate rūpa kāraṇam yathā na asti tathā uktam asati kāraṇe kutaḥ nirhetukam kāryam rūpam bhavet  na eva na eva iti anena sa avadhāraṇena pratiṣedha dvayena ahetuka tvāt asya ati aniṣṭatām darśayati yatas ca evam rūpam sarvathā vicāryamāṇam na saṃbhavati tasmāt  tattvadarśī yogī rūpa gatān kāṃścid na vikalpān vikalpayet  sa pratighā pratighasa nidarśana anidarśana atīta anāgata nīla pīta ādi vikalpān rūpa ālambanāt na kāṃścid parikalpayitum arhati iti arthaḥ api ca idam rūpa kāraṇam iṣyamāṇam sadṛśam kāryam niṣpādayet asadṛśam vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha na kāraṇasya sadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate na kāraṇasya asadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate tatra rūpa kāraṇam kaṭhina drava uṣṇa tarala svabhāvam bhautikam tu cakṣuḥ ādhyātmikam pañca cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādi āśrayaka rūpa prasāda ātmakam bāhyam tu rūpa ādi āyatana ādikam cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādi grāhya lakṣaṇam na mahābhūta svabhāvam iti atas  bhinna lakṣaṇa tvāt nirvāṇavat kārya kāraṇayoḥ sādṛśyam eva na asti iti na kāraṇasya sadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate na ca api sadṛśānām śāli bīja ādīnām paraspara kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ iti atas  na kāraṇasya sadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate tathā api na kāraṇasya asadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate bhinna lakṣaṇa tvāt nirvāṇavat eva iti abhiprāyaḥ yathā ca idam rūpam vicāryamāṇam sarvathā na upapadyate evam veda nādayaḥ  api iti atidiśan  āha vedanā citta saṃjñānām saṃskārāṇām ca sarvaśas  sarveṣām eva bhāvānām rūpeṇa eva samaḥ kramaḥ vedanā ādikam api sarvam rūpa vicāreṇa eva samam yojyam yathā eva hi ekasya dharmasya śūnyatā pratipādayitum iṣṭā mādhyamikena tathā eva sarva dharmāṇām api iti atas  vigrahe yaḥ parīhāram kṛte śūnyatayā vadet  sarvam tasya aparihṛtam samam sādhyena jāyate tatra para pakṣa dūṣaṇam vigrahaḥ śūnyatayā kāraṇa bhūtayā rūpam niḥsvabhāvam iti evam sa svabhāva vāde pratiṣiddhe yadi paraḥ parihāram brūyāt  vedanā ādayaḥ tāvat santi tadvat rūpam api asti iti tad etad sarvam tasya aparihṛtam bhavati yasmāt vedanā ādīnām api sadbhāvaḥ sādhyena rūpa sadbhāvena samaḥ  veditavyaḥ yathā rūpam sva kāraṇāt tattva anya tvena vicāryamāṇam asat  evam sparśa pratyayā vedanā vijñāna sahajā saṃjñā avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃskāra pratyayam ca vijñānam sva kāraṇāt sparśa ādeḥ tattva anyatva ādinā vicāryamāṇam na asti iti sarvam etad sādhya samam bhavati yathā vedanā ādayaḥ sādhya samāḥ evam lakṣya lakṣaṇa kārya kāraṇa avaya vya vayavādayaḥ  api sarva eva padārthāḥ rūpeṇa sādhyena samā iti kutas  parasya parīhāra saṃbhavet  sarvam vacanam asya sādhya samam bhavati iti sarvatra śāstre parīhāreṇa sādhya sama tvam mādhyamikena grāhaṇīyam iti ācāryaḥ śikṣayati yathā ca para pakṣa dūṣaṇe vihi atoyam vidhiḥ evam vyākhyāna kāle api iti āha vyākhyāne ya upālambham kṛte śūnyatayā vadet  sarvam tasya anupālabdham samam sādhyena jāyate vyākhyāna kāle api yaḥ śiṣya deśīyaḥ ca udyam upālambham kuryāt  tasya api tad ca udyam upālambha ākhyam pūrvavat sādhya samam veditavyam yathā uktam bhāvasya ekasya yaḥ  draṣṭā draṣṭā sarvasya sa smṛtaḥ ekasya śūnyatā yā eva sā eva sarvasya śūnyatā iti ārya gagana gañja samādhi sūtre api ekena dharmeṇa tu sarva dharmān anugacchate māya marīci sādṛśān agrāhya tucchānalikānaśāśvatān saḥ  bodhimaṇḍam nacireṇa gacchati iti samādhi rāja sūtre api yatha ñāta tayā ātma saṃjña tathā eva sarvatra peṣitā buddhiḥ sarve ca tad svabhāvā dharma viśuddhā gagana kalpāḥ ekena sarvam jānāti sarvam ekena paśyati kiyat bahu pi bhāvetvā na tasya utpadyate madaḥ iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara cittāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau skandha parīkṣā nāma caturtha  prakaraṇam dhātu parīkṣā pañcamam prakaraṇam atra āha dhātavaḥ santi pratiṣedha abhāvāt uktam ca bhagavatā ṣaṣ dhā tuḥ ayam mahā rāja puruṣa pudgala ityādi tatas ca pravacana pāṭhāt dhātuvat skandha āyatanāni eva santi iti ucyate syuḥ skandha āyatanāni yadi dhātava eva syuḥ katham iti āha na ākāśam vidyate kiṃcid pūrvam ākāśa lakṣaṇāt  alakṣaṇam prasajyeta syāt pūrvam yadi lakṣaṇāt  tatra ṣaṣ  dhātava uktāḥ pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśa vijñāna ākhyāḥ tatra ākāśam adhikṛtya ucyate dūṣaṇam svarūpa nirūpaṇāt iha ākāśasya anāvaraṇam lakṣaṇam ucyate yad  yasmāt pūrvam ākāśam anāvaraṇa lakṣaṇāt lakṣyam syāt  tatra lakṣaṇa pravartanāt anāvaraṇa lakṣaṇāt pūrvam na ākāśam lakṣya rūpam iti yadā ca evam na ākāśam vidyate kiṃcid pūrvam ākāśa lakṣaṇāt  alakṣaṇam prasajyeta syāt pūrvam yadi lakṣaṇāt  tathā hi alakṣaṇam pravartatām tad abhāve kha puṣpavat na asti ākāśam iti āha alakṣaṇaḥ  na kaścid ca bhāvaḥ saṃvidyate kvacid  iti atra āha lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ lakṣye bhavet  tad sadbhāvāt lakṣyam api asti iti etad api na asti yasmāt  asatya lakṣaṇe bhāve kramatām kuha lakṣaṇam lakṣaṇāt pūrvam alakṣaṇaḥ  bhāvaḥ na asti iti uktam tatas ca asati asaṃvidyamāne alakṣaṇe lakṣaṇa rahite bhāve kuha idānīm lakṣaṇaṃpravartatām iti na asti lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ api ca idam lakṣaṇam pravartamānam sa lakṣaṇe vā pravarteta alakṣaṇe vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyata iti āha na alakṣaṇe lakṣaṇasya pravṛttiḥ na sa lakṣaṇe sa lakṣaṇa alakṣaṇābhyām na api anyatra pravartate tatra alakṣaṇe khara viṣāṇavat na lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ sa lakṣaṇe api bhāve na lakṣaṇa pravṛtti rūpapadyate prayojana abhāvāt kim hi lakṣaṇavataḥ prasiddhasya bhāvasya punar lakṣaṇa kṛtyam syāt  iti anavasthā atiprasaṅgaḥ ca evam syāt  na hi asau kadācid na sa lakṣaṇaḥ syāt iti sadā eva lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ prasajyeta na ca etad iṣṭam tasmāt sa lakṣaṇe api bhāve na lakṣaṇa pravṛtti parupadyate prayojana abhāvāt tatra evam syāt  sa lakṣaṇa alakṣaṇābhyām anyatra pravartiṣyata iti ucyate sa lakṣaṇa alakṣaṇābhyām na api anyatra pravartate kim kāraṇam asadbhāvāt  yadi sa lakṣaṇaḥ  na alakṣaṇaḥ atha alakṣaṇaḥ  na sa lakṣaṇaḥ atas  sa lakṣaṇaḥ ca alakṣaṇaḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham etad  na ca vipratiṣiddham saṃbhavati tasmāt asaṃbhavāt eva sa lakṣaṇe ca alakṣaṇe ca lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ na upapadyate iti atha api syāt  yadi api na lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ tathā api lakṣyam asti iti etad api na asti yasmāt  lakṣaṇa asaṃpravṛttau ca na lakṣyam upapadyate yadā lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ eva na asti tadā katham lakṣyam syāt  na eva saṃbhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ atra āha lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ tvayā niṣiddhā na tu lakṣaṇam tatas ca vidyate lakṣyam lakṣaṇa sadbhāvāt  ucyate lakṣyasya anupapattau ca lakṣaṇasya api asaṃbhavaḥ lakṣaṇa asaṃpravṛttau ca na lakṣyam upapadyate iti pratipāditam tadā lakṣyasya anupapattau ca lakṣaṇasya api asaṃbhavaḥ nirāśraya tvāt  yadā ca evam lakṣaṇam na asti tadā lakṣaṇa sadbhāvāt vidyate lakṣyam iti yad uktam tad na yatas ca etad evam tasmāt na vidyate lakṣyam lakṣaṇam na eva vidyate iti nigamanam atra āha yadya api lakṣya lakṣaṇe na staḥ tathā pyā kāśam asti bhāva rūpam ca bhavat ākāśa lakṣyam lakṣaṇam vā syāt  tasmāt lakṣya lakṣaṇe api ṣṭa iti etad api ayuktam iti āha lakṣya lakṣaṇa nirmuktaḥ  na eva bhāvaḥ api vidyate lakṣya lakṣaṇe yathā na staḥ tathā uktam prāk  yadā anayoḥ abhāvaḥ tadā lakṣya lakṣaṇa rahita tvāt ākāśa kusumavat na asti ākāśam yadi ākāśam bhāvaḥ na bhavati abhāvaḥ tarhi astu etad api na asti yasmāt  avidyamāne bhāve ca kasya abhāvaḥ  bhaviṣyati yadā ākāśam bhāvaḥ na bhavati tadā bhāvasya asattve kasya abhāvaḥ kalpyatām vakṣyati hi bhāvasya ced aprasiddhiḥ abhāvaḥ  na eva sidhyati bhāvasya hi anyathābhāvam abhāvam bruvate janāḥ iti tasmāt  bhāva abhāvāt abhāvaḥ  api ākāśam na saṃbhavati rūpa abhāvaḥ ca ākāśam iti vyavasthāpyate yadi api rūpam syāt tadā rūpa abhāva ākāśam iti syāt  yadā ca yathā uktena nyāyena rūpam eva na asti tadā kasya abhāva ākāśam syāt  atra āha vidyete eva bhāva abhāvau tad parīkṣaka sadbhāvāt asti ca bhavān bhāva abhāvayoḥ parīkṣakaḥ ya eva āha avidyamāne bhāve ca kasya abhāvaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt  bhavataḥ  bhāva abhāva parīkṣakasya sadbhāvāt  parīkṣyau  api bhāva abhāvau vidyete iti ucyate etad api ayuktam yasmāt  bhāva abhāva vidharmā ca bhāva abhāvam avaiti kaḥ syātām bhāva abhāvau yadi tadā tayoḥ parīkṣakaḥ  bhāvaḥ va syāt abhāvaḥ  vā yadi bhāva iṣyate tasya lakṣya lakṣaṇa nirmuktaḥ  na eva bhāvaḥ api vidyate iti uktam dūṣaṇam atha abhāvaḥ avidyamāne bhāve ca kasya abhāvaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti atra uktam etad duṣaṇam na ca bhāva abhāva visadṛśa dharmā kaścid  tṛtīyaḥ padārthaḥ  asti yaḥ  anayoḥ avagamaka iti na asti bhāva abhāvayoḥ parīkṣakaḥ ata eva uktam bhagavatā bhāvān abhāvān iti yaḥ prajānati sa sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate yaḥ sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate sa ānimittam bhajate samādhim iti tathā yaḥ  api ca cintayi śūnyaka dharmān saḥ  api ku mārga papanna ku balaḥ akṣara kīrtita śūnyaka dharmāḥ te ca anakṣara akṣara uktāḥ śānta paśānta ya cintayi dharmān saḥ  api ca cinta na jātu na bhūtaḥ citta vitarkaṇa sarvi papañcāḥ sūkṣma acintiya budhyatha dharmān iti vistaraḥ idānīm pratipāditam artham nigamayan  āha tasmāt na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ  na lakṣyam na api lakṣaṇam ākāśam iti yathā ca ākāśam evam ākāśa samā dhātavaḥ pañca ye pare pṛthivī ādi dhātavaḥ  ye pañca pare avaśiṣyante te api ākāśavat  bhāva abhāva lakṣya lakṣaṇa parikalpa svarūpa rahitāḥ parijñeyā iti arthaḥ tad evam padārthānām svabhāve vyavasthite avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā anādi saṃsāra abhyasta tayā bhāva abhāva ādi viparīta darśanā nirvāṇa anugāmi aviparītanaiḥ svabhāvya darśana sat mārga paribhraṣṭāḥ astitvam ye tu paśyanti na astitvam ca alpabuddhayaḥ bhāvānām te na paśyanti draṣṭavya upaśamam śivam draṣṭavya upaśamam śiva lakṣaṇam sarva kalpanā jāla rahitam jñāna jñeya nivṛtti svabhāvam śivam parama artha svabhāvam parama artham ajaram amarama prapañcam nirvāṇam śūnyatā svabhāvam te na paśyanti manda buddhi tayā astitvam na astitvam ca abhiniviṣṭāḥ santa iti yathā uktam ārya ratna āvalyām nāstikaḥ  durgatim yāti sugatim yāti anāstikaḥ yathābhūta parijñānāt mokṣam advaya niśritaḥ iti ārya samādhi rāje ca uktam bhagavatā asti iti na asti iti ume api antā śuddhī aśuddhi iti ime api antā tasmāt ume anta vivarjayitvā madhye api sthānam na karoti paṇḍitaḥ asti iti na asti iti vivāda eṣaḥ śuddhī aśuddhi iti ayam vivādaḥ vivāda prāptyā na dukham praśāmyate avivāda prāptyā ca duḥkham nirudhyate iti tasmāt asaṃbhava eva yad sāṃsārikeṇa mārgeṇa nirvāṇam adhigamyata iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau dhātu parīkṣā nāma pañcamam prakaraṇam rāga rakta parīkṣā ṣaṣṭham prakaraṇam atra āha vidyanta eva skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ kutas  tad āśraya saṃkleśa upalabdheḥ iha yad na asti na tad āśraya saṃkleśa upalabdhiḥ asti bandhyā duhituḥ iva vandhyā sūnoḥ santi ca rāga ādayaḥ kleśāḥ saṃkleśa nibandhanam yathā uktam bhagavatā bālaḥ  bhikṣave aśrutavān pṛthagjanaḥ prajñaptim anupatitaḥ cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭvā saumanasya sthānīyāni abhiniviśate saḥ  abhiniviṣṭaḥ san rāgam utpādayati raktaḥ san rāga jam dveṣa jam moha jam karma abhisaṃskaroti kāyena vācā manasā iti vistaraḥ ucyate syuḥ skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ  yadi rāga ādaya eva kleśāḥ syuḥ iha ayam rāgaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ  bāla pṛthagjanaiḥ sati rakte nare parikalpyeta asati vā ubhayathā ca na yujyata iti āha rāgāt yadi bhavet pūrvam raktaḥ  rāga tiraskṛtaḥ tam pratītya bhavet rāgaḥ  rakte rāgaḥ  bhavet sati tatra rāgaḥ saktiḥ adhyavasānam saṅgaḥ  abhiniveśa iti paryāyāḥ raktaḥ  rāga āśrayaḥ sa yadi raktaḥ  rāgāt pūrvam rāga tiraskṛtaḥ  rāga rahitaḥ  bhavet  tadā tam rāga tiraskṛtam raktam pratītya rāgaḥ  bhavet  evam sakti rakte rāgaḥ  bhavet iti yuktam na tu evam saṃbhavati yad rāga rahitaḥ  raktaḥ syāt  arhatām api rāga prasaṅgāt  yadi evam sati rakte na rāgaḥ asati tarhi rakte rāgaḥ  astu etad api ayuktam iti āha rakte asati punā rāgaḥ kuta eva bhaviṣyati yadā sati rakte rāgaḥ  na asti tadā katham asati rakte nirāśrayaḥ  rāgaḥ setsyati na hi asati phale tad pakva tā saṃbhavati iti atra āha yadi api tvayā rāgaḥ  niṣiddhaḥ tathā api raktaḥ  asti apratiṣedhāt  na ca rāgam antareṇa raktaḥ  yuktaḥ tasmāt ayam api asti iti ucyate syāt rāgaḥ  yadi raktaḥ syāt  yasmāt ayam rakta iṣyamāṇaḥ sati vā rāge parikalpyeta asati vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha sati vāsati vā rāge rakte api eṣa samaḥ kramaḥ tatra yadi sati rāge raktaḥ parikalpyeta tatra api eṣa eva rāga anupapatti kramaḥ  anantara uktaḥ  rakte api tulyaḥ raktāt yadi bhavet pūrvam rāgaḥ  rakta tiraskṛtaḥ ityādi atha asati rāge rakta iṣyate etad api ayuktam yasmāt  rāge asati punā raktaḥ kuta eva bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt raktaḥ  api na asti rāga rakta abhāvāt ca skandhādayaḥ  api na santi iti atra āha na eva hi rāga raktayoḥ paurvāparyeṇa saṃbhavaḥ  yata idam dūṣaṇam syāt  kim tarhi rāga raktayoḥ saha eva udbhavaḥ citta saha bhūtena rāgeṇa hi cittam rajyate tad ca raktam iti atas  vidyete eva rāga raktau  iti ucyate evam api saha eva punar udbhūtiḥ na yuktā rāga raktayoḥ saha utpādaḥ  api na yuktaḥ  rāga raktayoḥ yasmāt  bhavetām rāga raktau hi nirapekṣau parasparam sahabhāvāt  savya itara gaḥ viṣāṇavat iti abhiprāyaḥ api ca anayaḥ  rāga raktayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ ekatve parikalpyeta pṛthaktve vā tatra yadi ekatve tad na yujyate yasmāt  na ekatve sahabhāvaḥ  asti kasmāt punar na asti iti āha na tena eva hi tad saha na hi rāgasva ātmā rāgāt avyatiriktaḥ  rāgeṇa saha iti vyapadiśyate idānīm pṛthaktve api sahabhāva abhāvam āha pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ  atha kuta eva bhaviṣyati na hi pṛthak bhūtayoḥ āloka andhakārayoḥ saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ vā sahabhāvaḥ  dṛṣṭa iti kim ca anyat  ekatve sahabhāvaḥ ced syāt sahāyam vinā api saḥ pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ ced syāt sahāyam vinā api saḥ yadi ekatve sahabhāvaḥ syāt  tadā yatra yatra eka tvam tatra tatra sahabhāva iti ekasya api sahabhāvaḥ syāt  pṛthaktve api sahabhāve iṣyamāṇe yatra yatra pṛthaktvam tatra tatra sahabhāva iti aśva ādi vyatiriktasya pṛthak avasthitasya goḥ asahāyasya sahabhāvaḥ syāt  kim ca pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ ca yadi kim rāga raktayoḥ siddhaḥ pṛthak pṛthagbhāvaḥ sahabhāvaḥ  yatas tayoḥ pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ ca rāga raktayoḥ parikalpyate kim anayoḥ siddhaḥ pṛthak pṛthagbhāvaḥ kim rāga nirapekṣaḥ  raktaḥ siddhaḥ  yatas tayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ syāt  pṛthak pṛthak siddhayoḥ eva hi gavāśvayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ na tu evam rāga raktau pṛthak pṛthak siddhau  iti na asti anayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ athavā pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayoḥ na sahabhāva iti kṛtvā siddhaḥ pṛthak pṛthak bhāvaḥ  yadi vā rāga raktayoḥ parikalpyate bhavatā kim idānīm sahabhāvena akiṃcitkareṇa parikalpitena iti āha sahabhāvam kimartham tu parikalpayase tayoḥ rāga raktayoḥ siddhayartham sahabhāvaḥ parikalpyate sa ca pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayoḥ na asti iti pṛthak pṛthak  siddhiḥ abhyupagamyate tvayā nanu evam sati siddha tvāt kim anayoḥ sahabhāvena kṛtyam atha pṛthak  na sidhyati iti evam sahabhāvam vikāṅkṣasi pṛthak pṛthak  rāga raktayoḥ siddhiḥ na asti iti kṛtvā yadi anayoḥ sahabhāvam icchasi sa ca pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayoḥ na asti iti sahabhāva prasiddhayartha pṛthaktvam bhūya icchasi nanu evam sati itaretara āśrayāyām siddhau sthitāyām kasya idānīm siddhau satyām kasya siddhiḥ astu yāvatā pṛthak bhāva aprasiddheḥ ca sahabhāvaḥ  na sidhyati katamasmin pṛthak bhāve sahabhāvam sati icchasi na asti eva sa pṛthagbhāvaḥ sahabhāva anapekṣaḥ  yasmin pṛthak bhāve sati sahabhāva siddhiḥ syāditi asaṃbhāvayan  āha katamasmin pṛthagbhāve sahabhāvam sati icchasi tad evam yathā udita vicāra parāmarśena rāga raktayoḥ asiddhim nigamayan  āha evam raktena rāgasya siddhiḥ na saha na asaha iti yathā ca rāga raktayoḥ na paurvāparyeṇa siddhiḥ na api sahabhāvena evam sarva bhāvānām api iti atidiśan  āha rāgavat sarva dharmāṇām siddhiḥ na saha na asaha iti dveṣa dviṣṭa moha mūḍha ādīnām rāga raktavat asiddhiḥ yojyate ata eva uktam bhagavatā yaḥ  rajyeta yatra vā rajyeta yena vā rajyeta yaḥ  duṣyeta yatra vā duṣyeta yena vā duṣyeta yaḥ  muhyeta yatra vā muhyeta yena vā muhyeta sa tam dharma na samanupaśyati tam dharma na upalabhate sa tam dharmam asam anupaśyan  anupalabhamānaḥ  araktaḥ  aduṣṭaḥ  amūḍhaḥ  aviparyasta cittaḥ samāhita iti ucyate tīrṇaḥ pāraga iti ucyate kṣema prāpta iti ucyate abhaya prāpta iti ucyate yāvat  kṣīṇa āsrava iti ucyate niḥkleśaḥ  vaśībhūtaḥ su vimukta cittaḥ su vimukta prajña ājāneyaḥ  mahābhāgaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ kṛta karaṇīyaḥ apahata bhāraḥ  anuprāpta svaka arthaḥ parikṣīṇa bhava saṃyojanaḥ samyak ājñā su vimukta cittaḥ sarva cetaḥ vaśitā parama pārami prāptaḥ śramaṇa iti ucyate iti vistaraḥ tathā ye rāga doṣa mada moha sabhāva jñātvā saṃkalpa hetu janitam vitatha pravṛttam na vikalpayanti na virāgam api iha teṣām [a āśu] sarva bhava bhāva vibhāvitānām iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara cittāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau rāga rakta parīkṣā nāma ṣaṣṭham prakaraṇam saṃskṛta parīkṣā saptamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyanta eva saṃskṛta svabhāvāḥ skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ utpāda ādi saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa sadbhāvāt uktam hi bhagavatā trīṇi imāni saṃskṛtasya saṃskṛta lakṣaṇāni saṃskṛtasya bhikṣavaḥ utpādaḥ  api prajñāyate vyayaḥ  api sthiti anyathātvam api iti na ca avidyamānasya khara viṣāṇasya iva jāti ādi lakṣaṇam asti tasmāt saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa upadeśāt vidyanta eva skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ iti ucyate syuḥ skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ saṃskṛta svabhāvāḥ tāvakena matena yadi jāti ādi lakṣaṇam eva bhavet  iha ayam utpādaḥ saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvena iṣyamāṇaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ  vā tad lakṣaṇa tvena iṣyate asaṃskṛtaḥ  vā tatra yadi saṃskṛta utpādaḥ tatra yuktā tri lakṣaṇī trayāṇām lakṣaṇānām samāhāraḥ tri lakṣaṇī iyam ca utpāda sthiti bhaṅga samāhāra svabhāva sarva saṃskṛta avyabhicāriṇī iti kṛtvā yadi utpādaḥ saṃskṛta iti parikalpyate tadā utpāde api tri lakṣaṇī prasajyate tatas ca rūpa ādivat lakṣya tvam utpādasya syāt  na saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvam atha utpāde api tri lakṣaṇī na iṣyate tadā tri lakṣaṇī rahita tvāt ākāśavat  saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvam asya avahīyate iti āha atha asaṃskṛta utpādaḥ katham saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam iti na etad saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam iti abhiprāyaḥ api ca ime utpāda ādayaḥ saṃskṛtasya lakṣaṇa tvena parikalpyamānā vyastā vā pṛthak vā lakṣaṇa tvena parikalpyeran samastā vā saha bhūtā vā ubhayathā ca na yujyata iti āha utpāda adya aḥ trayaḥ  vyastā na alam lakṣaṇa karmaṇi saṃskṛtasya samastāḥ syuḥ ekatra katham ekadā tatra vyastā lakṣaṇa karmaṇi na yujyante yadi utpāda kāle sthiti bhaṅgau na syātām tadā sthiti bhaṅga rahitasya ākāśasya iva saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvena anupapadya eva utpādaḥ atha sthiti kāle utpāda bhaṅgau na staḥ tadā tad rahitasya sthitiḥ syāt  utpāda bhaṅga rahitaḥ ca padārthaḥ  na asti eva iti na asya avidyamānasya kha puṣpavat  sthitiḥ yujyate kim ca sthiti yuktasya paścāt anitya tayā api yogaḥ  na syāt  tad virodhi dharma ākrānta tvāt atha syāt  pūrvam śāśvataḥ  bhūtvā paścāt aśāśvata iti na ca eka padārthaḥ śāśvataḥ ca aśāśvataḥ ca yukta iti na utpāda bhaṅga rahitasya sthitiḥ tathā yadi bhaṅga kāle sthiti utpādau na syātām evam api anutpannasya sthiti rahitasya khapuṣpasya vināśaḥ  api na asti iti evam tāvat utpāda āt ayaḥ  vyastā na alam lakṣaṇa karmaṇi na alam na paryāptā iti arthaḥ idānīm samastā api na yujyanta iti āha samastāḥ syuḥ ekatra katham ekadā ekatra padārthe ekasmin kāle paraspara viruddha tvāt rāga vairāgyavat  āloka andhakāravat vā na yujyanta iti abhiprāyaḥ yasmin  eva kṣaṇe padārthaḥ  jāyate tasmin  eva tiṣṭhati vinaśyati ca iti kaḥ sa cetāḥ pratipadyeta tasmāt samastānām api utpāda ādīnām saṃskṛtasya lakṣaṇa karmaṇi na asti sāmarthyam atha yad uktam ayadi saṃskṛta utpādaḥ  ityādi tena yadi utpāda ādīnām tri lakṣaṇī prāptā prasaktā tatas  kaḥ  doṣaḥ atha asaṃskṛtaḥ evam api adoṣa  iti ucyate utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām anyat saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam asti ced anavasthā evam na asti ced te na saṃskṛtāḥ nanu ca pakṣa dvaye api vihita eva doṣaḥ tatra kim punarukta abhidhānena iti satya muktaḥ  doṣaḥ sa khalu na ācāryeṇa kim tarhi vṛtti kāreṇa atha pūrva pratijñātam eva dūṣaṇa antara abhidhānena spaṣṭīkaraṇa artham punar ācāryaḥ  abhihitavān yadi utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām anyat utpāda ādikam saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam iṣyate tadā teṣām api anyat  teṣām api anyat  iti aparyavasāna doṣaḥ syāt  sati ca aparyavasāna doṣe kim pūrvam syāt  yata uttara kālam aparam bhavet iti vyavasthā bhāvāt asaṃbhava evam utpāda ādīnām iti abhiprāyaḥ athavā pūrvam mukhya tvāt utpādasya eva dūṣaṇam uktam adhunā tu sāmānyena iti na asti ced te na saṃskṛtā iti gata artham etad  atra āhuḥ sāṃmitīyāḥ santi ca utpāda ādīnām utpāda ādayaḥ na ca anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ lakṣaṇa anulakṣaṇānām paraspara niṣpādaka tvāt  yasmāt iha saṃskṛta dharmaḥ kuśalaḥ kliṣṭaḥ  vā utpadyamānaḥ ātmanā pañcadaśaḥ utpadyate sa dharmaḥ tasya ca utpādaḥ samanvāgamaḥ sthitiḥ jarā anitya tā yadi asau dharmaḥ kliṣṭaḥ  bhavati tasya mithyā vimuktiḥ atha śubhaḥ tasya samyak vimuktiḥ yadi nairyāṇikaḥ  bhavati tasya nairyāṇika tā atha anairyāṇikaḥ tasya anairyāṇika tā iti eṣa parivāraḥ idānīm utpāda sya apara utpādaḥ yāvat anaiḥ yāṇikatānaiḥ yāṇikatā iti eṣa parivārasya parivāraḥ tatra yaḥ  ayam maula utpāda sa ātmānam vihāya anyān  caturdaśa dharmān janayati utpāda utpāda saṃjñakaḥ tu anulakṣaṇa bhūta utpādaḥ  maulam eva utpādam janayati evam yāvat anaiḥ yāṇika tā caturdaśa dharmān na niryāṇayati na tad nirvāṇam prāpayati iti arthaḥ anairyāṇika tānaiḥ yāṇika tā tu na niryāṇayati tad evam utpāda ādīnām anavasthām pariharan  āha utpāda utpāda utpādaḥ  mūla utpādasya kevalam utpāda utpāda sutpādaḥ  maulaḥ  janayate punar  dvividhaḥ  hi utpādaḥ ekaḥ  maula utpādaḥ aparaḥ ca utpāda utpāda saṃjñakaḥ utpādasya utpāda iti kṛtvā tatra yaḥ  ayam utpāda utpāda saṃjñaka utpādaḥ sa mūla utpādasya kevalam utpādakaḥ tam ca idānīm utpādopāda ākhyam utpādam maula utpādaḥ  janayati tad evam paraspara nirvartanāt asti ca tri lakṣaṇī utpāda ādīnām na ca anavasthā prasaṅga iti atra ucyate utpāda utpāda utpādaḥ  mūla utpādasya te yadi maulena ajanitaḥ tam te sa katham janayiṣyati yadi tava utpādasya utpādaḥ  mūla utpādasya janaka iti matam sa katham idānīm maulena utpādena anutpāditaḥ san utpāda utpādaḥ  maulam janayiṣyati atha manyase utpādita eva maulena utpādena utpāda utpādaḥ  maulam janayiṣyati etad api asat iti āha sa te maulena janitaḥ  maulam janayate yadi maulaḥ sa tena ajanitaḥ tam utpādayate katham sa utpāda utpāda saṃjñaka utpādaḥ  maulena janitaḥ  yadi maulam janayati sa maula utpāda utpādena ajanitaḥ  avidyamānaḥ katham utpāda utpādam janayiṣyati tasmāt maulena janitaḥ san utpāda utpādaḥ  maulam janayati ite na yujyate tatas ca paraspara nirvartya nirvartakatva abhāvāt sa eva anavasthā prasaṅga iti na asti utpādaḥ atra āha utpadyamāna eva mūla utpāda utpāda utpādam utpādayati sa eva utpāda utpādaḥ  mūla utpādam janayiṣyati iti ucyate ayam utpadyamānaḥ te kāmam utpādayet imam yadi imam utpādayitum ajātaḥ śaknuyāt ayam kāma mayam mūla utpāda utpadyamāna utpādayet utpādam yadi ayam eva ajātaḥ śaknuyāt aparama jātam utpādayitum utpadyamānaḥ  hi nāma anāgataḥ sa ca ajātaḥ katham utpādayiṣyati iti na yuktam eva etad iti abhiprāyaḥ evam utpāda utpāde api vācyam atra āha na eva hi utpādasya apara utpādaḥ  asti yatas  anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ syāt  kim tarhi pradīpaḥ sva para ātmānau saṃprakāśayitā yathā utpādaḥ sva para ātmānau  ubhau  utpādayet tathā yathā pradīpaḥ prakāśa svabhāva tvāt ātmānam prakāśayati ghaṭa ādīn  ca evam utpādaḥ  api utpāda svabhāva tvāt ātmānam utpādayiṣyati param ca iti ucyate syāt etad evam yadi pradīpaḥ sva para ātmānau saṃprakāśayet  na ca evam yasmāt  pradīpe na andhakāraḥ  asti yatra ca asau pratiṣṭhitaḥ kim prakāśayati dīpaḥ prakāśaḥ  hi tamaḥ vadhaḥ iha prakāśaḥ  nāma tamasya saḥ  vadhaḥ tamaḥ ca pradīpasva ātmani tāvat na saṃbhavati virodhāt  yad tamaḥ  nighnataḥ sva ātma prakāśa tvam syāt  na ca api pradīpaḥ  yatra deśe tiṣṭhati tatra tamaḥ  asti yad tamaḥ  nighnataḥ pradīpasya para prakāśaka tvam syāt  atas  api na asti pradīpasya sva para ātma prakāśaka tvam yadā ca evam tadā pradīpavat utpādasya sva para ātmā utpādaka tvam na saṃbhaviṣyati iti ayuktam etad  atra āha yad etad uktam pradīpe na andhakāraḥ  asti iti etad asati andhakāra dhāte yuktam eva vaktum yasmāt tu utpadyamānena eva pradīpena tamaḥ  nihatam tatra pradīpe na andhakāraḥ  asti yatra ca pradīpaḥ  asti tatra api andhakāraḥ  na asti iti yujyate yadi pradīpena na andhakāra dhātar  kṛtaḥ tadā anutpanne iva pradīpe utpanne api ghaṭa ādayaḥ  na upalabhyeran andhakāra ghāta abhāvāt prāc avasthām iva tasmāt asti eva andhakāra ghāta lakṣaṇam prakāśanam pradīpasya tad ca anena utpadyamānena pradīpena kṛtam iti ucyate katham utpadyamānena pradīpena tamaḥ  hatam na utpadyamānaḥ  hi tamaḥ pradīpaḥ prāpnute yadā iha āloka andhakārayoḥ yaugapadya abhāvāt prāpteḥ abhāvaḥ yadā ca evam prāpteḥ abhāvaḥ tadā katham kena prakāreṇa idānīm utpadyamānena pradīpena tamaḥ  hatam iti yuktam parikalpayitum yasmāt ca evam utpadyamāna pradīpaḥ tamaḥ  na prāpnoti tasmāt na eva aprāpta tvāt pradīpaḥ kiṃcid api prakāśayati iti avasīyatām atha manyase yathā aprāptām eva avidyām jñānam nihanti aprāptam eva rūpam cakṣuḥ paśyati aprāptam eva ayaḥ ayaskāntaḥ  maṇiḥ ākarṣati evam eva aprāptam eva andhakāram pradīpaḥ  nihaniṣyati iti etad api asāram iti āha aprāpya eva pradīpena yadi vā nihatam tamaḥ ihasthaḥ sarva loka stham sa tamaḥ  nihaniṣyati yadi aprāpya eva pradīpena tamaḥ  nihatam evam sati ihastha eva pradīpaḥ sarva loka stham tamaḥ  nihaniṣyati aprāpta tvāt samīpa stham iva iti abhiprāyaḥ etena nyāyena jñānena avidyā ghātaḥ cakṣuṣā rūpa darśanam ayaskānta maṇinā ayaa ākarṣaṇam iva iti evamādikam sādhya samam jñeyam atha aprāptau  api satyām ayaskānta maṇi prabhṛtīnām yogya deśa avasthānām eva sva kārya kṛtvam debhaviṣyati iti ced  tad api na yuktam aprāptau hi satyām viprakṛṣṭa deśa antara avasthitavat avyavahita śāntara avasthitavat ca aprāpta tvāt  yogya deśa avasthitānām api yogya deśa avasthita tvam na yuktam iti kutaḥ yogya deśa avasthitānām sva kārya kṛt tvam prasetsyati dṛṣṭam etad lokata iti ced na etad evam yathā hi bhavān parikalpayati na tathā loke dṛṣṭam yasmāt  na lokaḥ prāpti aprāpti cintām evam ādau viṣaye avatārya pradīpa ādīnām prakāśakatva ādikam kalpayati yathā uditam tu vicāram anavatārya pradīpena tamaḥ  hatam cakṣuṣā rūpa darśanam ayaskānta maṇinā ayaa ākarṣaṇam ityādi icchati paśyatu vā loka evam tattva vicāra kāle tu lokasya aprāmāṇyāt na tena bādhā śakyate kartum evam tāvat aprāpya prakāśanam ayuktam prāptau  api viṣaya ādi grahaṇam ayuktam eva prāptiḥ hi ekatve sati bhavati yadā ca eka tvam tadā sva rūpavat darśana ākarṣaṇa ādikam na asti yadi api ca iyam prāpti aprāpti ādi cintā laukika vyavahāre na avatarati iti nirupapattika tvena mṛṣā artha tvāt asya tathā api tattva vicāre avatāryā mā bhūt paramārtha taḥ  api nirupapattika pakṣa abhyupagama iti alam prasaṅgena yadi ca sva para ātmānau pradīpaḥ prakāśayati iti parikalpyate tvayā tamasaḥ  api tarhi pratipakṣa bhūtasya sva para ātmanoḥ pracchādanam prakalpyatam iti āha pradīpaḥ sva para ātmānau saṃprakāśayate yadi tamaḥ  api sva para ātmānau chādayiṣyati asaṃśayam pratidvandvi tvāt pradīpavat  tamaḥ  api sva para ātma gatam vyāpāram kariṣyati tatas ca paravat ātmānam api chādayiṣyati yadi ca ātmānam chādayet tamaḥ tasya eva anupalabdhiḥ syāt  ghaṭa ādivat tamasā pracchādita tvāt  ata eva uktam ārya upāli pṛcchāyām iha sāsani sūramaṇīye pravrajathā gṛhiliṅga jahitvā phalavantu bhaviṣyatha śreṣṭhaḥ  eṣu nideśitu kāruṇikena pravrajitvā gṛhiliṅga jahitvā sarva phalasya bhaviṣyati prāptiḥ puna dharma sabhāva tulitvā sarva phalāna phalāna ca prāptiḥ alabhanta phalam tatha prāptim āścariyam puna jāyati teṣām ahaḥ ati kāruṇikaḥ  narasiṃhaḥ  suṣṭhupadeśita yukti jinena iti tathā ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre yathā hi dīpaḥ  layane cirasya kṛtaḥ  hi gehe puruṣeṇa kenacid  tatra andhakārasya na bhoti evam cira sthitaḥ  na ahamitas  gamiṣye tamondhakārasya na śaktiḥ asti kṛte pradīpe na vigacchanāya pratītya dīpam ca vinaśyate tama ubhayam pi śūnyam na ca kim ca manyati jñānam tathā ārya pratītya na āsravam ajñāna kleśa upacitam vigacchati saṃparka teṣām na kadāci vidyate jñānasya kleśasya ca nityakālam jñānam na kalpa iti añānu naḥ bhavet  jñānam pratītya eva vinaśyate tamaḥ  bhayam pi agrāhya khapuṣpa saṃnibham jñānam tathā ājñā anu bhayam pi śūnyam iti kim ca anyat  iha ayam utpādaḥ  yadi ātmānam utpādayet  sa utpannaḥ  vā sva ātmānam utpādayet  anutpannaḥ  vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha anutpannaḥ  ayam utpādaḥ sva ātmānam janayet katham atha utpannaḥ  janayate jāte kim janyate punar  yadi anutpanna utpādaḥ sva ātmānam utpādayet  maṇḍūka jaṭā śiromaṇiḥ api ātmānam utpādayet  atha utpanna utpādayet  kim utpannasya apareṇa utpādena prayojanam iti evam tāvat utpāda ātmānam na utpādayati idānīm param api yathā na utpādayati tathā pratipādayan  āha na utpadyamānam na utpannam na anutpannam kathaṃcana utpadyate tathā ākhyātam gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ yadi hi kiṃcid utpadyeta tad utpāda utpādayet  na tu kiṃcid utpadyate adhva traye api utpāda asaṃbhavāt etad ca gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ prāk eva uktam tatra yathā gatam na gamyate atīta vartamānayoḥ virodhāt  na api agatam gamyate anāgata vartamānayoḥ virodhāt  na api gamyamānam gamyate gatāgata vyatirikta gamyamāna anupalambhāt iti uktam evam utpadyamānaḥ  bhāvaḥ na utpadyate utpanna an utpanna vyatirekeṇa utpadyamāna abhāvāt utpannaḥ  api na utpadyate atīta vartamānayoḥ virodhāt  utpanna iti uparata utpatti kriya ucyate utpadyata iti vartamāna kriyā āviṣṭaḥ tatas ca utpanna utpadyate iti ucyamāne atīta vartamānayoḥ eka kālatā syāt  anutpannaḥ  api na utpadyate anāgata vartamānayoḥ virodhāt  tasmāt utpādaḥ param utpādayati iti na yuktam atra āha utpadyamānam eva utpadyate na utpannam na api anutpannam iti atha manyase utpanna an utpanna vyatirekeṇa utpadyamāna asaṃbhavāt na utpadyamānam utpadyata iti etad ca na asti yasmāt iha utpatti kriyā yuktam utpadyamānam iti vyapadiśyate tasmāt utpattau satyām utpattim pratītya utpadyamāna siddheḥ utpadyamānam eva utpadyate tad ca utpadyamānam utpāda utpādayati iti ucyate utpadyamānam utpattau  idam na kramate yadā katham utpadyamānam tu pratītya utpattim ucyate yad uktam utpattim pratītya utpadyamānam bhavati tad ca utpadyata iti nanu viśeṣata etad vaktavyam syāt  asya utpattim pratītya idam nāma utpadyamānam bhavati iti na ca evam ucyate na hi tad utpadyamānam viśeṣataḥ  nirdhārayitum śakyate idam tad utpadyamānam iti anutpanna tvāt tad nimitta grahaṇataḥ tatas ca utpadyamāna asaṃbhavāt utpatti kriyā api na asti iti katham asatyām utpattau tām pratītya utpadyamānam syāt  tasmāt utpadyamānam utpadyate tad ca utpāda utpādayati iti ayuktam atra āha ahaḥ bata aham atīva bhavataḥ  dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa padārtha nirapekṣāt atyanta nāstikāt vibhemi yaḥ  hi nāma bhavān  tathāgata pravacana vyākhyāna vyājena dūṣaṇa mātra kauśalam eva ātmanaḥ prakaṭayan parama ṛṣi gaditam idam pratyaya tā pratītya samutpāda lakṣaṇam parama artha satyam tathāgatānām nihanti iha bhagavatā tathāgatena prakṛti īśvara svabhāva kāla aṇu nārāyaṇa jaimini kaṇāda ka pila ādi tīrtha kara kartṛ vāda nirāsena sarva bhāvānām tattvam ādarśitam yad uta asmin sati idam bhavati asya utpādāt idam utpadyate yad uta avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ ityādya viparītam pratītyasamutpādam prakaṭayatā tasya ca tvayā na utpadyamānam na utpannam na anutpannam ityādinā dūṣaṇam vidadhatā tathāgata jananyāḥ pratītyasamutpatti mātuḥ vadha eva ācarita iti alam bhavatā sarva nāstikena tvayā iti ucyate na aham sakala daśa bala jananīm pratītyasamutpatti mātaram nihanmi bhavān eva tu parama gambhīra pratītya samutpāda adhimukti virahāt viparītam tad artham avadhārya asmākam eva adhilayam karoti nanu ca idam pratītya idam bhavati iti evam abhidhānena bhagavatā tathāgatena niḥsvabhāva tvam eva sarva dharmāṇām spaṣṭam āveditam yasmāt  pratītya yad yad bhavati tad tad śāntam svabhāvataḥ yaḥ  hi padārthaḥ  vidyamānaḥ sa sa svabhāvaḥ svena ātmanā svam svabhāvam anapāyinam bima rti sa saṃvidyamāna tvāt na eva anyat kiṃcid apekṣate na api utpadyate iti kṛtvā sa svabhāva bhāva abhyupagame sati kutas  pratītyasamutpāda iti bhavatā iva sa svabhāva tām bhāvānām abhyupagacchatā sarvathā pratītyasamutpāda eva bādhitaḥ  bhavati tatas ca parama dharma buddha darśanam api bādhitam bhavati yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam paśyati sa dharmam paśyati yaḥ  dharmam paśyati sa buddham paśyati iti āgamāt mayā tu yad pratītya bīja ākhyam kāraṇam yad bhavati aṅkura ākhyam kāryam tad ca ubhayam api śāntam svabhāva virahitam pratītyasamutpannam pratipādayatā sarvathā bhagavatām tathāgatānām pratītyasamutpatti mātā dyotitā bhavati yata evam tasmāt utpadyamānam ca śāntam utpattiḥ eva ca iti sphuṭam avasīyatām atra āha yad uktam utpadyamānam utpattau  idam na kramate yadā katham utpadyamānam tu pratītya utpattim ucyate iti tad ayuktam yasmāt idam utpadyamānam iti eva saṃbhavati tathā hi ghaṭa utpattim pratītya ghaṭa utpadyamānaḥ  bhavati tam ca utpadyamānam utpāda utpādayati iti ucyate etad api ayuktam yasmāt  yadi kaścid anutpannaḥ  bhāvaḥ saṃvidyate kvacid  utpadyeta sa kim tasmin bhāva utpadyate asati yadi kaścid anutpannaḥ utpādāt pūrvam ghaṭaḥ  nāma kvacid saṃvidyeta sa utpatti kriyām pratītya utpadyeta na ca evam kaścid utpādāt pūrvam kvacid asti tasmin  asati ghaṭe kim utpadyate atha syāt  yadi utpādāt pūrvam ghaṭaḥ  na asti tathā api utpannaḥ san ghaṭa saṃjñām pratilapsyate tad bhāvinyā saṃjñayā na doṣa iti etad api ayuktam yadi hi utpatti kriyā pravarteta tadā vartamānībhūtaḥ  bhāvaḥ ghaṭa ākhyām pratilabheta yadā tu anāgata bhāva asaṃbandhena kriyāyāḥ  apravṛttiḥ tadā kutaḥ vartamāna tā atha aghaṭa āśrayeṇa kriyā prārabhyeta tad vaktavyam yaḥ  asau aghaṭaḥ sa kim bhavituḥ mahati paṭaḥ uta na eva kiṃcid  yadi paṭa utpadyamānaḥ sa katham utpannaḥ san ghaṭaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti atha na evam kiṃcid  katham tad āśrayā kriyā kriyā pravartate katham vā sa utpannaḥ san ghaṭaḥ  bhavet  iti sarvathā bhāvitatva kalpanā apya yuktā tasmāt utpadyamānam api utpādaḥ  na utpādayat iti siddham api ca evam na yujyamānāyām api utpadyamānasya utpattau bhavataḥ  matam abhyupetya ucyate utpadyamānam utpādaḥ  yadi ca utpādayati ayam utpādayet tam utpādam utpādaḥ katamaḥ punar  yadi api utpadyamānam padārtham utpāda utpādayet bhavat matena idam tu vaktavyam tam idānīm utpādaḥ katamaḥ  aparaḥ utpādam utpādayiṣyati iti atha syāt  utpādasya apara utpādaḥ utpādakaḥ parikalpyeta tadā anavasthā doṣa prasaṅga iti āha anya utpādati enam yadi utpādaḥ  anavasthitiḥ etad ca uktam atha na asya apara utpāda iṣyate nanu evam sati vinā utpādena utpāda utpadyate iti evam prāpnoti tatas ca utpāda utpādyānām api padārthānām vinā eva utpādena utpattiḥ astu bhāva tvāt utpādavat iti pratipādayan  āha atha anutpāda utpannaḥ sarvam utpadyate tathā iti api ca utpāda ātmānam parān  ca utpādayati iti atra pakṣe dūṣaṇam eva na vaktavyam adhunā asmābhiḥ yasmāt atra pakṣe dūṣaṇam sataḥ ca tāvat utpatti rasataḥ ca na yujyate na sataḥ ca asataḥ ca iti pūrvam eva upapāditam na eva asataḥ  na eva sataḥ pratyayaḥ arthasya yujyate iti na san  āsanna sat asan dharmaḥ  nirvartate yadā ityādinā utpādaḥ  niṣiddha eva pūrvam tatas ca evam utpāde niṣiddhe utpadyamānam utpāda utpādayati sva para ātmānau vā utpādayati iti asyāḥ kalpanāyāḥ  na asti eva avatāra iti kuta etad prasetsyati utpāda utpadyate utpadyamānam utpadyate sva para ātmānau ca utpādayati iti kim ca anyat  iha ayam utpādaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ nirudhyamānasya anitya tā anugatasya vartamānasya vā bhāvasya parikalpyate anirudhyamānasya vā atīta anāgatasya anitya tā virahitasya ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha nirudhyamānasya utpattiḥ na bhāvasya upapadyate yaḥ ca anirudhyamānaḥ tu sa bhāvaḥ na upapadyate tatra nirudhyamānasya vartamānasya vidyamāna tvāt utpādaḥ  na upapadyate anirudhyamānasya api vināśa rahitasya atīta anāgatasya bhāva lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇasya khapuṣpasya iva na asti utpāda iti evam bhāvānām utpāda abhāvam pratipādya atas  param sthitiḥ vicāryate atra āha vidyata eva bhāvānām utpādaḥ tad bhāva bhāvi dharma sadbhāvāt na anutpannasya sthiti saṃbhavati iti utpāda bhāvena sthiteḥ bhāvāt  sthitiḥ utpāda bhāva bhāvinī bhavati tasmāt utpādaḥ  api asti tad bhāva bhāvi dharma sadbhāvāt iha yad na asti na tad bhāva bhāvi dharma sadbhāvaḥ tad yathā gagana kusuma saurabhyasya iti ucyate syāt utpādaḥ yadi tad bhāva bhāvinī sthitiḥ eva syāt  na tu asti tad evam na sthita bhāvaḥ tiṣṭhati asthita bhāvaḥ  na tiṣṭhati na tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhamānaḥ kaḥ  anutpannaḥ ca tiṣṭhati tatra sthitam na tiṣṭhati tatra sthiti kriyā nirodhāt asthita bhāvaḥ  api na tiṣṭhati sthiti rahita tvāt  tiṣṭhamānam api na tiṣṭhati sthiti dvaya prasaṅgāt  sthita āsthita vyatirikta saṃtiṣṭhamāna abhāvāt ca api ca kaḥ  anutpannaḥ ca tiṣṭhati iha utpāda pratiṣedhāt kaḥ asau  anutpannaḥ padārthaḥ  yaḥ tiṣṭhet iti sarvathā na asti sthitiḥ api ca iyam sthitiḥ nirudhyamānasya bhāvasya syāt anirudhyamānasya vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti pratipādayan  āha sthitiḥ nirudhyamānasya na bhāvasya upapadyate yaḥ ca anirudhyamānaḥ tu sa bhāvaḥ na upapadyate nirudhyamānasya nirodha abhimukhasya tāvat bhāvasya virodhinī sthitiḥ na saṃbhavati yaḥ ca api anirudhyamānaḥ sa bhāva eva na bhavati kutas tasya sthitiḥ bhaviṣyati api ca jarasā maraṇena ca sarva eva bhāvāḥ kṣaṇam api na tyajyante yadā ca etad evam tadā jarā maraṇa virodhinyāḥ sthiteḥ bhāveṣu pravṛtti avakāśa eva na asti iti pratipādayan  āha jarā maraṇa dharmeṣu sarva bhāveṣu sarvadā tiṣṭhanti katame bhāvā ye jarā maraṇam vinā ke hi nāma jarā maraṇa rahitā bhāvā yeṣām sthitiḥ syāt  tasmāt na asti eva sthitiḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ yadi ca asyāḥ sthiteḥ anyā vā sthitiḥ sthiti artham parikalpyeta svayam vā sva ātmānam sthāpayet  ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha sthityā anyayā sthiteḥ sthānam tayā eva ca na yujyate utpādasya yathā utpādaḥ  na ātmanā na para ātmanā aanutpannaḥ  ayam utpādaḥ sva ātmānam janayet katham  ityādinā yathā utpāda ātmānam na janayati iti uktam evam sthitiḥ api na ātmānam sthāpayati iti vaktavyam asthitā sthitiḥ eṣā ced sva ātmānam sthāpayet katham sthitā ced sthāpayati eṣā sthitāyām sthāpyate atha kim iti yojyam yathā ca anya utpādayati enam yadi utpādaḥ  anavasthitiḥ iti utpāde vyākhyātam evam sthitau  api vyākhyeyam atha anyā sthāpayati enām sthitiḥ yadi anavasthitiḥ iti evam sthitiḥ api na yuktā ata eva uktam bhagavatā asthitā hi ime dharmāḥ sthitiḥ ca eṣām na vidyate asthitiḥ sthiti śabdena svabhāvena na vidyate na sthitiḥ na api ca u jātiḥ lokanāthena deśitā lokanātham viditvā evam samādhim tena jānathā iti uktam ca ārya sacarya gāthāsu ākāśa niśrita sa māruta āpakhandhaḥ  tad niśritā iya mahī pṛthivī jagat ca sattvāna karma aupabhoga nidānam evam ākāśatha anu kṛta cittam etam artham yāvat  sthānam maya anu ayu thānu jinena uktaḥ  iti vistaraḥ atra āha vidyete eva sthiti utpādau tad sahacāri dharma sadbhāvāt iha utpāda sthiti lakṣaṇa sahacāriṇī saṃskṛtānām anitya tā asti tasmāt sthiti utpādau  api staḥ iti ucyate syāta sthiti utpādau yadi anitya tā eva syāt  na tu asti katham iti yasmāt  nirudhyate na aniruddham na niruddham nirudhyate tathā api nirudhyamānam kim ajātam nirudhyate yadi anitya tā iti kācid syāt  sā niruddhasya bhāvasya aniruddhasya vā nirudhyamānasya vā syāt  tatra niruddham nirudhyate iti na yuktam atīta vartamānayoḥ virodhāt  aniruddham api na yuktam nirodha virahita tvāt  yad aniruddham eva tad katham nirudhyata iti paraspara virodhāt ca tathā api nirudhyamānam na nirudhyate iti anena saṃbandhaḥ nirudhyamānam api na nirudhyate nirudhyamāna abhāvāt nirodha dvaya prasaṅgāt ca yatas ca evam triṣu api kāleṣu nirodha asaṃbhavaḥ tasmāt na asti eva nirodha iti kutas tad sahacāri sthiti utpāda saṃbhavaḥ syāt  api ca prāk utpāda pratiṣedhāt asaṃbhava eva nirodhasya iti āha kim ajātam nirudhyate iti api ca ayam nirodhaḥ sthitasya vā bhāvasya syāt asthitasya vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha sthitasya tāvat bhāvasya nirodhaḥ  na upapadyate sthitasya nirodha viruddhasya na asti nirodhaḥ na asthitasya api bhāvasya nirodha upapadyate asthitasya abhāvasya avidyamānasya nirodhaḥ  na asti iti sarvathā na asti nirodhaḥ kim ca anyat  yadi iha nirodhaḥ syāt  sa tayā eva avasthayā tasyāḥ  eva avasthāyāḥ syāt anyayā vā anyasyā avasthāyāḥ syāt  sarvathā ca na upapadyate iti pratipādayan  āha tayā eva avasthayā avasthā na hi sā eva nirudhyate anyayā avasthayā avasthā na ca anyā eva nirudhyate tayā eva tāvat kṣīra avasthayā sā eva kṣīra avasthā na nirudhyate sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt na api anyayā dadhi avasthayā kṣīra avasthā nirudhyate yadi hi kṣīra dadhi avasthayoḥ yaugapadyam syāt  syāt tayoḥ vināśi avināśaka bhāvaḥ na tu dadhi avasthāyām kṣīra avasthā asti yadā ca na asti tadā kāma satī vināśayet  yadi vināśayet  khara viṣāṇa tīkṣṇa tām api vināśayet  tasmāt anyayā api avasthayā na eva anya avasthā nirudhyate atra āha yadi api tayā eva avasthayā sā eva avasthyā anyayā vā avasthayā anya avasthā na nirudhyate tathā api kṣīra avasthāyāḥ tāvat nirodhaḥ  asti tatas ca utpādaḥ  api syāt iti ucyate ahaḥ bata ati jaḍa tām ātmanaḥ  bhavān prakaṭayati nanu ca pūrva uktena nyāyena yadā evam sarva dharmāṇām utpādaḥ  na upapadyate iti uktam tadā evam sarva dharmāṇām nirodhaḥ  na upapadyate iti sphuṭataram eva pratipāditam bhavati api ca nirodhaḥ  nāma yadi kaścid  syāt  sa sataḥ  vā bhāvasya syāt asataḥ  vā tatra sataḥ ca tāvat bhāvasya nirodhaḥ  na upapadyate svabhāvāt apracyutasya bhāvasya nirodhaḥ  na yuktaḥ yasmāt  ekatve na hi bhāvaḥ ca na abhāvaḥ ca upapadyate nirodhaḥ  hi nāma abhāvaḥ sa yasya bhavati sa na eva bhavati tatas ca sataḥ  bhāvasya nirodha iti bruvatā bhāva abhāvayoḥ eka adhikaraṇa tā abhyupagatā bhavati ekatve sati ubhayam na yujyate yadi tadānīm bhāvaḥ syāt  tadā nirodhena abhāvena āveśāt bhāva vyapadeśaḥ  ayuktaḥ atha abhāvaḥ saḥ  api asya na yujyate abhāva virodhinā bhāva rūpeṇa aviyogāt  tasmāt ekatve sati bhāva abhāvayoḥ sa padārthaḥ  na eva bhāvaḥ na api abhāva iti yujyate athavā paraspara viruddha tvāt āloka andhakāravat eka tve sati na hi bhāvaḥ ca na abhāvaḥ ca upapadyate evam tāvat sataḥ  bhāvasya nirodhaḥ  na yuktaḥ idānīm asataḥ  api na bhāvasya nirodha upapadyate avidyamānasya abhāvasya na vināśaḥ  asti vandhyā tanayasya iva avidyamāna tvāt  ata eva āha na dvitīyasya śirasa  chedanam vidyate yathā prasiddhā sattvasya eva narāṇām dvitīyasya śirasaḥ  dṛṣṭānta tvena upādānāt nirdeśa āpūrṇa tvāt na asti iti na upāttam tad evam asataḥ  bhāvasya nirodhaḥ  na saṃbhavati sataḥ  api na yaḥ ca ubhayatha api na saṃbhavati sa kena ātmanā sthitaḥ na asti eva nirodha iti pratīyatām kim ca anyat  yadi nirodhaḥ  nāma bhāvānām nirodhaka iti kalpyate tasya idānīm kim anyaḥ nirodha iṣyate uta na yadi iṣyate tad na yujyate na sva ātmanā nirodhaḥ  asti nirodhaḥ  na para ātmanā katham punar na asti iti pratipādayan  āha utpādasya yathā utpādaḥ  na ātmanā na para ātmanā tatra yathā anutpannaḥ  ayam utpādaḥ sva ātmānam janayet katham ityādinā utpādaḥ sva ātmānam na utpādayati evam nirodhaḥ  api sva ātmānam na nirodhayati katham iti ucyate aniruddhaḥ  nirodhaḥ  ayam sva ātmānam nāśayet katham atha naṣṭaḥ  nāśayati naṣṭe kim na aśyate punar  iti samam utpādena vaktavyam evam ca sva ātmanā na nirodhaḥ  asti nirodha idānīm para ātmanā api na asti katham tatra yathā utpāde gaditam aanya utpādayati enam  ityādi evam nirodhe api vaktavyam anyaḥ  vināśayati enam na āśaḥ yadi anavasthitiḥ atha avināśaḥ  naṣṭaḥ  ayam sarvam naśyatu te tathā iti tad evam para ātmanā api nirodhaḥ  na saṃbhavati iti na asti nirodhasya nirodhaḥ atha manyase na asti eva nirodhasya nirodha iti tad ayuktam yadi hi nirodhasya nirodhaḥ  na syāta tadā nirodha rahita tvāt saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam avahīyate tad evam yadi vināśasya vināśaḥ parikalpyate tathā api na yuktaḥ  vināśaḥ atha na parikalpyate tathā api na yukta iti katham tu idānīm vināśaḥ  yokṣyate parasya atha syāt  tathā api evam eva vicāre sati vināśaḥ  bhavataḥ  api na yujyate tatas  ya ubhayoḥ doṣaḥ na tena ekaḥ ca udyaḥ  bhavati iti ucyate na eva idam codyam mama āpatati kim kāraṇam ye sva ātmanā niḥsvabhāvā bhāvāḥ te ca niḥsvabhāvā eva santaḥ  bālānām idaṃsatya abhiniveśinām vyavahāra patham upayānti avicāra prasiddhena eva nyāyena iti teṣu na asti yathā udita vicāra avatāraḥ  asmākam māyā svapna gandharvanagara ādivat tu laukikāḥ padārthā nirupapattikā eva santaḥ sarva lokasya avidyā timira upahatam atinayanasya prasiddhim upagatā iti paraspara apekṣayā eva kevalam prasiddhim upagatā bālaiḥ abhyupagamyante yathā uktam śatake alāta cakra nirmāṇa svapna māyā ambu candrakaiḥ dhūmikā antar pratiśrutkā marī ci abhraiḥ samaḥ  bhavaḥ tasmāt sati utpāde utpādyam sati utpādye utpādaḥ sati nirodhe nirodhyam sati nirodhye nirodhaḥ iti evam laukikasya vyavahārasya abhyupagamāt kutaḥ asmad pakṣe sama prasaṅgi tā bhavitum arhati yaḥ tu vināśasya ahetuka tvam abhyupetya kṣaṇikatām saṃskārāṇām āha tasya nirhetuka tvāt  kha puṣpavat vināśa abhāvāt kutas  kṣaṇika tvam bhāvānām setsyati kutaḥ vināśa rahitānām saṃskṛta tvam api iti sarvam eva asamañjasam tasya jāyate jāti pratyayam jarā maraṇam saṃskṛta lakṣaṇānām ca saṃskāra skandha antar bhāva varṇayatā bhagavatā nanu sa hetuka tvam spaṣṭam ādarśitam vināśasya jāti mātra apekṣa tvāt ca asya kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ  api sukha sādhya iti sarvam sustham jāyate atha syāt  vināśaḥ  hi nāma abhāvaḥ yaḥ ca abhāvaḥ kim tasya hetunā kartavyam atas  nirhetukaḥ  vināśa iti nanu ca bhāve api hetu abhāva prasaṅgaḥ  bhavati bhāvaḥ hi nāma vidyamānaḥ yaḥ ca vidyamānaḥ tasya ca kim hetunā prayojanam na hi jātam punar api janyate tasmāt sarvatra eva hetvabhāva prasaṅgāt ayuktam etad  api ca yathā utpādaḥ sa hetukaḥ pūrvam abhāvāt paścāt ca bhāvāt  evam vināśaḥ  api iṣyatām vināśaḥ  hi na sarvadā bhavati utpādāt pūrvam abhāvāt paścāt ca bhāvāt  yad ca ucyate yaḥ ca abhāvaḥ tasya kim hetunā kartavyam iti tad ayuktam yasmāt na vayam vināśasya hetunā kiṃcid kriyamāṇam icchāmaḥ kim tarhi vināśa eva kriyate iti varṇayāmaḥ nanu evam sati kriyamāṇa tvāt vināśaḥ  api bhāvaḥ prāpnoti iti ced  iṣyata eva etad  vināśaḥ  hi sva rūpa apekṣayā bhāvaḥ rūpa ādi dharma nivṛtti svabhāva tvāt tu na bhāvaḥ api ca maraṇam api dvividha kārya pratyupasthāpanam saṃskāra vidhvaṃsanam ca karoti aparijñāna anupacchedam ca iti āgamāt katham na sa hetukaḥ  vināśaḥ api ca kalpita abhāva lakṣaṇāyāḥ ca śūnyatāyāḥ pareṇa bhāva rūpa tām abhyupagacchatā katham abhāvasya bhāva tvam na abhyupagatam bhavati bhāva tvāt ca katham asaṃskṛta tvam śūnyatāyāḥ syāt  atas  sarvam abhyupetam vihīyate bhavatā ata eva vakṣyati bhavet abhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam ubhayam katham na saṃskṛtam hi nirvāṇam bhāva abhāvau ca saṃskṛtau iti alam prasaṅgena prakṛtam eva vyākhyāsyāmaḥ atra āha yadi utpāda sthiti bhaṅgāḥ saṃskṛtasya niṣiddhāḥ tathā api saṃskṛtam asti viśeṣa lakṣaṇa yuktam tathā hi kāṭhinya ādikam sāsnādikam ca tasya viśeṣa lakṣaṇam upadiśyate tasmāt saṃskṛtasya sadbhāvāt tad lakṣaṇam api asti iti ucyate syāt evam yadi saṃskṛtam eva vastu syāt  kutas  yasmāt  utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām asiddheḥ na asti saṃskṛtam yadā yathā uktena nyāyena utpāda sthiti bhaṅgā eva niṣiddhāḥ tadā kutas  saṃskṛtam vastu tad viśeṣa lakṣaṇam api asti iti atra āha vidyata eva saṃskṛtam tad pratipakṣā saṃskṛta sadbhāvāt ucyate syāt etad evam yadi asaṃskṛtam eva syāt  yasmāt  saṃskṛtasya aprasiddhau ca katham setsyati asaṃskṛtam atra eke ākāśa apratisaṃkhyā nirodha nirvāṇāni asaṃskṛtāni iti kalpayanti apare śūnyatām tathatā lakṣaṇām asaṃskṛtām parikalpayanti tad etad sarvam saṃskṛtasya aprasiddhau satyām na asti eva iti spaṣṭam ādarśitam atra āha yadi utpāda sthiti bhaṅgā na santi iti avadhāritam yad tarhi idam anāvaraṇa jñāninā muninā  saṃskṛtasya bhikṣavaḥ utpādaḥ  api prajñāyate vyayaḥ  api sthiti anyathātvam api  iti udāhṛtam tad katham veditavyam iti ucyate yathā māyā yathā svapnaḥ  gandharvanagaram yathā tathā utpādaḥ tathā sthānam tathā bhaṅga udāhṛtam yathā māyā ādayaḥ svabhāvena anutpannā avidyamānā māyā ādi śabda vācyā māyā ādi vijñāna gamyāḥ ca lokasya evam ete api loka prasiddhi mātreṇa utpāda ādayaḥ svabhāvena avidyamānā api bhagavatā tathāvidha vineya jana anugraha cikīrṣuṇā nirdiṣṭā iti ata eva uktam tvac snāyu māṃsa asthi samucchraye ca utpādya saṃjñām mama patniḥ eṣā mūḍhā hi balā janayanti rāgam striyaḥ  na jānanti yathā eva māyām yathā kumārī supina antarasmin sā putra jātam ca mṛtam ca paśyati jāte ati tuṣṭā mṛti daurmana sthitā tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān yathā eva gandharva puram marīcikā yathā eva māyā supinam yathā eva svabhāva śūnyā tu nimitta bhāvanā tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān saṃskṛta asaṃskṛta dharma viviktā na asti vikalpana teṣam ṛṣīṇām sarva gatīṣu asaṃskṛta prāptā dṛṣṭi gata ihi sadā eva viviktā nityam arakta aduṣṭa amūḍhāḥ tasya sa bhāva samāhita cittā eṣa samādhi balī balavantaḥ  yaḥ  imu jānati śūnyaka dharmān iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara cittāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau saṃskṛta parīkṣā nāma saptamam prakaraṇam karma kāraka parīkṣā aṣṭamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyanta eva saṃskṛta svabhāvataḥ  vijñāna ādayaḥ saṃskṛtā dharmāḥ tad hetuka karma kāraka sadbhāvāt uktam hi bhagavatā avidyā anugataḥ  ayam bhikṣavaḥ puruṣa pudgalaḥ puṇyān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti apuṇyān api āniñjayān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti ityādinā karmaṇām kārakaḥ  vyapadiṣṭaḥ tad karma phalam ca vijñāna ādikam upadiṣṭam yasya ca kārakaḥ  asti tad asti tad yathā ghaṭaḥ yad na asti na tasya kārakaḥ tad yathā kūrma roma prāvārasya iti ucyate syāt vijñāna ādikam saṃskṛtam yadi tasya niṣpādaka karma kārakau syātām na tu staḥ yasmāt  sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ karma sadbhūtam na karoti ayam kārakaḥ  na api asadbhūtaḥ karma asadbhūtam īhate tatra karoti iti kārakaḥ kartā kurvāṇasya eva kiṃcid  kāraka vyapadeśaḥ  na akurvāṇasya tad ca karaṇam sadbhūtasya vā kartuḥ parikalpyeta asadbhūtasya vā sat asat bhūtasya vā kriyate iti karma kartuḥ īpsitatamam tad api trividham sat bhūtam asat bhūtam sat asat bhūtam ca tatra sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ kriyā yuktaḥ sadbhūtam kriyā yuktam karma na karoti iti ekā pratijñā idānīm asat bhūtaḥ  api kriyā kāraka rahitaḥ  asadbhutam kriyā rahitam karma na karoti iti aparā pratijñā tatra ādyām prasādhayitum āha sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti karma ca syāt akartṛkam kriyā nibandhana tvāt kāraka vyapadeśasya karoti kriyā yukta eva kaścid sadbhūtaḥ kāraka vyapadeśam labhate tatas ca tasya evaṃvidhasya kriyā hetuka labdha kāraka vyapadeśasya aparā kriyā na asti yayā karma kuryāt  kriyā bhāvāt ca yadā kārakaḥ karma na karoti tadā kāraka nirapekṣam akartṛkam karma syāt  na ca akartṛkam karma saṃbhavati bandhyā sūnoḥ iva ghaṭa karaṇam iti evam tāvat  sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti karma ca syāt akartṛkam iti doṣa prasaṅgāt  sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ karma na karoti idānīm sadbhūtam api karma kārakaḥ  na karoti iti pratipādayan  āha sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti kartā ca syāt akarmakaḥ sadbhūtam nāma karma kriyā yuktam tasya idānīm kriyā nibandhana labdha karma vyapadeśasya aparā kriyā na asti yayā karma kriyeta iti evam tāvat sadbhūtasya karmaṇaḥ kriyā na asti yadā na asti parā kriyā tadā kārakaḥ tad sat bhūtam karma na eva karoti yadā ca na karoti karmaṇaḥ  dvitīya kriyā bhāvāt tadā akarmaka eva avidyamāna karmaka eva tasya karmaṇaḥ kārakaḥ syāt  na ca etad yaktam na hi akṛta ānantarya karmaṇaḥ ānantarya karma kāraka tvam dṛṣṭam iti evam sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ sadbhūtam karma na karoti iti saṃsādhya idānīm yathā asat bhūtam api karma asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ  na karoti tathā pratipādayan  āha karoti yadi asat bhūtaḥ  asat bhūtam karma kārakaḥ ahetukam bhavet karma kartā ca ahetukaḥ  bhavet  asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ  yaḥ kriyā rahitaḥ kriyā ca kāraka vyapadeśe hetuḥ iti kriyā rahita kārakaḥ  api nirhetukaḥ syāt  karma api asadbhūtam nirhetukam syāt  sati ca ahetuka vāda abhyupagame kāryam ca kāraṇam ca sarvam apoditam syāt iti āha hetau  asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca na vidyate sati eva hi hetoḥ abhyupagame hetunā yad niṣpādyate tad  kāryam tasya ca yaḥ  niṣpādakaḥ tad kāraṇam iti yujyate tad yathā ghaṭasya mṛd hetuḥ ghaṭaḥ kāryam tasya ca cakra ādayaḥ sahakāri kāraṇam ahetuka vāda abhyupagame tu hetu anapekṣa tvāt maṇḍūka jaṭā śiraḥ maṇi maya ghaṭavat na syāt ayam ghaṭaḥ asati ghaṭe kutas tad kāraṇam iti evam hetau  asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca na vidyate tatas ca tad abhāve kriyā kartā karaṇam ca na vidyate tad abhāve kārya kāraṇa bhāve kim kurvāṇasya kriyā saṃbhavet  kasyām vā kriyāyām kumbhakārasya svātantryāt kartṛ tvam syāt  na ca api mṛdām tādātmya pravṛttyā sādhakatama tvena karaṇa tvam yujyata iti evam tāvat  tad abhāve kriyā kartā karaṇam ca na vidyate tatas ca dharma adharmau na vidyete kriyā ādīnām asaṃbhave iha yadā devadattaḥ prāṇa atipāta virati kriyā svātantryāt kartā san svatantra kāryeṇa karaṇa bhūtena prāṇa atipāta virati kriyām karoti tadā asya dharma upajāyate evam daśasu api kuśaleṣu karma patheṣu kuśala kriyā niṣpādyeṣu ratnatraya mātā pitṛ tad anya pūjya pūjā ādi lakṣaṇeṣu ca kuśala dharma prārambheṣu yojyam evam adharme api prāṇa atipāta ādi lakṣaṇe kuśala viparyayeṇa kriyā kartṛ karaṇānām abhāve sati karmaṇā ām abhāva prasaṅga udbhāvanīyaḥ yadā ca evam dharma adharmau na saṃbhavataḥ tadā tad phalam api na asti eva iti pratipādayan  āha dharme ca asati adharme ca phalam tad jam na vidyate dharma adharma janitam iṣṭa aniṣṭa phalam sugati durgatyoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ abhāve sati na syāt  tatas ca phale asati na mokṣāya na svargāya upapadyate mārgaḥ yadi hi phalam iṣṭa aniṣṭam syāta syāt laukikasya mārgasya dhyāna ārūpya samādhi samāpatti lakṣaṇam svargaḥ tadānīm tad artham laukika mārga bhāvanā jyāyasī syāt  kugati gamana karma patha virati sāphalyam ca syāt  yadi ca mokṣa lakṣaṇam nirvāṇam phalam syāt  tad artha loka uttara ārya aṣṭa aṅga mārga bhāva nāsā phalyam syāt  yadā tu phalam na asti tadā phale asati na mokṣāya na svargāya upapadyate mārgaḥ kim ca evam phala abhāve sati sarva kriyāṇām ca nairarthakyam prasajyate yā api hi etāḥ kṛṣi vāṇijya bala bhṛti gata ādikāḥ kriyāḥ phala artha prārabhyante tā api sarvāḥ phala abhāve sati na upapadyanta iti evam sarva kriyāṇām nairarthakyam prasajyate bhavatām na ca āsām nairarthakyam tasmāt niravaśeṣa doṣa viṣa vṛkṣa ākara bhūtaḥ  ayam svarga apavarga apavādī naraka ādi mahā pāya prapāta vartana hetuḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa hetu padārtha virodhi iti kṛtvā saddhiḥ asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ  asat bhūtam karma karoti iti pakṣaḥ  nikṛṣṭa eva iti tyājyaḥ tad evam pratijñā dvayam saṃsādhya idānīm ubhaya rūpaḥ kārakaḥ ubhaya rūpam api karma na karoti iti āha kārakaḥ sat asat bhūtaḥ sat asat kurute na tad  tatra yad etad asat bhūtam karma kriyā yuktam akriyā yuktam ca tad  sat asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ  na karoti iti yasmāt  paraspara viruddham hi sat ca asat ca ekatas  kutas  ekaḥ padārthaḥ ekasmin kāle kriyā yuktaḥ ca akriyā yuktaḥ ca iti na yujyata eva etad  tatas ca sat asat bhūtaḥ  api kārakaḥ sat asat bhūtam karma na karoti avidyamāna tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ evam same pakṣe dūṣaṇam udbhāvya viṣama pakṣasya api nirācikīrṣayā āha satā ca kriyate na āsannāsatā kriyate ca sat  kartrā satā sat bhūtena tāvat kartrā kriyā yuktena asat bhūtam asat akriyā yuktam karma na kriyate yasmāt  sarve prasajyante doṣāḥ tatra ta eva hi sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti karma ca syāt akartṛkam iti evam tāvat  sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ karma na karoti na api asadbhūtam karma kriyate asat bhūtam hi karma ahetukam bhavet  tatas ca hetau  asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca na vidyate ityādinā sarvam dūṣaṇam āpadyate tasmāt pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ dūṣita tvāt asya viṣama pakṣasya na punar hetoḥ upādānam anuṣṭhīyate yathā ca etad  satā kartrā asat karma na kriyate iti pratipāditam evam asatā kartrā akriyā yuktena satkarma na kriyate iti vyākhyeya m ukta patha anusāreṇa evam tāvat viṣama pakṣe eka eka pada parāmarśena dūṣaṇam abhidhāya idānīm ekaikasya padasya pada dvaya parāmarśena dūṣaṇa abhidhānam āha na asat bhūtam na sadbhūtaḥ sadasat bhūtam eva vā karoti kārakaḥ karma pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ sa kārakaḥ sadbhūtaḥ asat bhūtam karma sadasat bhūtam eva vā na karoti iti katham iti āha pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ iti tatra asat bhūtasya kriyā na asti  ityādinā sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ  na karoti asat bhūtam api karma na kriyate aahetukam bhavet karma  aheta ā  asati kāryam ca  ityādinā vihita doṣāt  sat asat bhūtam api karma na kriyate paraspara viruddham hi sat ca asat ca ekatas  kutas  iti vacanāt  evam tāvat sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ  asat bhūtam sat asat bhutam ca karma na karoti idānīm asat bhūtaḥ  api kārakaḥ sadbhūtam karma sat asat bhūtam ca karma na karoti iti āha na asat bhūtaḥ  api sadbhūtam sadasat bhūtam eva vā karoti kārakaḥ karma pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ  nirhetukaḥ  bhavet  aheta ā  asati kāryam ca  ityādinā ukta doṣāt asadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ  na karoti sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti kartā ca syāt akarmakaḥ iti prasaṅgāt  sadbhūtam karma na kriyate sat asat bhūtam api karma na kriyate paraspara viruddham hi sat ca asat ca ekatas  kutas  iti vacanāt  idānīm sat asat bhūtaḥ  api kārakaḥ ekaika eva ubhaya rūpaḥ san yathā sat bhūtam asat bhūtam ca bhinna saṃketam karma na karoti tathā pratipādayan  āha karoti sat asat bhūtaḥ  na sannāsat ca kārakaḥ karma tad tu vijānīyāt pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ paraspara viruddham hi sat ca asat ca ekatas  kutas  iti vacanāt sadasat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ  na karoti sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti kartā ca syāt akarmakaḥ iti prasaṅgāt sadbhūtam karma na kriyate asat bhūtam api karma ahetukam aheta ā  asati kārya ca  ityādinā ukta doṣān na kriyate yatas ca evam sama pakṣeṣu viṣama pakṣeṣu ca kartuḥ karmaṇaḥ ca sarvathā siddhiḥ ayuktā tasmāt yad uktam vidyanta eva vijñāna ādayaḥ saṃskṛtā dharmāḥ saṃskṛta svabhāvāḥ tad hetuka karma kāraka sadbhāvāt iti tad ayuktam atra āha kim avadhāritam etad bhavatā na santi bhāvā iti na hi bhavataḥ tu sa svabhāva vādinaḥ svabhāvasya bhāvānām vaidhuryāt sarva bhāva apavādaḥ saṃbhāvyate vayam tu pratītya utpanna tvāt sarva bhāvānām svabhāvam evana upalabhāmahe tad kasya apavādam kariṣyāmaḥ yathā uktam ārya ratna āvalyām marīci toyam iti etad iti matvā āgataḥ  atra san yadi na asti iti tad toyam gṛhṇīyāt mūḍha eva saḥ marīci pratimam lokam evam asti iti gṛhṇataḥ na asti iti ca api mohaḥ  ayam sati mohe na mucyate ajñāna kalpitam pūrvam paścāt tatva artha nirṇaye yadā na labhate bhāvam eva abhāvaḥ tadā kuha iti tad evam niḥsvabhāvānām sarva bhāvānām kutaḥ yathā ukta prakāra siddhiḥ tasmāt laukikam viparyāsam abhyupetya sāṃvṛtānām padārthānām marīcikā jala kalpānām idaṃpratyaya tā mātra abhyupagamena eva prasiddhiḥ na anyena iti āha pratītya kārakaḥ karma tam pratītya ca kārakam karma pravartate na anyat paśyāmaḥ siddhi kāraṇam iha akurvāṇasya karma nirapekṣasya kārakatva abhāvāt karma apekṣya kārakasya kāraka tvam bhavati kārakeṇa ca akriyamāṇasya kasyacid karmatva abhāvāt kriyamāṇasya eva karma vyapadeśāt tam kārakam pratītya karma pravartate iti evam karma kārakayoḥ paraspara āpekṣikīm siddhim muktvā na anyat siddhi kāraṇam paśyāmaḥ yathā ca karma kārakayoḥ paraspara āpekṣikī siddhiḥ evam anyeṣām api bhāvānām iti ati diśan  āha evam vidyāt upādānam vyutsargāt iti karmaṇaḥ kartuḥ ca evam iti anena anantarām
