karma kāraka prajñaptim darśayati upāttiḥ upādānam anena ca upātti kriyām āha sā ca sva sādhanam kartāram upādātāram karma ca upādānam saṃnidhāpayati tayoḥ ca upādeya upādātroḥ paraspara apekṣayoḥ karma kārakavat eva siddhiḥ na svābhāvikī kasmāt punar  svābhāvikī na bhavati iti āha vyutsargāt iti karmaṇaḥ kartuḥ ca iti iti śabdaḥ  hetu parāmarśī vyutsargaḥ  vyudāsaḥ tatas ca ayam artha upapadyate yaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ karmaṇaḥ ca vyutsargaḥ  asmābhiḥ uktaḥ taiḥ eva hetubhiḥ upādātā upādeyam ca pratiṣiddham veditavyam na ca kevala m anayoḥ anyonya āpekṣikī siddhiḥ katurḥ ca karmaṇaḥ ca pratiṣedhena avaseyā api ca karma kartṛbhyām śeṣān bhāvān vibhāvayet  prājña iti vākya śeṣaḥ karmakāra kopa ādeya upādātṛ vyatiriktā ye anye bhāvā janya janaka gantṛ gamana draṣṭavya darśana lakṣya lakṣaṇa utpādya utpādakāḥ tathā avayava avayavi guṇa guṇi pramāṇa prameya ādayaḥ  niravaśeṣā bhāvāḥ teṣām kartṛ karma vicāreṇa svabhāvataḥ  astitvam pratiṣidhya paraspara āpekṣikīm eva siddhi prājñaḥ  nirmumukṣuḥ jāti jarā maraṇa ādi bandhanebhyaḥ  mokṣāya vibhāvayet  eṣām ca vistareṇa vicāraḥ  madhyamaka avatāra ādibhyaḥ  avaseyaḥ nanu ca śeṣān bhāvān vibhāvayet iti anena eva upādāna upādāt na uradhi gata tvāt upādāna upādānam punar ayuktam satyam etad  tathā api tattva vicāre prādhānya jñāpana artham upādāna upādātra ubhedena upādānam tathā hi uttareṣu prakaraṇeṣu bhūyasā anayoḥ eva vicāraḥ  bhaviṣyati iti ata eva uktam bhagavatā ārya upāli paripṛcchāyām bhaya darśita nairayikam me sattva sahasra sa vejita na eke na ca vidyati kaściha sattva yaḥ  cyutu gacchati ghoram apāyam na ca kāraku kāraṇam santi yehi kṛtā asi tomara śastrāḥ kalpa vaśena tu paśyati tatra kāyi patanti apāyita śastrāḥ citra manorama sajjita puṣpāḥ svarṇa vimāna jalanti manojñāḥ teṣu api kāraku na astiha kaści te api ca sthāpita kalpa vaśena kalpa vaśena vikalpitu lokaḥ saṃjña gaheṇa vikalpitu bālaḥ saḥ  ca gahaḥ  agahaḥ asa bhūtaḥ  māya marīci samā hi vikalpāḥ iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau karma kāraka parīkṣā nāma aṣṭamam prakaraṇam pūrva parīkṣā navamam prakaraṇam atra āha yad uktam aevam vidyāt upādānam vyutsargāt iti karmaṇaḥ kartuḥ ca  iti tad ayuktam yasmāt  darśana śravaṇa ādīni vedanā ādīni ca api atha bhavanti yasya prāgebhyaḥ saḥ  asti iti eke vadanti uta yasya upādātuḥ darśana śravaṇa ghrāṇa rasana ādīni vedanā sparśa manaskāra ādīni ca bhavanti sa upādātā pūrvam ebhya upādānebhyaḥ  asti iti sāṃmitīyā vadanti kim kāraṇam yasmāt  katham hi avidyamānasya darśana ādi bhaviṣyati bhāvasya tasmāt prāgebhyaḥ saḥ  asti bhāvaḥ vyavasthitaḥ iha vidyamāna eva devadattaḥ  dhana upādānam kurute na avidyamānaḥ  vandhyā tanayaḥ evam yadi tāvat pudgalaḥ  darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam vyavasthitaḥ  na syāt  na asau darśana ādikasya upādānam akariṣyat tasmāt asti asau dhanāt prāk eva sthita deva dattavat darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam pudgalaḥ  yaḥ  asya upādānam kariṣyati iti ucyate darśana śravaṇa ādibhyaḥ  vedanā ādibhya eva ca yaḥ prāc vyavasthitaḥ  bhāvaḥ kena prajñapyate atha saḥ yau asau pudgalaḥ  darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam asti iti vyavasthāpyate sa kena prajñapyatām pudgala prajñapteḥ hi darśana ādikam kāraṇam sa yadi tebhyaḥ prāc vyavasthitaḥ  asti iti kalpyate tadā darśana nirapekṣaḥ syāt  ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ yaḥ ca sva kāraṇa nirapekṣaḥ sa nirhetukaḥ  dhana ādi nirapekṣaḥ dhanikavat na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ kim ca anyat  vinā api darśana ādīni yadi ca asau vyavasthitaḥ amūni api bhaviṣyanti vinā tena na saṃśayaḥ yadi manyase darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam pudgalaḥ  nāma asti sa darśana ādikam upādānam upādatte iti nanu evam sati nirasta saṃśayam amūni api darśana ādīni vinā pudgalena bhaviṣyanti tathā hi devadattaḥ  dhana saṃbandhāt pūrvam dhana vyatiriktaḥ  vyavasthitaḥ san artha antara bhūtam eva pṛthak siddham dhanam upādatte evam upādātuḥ api sva ātma vyatirekeṇa artha antara bhūtam darśana ādikam upādānam syāt  na tu saṃbhavati iti āha ajyate kenacid kaścid  kiṃcid kenacid ajyate kutas  kiṃcid vinā kaścid  kiṃcid kaṃcid vinā kutas  iha bīja ākhyena kāraṇena kiṃcid kāryam abhivyajyate aṅkura ākhyam tena ca kāryeṇa kiṃcid  kāraṇam abhivyajyate bīja ākhyam asya idam kāraṇam idam asya kāryam iti evam yadi kenacid darśana ādikena upādānena kaścid ātma svabhāvaḥ  abhivyajyate asya ayam upādātā iti kenacid ca ātmanā kiṃcid upādānam darśana ādikam abhivyajyate idam asya upādānam iti tadānīm syāt paraspara apekṣayoḥ upādāna upādātroḥ siddhiḥ yadā tu upādātāram vinā pṛthak  siddham darśana ādikam abhyupagamyate tadā tad nirāśrayam asat eva tasmāt na asti ubhayoḥ api siddhiḥ iti na yuktam etad  darśana ādibhyaḥ pṛthak avasthita upādāta iti atra āha yad uktam darśana śravaṇa ādibhya ityādi atra ucyate yadi sarvebhyaḥ  darśana ādibhya prāk avasthita iti abhyupagatam syāt  syāt eṣa doṣaḥ yadā tu sarvebhyaḥ  darśana ādibhyaḥ kaścid pūrvaḥ  na vidyate kim tarhi ekaikasmāt pūrvaḥ vidyate yadā ca evam tadā ajyate darśana ādīnām anyena punar anyadā yadā darśanena draṣṭā iti abhivyajyate na tadā śravaṇa ādīni upādāya prajñapyate tatas ca pūrva ukta doṣān avasara iti ucyate etad api na yuktam darśana ādi rahitasya nirupādānasya nirhetukasya nirañjanasya astitva asaṃbhavāt sarvebhyaḥ  darśana ādibhyaḥ  yadi pūrvaḥ na vidyate iti parikalpyate evam api ekaikasmāt katham pūrvaḥ darśana ādeḥ sa vidyate yaḥ  hi sarvebhyaḥ pūrvaḥ na bhavati sa ekaikasmāt api na bhavati tad yathā sarvebhyaḥ  vṛkṣebhya prāk  vanam na asti tadā ekaikasmāt api na asti sarvāsām ca sikatānām taila janana abhāve sati ekaikasya api sikatāyāḥ tailam na asti api ca yaḥ  hi ekaikasmāt pūrvaḥ bhavati nanu sa sarvebhyaḥ  api pūrvam eva iti abhyupagatam bhavati ekaika vyatirekeṇa sarvasya abhāvāt  tasmāt na yuktam ekaikasmāt pūrvaḥ vidyata iti itas ca na yuktam yasmāt  draṣṭā sa eva sa śrotā sa eva yadi vedakaḥ tadā ekaikasmāt bhavet pūrvam na ca yuktam vaktum sa eva draṣṭā sa eva śrotā iti yadi syāt  tadā darśana kriyā rahitasya api śrotuḥ draṣṭṭa tvam syāt  śravaṇa kriyā rahitasya api draṣṭuḥ śrotṛ tvam syāt  na ca evam dṛṣṭam yad darśana kriyā rahitaḥ  api draṣṭā syāt  śravaṇa kriyā rahitaḥ ca śrotā iti ata eva āha evam ca etad na yujyate iti pratikriyam ca kāraka bhedāt kuta etad evam bhaviṣyati iti pratipādayan  āha evam ca etad na yujyata iti ācārya buddha pālitaḥ tu vyācaṣṭe ekatve hi ātmanaḥ indriya antara gamana prasaṅgaḥ puruṣasya syāt  vātāyana antara upagamanavat iti asya ācārya bhāva vivekaḥ  dūṣaṇam āha sarva gatasya ātmanaḥ  na indriya antara gamanam asti iti ayuktaḥ prasaṅga doṣa iti tad etad ayuktam sva yūthya parikalpita pudgala vāda nirāsasya prastuta tvāt  tasya ca sarva gatatva apratijñānāt  tasmāt  yukta eva prasaṅga doṣa atha api yathā ukta doṣa parijihīrṣayā draṣṭā anya eva śrotānyaḥ  vedakaḥ  anyaḥ punar yadi parikalpyate tad api na yuktam evam hīṣyamāṇe sati syāt  draṣṭari śrotā bahu tvam ca ātmanām bhavet  tad yathā goḥ anyaḥ  aśvaḥ na hi gavi sati na bhavati yaugapadyena evam yadi draṣṭuḥ anyaḥ śrotā syāt  sa draṣṭari api sati syāt yaugapadyena na ca evam iṣyate iti na asti anya tvam api ca evam sati bahava eva ātmānaḥ prāpnuvanti draṣṭṭa śrotṛ vedaka ādīnām pṛthak  pṛthak  siddhayupagamāt  tasmāt ekaikasmāt api darśana ādeḥ pūrvam na asti pudgalaḥ  nāma kaścid  atra āha vidyata eva pūrvam sa sarvebhyaḥ  darśana ādibhya ātmā atha matam yadi asti kena prajñapyate sa iti yad ucyate iha darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam nāma rūpa avasthāyām catvāri mahābhūtāni santi yatas  kramāt nāma rūpa pratyayam ṣaṣ āyatanam iti darśana śravaṇa ādīni utpadyante tasmāt darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam catur mahā bhūta upādānam eva asti iti evam api darśana śravaṇa ādīni vedanā ādīni ca api atha bhavanti yebhyaḥ teṣu eṣa bhūteṣu api na vidyate yebhyaḥ  mahābhūtebhyaḥ  darśana ādikam utpadyate teṣu api mahābhūta upādāna nimittakaḥ  api eṣa na yujyate pūrveṇa eva hetunā iti abhiprāyaḥ tatra yathā pūrvam uktam kutas  kiṃcid vinā kaścid kiṃcid kaṃcid vinā kutas  iti iha api tathā eva vaktavyam mahābhūta upādānāt yaḥ ca ātmā pūrvam siddhaḥ syāt  sa mahābhūtāni upādāya syāt  na ca evam nirhetuka tvāt  yaḥ ca na asti sa katham mahābhūtāni upādāsyati iti darśana upādānavat bhūta upādāne api dūṣaṇam uktam eva iti na punar ucyate atra āha yadi api evam ātmā pratiṣiddhaḥ tathā api darśana ādikam asti apratiṣedhāt  na ca anātma svabhāvānām ghaṭa ādīnām darśana ādi saṃbandhaḥ  asti tasmāt saṃbandhī vidyata eva ātmā iti ucyate syāt ātmā yadi darśana ādīni eva syuḥ na tu santi yasya darśana ādīni upādānam sa yadā na asti iti pratipāditam tadā tasmin  ātmani upādātari asati kutaḥ darśana ādīnām upādāna bhūtānām astitvam iti āha darśana śravaṇa ādīni vedanā ādīni ca api atha na vidyate ced yasya sa na vidyanta imāni api yasya darśana ādīni parikalpyante sa yadā na asti iti uktam nanu tadā eva darśana ādikam api na asti iti spaṣṭam ādarśitam bhavati tatas ca darśana ādi abhāvāt na asti eva ātmā iti atra āha kim khalu bhavataḥ  niścitam etad na asti eva ātmā iti kena etad uktam nanu ca anantaram eva uktam darśana ādi abhāvāt ātmā api na asti iti uktam etadā īsmābhiḥ na tu asya arthaḥ  bhavatā samyak niḥ citaḥ yatas  bhāva rūpa ātmā iti parikalpitaḥ sa svabhāvataḥ  na vidyate tasya ca mayā svabhāva abhiniveśa nivartakam eva vacanamuktam asat viparyāsa pratipakṣeṇa na tu asya abhāvaḥ parikalpitaḥ dvayam hi etad  parityājyam yaḥ ca bhāveṣu abhiniveśaḥ yaḥ ca abhāveṣu abhiniveśa iti yathā uktam ārya devena yaḥ tava ātmā mama anātmā tena ātma aniyamān na saḥ nanu anityeṣu bhāveṣu kalpanā nāma jāyate iti etad eva pratipādayan  āha prāk  ca yaḥ  darśana ādibhyaḥ sāṃpratam ca ūrdhvam eva ca na vidyate asti na asti iti nivṛttāḥ tatra kalpanāḥ prāk  tāvat darśana ādibhya ātmā na asti tatra hi tasya astitva abhāvāt darśana ādi saha bhūtaḥ  api na asti pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayoḥ sahabhāva adarśanāt  śaśa śṛṅgayoḥ iva ātma upādānayoḥ ca paraspara nirapekṣayaḥ pṛthak pṛthak asiddha tvāt  sāṃpratam api na asti urdhvam api yadi hi pūrvam darśana ādīni syuḥ uttara kālam ātmā syāt  tadānīm ūrdhvam saṃbhavet  na ca evam akartṛkasya karmaṇaḥ  asiddha tvāt  yaḥ ca evam ātmā darśana ādibhyaḥ prāk  paścāt  yugapad ca parīkṣyamāṇaḥ  na asti tasya idānīm anupalabdha svabhāvasya astitvam na astitvam vā kaḥ parikalpayet prājñaḥ tasmāt karma kārakavat eva upādāna upādātroḥ paraspara apekṣā siddhiḥ na svābhāvikī iti sthitam ata eva uktam bhagavatā ārya samādhi rāja bhaṭṭārake tahi kāli saḥ  daśa balaḥ  anaghaḥ jinu bhāṣate imu samādhi varam su pinā upamā bhagavatī sakalā na hi kaści jāyati na ca u mriyate na ca sattvu labhyati na jīvu naraḥ  imi dharma phena kadalī sadṛśāḥ māyā upamā gagana vidyu samā daka candra saṃnibha marīci samāḥ na ca asmi loki mṛtu kaści naraḥ  para loke  saṃkramati gacchati vā na ca karma naśyati kadāci kṛtam phalu deti kṛṣṇa śubha saṃsarataḥ  na ca śāśvatam na ca uccheda punaḥ na ca karma saṃcayu na ca api sthitiḥ na ca saḥ  api kṛtva punar ā aspṛśati na ca anyu kṛtva puna vedayate na ca saṃkramaḥ  na ca punā āgamanam na ca sarvam asti na ca na asti punar  na ca dṛṣṭi sthāna gati śuddhiḥ iha na ca sattva cāra supaśānta gati anutpāda śānta animitta padam sugatāna gocara jināna guṇā bala dhāraṇī daśa balāna balam buddha aniyam vṛṣamitā paramā iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau pūrva parīkṣā nāma navamam prakaraṇam agni indhana parīkṣā daśamam prakaraṇam atra āha yad idam uktam tasmāt karma kārakavat eva upādāna upādātroḥ api na svābhāvikī siddhiḥ iti tad ayuktam sa apekṣāṇām api padārthānām sa svābhāvya darśanāt tathā hi agniḥ indhanam apekṣya bhavati na ca niḥsvabhāvaḥ  agniḥ tasya auṣṇya dāhakatva ādi svabhāva kārya upalambhāt  evam agnim apekṣya indhanam bhavati na ca tad niḥsvabhāvam bāhya mahābhūta catuṣṭaya svabhāva tvāt evam upādānasa apekṣaḥ  api upādātā svabhāvataḥ  bhaviṣyati upādātṛ sa apekṣam ca upādānam iti agni indhanavat etau bhaviṣyata upādāna upādātārau  iti ucyate syāt etad evam yadi agni indhane eva syātām na tu staḥ katham iha yadi agni indhane syātām niyatam te eka tvena vā syātām anya tvena vā ubhayathā tu na yujyata iti āha yad indhanam sa ced agniḥ eka tvam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ indhanāt api ṛte bhavet  tatra idhyate yad  tad indhanam dāhyam kāṣṭha ādika saṃbhūtam tasya dagdhā kartā agniḥ tatra yadi tāvat  yad indhanam sa eva agniḥ iti parikalpyate tadā kartṛ karmaṇoḥ eka tvam syāt  na ca evam dṛṣṭam ghaṭa kumbhakārayoḥ chet tṛ  chettavyayoḥ ca ekatva prasaṅgāt  tasya ca anabhyupagamāt  atha anya tvam evam api yadi indhanāt anyaḥ  agniḥ syāt  tadā indhana nirapekṣasya agneḥ upalabdhiḥ syāt  na hi ghaṭāt anyaḥ paṭaḥ tad nirapekṣaḥ  na dṛṣṭaḥ na ca evam indhana nirapekṣaḥ  agniḥ iti na yuktam etad  api ca yadi indhanāt anyaḥ  agniḥ syāt  tadānīm nitya pradīpta eva syāt apradīpana hetukaḥ punar ārambha vaiyarthyam evam ca akarmakaḥ sati indhanāt pṛthak bhūtaḥ  agniḥ iṣyamāṇaḥ  nitya pradīpta eva syāt  apradīpana hetukaḥ ca syāt  punar ārambha vaiyarthyam ca syāt  evam ca sati akarmaka eva syāt  amum eva artham pratipādayitu kāma āha paratra nirapekṣa tvāt apradīpana hetukaḥ punar ārambha vaiyarthyam nitya dīptaḥ prasajyate iti tatra pradīpyate tad iti pradīpanam indhanam pradīpanam hetuḥ asya iti pradīpana hetuka na pradīpana hetukaḥ apradīpana hetukaḥ yadi pradīpanāt anyaḥ  agniḥ syāt  tadā indhana nirapekṣaḥ syāt  yaḥ  hi yasmāt anyaḥ sa tad nirapekṣaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ tatas ca paratra nirapekṣa tvāt apradīpana hetukaḥ syāt  pradīpana sāpekṣasya hi agneḥ tad abhāve syāt nirvāṇam yadā tu pradīpana nirapekṣa tadā nirvāṇa pratyaya vaikalyāt nitya pradīpta eva bhavet  nitya pradīpte ca agnau sati agneḥ aparinirvāṇa artham ca asya upādāna saṃdhukṣaṇa ādikam vyartham eva syāt  evam ca sati akarmakaḥ  agniḥ kartā syāt  na ca avidyamāna karmakasya kartṛ tvam vandhyā sutasya iva tasmāt indhanāt agneḥ anyatvam iti na yujyate atra āha yad etad uktam anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ indhanāt api ṛte bhavet  iti tad ayuktam iha anya tve api sati agni indhanayoḥ na vinā eva indhanena agneḥ astitvam yasmāt jvālā parigataḥ  arthaḥ  dāhyatva lakṣaṇaḥ indhanam tad āśrayeṇa ca agniḥ upalabhyate na pṛthak  yadā ca etad evam agni saṃbandhāt eva indhana vyapadeśaḥ  bhavati indhana āśrayeṇa ca agniḥ upalabhyate na pṛthak  tadā anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ ityādi doṣa prasaṅgasya na asti eva avasara iti asya pakṣasyāṣya yukta tām udbhāvayan  āha tatra etasmāt idhyamānam indhanam bhavati iti ced  kena idhyatām indhanam tad tāvat mātram idam yadā yadi manyase jvālā parigataḥ  arthaḥ  dāhya lakṣaṇaḥ indhanam tad āśrayaḥ ca agniḥ iti evam api parikalpyamāne indhanam agniḥ dahati iti na upapadyate yasmāt  kena idhyatām indhanam tad tāvat mātram idam yadā iha indhanam agniḥ dahati iti parikalpyamāne jvālā parigatam dāhyam indhanam iti na ca etad vayatirekeṇa aparam agnim paśyāmaḥ  yena indhanam dahyeta yasmāt etāvat mātram idam upalabhyate yad uta jvālā parigatam dāhya mātram yadā ca etad vayatiriktaḥ  na asti agniḥ tadā kena tad indhanam dāhyatām tāvat mātram idam yadā idhyamāna mātram idam yadā iti arthaḥ tasmāt na agniḥ indhanam dahati tadvayati rikta agni abhāvāt yadā ca evam tadā kutas  kasyacid jvālā parigatiḥ iti sa eva doṣaḥ  na vepate api ca anyatva abhyupagame agni indhanayoḥ idhyamāna vyapadeśa abhāvāt kuta idhyamānam indhanam kutaḥ vā indhanam agniḥ dhakṣyati iti pratipādayan  āha anyaḥ  na prāpsyate aprāptaḥ  na dhakṣyati adahan punar  na nirvāsyati anirvāṇaḥ sthāsyate vā sva liṅgavān yadi indhanāt anyaḥ  agniḥ syāt  saḥ  anya tvāt andhakāram iva indhanam na prāpnuyāt  na ca dhakṣyati aprāpta tvāt viprakṛṣṭa deśa avasthitam iva iti abhiprāyaḥ evam ca idhyamānam indhanam bhavati iti na upapannam eva tatas ca agneḥ nirvāṇam na syāt  anirvāṇaḥ ca sva liṅgavān eva sthāsyati pradīpta iti arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ  avadhāraṇe draṣṭavyaḥ  vikalpa arthaḥ  vā sva liṅgavān eva agniḥ sthāsyati yadi vā na asti anya tvam agneḥ indhanāt iti samuccaye vā anyaḥ  na prāpsyati na dhakṣyati na ca nirvāsyati sva liṅgavān  ca sthāsyati tasmāt ayuktam indhanāt anya tvam agneḥ atra āha ayuktam agni indhanayoḥ anya tvam yasmāt na prāpsyate aprāptaḥ  na dhakṣyati adahan punar ityādi tad ayuktam dṛṣṭā hi anya tve strī puruṣayoḥ prāptiḥ evam agni indhanayoḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate anya eva indhanāt agniḥ indhanam prāpnuyāt yadi strī saṃprāpnoti puruṣam puruṣaḥ ca striyam yathā syāt etad evam yadi strī puruṣavat paraspara anapekṣā agni indhanayoḥ siddhiḥ syāt  na tu asti iti āha anya eva indhanāt agniḥ indhanam kāmam āpnuyāt  agni indhane yadi syātām anyonyena tiraskṛte na tu evam saṃbhavati yad indhana nirapekṣaḥ  agniḥ syāt  agni nirapekṣam ca indhanam iti tasmāt  dṛṣṭānta vaiyarthyam anyonya apekṣā adhīna janmanām sati anya tve yeṣām prāptiḥ siddhā teṣām eva dṛṣṭānta tvena upādānam nyāyyam syāt  te ca na saṃbhavanti iti na yuktam etad anya tve sati prāptiḥ asti iti atra āha yadi api agni indhanayoḥ strī puruṣavat paraspara nirapekṣā siddhiḥ na asti tathā api paraspara apekṣā tāvat asti tatas ca asti eva agni in dhanayoḥ svarūpa siddhiḥ paraspara sāpekṣa tvāt na hi avidyamānayoḥ vandhyā putra duhitroḥ paraspara apekṣa tā dṛṣṭā iti ucyate evam api yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ apekṣya agnim yadi indhanam katarat pūrva niṣpannam yad apekṣya agniḥ indhanam asya indhanasya ayam agniḥ dāhakaḥ kartā iti evam yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ vyavasthāpyate asya agneḥ idam indhanam karma iti evam agnim apekṣya yadi indhanam tad  katarat anayoḥ pūrva niṣpannam kim indhanam yad apekṣya agni syāt  uta agniḥ yam apekṣya indhanam syāt  tatra yadi indhanam pūrva niṣpannam iti kalpyate tad ayuktam agni nirapekṣasya anidhyamānasya indhanatva abhāvāt  tṛṇa ādeḥ sarvasya ca eva indhanatva prasaṅgāt  atha pūrvam agniḥ paścāt indhanam iti tad api ayuktam indhanāt pūrva siddhasya agneḥ asaṃbhavāt  nirhetukatva prasaṅgāt  paścāt ca apekṣayā niṣprayojana tvāt  tasmāt na asti atra kiṃcid pūrva siddham yad apekṣya itarasya siddhi syāt  atha api manyase pūrvam indhanam paścāt agniḥ iti evam api yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ agneḥ siddhasya sādhanam bhaviṣyati yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ bhaviṣyati iti parikalpyate evam tarhi siddhasya sataḥ  agneḥ punar api sādhanam syāt  vidyamānasya eva padārthasya siddha rūpasya apekṣā yujyate na hi avidyamānaḥ  devadattaḥ  gṛhe kaṃcid apekṣate evam yadi agniḥ vidyamānaḥ  na syāt  na asau  indhanam apekṣate tasmāt astitvam agne rambhu peyam tadā ca kim asya indhanasya apekṣayā punar  kartavyam na hi siddhaḥ  agniḥ punar indhanena kartavyaḥ  yad artham indhana apekṣā sāphalyam syāt  tasmāt indhanam apekṣya agniḥ bhavati iti na yuktam api ca yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ bhavati iti parikalpyate evam sati indhanam ca api bhaviṣyati niragnikam yadi indhanam asiddham syāt  na eva tad agninā apekṣyeta asiddhasya apekṣā yogāt tasmāt niragnikasya indhanasya siddhiḥ abhyupeyā na ca evam etad iti na yuktam etad iti atha matam yaugapadyena eva indhana siddhayā agni siddhiḥ agni siddhayā ca indhana siddiḥ tatas ca ekasya api pūrva siddhayanabhyupagamāt tatra yad uktam katarat pūrva niṣpannam yad apekṣya agniḥ indhanam iti tad ayuktam iti ucyate evam apīṣyamāṇe ubhayasya api na asti siddhiḥ yasmāt  yaḥ  apekṣya sidhyate bhāvaḥ tam eva apekṣya sidhyati yadi yaḥ  apekṣitavyaḥ sa sidhyatām kam apekṣya kaḥ tatra yadi yaḥ agni ākhyaḥ  bhāvaḥ yam indhana ākhyam bhāvam apekṣya sidhyati indhana ākhyaḥ ca bhāvaḥ yaḥ  agninā ātma siddhayartham apekṣitavyaḥ sa yadi tam eva agni ākhyam padārtham apekṣya sidhyati kathyatām idānīm sidhyatām kam apekṣya kaḥ iti yadā ca agni abhāve sati indhanasya siddhiḥ eva na asti tadā akāraṇasya indhanasya abhāvāt  kutas tad hetukaḥ agniḥ prasetsyati evam ya indhana ākhyaḥ  bhāvaḥ yam agni ākhyam bhāvam apekṣya sidhyati agni ākhyaḥ ca bhāvaḥ yaḥ indhana ākhyena ātma siddhayartham apekṣitavyaḥ sa yadi tam eva indhana ākhyam bhāvam apekṣya sidhyati kathyatām kim idānīm sidhyatām kam apekṣya kaḥ iti yadā hi indhana abhāve sati agneḥ siddhiḥ na asti tadā niṣkāraṇasya agneḥ abhāvāt  kutas tad hetukam indhanam itas ca agni indhanayoḥ paraspara apekṣayā api siddhiḥ asatī siddha asiddhayoḥ apekṣā bhāvāt iti pratipādayan  āha yaḥ  apekṣya sidhyate bhāvaḥ saḥ  asiddhaḥ  apekṣate katham atha api apekṣate siddhaḥ tu apekṣā asya na yujyate yaḥ  hi agni ākhyaḥ  bhāvaḥ indhana ākhyam bhāvam apekṣya sidhyati saḥ asiddhaḥ  vā indhanam apekṣate siddhaḥ  vā yadi asiddhaḥ tadā asiddha tvāt  khara viṣāṇavat na indhanam apekṣeta atha siddhaḥ siddha tvāt  kim asya indhana apekṣayā na hi siddham punar api sādhyate vaiyarthyāt  evam indhane api vācyam tasmāt na agni in dhanayoḥ paraspara apekṣayā yaugapadyena vā siddhiḥ iti yatas ca evam tasmāt  apekṣya indhanam agniḥ na atha syāt  anapekṣya agniḥ tarhi bhaviṣyati iti etad api na yuktam iti āha na anapekṣya agniḥ indhanam anyatva pratiṣedhāt ahetukatva prasaṅgāt ca yathā ca agniḥ apekṣya vā anapekṣya vā indhanam saṃbhavati evam indhanam api iti āha apekṣya indhanam agnim na na anapekṣya agnim indhanam etad ca anantaram eva gata artha tvāt na punar ucyate atra āha kim anayā asmākam ati sūkṣma īkṣikayā prayojanam ye vayam brūmaḥ yasmāt agninā idhyamānam indhanam pratyakṣata upalabhyate tasmāt te eva agni indhane iti ucyate syāt etad evam yadi agniḥ indhanam dahet  yadi indhane agniḥ saṃbhavet  sa indhanam dahet  na tu saṃbhavati iti āha āgacchati anyatas  na agniḥ indhane agniḥ na vidyate indhana vyatiriktāt tāvat kutaścid anyataḥ agneḥ āgamanam na asti tasya adṛṣṭa tvāt  nirindhanasya ca ahetukasya agneḥ āgamana abhāvāt sa indhanasya ca āgamane prayojana abhāvāt tatra api ca indhane tulya paryanuyogāt  anavasthā prasaṅgāt ca āgacchati anyatas  na agniḥ tathā indhane api agniḥ na saṃbhavati tatra anupalabhyamāna tvāt  atha syāt  vidyamānasya api mūla udaka ādivat abhivyañjaka pratyaya vaikalyāt pūrvam anupalabhyamāna tvam araṇi nigharṣaṇāt abhivyañjaka pratyaya saṃbhavāt tu paścāt upalabdhiḥ iti idam eva tāvat saṃpradhāryate kim punar mūla udaka ādīnām abhivyañjakaiḥ pratyayaiḥ kriyata iti tatra svarūpam tāvat na kriyate vidyamāna tvāt  abhivyaktiḥ kriyata iti ced  kā iyam abhivyaktiḥ nāma prakāśa ta iti ced  evam tarhi sā eva kriyate pūrvam avidyamāna tvāt asyāḥ satkārya vāda tyāgaḥ ca evam jāyate abhivyakteḥ pūrvam avidyamāna tvāt paścāt ca bhāvāt  svarūpasya ca utpatti pratyaya nirapekṣa tvāt khapuṣpavat abhivyakti pratyaya sāpekṣatā api na syāt  api ca iyam abhivyaktiḥ abhivyaktasya vā bhāvasya parikalpyeta anabhivyaktasya vā tatra tāvat  yad abhivyaktam tad na abhivyajyate tasya abhivyakti vaiyarthyāt  aniṣṭa doṣa prasaṅgāt ca anabhivyaktam api na abhivyajyate kha puṣpavat ana bhivyakta tvāt  iti evam abhivyaktiḥ na saṃbhavati atha api syāt  vidyamānasya eva pratyayaiḥ sthaulyam kriyate iti evam api yad eva sthaulyam pūrvam na asti iti tad eva kriyata iti kutas  sthaulya āpādanam abhivyaktiḥ saukṣmyasya ca nirhetukasya asaṃbhavāt kasya sthūla tā āpādanāt abhivyaktiḥ syāt iti tad evam sarvathā indhane agneḥ na saṃbhava iti indhane agniḥ na vidyate na ca avidyamāna agninā indhanasya dahanam upajāyate iti asatyam eva etad upalabhate bhavān api ca yathā pūrvam gatāgata gamyamānānām dūṣaṇam uktam atra indhane śeṣa muktam gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ agninā indhanam dahyamānam upalabhyate iti atra indhana prastāve śeṣam dūṣaṇam gamyamāna gata āgata dūṣaṇena veditavyam ukta pāṭha viparyayeṇa dagdham na dahyate tāvat adagdham na eva dahyate dagdhā dagdha vinirmuktam dahyamānam na dahyate ityādinā yata evam atas  na asti agninā indhanasya dahanam iti veditavyam idānīm yathā upapāditam artham nigamayan  āha indhanam punar agniḥ na na agniḥ anyatra ca indhanāt  na agniḥ indhanavān na agnau  indhanāni na teṣu saḥ tatra yad indhanam sa ced agniḥ eka tvam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ bhavet  iti anena agni indhanayorakatva pratiṣedhāt indhanam punar agniḥ na anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ indhanāt api ṛte bhavet  ityādinā anyatvasya pratiṣedhāt  na agniḥ anyatra ca indhanāt  tattva anyatva ubhaya pakṣa pratiṣedhāt eva tadvat pakṣa ādhāra ādheya pakṣāṇām api arthataḥ pratiṣiddha tvāt tān api nigamayan  āha na agniḥ indhanavān na agnau  indhanāni na teṣu saḥ iti tatra agniḥ indhanavān na bhavati indhanam asya asmin vā vidyata iti vyatirekeṇa vā vyutpādena avyatirekeṇa vā tatra vyatirekeṇa tad yathā gomān devadattaḥ avyatirekeṇa buddhimān devadattaḥ  rūpavān ityādi agni indhanayoḥ ca pakṣa dvayasya api pratiṣiddha tvāt indhanavān agniḥ iti pratiṣedhaḥ  vihitaḥ anyat ca kuṇḍam dadhna ādhāra tām pratipadyate na ca indhanāt anya tvam agneḥ asti iti na agnau  indhanāni iti yujyate na api indhane asti agniḥ anyatva pratiṣedhāt iti evam ādhāra ādheya tā pratiṣedhaḥ  api arthata upapādita eva yathā ca agniḥ pañcadhā vicāryamāṇaḥ  na saṃbhavati evam ātmā api iti atidiśan  āha agni indhanābhyām vyākhyāta ātma upādānayoḥ kramaḥ sarvaḥ  niravaśeṣeṇa tatra upādīyate iti upādānam pañca upādāna skandhāḥ yaḥ tān upādāya prajñapyate sa upādātā grahītā niṣpādaka ātmā iti ucyate ahaṃkāra viṣaya tvāt āhita utpāditaḥ  ahaṃmānaḥ  asmin  iti tad asya ātmana upādānasya ca yaḥ kramaḥ siddhiḥ sa sarvaḥ  agni indhanābhyām vyākhyātaḥ  avagantavyaḥ  niravaśeṣeṇa kaḥ punar  sarvasya niravaśeṣasya ca bhedaḥ sarva grahaṇena eva pañca pakṣāḥ samanantara prakrānta abhisaṃbadhyante sarve ete pañca api pakṣāḥ agni indhanavat ātma upādānayoḥ api avikalā ḍhaukanīyāḥ yaḥ ca eyā pratipādane upapatti kramaḥ prāk upavarṇitaḥ tena niravaśeṣeṇa ātma upādānayoḥ pratiṣedhaḥ  veditavyaḥ iti anena sarva ātmanā pratiṣedha sāmyam agni indhanābhyām ātma upādānayoḥ veditavyam iti upadarśana artham sarvaḥ  nirava śeṣeṇa iti āha tatra yad eva upādānam sa eva ātmā iti evam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt na yujyate na api anyat upādānam anya upādātā skandha vyatirekeṇa api ātma upalabdhi prasaṅgāt  paratra nirapekṣa tvāt itya ādi prasaṅgāt ca ekatva anyatva pratiṣedhāt ca skandhavān aṣya ātmā na bhavati anyatva abhāvāt ca na ātmani skandhā na skandheṣu ātmā yata evam pañcasu prakāreṣu ātmanaḥ  na sattvam tasmāt karma kārakavat eva ātma upādānayoḥ paraspara āpekṣikī siddhiḥ iti sthitam yaḥ ca ayam ātma upādānayoḥ kramaḥ sa na anayoḥ eva kim tarhi sārdham ghaṭa paṭa ādibhiḥ niravaśeṣaiḥ padārthaiḥ sarvathā vyākhyātaḥ  veditavyaḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ  hi kārya kāraṇa bhūta  avayava avayavi bhūtā lakṣaṇa lakṣya bhūtāḥ  guṇna guṇi bhūtā vā syuḥ tatra mṛd daṇḍa cakra sūtra salila kulāla karavyāya āmādayaḥ  ghaṭasya kāraṇa bhūtāḥ ghaṭaḥ kārya bhūtaḥ kapāla āt ayaḥ  nīlādayaḥ  vā avayava bhūtāḥ ghaṭaḥ  avayavī pṛthu budhna lamba oṣṭha dīrgha grīvatva ādīni lakṣaṇāni ghaṭaḥ  lakṣyaḥ śyāma tvāt ayaḥ  guṇāḥ ghaṭaḥ  guṇī iti evam vyavasthāpya agni indhanavat  kramaḥ  yojyaḥ eṣām ca ghaṭa ādīnām ātma upādānayoḥ ca madhyamaka avatāra prakaraṇāt  vyākhyānam avaseyam tad evam karma kārakavat ātma upādānayoḥ ghaṭa ādīnām ca paraspara apekṣikyām siddhau vyavasthitāyām tathāgata vacanā viparīta artha avabodha abhimāni tayā tīrthyamata upa kalpita padārtha vyavasthām saugata pravacana artha tvena upanīya ati mūḍha tayā ātmanaḥ ca sa tattvam ye bhāvānām ca pṛthak pṛthak  nirdiśanti na tān manye śāsanasya artha kovidān tatra saha tena vartata iti satat satatas  bhāvaḥ sa tattvam apṛthak tvam ananya tvam eka tvam iti arthaḥ tad etad sa tattvam ye varṇayanti na tān ācāryaḥ śāsana artha paṇḍitān manyate tad yathā ātmā upādānena prajñapyate yena saha eva tena upādānena saṃbhavati sa na pṛthak  avyatirekeṇa eva bhavati iti arthaḥ evam yena kāraṇena mṛdādinā ghaṭaḥ prajñapyate tad avyatirekeṇa eva sa bhavati na pṛthak  evam ātmanaḥ  bhāvānām ca sa tattvam ye varṇayanti na te parama gambhīrasya pratītyasamutpāda stha śāśvata uccheda rahitasya upādāya prajñapti abhidhānasya tattvam paśyanti pṛthak  pṛthak  ca ye nirdiśanti pṛthak iti ātmānam pṛthak upādānam pṛthak  kāryam pṛthak  kāraṇam ityādinā anya tvam paśyanti amūn api na śāsanasya artha kovidāna ācāryaḥ  manyate yathā uktam ekatva anyatva rahitam pratiśrutka upamam jagat  saṃkrāntim āsādya gatam buddhavān  tvam aninditaḥ evam ca agni indhana parīkṣayā adhigata dharma tattva paramasya yoginaḥ kalpena akāla ālipsitaiḥ api na eva vapuḥ dahyate rāga dveṣa moha hutāśanaiḥ api vā iti yathā uktam bhagavatā yatha gagaṇu na jātu dagdha pūrvam su bahubhi kalpa śataiḥ hi dahyamānam gagana sama vijānamāna dharmān saḥ  api na dahyati jātu sa agni madhye sarvi hi jvalamāṇi buddha kṣetre praṇidhi karoti samādhiye sthihitvā jvalata ayu praśāmyatām aśeṣa pṛthivi vinaśyipi na evasya anyathātvam tathā araṇim yatha ca uttarāraṇim hasta vyāyāmu trayebhi saṃgatiḥ iti pratyayataḥ  agni jāyate jātu kṛtu kārya laghū nirudhyate atha paṇḍitu kaści mārgate kuta ayam āgatu kutra yāti vā vidiśaḥ  diśa sarvi mārgataḥ  na agatiḥ na asya gatiḥ ca labhyati skandha āyatanāni dhātavaḥ śūnya ādhyātmika śūnya bāhirāḥ sarva ātma vivikta nālayā dharma ākāśa sabhāva lakṣaṇāḥ imu īdṛśa dharma lakṣaṇā buddha dīpaṃkara darśane tvayā anubuddha yatha tvayā ātmanā tatha bodha īhi sa deva mānuṣān viparītaa bhūta kalpitai rāga doṣaiḥ paridahyate jagat  kṛpa megha śama ambu śītalām muñca dhārām amṛtasya nāyaka iti vistaraḥ iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau agni indhana parīkṣā nāma daśamam prakaraṇam pūrva apara koṭi parīkṣā ekādaśamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyata eva ātmā saṃsāra sadbhāvāt  yadi hi ātmā na syāt  kasya pañcagatike ājavaṃjavībhāvena janma maraṇa paraṃparayā saṃsaraṇam syāt  uktam hi bhagavatā anavara agraḥ  hi bhikṣavaḥ  jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāraḥ iti avidyā nīvaraṇānām sattvānām tṛṣṇā saṃyojanānām tṛṣṇā gaṇḍuḥ baddhānām saṃsaratām saṃdhāvatām pūrvā koṭiḥ na prajñāyata iti yadā ca bhagavat upadeśāt saṃsāraḥ  asti tadā saṃsartā api asti sa ca ātmā ucyata iti ucyate syāt ātmā yadā saṃsāra eva syāt  katham yasmāt asya pūrvā prajñāyate koṭiḥ na iti uvāca mahā muniḥ saṃsāraḥ  anavara agraḥ  hi na asya ādiḥ na api paścimam koṭiḥ bhāgaḥ  deśa iti paryāyāḥ pūrvā koṭiḥ pūrvaḥ deśa iti arthaḥ yadi hi saṃsāraḥ  nāma kaścid  syāt  niyatam tasya pūrvam api syāt  paścimam api ghaṭa ādīnām iva uktam ca bhagavatā anavara agraḥ  hi bhikṣavaḥ  jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāra iti yad eva avara agre na staḥ saṃsārasya anavara agra vacanāt  saṃsāra eva na asti iti nanu spaṣṭam ādeśayāmāsa bhagavān tasmāt na asti saṃsāraḥ pūrva apara koṭayanupalambhāt  alāta cakravat  iti sthitam atra idam vicāryate yadi pūrvam ca aparam ca saṃsārasya niṣiddham bhagavatā katham punar idam āha tasmāt tarhi saṃsāra kṣayāya pratipatsyāmaha iti evam vaḥ  bhikṣavaḥ śikṣitavyam iti ucyate avidyā nīvaraṇānām sattvānām ityādi viśeṣaṇa upādānāt teṣām eva ayam anavara agraḥ saṃsāra iti pratīyate na punar tattva jñāna anila balāt samunmūlita avidyā nīvaraṇa tarūṇām teṣām tu loka uttara mārga jñāna agninā dagdha aśeṣa kleśa vāsanā mūla niḥśeṣa pādapānām bhavati eva antar  iti vijñeyam katham punar ādiḥ ahitānām anta upadeśa iti yāvat  dṛṣṭam etad  bāhyeṣu vrīhi ādiṣu ādya bhāve api dahana ādi saṃparkāt anta sadbhāvaḥ yathā uktam ārya deva pādaiḥ yathā bījasya dṛṣṭaḥ  antaḥ na ca ādiḥ tasya vidyate tathā kāraṇa vaikalyāt janmanaḥ  api na saṃbhavaḥ iti sa ca anta upadeśaḥ  laukika eva vyavahāre sthitvā saṃsāra cāraka avabaddhānām utsāhana artham sattvānām deśitaḥ  laukika jñāna apekṣayā vastuka cintāyām tu saṃsāra eva na asti tad kutaḥ asya parikṣayaḥ pradīpa avasthāyām rajjūraga parikṣayavat  atra āha yadi evam laukika jñāna apekṣayā antavat  ādiḥ api kim na ucyate ucyate ahetuka doṣa prasaṅgāt  laukika jñāna apekṣayā api saṃsārasya ādeḥ abhāva iti ubhayathā api ādeḥ abhāva eva iti vijñeyam atra āha yadya api avara agre na staḥ saṃsārasya tathā api madhyam asti apratiṣedhāt  tatas ca asti saṃsāraḥ  madhya sadbhāvāt  iha yad na asti na tasya madhyam asti tad yathā kūrma roma prāvaraṇasya iti hāsyaḥ khalu asi nanu ca bhoḥ na eva agram na avaram yasya tasya madhyam kutaḥ bhavet  agram iti ādiḥ pūrvam prathamam ucyate avaram iti avasānam antar  vyavaccheda ucyate yasya saṃsārasya ādiḥ antaḥ ca pratiṣiddhaḥ tasya kutaḥ madhyam bhaviṣyati tatas ca saṃjñā mātrakam eva viparyāsa para vaśa mānasānām saṃsāraḥ ādi madhya avasāna virahita tvāt ākāśavat alāta cakra ādivat iti bhāvaḥ saṃsāra abhāvāt ca na asti ātmā iti yata evam saṃsārasya ādi madhya avasānāni na santi ata eva saṃsāra abhāvāt jāti jarā maraṇa ādīnām pūrva apara sahakramā api na eva santi iti āha tasmāt na atra upapadyante pūrva apara saha kramāḥ yathā ca na upapadyante tathā pratipādayan  āha pūrvam jātiḥ yadi bhavet jarā maraṇam uttaram nirjara amaraṇā jātiḥ bhavet jāyeta ca amṛtaḥ yadi pūrvam jātiḥ bhavet  tadā maraṇa sahitā syāt  na ca jarā ādi rahitā jātiḥ yujyate asaṃskṛtatva prasaṅgāt  jarā maraṇa rahitasya bhāvasya jātau parikalpyamānāyām anyatra amṛtasya eva devadattasya prathamam iha jātiḥ parikalpyamānā syāt  tatas ca ādimān saṃsāraḥ syāt ahetuka doṣaḥ ca abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti evam pūrva anta kalpanā ca na syāt  abhūtvā ca pūrvam paścāt iha utpādaḥ syāt  atha syāt  āmra ādīnām yathā pūrvam vinā api jarā maraṇa saṃbandhāt  prathamam eva utpādaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ evam ātmānaḥ  api iti na evam sādhya sama tvāt  āmra ādīnām api hi sva bīja nirodhe samutpadyamāna tvāt  na anyatra avinaṣṭānām utpāda iti samam etad  pūrveṇa atha syāt  anyat eva vṛkṣāt bījam atas  anyatra avināśa pūrvaka eva vṛkṣasya utpāda iti na evam kārya kāraṇayoḥ anyatvasya asiddha tvāt tathā ca vakṣyati pratītya yad yad bhavati na hi tāvat tad eva tad  na ca anyat api tad tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam na ca bījāt vṛkṣasya anya tvam atas  sādhya samam etad  yatas ca anyatra amṛtasya iha utpādaḥ  na asti na pūrvam jātiḥ abhyupeyā atha pūrvam jarā maraṇam paścāt jātiḥ evam api paścāt jātiḥ yadi bhavet jarā maraṇam āditas  ahetukam ajātasya syāt jarā maraṇam katham jāti pratyayam jarā maraṇam iti vacanāt jāti hetukam jarā maraṇam uktam bhagavatā yadi etad pūrvam syāt tadā nirhetukam syāt  tasmāt na yuktam etad  yatas  api uktam yatha ukkhitte loḍhammi ukkheve atthi kāraṇam ṣaḍane kāraṇam ṇatthi aṇṇam ukkheva kāraṇā iti yathā aṣyatra utkṣepaḥ patana kāraṇam na anyat  evam iha api jātim evakāraṇa tvena vināśasya varṇa yāmaḥ  na anyat  iti na asti ahetuka tā vināśasya jāti hetuka tvāt ca asya udgamanam eva vināśasya hetuḥ iti kṛtvā eṣā api gāthā sunītā bhavati evime saṃkhatā dhammā saṃbhavanti sa kāraṇā sa bhāva eva dhammāṇam yam vibhonti samuggatā iti idānīm sahabhāvena api jāti jarā maraṇānām asadbhāvam pratipādayan  āha na jarā maraṇena eva jātiḥ ca saha yujyate mriyeta jāyamānaḥ ca syāt ca ahetu katobhayoḥ yadi sahabhāvaḥ  jāti jarā maraṇānām syāt  tadā jāyamānasya maraṇam syāt  na ca etad yuktam na ca paraspara viruddha tvāt āloka andhakāravat eka kālatā yuktā na ca evam loke dṛṣṭam yad jāyamāna eva mriyate iti api ca ahetuka tvam jāti ādīnām sahabhāva kalpanāyām syāt  na hi saha bhūtayoḥ savya itara gaḥ viṣāṇayoḥ anyonya hetuka tā dṛṣṭā iti na yuktam etad  tad evam yatra na prabhavanti ete pūrva apara saha kramāḥ prapañcayanti tām jātim tad jarā maraṇam ca kim yasyām jātau yatra jarā maraṇe ete pūrva apara saha kramāḥ na santi tām jātim anupalabhamānā āryāḥ kim prapañcayanti kiṃśabdaḥ  asaṃbhave na eva prapañcayanti iti arthaḥ athavā evam avidyamāneṣu jāti ādiṣu tām jāti bha vidyamānām bālāḥ kim prapañcayanti tad ca jarā maraṇam yad na saṃvidyate tasmāt avastuka eva bālānām prapañca iti abhiprāyaḥ yathā ca saṃsārasya pūrvā koṭiḥ na asti evam anyeṣām api bhāvānām iti āha kāryam ca kāraṇam ca eva lakṣyam lakṣaṇam eva ca vedanā vedakaḥ ca eva santi arthā ye ca kecana pūrvā na vidyate koṭiḥ saṃsārasya na kevalam sarveṣām api bhāvānām pūrvā koṭiḥ na vidyate tatra yadi pūrvam kāraṇam paścāt kāryam syāt  akārya kam kāraṇam nirhetukam syāt  atha pūrvam kāryam paścāt kāraṇam evam api kāraṇāt pūrvam kāryam nirhetukam eva syāt  atha yugapad kārya kāraṇe syātām evam ubhayam api ahetukam syāt  evam lakṣya lakṣaṇe vedanā vedakau ca yojyau na ca kevalam saṃsārasya vyākhyānena kārya kāraṇa ādikam vyākhyātam veditavyam api ca ye api ante padārthā jñāna jñeya pramāṇa prameya sādhana sādhya avayava avayavi guṇa guṇī ādayaḥ teṣām api pūrvā koṭiḥ na vidyata iti yojyam ata eva ārya ratna megha sūtre ārya sarva nīvaraṇa viṣkambhiṇā mahā bodhisattvena bhagavān stutaḥ ādiśāntā hi anutpannāḥ prakṛtyā eva ca nirvṛtāḥ dharmāḥ te vivṛtā nātha dharma cakra pravartane iti tathā ādita śūnya anāgata dharmā naḥ gata asthita sthāna viviktāḥ nityam asāraka māyasa bhāvāḥ śuddha viśuddha nabha upama sarvi yam ca pabhāṣati dharma jinasya tam ca na paśyati saḥ  akṣayatāya ādiniḥ ātma nisattvimi dharmāḥ tān  ca ca pabhāṣati naḥ ca kṣapā iti kalpita buccati kalpita mātram antu na labhyati saṃsaramāṇe koṭi alakṣaṇa yā puri āsīdeti anāgati pratyaya tāye karma kriyā ca pravartati evam hīna autkṛṣṭa tayā samudenti jaḍḍaka dharma sadā prakṛtīye śūnya nirātma vijānatha sarvān ityādi iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau pūrva apara koṭi parīkṣā nāma ekādaśamam prakaraṇam duḥkha parīkṣā dvādaśamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyata eva ātmā tad saṃbandhi duḥkha sadbhāvāt iha hi pañca upādāna skandhā duḥkham iti ucyate tad ca asti tena ca duḥkhena kasyacid bhavitavyam na nirāśrayeṇa iti atas  vidyata eva duḥkhasya āśrayaḥ sa ca ātmā iti ucyate syāt ātmā yadi duḥkham eva syāt  tad hi bhavet  svayam kṛtam vā para kṛtam vā ubhaya kṛtam vā hetuḥ ahitam vā sarvathā ca iṣyamāṇam tad kāryam eva na asti iti pratipādayan  āha svayam kṛtam para kṛtam dvābhyām kṛtam ahetukam duḥkham iti eka icchanti tad ca kāryam na yujyate tatra eke vādinaḥ svayam kṛtam duḥkham iti pratipannāḥ apare punar  para kṛtam anye ca ubhaya kṛtam kecid ahetu samutpannam eva duḥkham iti pratipannāḥ sarvathā ca tad duḥkham iṣyamāṇam kāryam kartavyam na yujyate tad etad pratijñā mātrakam iti tad pratipādayan  āha svayam kṛtam yadi bhavet pratītya na tatas  bhavet  skandhān imānamī skandhāḥ saṃbhavanti pratītya hi yasmāt imān maraṇa antikān skandhān pratītya ime aupapattyā aṃśikāḥ skandhā utpadyante tasmāt svayam kṛtam duḥkham iti na upapadyate idānīm para kṛtam api duḥkham yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha yadi amībhya ime anye syuḥ ebhyaḥ  vāmī pare yadi bhavet para kṛtam duḥkham paraiḥ ebhiḥ amī kṛtāḥ yadā amībhyaḥ  maraṇa antikebhyaḥ skandhebhyaḥ ime aupapattyā aṃśikāḥ skandhā anye syuḥ ebhyaḥ  vā aupapattyā aṃśikebhyaḥ amī maraṇa antikā skandhāḥ pare syuḥ syāt tadānīm para kṛtam duḥkham na ca eṣām anya tvam dṛṣṭam hetu phala saṃbandha avasthānāt vakṣyati hi pratītya yad yad bhavati na hi tāvat tad eva tad  na ca anyat api tad tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam iti atas  para kṛtam api duḥkham na saṃbhavati yadi hi anya tvam syāt  tadā sati anya tve etaiḥ para bhūtaiḥ skandhaiḥ amī para bhūtāḥ kṛtā iti yuktam vaktum syāt  na ca etad evam iti para kṛtam api duḥkham na saṃbhavati atha syāt  na brūmaḥ  yasmāt duḥkhena eva duḥkham kṛtam atas  svayam kṛtam iti kim tarhi sva pudgalena yasmāt svayam eva kṛtam na apareṇa kṛtvā dattam iti atas  svayam kṛtam duḥkham iti brūmaḥ ucyate sva pudgala kṛtam duḥkham yadi duḥkham punar vinā sva pudgalaḥ sa katamaḥ  yena duḥkham svayam kṛtam yad etad manuṣya duḥkham pañca upādāna skandha lakṣaṇam svayam pudgalena kṛtam iti parikalpyate kalpyatām asau pudgalaḥ  yena tad duḥkham svayam kṛtam yadi tāvat yena duḥkhena sva pudgalaḥ prajñapyate tad eva duḥkham tena kṛtam iti sa bhedena kathyatām idam tad duḥkham ayam asya kartā iti atha api manuṣya duḥkha upādānena pudgalena tad eva duḥkham kṛtam syāt  na tarhi sva pudgala kṛtam tad  para pudgala kṛtam eva syāt  atha upādāna bhede api pudgala abheda iṣyate etad ca na asti upādāna vyatiriktasya bhinnasya pudgalasya darśayitum aśakyatvāt  evam tāvat  sva pudgala kṛtam duḥkham na bhavati atra āha ka evam āha sva pudgala kṛtam duḥkham iti kim tarhi para pudgala jam duḥkham anya eva deva duḥkhāt manuṣya pudgalaḥ manuṣya pudgalaḥ ca deva duḥkham kṛtvā yasmāt deva pudgalāya dadāti tena ca deva duḥkhena devapudgalaḥ prajñapyate tasmāt tasya pudgalasya tad duḥkham para pudgala jam eva bhavati ucyate para pudgala jam duḥkham yadi yasmai pradīyate pareṇa kṛtvā tad duḥkham sa duḥkhena vinā kutas  yadi deva duḥkham manuṣya pudgala kṛtam tena ca manuṣya pudgalena tad duḥkham kṛtvā parasmai deva pudgalāya pradīyata iti sa deva pudgalaḥ  deva duḥkha vinirmuktaḥ kutaḥ yasmai pradīyeta iti evam tāvat apara pudgala jasya duḥkhasya pratigrāhaka eva na asti idānīm yaḥ ca dadāti asau  api na asti iti āha para pudgala jam duḥkham yadi kaḥ parapudgalaḥ vinā duḥkhena yaḥ kṛtvā parasmai prahiṇoti tad  yena upādānena sa manuṣya pudgalaḥ prajñapyate sa manuṣya upādāna vyatiriktaḥ katamaḥ  yaḥ  deva pudgalāya deva duḥkham kṛtvā praheṣyati tasmāt para pudgala jam api duḥkham na saṃbhavati tatas ca svayaṃkṛtasya aprasiddheḥ duḥkham para kṛtam kṛtaḥ paraḥ  hi duḥkham yad kuryāt tad tasya syāt svayam kṛtam yadi deva pudgala duḥkham manuṣya pudgalena kṛta tvāt para kṛtam bhavati nanu manuṣya pudgalasya svayaṃkṛtam eva tad bhavati etad ca na asti iti uktam tatas  svayaṃkṛtasya aprasiddheḥ yadā manuṣya pudgalena svayam tad duḥkham na kṛtam tadā kutas  para pudgalasya deva ākhyasya tad duḥkham para kṛtam bhaviṣyati iti atas  api para kṛtam duḥkham na saṃbhavati idānīm prakaraṇa antareṇa api pakṣa dvaya asaṃbhavam pratipādayan  āha na tāvat sva kṛtam duḥkham na hi tena eva tad kṛtam paraḥ  na ātma kṛtaḥ ced syāt duḥkham para kṛtam katham itas ca sva parābhyām duḥkhasya karaṇam na yujyate yasmāt na tāvat sva kṛtam duḥkham kim kāraṇam yasmāt na tena eva hi tad  kṛtam sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt  atas  sva kṛtam na asti na para kṛtam api yasmāt yaḥ  asau paraḥ karoti iti parikalpyate sa eva tāvat na ātmanā kṛtaḥ  na ātmanā niṣpannaḥ tasya api hetu antara apekṣaṇāt  yaḥ ca sva ātmanā na niṣpannaḥ sa katham avidyamāna svabhāvaḥ san param kariṣyati iti na yuktam etad  idānīm ubhaya kṛtam api duḥkham asat iti āha syāt ubhābhyām kṛtam duḥkham syāt ekaika kṛtam yadi yadi hi ekaikena duḥkhasya karaṇam syāt  syāt tadānīm ubhābhyām kṛtam duḥkham na ca ekaika kṛtam tad  ukta doṣāt  na ca ekaikena prāṇa atipāte kṛte dvābhyām kṛta iti vyapadeśaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ idānīm nirhetukam api duḥkham yathā na asti tathā pratipadayan  āha para ākāra asvayaṃkāram duḥkham ahetukam kutas  pareṇa akāraḥ  akaraṇam yasya iti para ākāram na svayaṃkāraḥ  asya iti asvayaṃkāram yadi duḥkham svayaṃkṛtam na asti para kṛtam api na asti yathā uktena nyāyena tad idānīm kuta eva nirhetukam bhaviṣyati khapuṣpa saugandhyavat  duḥkha abhāvāt kutas tasya āśraya bhūta ātmā yathā ca caturdhā vicāryamāṇam duḥkham asat  evam bāhyā api bīja aṅkura ghaṭa paṭādayaḥ  bhāvā veditavyāḥ iti pratipādayan  āha na kevalam hi duḥkhasya cāturvidhyam na vidyate sarveṣām bāhyānām api bhāvānām cāturvidhyam na vidyate pūrvavat sarva samam yojyam yadi khalu eṣām duḥkha ādīnām cāturvidhyā asaṃbhavaḥ tad katamena tarhi idānīm prakāreṇa eṣām siddhiḥ iti ucyate svabhāvataḥ  yadi etāni duḥkha ādīni syuḥ niyatam eṣām caturṇām prakārāṇām anyatamena prakāreṇa siddhiḥ syāt  na tu asti tasmāt svabhāvataḥ  na santi duḥkha ādīni iti avasīyate atha viparyāsa mātra labdha ātma sattākāyāḥ  duḥkha ādi saṃvṛteḥ pratītyasamutpāda vyavasthā mṛgyate tadā karma kāraka parīkṣā prakaraṇa vihita vidhinā yathā udita pakṣa catuṣṭaya tiraskāreṇa idaṃpratyaya tā mātra artha pratītyasamutpāda siddhayā siddhiḥ abhyupeyā yathā uktam svayaṃkṛtam para kṛtam dvābhyām kṛtam ahetukam tārkikaiḥ iṣyate duḥkham tvayā tu uktam pratītyajam iti uktam ca bhagavatā ārya upāli pṛcchāyām tathā saṃvṛti bhāṣitu dharma jinena saṃskṛta asaṃskṛta paśyatha eva na astiha bhūtatu ātma naraḥ  vā ettaku lakṣaṇa sarva jagasya kṛṣṇa śubham ca na naśyati karma ātmana kṛtva ca vedayitavyam naḥ api tu saṃkrama karma phalasya naḥ ca ahetuka pratyanubhoti sarvi bhavā alikā vasikāḥ ca riktaka tucchaka phena samāḥ ca māya marīci samā sada śūnyā deśituḥ saṃvṛtu te ca viviktāḥ śaila guhā giri durga nadīṣu yad va pratiśruka jāyi pratītya evimu saṃskṛta sarvi vijāna māya marīci samam jagu sarvam ityādi iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau duḥkha parīkṣā nāma dvādaśamam prakaraṇam saṃskāra parīkṣā trayodaśamam prakaraṇam yatas ca evam samanantara atikrānta prakaraṇa vidhinā sva para ubhaya kṛta tvam ahetu samutpana tvam ca nirūpyamāṇam bhāvānām asat anyaḥ ca utpādakaḥ  vidhiḥ asan utpanna rūpa tvena ca ete bhāvā avidyā timira upahatam ati nayanānām bāla pṛthagjanānām khyānti tasmāt niḥsvabhāvā eva santaḥ  bālānām visaṃvādakā māyā kari tu raga ādivat  tad anabhijñānām na tu vijñānām ata eva sarva dharma svābhāva avyāparokṣadhī nayanaḥ samunmūlita aśeṣa avidyā vāsanaḥ catur viparyāsa viparyastā trāṇa sattva paritrāṇāya aviparītanaiḥ svābhāvya upadeśa tad paraḥ  buddhaḥ  jagat vibodha kaḥ  mahākāruṇikaḥ tad mṛṣā moṣa dharma yad bhagavān iti abhāṣata sarve ca moṣa dharmāṇaḥ saṃskārāḥ tena te mṛṣā sūtre uktam tad mṛṣā moṣa dharma yad idam saṃskṛtam etad hi khalu bhikṣavaḥ paramam satyam yad idamamoṣa dharma nirvāṇam sarva saṃskārāḥ ca mṛṣā moṣa dharmāṇaḥ iti tathā na asti atra tathatā avitatha tā vā moṣa dharmakam api etad pralopa dharmakam api etad iti tad anena nyāyena yad moṣa dharma tad mṛṣā iti evam yasmāt uktavān  tathāgataḥ  bhagavān sarve ca moṣa dharmāṇaḥ saṃskārāḥ tasmāt moṣa dharmaka tvena te saṃskārā mṛṣā bhavanti citrakarayantra dārikāvat  lakṣaṇa upeta yantra maya vāraṇa vañcita udayanavat sarājavat tatra visaṃvādakam moṣa dharmakam vitatha khyātyā alāta cakravat  atas  niḥsvabhāva tvena mṛṣā sarva saṃskārāḥ moṣa dharmaka tvāt  marīcikā ādi jalavat  yad tu satyam na tad moṣa dharmakam tad yathā nirvāṇam ekam tatas ca vihitayā upapattyā asmāt ca āgamāt  siddham sarva bhāvānām naiḥsvābhāvyam śūnyāḥ sarva dharmā niḥsvabhāva yogena iti ca prajñāpāramitā ardha śatikā pāṭhāt  atra āha yadi evam moṣa dharmaka tvena sarva saṃskārāṇām mṛṣā tvam pratipāditam bhavatā nanu evam sati na santi sarve bhāvā iti sarva padārtha apavādinī mithyā dṛṣṭiḥ eva syāt  ucyate satyam moṣa dharmakāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ ye adya api bhavantam muṣṇanti nanu ca bhoḥ tad mṛṣā moṣa dharma yad yadi kim tatra muṣyate yadā asmābhiḥ tad mṛṣā moṣa dharmakam iti uktam tadā kim tatra muṣyate kim tatra abhāvaḥ  bhavati kaścid yadi padārthaḥ  abhaviṣyat  syāt tasya apavādāt abhāva darśanāt mithyādṛṣṭiḥ yadā tu padārtham eva kaṃcid na paśyāmaḥ tadā kim tatra muṣyate na eva kiṃcid abhāvaḥ  bhavati iti ayuktaḥ  ayam upālambhaḥ  bhavataḥ atra āha yadi abhāva darśanam api na pratipādyate kim punar anena āgamena pratipādyata iti ucyate etad tu uktam bhagavatā śūnyatā paridīpakam yad etad uktam bhagavatā tad na bhāvānām abhāva paridīpakam kim tarhi śūnyatā paridīpakam svabhāva anutpāda paridīpakam iti arthaḥ yathā uktam anavatapta hradāpa saṃkramaṇa sūtre yaḥ pratyayaiḥ jāyati sa hi ajātaḥ  naḥ tasya utpādu sabhāvataḥ  asti yaḥ pratyaya adhīnu sa śūnya uktaḥ  yaḥ śūnyatām jānati saḥ  apramattaḥ iti atra āha na ayam āgamaḥ  bhāva svabhāva anutpādam paridīpayati kim tarhi niḥsvabhāva tvam svabhāvasya anavasthāyi tvam vināśi tvam iti kuta etad iti ced  bhāvānām niḥsvabhāva tvam anyathā bhāva darśanāt vicāryamāṇānām anyathātvam vipariṇāma darśanāt  iti arthaḥ etad uktam bhavati yadi bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ  na syāt  tadānīm na eva eṣām anyathātvam upalabhyeta upalabhyate ca pariṇāmaḥ tasmāt svabhāvān ava sthāyi tvam eva sūtra artha iti vijñeyam itas ca etad evam yasmāt  asvabhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ na asti bhāvānām śūnyatā yatas  yaḥ  hi asvabhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ sa na asti bhāvānām ca śūnyatā dharma iṣyate na ca asati dharmiṇi tad āśritaḥ  dharma upapadyate na hi asati vandhyā tanaye tad śayām ata upapadyata iti tasmāt asti eva bhāvānām svabhāva iti api ca kasya syāt anyathā bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ ced na vidyate yadi bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ  na syāt  yaḥ  ayam vipariṇāma lakṣaṇaḥ anyathā bhāvaḥ sa kasya syāt iti atra ucyate evam api parikalpyamāne kasya syāt anyathā bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ  yadi vidyate iha yaḥ  dharmaḥ  yam padārtham na vyabhicarati sa tasya svabhāva iti vyapadiśyate apara pratibaddha tvāt  agneḥ auṣṇyam hi loke tad avyabhicāri tvāt svabhāva iti ucyate tad eva auṣṇyam apsu upalabhyamānam para pratyaya saṃbhūta tvāt kṛtrima tvāt na svabhāva iti yadā ca evam avyabhicāriṇā svabhāvena bhavitavyam tadā asya avyabhicāri tvāt anyathā bhāvaḥ syāt abhāvaḥ na hi agniḥ śaityam pratipadyate evam bhāvānām sati svabhāva abhyupagame anyathātvam eva na saṃbhavet  upalabhyate ca eṣām anyathātvam atas  na asti svabhāvaḥ api ca ayam anyathā abhāva u bhāvānām na eva saṃbhavati yad darśanāt sa svabhāva tā syāt  yathā ca na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha tasya eva na anyathā abhāvaḥ  na api anyasya eva yujyate yuvā na jīryate yasmāt yasmāt jīrṇaḥ  na jīryate tasya eva tāvat  prāgvat  prāk avasthāyām vartamānasya bhāvasya anyathātvam na upapadyate tathā hi yūnaḥ  yuvā avasthāyām eva vartamānasya na asti anyathātvam atha api avasthā antara prāptasya eva anyathātvam parikalpyate tad api na upapadyate anyathātvam nāma jarāyāḥ paryāyaḥ tad yadi yūnaḥ  na iṣyate anyasya eva jīrṇasya bhavati iti tad api na yujyate yasmāt na hi jīrṇasya punar jarayā saṃbandhaḥ niṣprayojana tvāt  kim hi jīrṇasya punar jarayā saṃbandhaḥ kuryāt  tad āgamana antareṇa jīrṇa tā bhāvāt jīrṇaḥ  jīryata iti na yujyate atha yūna eva anyathā bhāvaḥ tad ayuktam aprāpta jarā avasthasya yuvā iti vyapadeśāt  avasthā dvayasya ca paraspara viruddha tvāt api ca tasya ced an yathā bhāvaḥ kṣīram eva bhavet dadhi atha syāt  kṣīra avasthā parityāgena dadhi avasthā bhavati atas  na kṣīram eva dadhi bhavati iti ucyate yadi kṣīram dadhi bhavati iti na iṣyate paraspara virodhāt  kṣīrāt anyasya kasya atha dadhibhāvaḥ  bhaviṣyati kim udakasya dadhibhāvaḥ  bhavatu tasmāt asaṃbaddham eva tad anyasya dadhibhāvaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti tad evam anyathātva asaṃbhavāt  kutas tad darśanāt  sa svabhāva tā bhāvānām prasetsyati iti na yuktam etad  yathā uktam ārya ratnākara mahāyāna sūtre yaḥ  na pi jāyati naḥ cupapadyī naḥ cyavate na pi jīryati dharmaḥ tam jinu darśayatī narasiṃha tatra nideśayi sattva mahā ṛṣī yasya svabhāva na vidyati kaści naḥ apara bhāvatu kenaci labdhaḥ na antarataḥ na pi bāhiratas  vā labhyati tatra niveśayi nāthaḥ śānta gatī kathitā sugatena naḥ ca gatī upapadyati kāci tatra ca vyoharasī gati muktaḥ  mukta ku mocayasī bahu sattvān sarvi vadesi nirātmaka dharmān sattvatu grāhatu mocasi lokam mukta svayam gatitaḥ  gati muktaḥ  tenasi pāragataḥ  na ca tīrṇaḥ pāragataḥ  asi bhava arṇava tīrṇaḥ pāragataḥ  na ca labhyati kaści pāru na vidyati na api apāru pāragataḥ  asmi vadesi ca vākyam vāca na vidyati yām ca vadesi yam pi vadesi na vidyati tam pi yasya vadesi na vidyati saḥ  api yaḥ  api vijānati saḥ  api asantaḥ  tatra praṇaṣṭu jagam imu sarvam vitatha vikalpa niveśa vaśena śānta vijānati yaḥ  naru dharmām stehi tathā agatu dṛṣṭa svayaṃbhūḥ śānta prajānati dharma praṇītān prīti sa vindati toṣati sattvān saḥ  bhavatī jinu jitvena kleśān ātma tena vijānita bodhi jinānām buddhiya bodhayate sa jagam pi ityādi yad ca uktam asvabhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ na eva asti śūnyatā ca bhāvānām iṣyate tasmāt asti śūnyatāa śrayaḥ  bhāva svabhāva iti etad api na yujyate iti āha yadi aśūnyam bhavet kiṃcid syāt śūnyam iti kiṃcana na kiṃcid asti aśūnyam ca kutas  śūnyam bhaviṣyati yadi śūnyatā nāma kācid  syāt  tadā tad āśrayaḥ  bhāva svabhāvaḥ syāt  na tu evam iha hi śūnyatā nāma iti sarva dharmāṇām sāmānya lakṣaṇam iti abhyupagamāt aśūnya dharma abhāvāt aśūnyata eva na asti yadā ca aśūnyāḥ padārthā na santi aśūnyatā ca na asti tadā pratipakṣa nirapekṣa tvāt śūnya tā api kha puṣpa mālāvat na asti iti avasīyatām yadā ca śūnyatā na asti tadā atad āśrayā api padārthā na santi iti sthitam avikalam atra āha trīṇi vimokṣa mukhāni śūnyatā nimitta apraṇihita ākhyāni vimuktaye vineyebhyaḥ  bhagavatā nirdiṣṭāni sarva tīrthika samayāsādhāraṇāni saugata eva pravacane samupalabhyante yeṣām upadeśa artham eva buddhā bhagavantaḥ  aśeṣa tīrthya vāda mahā moha andhakāra anugata jagati jagat eka pradīpā nairātmya upadeśa avicchinna śikhā utpadyante sa bhavān  tathāgata pravacana vyākhyāna vyājena idānīm tām eva śūnyatām pratikṣeptum ārabdhavān iti alam bhavatā svarga apavarga mārga samucchedakena iti ucyate ahaḥ vata bhavān ati unmukha iva atyanta viparyāsāt nirvāṇa pura gāminam śivam ṛjum paramam panthānam avadhūya bhāva abhiniveśavyā kulitam saṃsāra kāntāra anugam eva mārgam mokṣa pura gāmi tvena samāśritaḥ  nirmumukṣuḥ san saṃsāra aṭavī kāntāraḥ sadbhiḥ upālabhya eva san abhimāna abhiniveśa graha pavaraśatayā tān eva upālabhate nanu bhoḥ niravaśeṣa kleśa vyādhi cikitsakaiḥ mahā vaidya rājaiḥ śūnyatā sarva dṛṣṭīnām proktā niḥsaraṇam jinaiḥ yeṣām tu śūnyatā dṛṣṭiḥ tān asādhyān babhāṣire iha sarveṣām eva dṛṣṭi kṛtānām sarva graha abhiniveśānām yaniḥsaraṇam apravṛttiḥ sā śūnyatā na ca dṛṣṭi kṛtānām nivṛtti mātram bhāvaḥ ye tu tasyām api śūnyatāyām bhāva abhiniveśinaḥ tān prati avācakā vayam iti kutaḥ asmad upadeśāt sakala kalpanā vyāvṛttyā mokṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati yaḥ na kiṃcid api te paṇyam dāsyāmi iti uktaḥ sa ced  adehi bhoḥ tad eva mahyam nakiṃcid nāma paṇyam  iti brūyāt  sa kena upāyena śakyaḥ paṇya abhāvam grāhayitum evam yeṣām śūnyatāyām api bhāva abhiniveśaḥ kena idānīm sa teṣām tasyām bhāva abhiniveśaḥ  niṣidhyatām iti atas  mahā bhaiṣajye api doṣa saṃjñi tvāt  parama cikitsakaiḥ mahā vaidyaiḥ tathāgataiḥ pratyākhyātā eva te yathā uktam bhagavatā ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre yad na śūnyatayā dharmān śūnyān karoti api tu dharmā eva śūnyāḥ yad na animittena dharmān animittān karoti api tu dharmā eva animittāḥ yad na apraṇihitena dharmān apraṇihitān karoti api tu dharmā eva apraṇihitāḥ yā evam pratyavekṣā iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā pratipad dharmāṇām bhūta pratyavekṣā ye hi kāśyapa śūnyatā upalambhena śūnyatām pratisaranti tān aham naṣṭa praṇaṣṭān iti vadāmi iti pravacanāt  tathā varam khalu kāśyapa sumeru mātrā pudgala dṛṣṭiḥ āśritā na tu eva abhāva abhiniveśikasya śūnyatā dṛṣṭiḥ tad kasya hetoḥ sarva dṛṣṭi kṛtānām hi kāśyapa śūnyatā niḥsaraṇam yasya khalu punar  śūnyatā eva dṛṣṭiḥ tam aham acikitsyam iti vadāmi tad yathā kāśyapa glānaḥ puruṣaḥ syāt  tasmai vaidyaḥ  bhaiṣajyam dadyāt  tasya tad bhaiṣajyam sarva doṣān uccārya svayam koṣṭha gatam na niḥsaret  tad kim manyase kāśyapa api tu sa puruṣaḥ tatas  glānyāt muktaḥ  bhavet  naḥ hi idam bhagavan gāḍhataram tasya puruṣasya glānyam bhavet  yasya tad bhaiṣajyam sarva doṣān uccārya koṣṭha gatam na niḥsaret  bhagavān āha evam eva kāśyapa sarva dṛṣṭi kṛtānām śūnyatā niḥsaraṇam yasya khalu punar  śūnyatā eva dṛṣṭiḥ tam aham acikitsyam iti vadāmi iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau saṃskāra parīkṣā nāma trayodaśamam prakaraṇam saṃsarga parīkṣā caturdaśamam prakaraṇam atra āha asti eva bhāva svabhāvaḥ tad saṃsarga upadeśāt iha yad na asti na tasya saṃsargaḥ tad yathā vandhyā suta duhitroḥ asti ca saṃskārāṇām saṃsarga upadeśaḥ cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpāṇi ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam trayāṇām saṃnipātaḥ sparśaḥ sparśa sahajā vedanā iti vistaraḥ tathā saṃjñā ca vedanā ca saṃsṛṣṭau  etau dharmau na asaṃsṛṣṭau  iti saṃskārāṇām saṃsarga upadeśaḥ tad evam saṃsarga upadeśāt vidyata eva bhāva svabhāva iti ucyate syāt etad evam yadi saṃsarga eva bhavataḥ  bhavet  na tu asti yasmāt  draṣṭavyam darśanam draṣṭā trīṇi etāni dviśaḥ dviśas  sarvaśas ca na saṃsargam anyonyena brajanti uta tatra draṣṭavyam rūpam darśanam cakṣuḥ draṣṭā vijñānam eṣām trayāṇām dviśaḥ dviśas  saṃsargaḥ  na asti cakṣuṣaḥ  rūpasya ca cakṣuṣaḥ  vijñānasya ca vijñānasya rūpasya ca saṃsargaḥ  na asti iti evam dviśaḥ dviśas  saṃsargaḥ  na bhavati sarvaśas  api trayāṇām api eṣām yugapad ca saṃsargaḥ  na asti yathā ca draṣṭavya darśana draṣṭaṇām dviśaḥ dviśas  sarvaśas ca saṃsarga abhāvaḥ evam rāgaḥ ca raktaḥ ca rañjanīyam ca dṛśyatām rāgasya raktasya ca saṃsargaḥ  na asti rāgasya rañjanīyasya ca trayāṇām api yugapad saṃsargaḥ  na asti yathā ca eṣām evam traidhena śeṣāḥ kleśāḥ ca śeṣāṇi āyatanāni ca anyonyena saṃsargam na vrajanti trayaḥ prakārāḥ tridhā tridhā bhāvaḥ traidham tena traidhena śeṣāḥ kleśā dveṣa moha ādayaḥ te ete dveṣa dviṣṭa dveṣaṇīya ādinā traidhena śrotra śrotṛ śrota vyādinā ca kasmāt punar eteṣām saṃsargaḥ  na asti iti āha anyena anyasya saṃsargaḥ tad ca anya tvaṃna vidyate draṣṭavya prabhṛtīnām yad na saṃsargam vrajanti atas  yad iti ayam yasmāt arthe yadi draṣṭavī ādīnām parasparam anya tvam syāt  tadā kṣīrodakayoḥ iva anyena anyasya saṃsargaḥ syāt  tad ca anya tvam yasmāt eṣām draṣṭavya prabhṛtīnām na saṃbhavati atas  na ete saṃsarga brajanti api ca na ca kevalam anya tvam draṣṭavī ādeḥ na vidyate kasyacid kenacid sārdham na anya tvam upapadyate na ca kevalam kārya kāraṇa bhāva sthitānām draṣṭavī ādīnām anya tvam na saṃbhavati ghaṭa paṭa ādīnām api padārthānām sarveṣām na eva saṃbhavati iti avasīyatām yathā ca eṣām draṣṭavya prabhṛtīnām parasparataḥ  anya tvam asat  tathā pratipādayan  āha anyat anyat pratītya anyat na anyat anyat ṛte anyatas  yad pratītya ca yad tasmāt tad anyat na upapadyate iha yad etad  ghaṭa ākhyam vastu paṭāt anyat iti vyapadiśyate tad etad anyat anyat pratītya anyat bhavati anya vastunaḥ ṛte ṛte anyatas  vinā anyat  anyat anyat na bhavati yad ca paṭa ākhyam vastu anyat  ghaṭa ākhyam vastu pratītya anyat bhavati tasmāt paṭa ākhyāt vastunaḥ tad  ghaṭa ākhyam vastu na anyat bhavati iti avasīyatām yasmāt  yad pratītya yad bhavati tasmāt tad anyat na bhavati sa apekṣa tvāt  bīja aṅkuravat  hrasva dīrghavat ca iti tathā ca vakṣyati pratītya yad yad bhavati na hi tāvat tad eva tad  na ca anyat api tad tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatat  iti atra āha yadi ghaṭāt anyaḥ paṭaḥ syāt  tam ca pṛthak bhūtam paṭam apekṣya anyaḥ  ghaṭaḥ syāt  tadā kaḥ  doṣa iti ucyate yadi anyat anyat anyasmāt anyasmāt api ṛte bhavet  tad anyat anyat anyasmāt ṛte na asti ca na asti atas  ekaḥ  atra anya śabda upadarśane aparaḥ ca artha antara parāmarśī anyaḥ ca prasiddha uccāraṇam iti anya śabda traya upādānam yadi hi etad  ghaṭa ākhyam vastu paṭāt anyasmāt anyat  syāt  tad  ghaṭa ākhyam vastu anyasmāt api paṭa ākhyāt ṛte anyat bhavet  tadā ca paṭa nirapekṣasya eva ekaikasya ghaṭasya anya tvam bhavet  yad hi yasmāt anyat  tad tena vinā api siddhayati tad yathā sa eva ghaṭaḥ  na sva rūpa niṣpattau  anyam paṭam apekṣate evam anya tvam api yadi ghaṭasya anyasmāt paṭāt ṛte bhavet  tadānīm paṭa nirapekṣasya ghaṭasya para tvam syāt  na tu ekaikasya paṭa nirapekṣasya ghaṭasya anya tvam dṛṣṭam tasmāt anyat bhavati iti bruvatā yad apekṣya yad anyat  tatas tad anyat na bhavati iti sphuṭam abhyupetam bhavati atra āha yadi khalu anya tvam evam kutaścid kasyacid na asti nanu idam api tadā na saṃbhavati vaktum yasmāt anyat pratītya anyat anyat bhavati iti tasmāt eva tad anyat anyat na bhavati iti ucyate yata eva hi paraspara āpekṣikī bhāvānām anyatva siddhiḥ ata eva anyat iti ucyate laukike vyavahāre sthitvā vastutas tu parīkṣyamāṇam anya tvam na saṃbhavati iti brūmaḥ yadi tarhi evam api avidyamāne api anya tve loka saṃvṛtyā paṭāt anyaḥ  ghaṭa iti vyapadiśyate atha kasmāt  bīja aṅkurayoḥ api evam anya tvam na vyapadiśyate ucyate na eva hi lokaḥ  ghaṭa paṭayoḥ iva bīja aṅkurayoḥ anya tvam pratipadyate ghaṭa paṭayoḥ iva janya janakatva abhāva prasaṅgāt  yaugapadya bhāva prasaṅgāt  api ca yasmāt bīja mātram u tvā bīja kāryam vṛkṣam upadarśayati pumān loke ayam vṛkṣaḥ  mayā upta iti tasmāt loke api kārya kāraṇa bhūtānām na asti eva paratvam iti vyavasthāpyate atra āha yadi padārtha antare padārtha antara sāpekṣā para buddhiḥ syāt  syāt eṣa doṣaḥ tasmāt tad anyat na bhavati iti na tu evam brūmaḥ kim tarhi iha anya tvam nāma sāmānya viśeṣaḥ  asti tad yatra samavetam sa padārthaḥ padārtha antara nirapekṣayā api para iti ucyate tasmāt ukta doṣa anavasaraḥ  asmad pakṣe iti ucyate syāt etad evam yadi anya tvam eva syāt  na tu asti iha idam anya tvam kalpyamānam anyasmin vā kalpyeta ananyasmin vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyata iti pratipādayan  āha na anyasmin vidyate anya tvam ananyasmin  vidyate tatra anyasmin  anya tvam asti iti kalpyate kim tadānīm anyatva parikalpanayā anya vyapadeśa siddhayartham hi bhavatā anya tvam parikalpyate sa ca anya vyapadeśaḥ  vinā api anya tvena siddha eva yasmāt labdha ani avyapadeśa eva padārthe anyasmin anya tvam kalpyate iti evam tāvat anyasmin  anya tvam na saṃbhavati idānīm ananyasmin  api anya tvam na asti yasmāt ananya ucyate ekaḥ tatra ca anyatva viruddham eka tvam asti iti yatas  virodhāt ananyasmin  api anya tvam na saṃbhavati yad ca idānīm na anyasmin  ananyasmin vidyate tadvayatiriktasya padārtha antarasya asaṃbhavāt  etad vayatirikte api padārthe na saṃbhavati tatra eva asti yadā ca evam anya tvam eva na asti tadā anyatva samavāya nibandhanaḥ anya buddhi dhvani pravṛtti hetuḥ anyaḥ  api padārthaḥ  na asti iti siddham atra āha yadi api anya tvam na asti tathā api anyaḥ tāvat asti na ca asati anya tve anyaḥ  bhavitum arhati atas  anya tvam bhaviṣyati iti ucyate avidyamāne ca anya tve na asti anyat vā tad eva vā yadā anya tvam eva na asti iti prāk  pratipāditam tadā kutas  asati anya tve anyat vā tad eva vā bhaviṣyati tad eva iti ananya tvam iti arthaḥ tasmāt na asti anyat vā tad eva vā atra āha vidyanta eva darśana ādayaḥ saṃsarga sadbhāvāt iha darśana ādīnām yadi api anya tvam na asti iti pratipāditam tathā api trayāṇām saṃnipātaḥ saṃgatiḥ sparśa iti saṃsargaḥ  asti tatas ca saṃsarga sadbhāvāt  vidyanta eva darśana ādaya iti ucyate syuḥ evam yadi teṣām saṃsarga eva syāt  na tu asti yathā ca na asti tathā pratipādayan  āha na tena tasya saṃsargaḥ  na anyena anyasya yujyate iha yadi darśana ādīnām saṃsargaḥ syāt  sa eka tvena vā parikalpyeta anya tvena vā tatra ekatve na asti saṃsargaḥ na hi ekakam kṣīram udaka nirapekṣam udakena saṃsṛjyata iti ucyate pṛthaktve api saṃsargaḥ  na asti na hi udakāt pṛthak avasthitam kṣīram udakena saṃsṛjyata iti kathyate evam darśana ādīnām yadi ekatve sati saṃsargaḥ parikalpyate saḥ  anupapannaḥ ekakasya api cakṣuṣaḥ saṃsṛṣṭi prasaṅgāt  atha pṛthaktvam evam api anupapannaḥ ekakasya api cakṣuṣaḥ  rūpa ādibhyaḥ pṛthak bhūtasya saṃsṛṣṭi prasaṅgāt  asati saṃsarge na asti darśana ādikam iti siddham atra āha yadi api saṃsargaḥ  na asti tathā api saṃsṛjyamānam saṃsṛṣṭam saṃsraṣṭā ca asti tad apratiṣedhāt na ca saṃsargam antareṇa saṃsṛjyamānam saṃsṛṣṭam saṃsraṣṭā ca saṃbhavati tasmāt saṃsargaḥ  api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate etad api na yuktam yasmāt yadā saṃsarga eva na asti iti pratipāditam asati ca saṃsarge tadā kutas  saṃsṛjyamāna ādikam tatra vartamāna saṃsarga kriyā sādhana karma bhūtam saṃsṛjyamānam saṃsṛṣṭam niṣpanna saṃsarga kriyam saṃsraṣṭā kartā kriyā niṣpattau svātantryeṇa avasthitaḥ tad atra saṃsarga abhāvāt eva saṃsṛjyamāna ādikam apaśyan  tad pratiṣedham nigamayan  āha saṃsṛjyamānam saṃsṛṣṭaṃsaṃsraṣṭā ca na vidyate iti yathā uktam bhagavatā [upāli paripṛcchāyām] sarva sa yogi tu paśyati cakṣuḥ tatra na paśyati pratyaya hīnam [na eva ca] cakṣu papaśyati [rūpaṃ] tena sa yoga viyoga vikalpaḥ āloka samāśrita paśyati cakṣu rūpa manorama citra vicitram yena ca yoga samāśrita cakṣuḥ tena na paśyati cakṣu kadāci te parinirvṛta laukika śūrā yehi svabhāvata jñātibhi dharmāḥ kāma guṇaiḥ hi caranti asaṅgāḥ saṅga vivarjiya sattva vinenti naḥ pi ca sattva na jīviha kaści sattva hitam ca karonti jinendrāḥ sattvu na asti karonti ca artham saṅgu na vidyati atra kadāci tasya na vidyati vedana loke tathā bhāvitu mārga pavartitu jñāna śūnyaka dharma nirātmaka sarvi yena vibhāvita bhontim i dharmāḥ tasya bhavet pratibhānam anantam iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau saṃsarga parīkṣā nāma caturdaśamam prakaraṇam svabhāva parīkṣā pañcadaśamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyata eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ tad niṣpādaka hetu pratyaya upādānāt  iha yad na asti na tasya niṣpādaka hetu pratyaya upādānam asti yathā khapuṣpasya upādīyante ca bīja avidyādayaḥ  hetu pratyayā aṅkara saṃskāra ādīnām niṣpādakāḥ iti atas  vidyata eva bhāva svabhāva iti ucyate yadi bhāvānām saṃskāra aṅkura ādīnām svabhāvaḥ  asti kim idānīm vidyamānānām hetu pratyayaiḥ prayojanam yathā vartamānībhūtānām saṃskāra aṅkura ādīnām bhūyas niṣpattaye avidyā bīja ādīnām upādānam kriyate evam anyat api tad utpattaye na kartavyam syāt  tad svabhāvasya vidyamāna tvāt iti pratipādayan  āha na saṃbhavaḥ svabhāvasya yuktaḥ pratyaya hetubhiḥ atha syāt  na eva utpādāt pūrvam kasyacid bhāvasya svabhāvaḥ  asti yatas  asya vidyamāna tvāt utpatti vaiyarthyam syāt  kim tarhi utpādāt pūrvam avidyamānasya eva svabhāvasya hetu pratyayān pratītya paścāt utpādaḥ  bhavati iti evam apīḥyamāṇe hetu pratyaya saṃbhūtaḥ svabhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ  bhavet  atha syāt  iṣyata eva hetu pratyaya saṃbhūta tvāt svabhāvasya kṛtaka tvam tasmāt kṛtakasya eva svabhāvasya abhyupagamāt  kṛtakatva prasaṅgaḥ  na asmākam bādhaka iti etad api na yuktam iti āha svabhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ  nāma bhaviṣyati punar  katham kṛtakaḥ ca iti svabhāvaḥ ca iti paraspara viruddha tvāt asaṃgata artham etad  iha hi svar  bhāvaḥ svabhāva iti vyutpatteḥ yaḥ kṛtakaḥ padārthaḥ sa loke na eva svabhāva iti vyapadiśyate tad yathā apāmauṣpyam dhātu piśāca pratyaya niṣpāditaḥ karkeṭana ādīnām padmarāga ādi bhāvaḥ ca yaḥ tu akṛtakaḥ sa svabhāvaḥ tad yathā agneḥ auṣṇyam jātānām padmarāga ādīnām padmarāga ādi svabhāvaḥ ca sa hi teṣām padārtha antara saṃparkā janita tvāt svabhāva iti ucyate tad evam akṛtakaḥ svabhāva iti loka vyavahāre vyavasthite vayam idānīm brūmaḥ yad etad auṣṇyam tad aṣi agneḥ svabhāvaḥ  na bhavati iti gṛhyatām kṛtaka tvāt  iha maṇi indhana āditya samāgama āt araṇi nirdharṣaṇa ādeḥ ca agneḥ hetu pratyaya sāpekṣa tā eva upalabhyate na ca agni vyatiriktam auṣṇyam saṃbhavati tasmāt auṣṇyam api hetu pratyaya janitam tatas ca kṛtakam kṛtaka tvāt ca apām auṣṇyavat  svabhāvaḥ  na eva bhavati iti sphuṭam avasīyate nanu ca gopāla aṅganā jana prasiddham etad  agneḥ auṣṇyam svabhāva iti kim khalu asmābhiḥ uktam na prasiddham iti etad tu vayam brūmaḥ na ayam svabhāvaḥ  bhavitum arhati svabhāva lakṣaṇa viyukta tvāt avidyā viparyāsa anugamāt tu lokaḥ  niḥsvabhāvam eva bhāva jātam sa svabhāva tvena pratipannaḥ yathā hi taimirikāḥ timira pratyayāt asantam eva keśa ādi svabhāvam sa svabhāva tvena abhiniviṣṭāḥ evam avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā bālā niḥsvabhāvam bhāva jātam sa svabhāva tvena abhiniviṣṭā yathā abhiniveśam lakṣaṇam ācakṣate agneḥ auṣṇyam sva lakṣaṇam tatas  anyatra anupalambhāt asādhāraṇa tvena svam eva lakṣaṇam iti kṛtvā bāla jana prasiddhayā eva ca bhagavatā tad eva eṣām sāṃvṛtam svarūpam abhidharme vyavasthāpitam sādhāraṇam tu anityatva ādikam sāmānya lakṣaṇam iti ca uktam yadā tu vigata avidyā timira avadāta prajñā cakṣuṣām darśanam apekṣyate tadā vitimiraiḥ taimirika upalabdha keśa adarśanavat bāla jana mati parikalpita anupalabdha svabhāvaiḥ āryaiḥ pura ucyate para hita vyāpāraiḥ na ayam svabhāvaḥ  bhāvānām iti yathā uktam ārya laṅka avatāra sūtre keśoṇḍukam yathā mithyā gṛhyate taimirikaiḥ janaiḥ tathā bhāva vikalpaḥ  ayam mithyā bālaiḥ vikalpyate na svabhāvaḥ  na vijñaptiḥ na ca vastu na ca ālayaḥ bālaiḥ vikalpitā hi ete śava bhūtaiḥ ku tārkikaiḥ iti tathā svabhāva anutpattim saṃdhāya mahāmate mayā sarva dharmā anutpannā iti uktāḥ iti vistaraḥ atra āha yadi khalu idam agni ādeḥ auṣṇya ādikam hetu pratyaya saṃbhūta tvena kṛtaka tvāt niḥsvabhāvam iti ucyate kim idānīm tad svabhāvasya lakṣaṇam kaḥ ca asau svabhāva iti vaktavyam ucyate akṛtrimaḥ svabhāvaḥ  hi nirapekṣaḥ paratra ca iha svar  bhāvaḥ svabhāva iti yasya padārthasya yad ātmīyam rūpam tad tasya svabhāva iti vyapadiśyate kim ca kasya ātmīyam yadi asya akṛtrimam yad tu kṛtrimam na tad tasya ātmīyam tad yathā apām auṣṇyam yad ca yasya āyat tam tad api tad ātmīyam tad yathā sve bhṛtyāḥ svāni dhanāni yad tu yasya parāyattam na tad tasya ātmīyam tad yathā tāvat kālikā yācitakamasvatantram yatas ca evam kṛtrimasya para sa apekṣasya ca svabhāva tvam na iṣṭam ata eva auṣṇyam agneḥ hetu pratyaya pratibaddha tvāt pūrvaṃm abhūtvā paścāt utpādena kṛtaka tvāt na svabhāva iti yujyate yatas ca etad evam atas  yad eva agneḥ kāla traye api avyabhicāri nijam rūpam akṛtrimam pūrvam abhūtvā paścāt yad na bhavati yad ca hetu pratyaya sāpekṣam na bhavati apāmauṣṇyavat  pārāvāravat  dīrgha hrasvavat vā tad  svabhāva iti vyapadiśyate kim khalu agneḥ tad ittham svarūpam asti na tad asti na ca api na asti svarūpataḥ yadi api evam tathā api śrotṛṇām uttrāsa parivarjana artham saṃvṛtyā samāropya tad asti iti brūmaḥ yathā uktam bhagavatā anakṣarasya dharmasya śrutiḥ kā deśanā ca kā śrūyate deśyate ca api samāropāt anakṣaraḥ iti iha api ca vakṣyati śūnyam iti na vaktavyam aśūnyam iti vā bhavet  ubhayam na ubhayam ca iti prajñapti artham tu kathyate yadi khalu tad adhyāropāt bhavadbhiḥ asti iti ucyate kīdṛśam tad  yā sā dharmāṇām dharmatā nāma sā eva tad svarūpam atha kā iyam dharmāṇām dharmatā dharmāṇām svabhāvaḥ kaḥ  ayam svabhāvaḥ prakṛtiḥ kā ca iyam prakṛtiḥ yā iyam śūnyatā kā iyam śūnyatā naiḥsvābhāvyam kim idam naiḥsvābhāvyam tathatā kā iyam tathatā tathā abhāvaḥ  avikāri tvam sadā eva sthāyitā sarvathā anutpāda eva hi agni ādīnām para nirapekṣa tvāt akṛtrima tvāt svabhāva iti ucyate etad uktam bhavati avidyā timira prabhāva upalabdham bhāva jātam yena ātmanā vigata avidyā timirāṇām āryāṇām adarśana yogena viṣaya tvam upayāti tad eva svarūpam eṣām svabhāva iti vyavasthāpyate tasya ca idam lakṣaṇam akṛtrimaḥ svabhāvaḥ  hi nirapekṣaḥ paratra ca iti vyavasthāpayāṃbabhūvuḥ ācāryā iti vijñeyam sa ca eṣa bhāvānām anutpāda ātmakaḥ svabhāva akiṃcit tvena abhāva mātra tvāt asvabhāva eva iti kṛtvā na asti bhāva svabhāva iti vijñeyam yathā uktam bhagavatā bhāvān abhāvān iti yaḥ prajānati sa sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate yaḥ sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate sa ānimittam spṛśate samādhim iti atra āha yadi api svabhāvaḥ  na asti bhāvānām tathā api para bhāvaḥ tāvat asti tad apratiṣedhāt sati ca para bhāve svabhāvaḥ  api bhaviṣyati svabhāvam antareṇa para bhāva aprasiddheḥ iti ucyate kutas  svabhāvasya abhāve para bhāvaḥ  bhaviṣyati svabhāvaḥ para bhāvasya para bhāvaḥ  hi kathyate iha svabhāva eva hi loke kaścid svabhāva antara apekṣayā para iti vyapadiśyate yadi hi agneḥ auṣṇyam svabhāvaḥ syāt  drava svabhāva salila sāpekṣayā para bhāva iti vyapadiśyeta yadā tu mumukṣubhiḥ vicāryamāṇasya kasyacid svabhāva eva na asti tadā kutas  para tvam syāt  para bhāvāt ca svabhāvaḥ  api na asti iti siddham atra āha yadi api svabhāva para bhāvau na staḥ tathā api bhāvaḥ tāvat asti apratiṣedhāt  sa ca bhāvaḥ bhavan svabhāvaḥ  vā bhavet  para bhāvaḥ  vā tasmāt svabhāva para bhāvau  api bhaviṣyata iti ucyate svabhāva para bhāvābhyām ṛte bhāvaḥ kutas  punar  svabhāve para bhāve vā sati bhāvaḥ hi sidhyati bhāvaḥ hi parikalpyamānaḥ svabhāvaḥ  vā bhavet  para bhāvaḥ  vā tau ca pūrva ukta vidhinā na staḥ iti tayoḥ abhāvāt bhāvaḥ  api na asti iti avadhāryatām atra āha yadi api bhavatā bhāvaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ tathā api abhāvaḥ  asti pratiṣedha abhāvāt tatas ca bhāvaḥ api bhaviṣyati pratidvandvi sadbhāvāt  abhāvavat iti ucyate syāt bhāvaḥ yadi abhāva eva syāt  na tu asti iti āha bhāvasya ced aprasiddhiḥ abhāvaḥ  na eva sidhyati bhāvasya hi anyathābhāvam abhāvam vruvate janāḥ iha hi yadi bhāvaḥ nāma kaścid abhaviṣyat syāt tasyānyathā bhāvāt abhāvaḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ  hi vartamāna avasthāyāḥ pracyutāḥ santaḥ anyathābhāvam āpannāḥ abhāva dhvani vācyā bhavanti loke yadā tu amī ghaṭa ādayaḥ  bhāva rūpa tvena eva asiddhāḥ tadā kutaḥ avidyamāna svabhāvānām anyathātvam iti atas  abhāvaḥ  api na asti tad evam sarvathā svabhāva para bhāva bhāva abhāveṣu anupapadyamāneṣu avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā viparītam svabhāvam para bhāvam ca bhāvam ca abhāvam eva ca ye paśyanti na paśyanti te tattvam buddha śāsane ye hi tathāgata pravacanā viparīta vyākhyāna abhimānitayā pṛthivyāḥ kāṭhinyam svabhāvaḥ vedanāyāḥ  viṣaya anubhavaḥ vijñānasya viṣaya prativijñaptiḥ svabhāvaḥ iti evam svabhāvam bhāvānām varṇayanti anyat vijñānam anyat rūpam anyā eva ca vedanā iti evam para bhāvam varṇayanti vartamāna avastham ca vijñāna ādikam bhāva tvena ye varṇayanti vijñāna ādikam eva ca atīta tām āpannam abhāva iti na te parama gambhīrasya pratītyasamutpādasya tattvam varṇayanti yasmāt yathā udita upapatti viruddham svabhāva para bhāva ādīnām astitvam na ca upapatti viruddham padārtha svabhāvam anuvarṇayanti tathāgatāḥ svayam aviparīta aśeṣa padārtha tattva saṃbodhāt  ata eva buddhānām eva bhagavatām vacanam pramāṇam iti upavarṇayanti vicakṣaṇāḥ sa upapattika tvena avisaṃvādaka tvāt  ata eva ca āptebhyaḥ prahīṇa aśeṣa doṣebhya āgata tvāt  āgamayati iti samantāt  tattvam gamayati iti vā āmi mukhyāt gamanāt vā tad āśrayeṇa lokasya nirvāṇa gamanāt  saṃbuddha vacanasya eva āgama tvam vyavasthāpyate tad anya matānām tu upapatti viyukta tvāt na prāmāṇyam āgama ābhāsa tvam ca vyavasthāpyate yasmāt ca etāni svabhāva para bhāva bhāva abhāva darśanāni yukti vidhura tvāt na tattvāni ata eva mumukṣūṇām vineya janānām kātyāyana avavāde ca asti iti na asti iti ca ubhayam pratiṣiddham bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvinā uktam hi bhagavatā ārya kātyāyana avavāda sūtre yad bhūyasā kātyāyana ayam lokaḥ  astitān vā abhiniviṣṭaḥ  na astitām ca tena na parimucyate jāti jarā vyādhi maraṇa śoka parideva duḥkha daurmanasya upāyāsebhyaḥ  na parimucyate pāñcagatikāt saṃsāra cāraka āgāra bandhanāt na parimucyate mātṛ maraṇa saṃtāpa duḥkhāt na parimucyate pitṛ maraṇa saṃtāpa duḥkhāt iti vistaraḥ idam ca sūtram sarva nikāyeṣu paṭhayate tad asmāt āgamāt  yathā upavarṇitāyāḥ ca upapatteḥ na arhati prājña svabhāva para bhāva bhāva abhāva darśanam tathāgata vacanāt atyanta viruddham āsthātum bhagavatā pratiṣiddha tvāt  kiṃviśiṣṭena bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvinā bhāva abhāvau vibhāvayitum śīlam asya iti bhāva abhāva vibhāvī yathā avasthita bhāva abhāva aviparīta svabhāva parijñānāt  bhāva abhāva vibhāvi iti bhagavān eva ucyate tena bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvinā yasmāt astitvaṃca na astitvam ca ubhayam etad  pratiṣiddham tasmāt na yuktam bhāva abhāva darśanam tattvam iti āsthātum tathā asti iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ  antar  na asti iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ  antar  yad enayoḥ antayoḥ madhyam tad arūpyam anidarśanam apratiṣṭham anābhā sam aniketam avijñaptikam iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamām pratipad  bhūta pratyavekṣā iti tathā asti iti na asti iti ubhe api antā śuddhī aśuddhi iti ime api antā tasmāt ubhe anta vivarjayitvā madhye api sthānam na karoti paṇḍitaḥ asti iti na asti iti vivāda eṣaḥ śuddhī aśuddhi iti ayam vivādaḥ vivāda prāptyā na duḥkham praśāmyati avivāda prāptyā ca duḥkham nirudhyate iti atra āha yadi punar evam agni ādīnām svabhāvata eva astitvam syāt  kaḥ  doṣaḥ syāt  ukta doṣaḥ hetu pratyaya saṃbhūtaḥ svabhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ  bhavet  ityādinā api ca yadi ayam eṣām agni ādīnām svabhāvaḥ syāt  tasya vidyamānasya sataḥ  na syāt  punar anyathātvam iti pratipādayan  āha yadi astitvam prakṛtyā syāt na bhavet asya na astitā yadi agni ādeḥ bhāvasya prakṛtyā svabhāvataḥ  astitvam tadā asya svabhāvasya prakṛtyā vidyamānasya punar anyathātvam na syāt  yasmāt  prakṛteḥ anyathā bhāva u na hi jātu upapadyate yadi eṣām agni ādīnām iyam eva prakṛtiḥ syāt  svabhāvaḥ syāt  tadā prakṛteḥ avikāriṇī tvāt na kadācid punar anyathā abhāva upapadyeta na hi ākāśasya anāvaraṇa tvam kadācid api anyathātvam pratipadyate evam agni ādīnām api prakṛtyā vidyamānānām punar anyathātvam na syāt  upalabhate ca bhavān eṣām anyathātva prabandha uparama lakṣaṇam vināśam tasmāt vipariṇāma dharmi tvāt apām auṣṇyavat  na ayam eṣām svabhāva iti pratīyatām atra āha yadi prakṛtyā vidyamānasya anyathātvā asaṃbhavāt anyathātvasya ca upalabhyamāna tvāt  prakṛtiḥ eṣām bhāvānām na asti iti ucyate nanu ca evam api prakṛtau kasya ca asatyām anyathātvam bhaviṣyati kasya idānīm prakṛtyā sva rūpeṇa avidyamānasya khapuṣpasya iva anyathātvam bhaviṣyati tasmāt avidyamāna prakṛtikasya anyathā ātvā anupalambhāt  anyathātvasya ca darśanāt  asti eva svabhāva iti ucyate yadi tāvakena matena prakṛtyā svabhāvena asaṃvidyamānasya anyathātva abhāvāt  anyathātvasya ca darśanāt prakṛtiḥ iti ucyate evam api prakṛtau kasya ca satyām anyathātvam bhaviṣyati kasya idānīm prakṛtyā svabhāvena vidyamānasya vartamānasya eva anyathātvam bhaviṣyati tasmāt  prakṛtyā vidyamānasya anyathātvam na asti iti sarvathā anyathātvā asaṃbhava eva tatas ca na asti prakṛtiḥ bhāvānām ioti vijñeyam yad ca api uktam anyathātvasya darśanāt na asti prakṛtiḥ iti tad api para prasiddhayā anyathātva darśanam adhikṛtya uktam na tu asmābhiḥ kadācid api kasyacid anyathātvam abhyupetam tad evam atyantatas prakṛtau  asaṃvidyamānāyām sarva dharmeṣu asaṃvidyamāneṣu asvabhāveṣu tad anyathātve ca asaṃvidyamāne yaḥ  hi idānīm astitvam na astitvam ca bhāvānām parikalpayati tasya evam parikalpayataḥ  niyatam eva asti iti śāśvata grāhaḥ  na asti iti uccheda darśanam prasajyata iti vākya śeṣaḥ tad ca etad  śāśvata uccheda darśanam svarga apavarga mārga antarāya kara tvāt  yasmāt mahānartha karam tasmāt astitvana astitve na aśrīyeta vicakṣaṇaḥ kasmāt punarbhāva abhāva darśane sati śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ  bhavati iti yasmāt  asti yad hi svabhāvena na tad na asti iti śāśvatam na asti idānīm abhūt pūrvam iti ucchedaḥ prasajyate yad  svabhāvena asti iti ucyate svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt na tad  kadācid api na asti iti evam bhāvasya astitva abhyupagame sati śāśvata darśanam āpadyate pūrvam ca vartamāna avasthāyām bhāva svarūpam abhyupetya idānīm tad vinaṣṭa tvāt na astiti paścāt abhyupagacchataḥ uccheda darśanam prasajyate yasya tu bhāva svabhāva eva na upapadyate na tasya śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ bhāva svabhāva anupalambhāt  nanu ca bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ  na asti iti abhyupagacchataḥ  mā bhūt bhāva darśana abhāvāt śāśvata darśanam uccheda darśanam tu niyatam prasajyate iti na evam abhāva darśanam bhavati yaḥ  hi pūrvam bhāva svabhāvam abhyupetya paścāt  tad nivṛttim ālambate tasya pūrva upalabdha svabhāva apavādāt syāt abhāva darśanam yaḥ tu taimirika upalabdha keśeṣu iva vitaimirikaḥ  na kiṃcid upalabhate sa na asti iti bruvan kiṃcid na asti iti brūyāt  pratiṣedhya abhāvāt viparyastānām tu mithyā abhiniveśa nivṛtti artham ataimirikā iva vayam brūmaḥ na santi sarva bhāvāḥ iti na ca evam bruvatām asmākam para hita vyāpāra parāyaṇānām uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ yathā uktam sūtre yaḥ  hi bhagavan pūrvam rāga dveṣa moha bhāva abhyupagamam kṛtvā paścāt na santi rāga dveṣa moha bhāvā iti bravīti sa bhagavan vai nāstikaḥ  bhavati iti vistaraḥ yaḥ tu paratantra citta caitta vaḥ tu mātram abhyupetya tasya parikalpita svabhāva abhāvāt astitva darśanam pariharati saṃkleśa vyavadāna nibandhanasya ca paratantra vastu mātra sadbhāvāt na astitva darśanam pariharati tasya parikalpitasya avidyamāna tvāt  paratantrasya ca vidyamāna tvāt  astitvanā astitva darśana dvayasya api upanipātāt  kutaḥ anta dvaya parihāraḥ hetu pratyaya janitasya ca sa svabhāvena ayuktatva pratipādanāt ayuktam eva asya vyākhyānam tad evam madhyamaka darśane eva astitva nā astitva dvaya darśanasya aprasaṅgaḥ na vijñāna vādi darśana ādiṣu iti vijñeyam ata eva uktam ārya ratna āvalyām sa sāṃkhī ā aullūkya nirgrantha pudgala skandha vādinam pṛccha lokam yadi vadati astināsti vyatikramam dharmayautakam iti asmāt astināsti vyatikramam viddhi gambhīram iti ukta buddhānām śāsana amṛtam iti tathāvidha vineya jana bodha anurodhāt tu parama artha darśanasya upāya bhūta tvāt  neyārtha tvena bhagavatā mahā karuṇā paratantra tayā vijñāna ādi vādaḥ  deśitaḥ sāṃmitīya pudgala vādavat  na nīta arthaḥ iti vijñeyam yathā uktam ārya samādhi rāja bhaṭṭārake nīta artha sūtra anta viśeṣa jānati yathā upadiṣṭā sugatena śūnyatā yasmin punar  pudgala sattva pūruṣaḥ  neyārthataḥ  jānati sarva dharmān etad ca ārya akṣayam ati nirdeśa ādiṣu vistareṇa boddhavyam iti bhāva abhāva darśana dvaya prasaṅgaḥ  yāvat  tāvat saṃsāra iti avetya mumukṣubhiḥ etad darśana dvaya nirāsena sadbhiḥ madhyamā pratipad  bhāvanīyā yathāvat iti etad ca uktam bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvayi jñānam sarvi acintiya sarvi abhūtam ye puna citta vaśa anuga bālāḥ te dukhitā bhava koṭi śateṣu bhāvān abhāvān iti yaḥ prajānatī sa sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate yaḥ sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate sa ānimittam spṛśate samādhim iti tathā smarāmi aham pūrvam atīta adhvani acintiye kalpi narāṇam uttamaḥ utpannu loka artha karaḥ  mahā ṛṣī nāmena saḥ  abhāva samudgataḥ  abhūt  sa jāta mātraḥ  gagane sthihitvā sarvāṇa dharmāṇa bhāva deśayi tadā anurūpam kṛta nāmadheyam śabdena sarvam tri sahasra vijñayī deva api sarve pramumocu śabdam abhāva nāmā iti jinaḥ bhaviṣyati yaḥ  jāta mātraḥ pada sapta prakraman abhāva dharmāṇa samam prakāśayī buddhaḥ  yadā bheṣyati dharmarājaḥ sarvāṇa dharmāṇa prakāśakaḥ  muniḥ tṛṇa gulma vṛkṣa oṣadhi śaila parvate abhāva dharmāṇa ravaḥ  bhaviṣyati yāvanti śabda astahi lokadhātau sarve hi abhāvā na hi kaści bhāvaḥ tāvanti khaḥ tasya tathāgatasya ravu niścarī loka vināyakasya iti bhavati iti bhāvaḥ sattā na vidyate sattā svabhāvaḥ sarva bhāvānām iti abhāvāḥ sarva dharmāḥ śūnyāḥ sarva dharmā niḥsvabhāva yogena iti prajñāpāramitā pāṭhāt  bhāva svabhāvasya anupapatteḥ abhāva dharmāṇa ravaḥ  bhaviṣyati ityādinā sūtra arthaḥ  avagantavyaḥ yāvanti śabda astahi lokadhātau sarve hi abhāvā na hi kaści bhāvaḥ ityādi bhūtvā abhāva pratiṣedha vivakṣita tvāt  bhāva abhāva artha eva svabhāva abhāva arthaḥ iti ācārya
