candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau svabhāva parīkṣā nāma pañcadaśamam prakaraṇam bandha mokṣa parīkṣā ṣoḍaśamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyata eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ saṃsāra sadbhāvāt  iha saṃsaraṇam saṃsṛtiḥ gateḥ gati antara gamanam saṃsāra iti ucyate yadi bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ  na syāt  kasya gateḥ gati antara gamanam saṃsāraḥ syāt  na hi avidyamānānām vandhyā sūnu saṃskārāṇām saṃsaraṇam dṛṣṭam tasmāt  saṃsāra sadbhāvāt  vidyata eva bhāvānām svabhāva iti ucyate syāt bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ yadi saṃsāra eva bhavet  na tu asti iha yadi saṃsāraḥ syāt  sa niyatam saṃskārāṇām vā bhavet  sattvasya vā kim ca atas  ubhayathā ca doṣa iti āha saṃskārāḥ saṃsaranti ced na nityāḥ saṃsaranti te saṃsaranti ca na anityāḥ sattve api eṣa samaḥ kramaḥ tatra yadi saṃskārāḥ saṃsaranti iti parikalpyate kim te nityāḥ saṃsaranti uta anityāḥ tatra na nityāḥ saṃsaranti niṣkriya tvāt  anityānām ca ghaṭa ādīnām sa kriyatva upalambhāt  atha anityāḥ ye hi akriyāḥ te utpāda samanantaram eva vinaṣṭāḥ ye ca vinaṣṭāḥ kutas teṣām avidyamāna tvāt vandhyā sūnu saṃskārāṇām iva kvacid  gamanam iti evam anityānām api na asti saṃsāraḥ atha api syāt  anityā eva santaḥ  hetu phala saṃbandha paraṃparayā avicchinna kramāḥ saṃtānena ca pravartamānāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃsaranti iti etad api na upapadyate kutas  yad  tāvat utpadyate kāryam tasya saṃsāraḥ  na asti kutaścid ana āgamanāt  kvacid ca āgamanāt  yad ca kāraṇam naṣṭam tasya api saṃsāraḥ  na asti kutaścid ana āgamanāt  kvacid ca āgamanāt  saṃskāra mātra vyatirekeṇa atīta anāgatayoḥ asiddha tvāt naṣṭa ajāta tvena avidyamāna tvāt  uttarasmin kṣaṇe utpanne pūrvaḥ saṃsarati iti ced  yadi pūrva uttarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ eka tvam syāt  syāt etad evam na tu eka tvam asti kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt cakṣū rūpa cakṣuḥ vijñānānām na asti ca kim ca ekatve sati pūrva uttara kṣaṇa vācya tā eva na syāt  na hi ekaḥ  devadattaḥ ekadā pūrvaḥ ca uttaraḥ ca iti vyapadiśyate evam iha api eka tvāt  pūrva uttara kṣaṇa vyapadeśa eva na syāt  api ca pūrva kṣaṇaḥ  naṣṭa iti na syāt uttara kṣaṇavat avyatirikta tvāt uttarakṣaṇa utpanna iti na syāt  pūrvakṣaṇavat avyatirikta tvāt atha anya tve sati saṃsaraṇam syāt  evam sati arhatām api saṃsaraṇam syāt  anyasya pṛthagjanasya saṃsāra utpatti sadbhāvāt  nirvṛtaḥ ca pradīpaḥ pradīpa antare jvalati iti syāt  kim ca anyat  naṣṭāt vā pūrvakṣaṇāt uttarasya kṣaṇasya udayaḥ syāt anaṣṭāt naśyamānāt vā tatra yadi naṣṭa āt iṣyate vahni dagdhāt api bījāt aṅkura udayaḥ syāt  tatas ca nirhetukaḥ syāt  atha anaṣṭāt  evam api avikṛte api bīje aṅkura udayaḥ syāt  kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca yaugapadyam syāt  nirhetukaḥ ca utpādaḥ syāt  naśyamānāt iti ced  naṣṭān aṣṭa vyatirekeṇa naśyamāna abhāvāt naṣṭān aṣṭayoḥ ca vihita doṣa tvāt naśyamānāt api na asti utpattiḥ iti kutas  kārya kāraṇa vyavasthā pūrva uttara kṣaṇa vyavasthā vā bhaviṣyati yadā ca pūrva uttara kṣaṇa vyavasthā kārya kāraṇa vyavasthā ca na asti tadā saṃtānaḥ  api na asti tad abhāvāt na asti bhavatām saṃsāra iti anityānām api saṃskārāṇām na asti saṃsāra iti atra eke varṇayanti satyam saṃskārā na saṃsaranti utpatti vidhura tvāt  kim tarhi sattvaḥ saṃsarati iti ucyate sattve api eṣa samaḥ kramaḥ sattvaḥ saṃsarati iti ucyamāne kim asau nityaḥ saṃsarati uta anityaḥ iti vicāryamāṇe ya eva saṃskārāṇām saṃsaraṇa anupapatti kramaḥ sa sama tvāt sattve api samaḥ  nipatati tasmāt sattvaḥ  api na saṃsarati atra āha na eva hi sattva saṃskārāṇām saṃsāra anupapatti kramaḥ samaḥ  bhavitum arhati yasmāt iha saṃskārāṇām nitya anitya bhūtānām saṃsaraṇam na asti iti uktam na ca evam ātmā nitya anitya bhūtaḥ tasya hi skandhebhyaḥ tattva anyatva avakta vya tāvat  nitya tvena anitya tvena api avaktavyatā vyavasthāpyate tasmāt ātmā eva saṃsarati iti na ca ukta doṣa prasaṅga iti ucyate pudgalaḥ saṃsarati ced skandha āyatana dhātuṣu pañcadhā mṛgyamāṇaḥ  asau na asti kaḥ saṃsariṣyati yadi pudgalaḥ  nāma kaścid  syāt  sa saṃsaret  na tu asti yasmāt  skandha āyatana dhātuṣu pañcadhā mṛgyamāṇaḥ  na asti katham kṛtvā indhanam punar agniḥ na na agniḥ anyatra ca indhanāt  na agniḥ indhanavān na agnau  indhanāni na teṣu saḥ agni indhanābhyām vyākhyāta ātma upādānayoḥ kramaḥ iti evam skandha āyatana dhātu svabhāva ātmā na bhavati na api tebhyaḥ  vyatiriktaḥ na skandha āyatana dhātumān na skandha āyatana dhātuṣu ātmā na ātmani skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ iti evam pañcadhā mṛgyamāṇa  ātmā na saṃbhavati pūrva uditena nyāyena yaḥ ca idānīm skandha āyatana dhātuṣu evam vicāryamāṇaḥ pañcadhā na saṃbhavati sa katham avidyamānaḥ san saṃsariṣyati iti evam ātmanaḥ  api na asti saṃsāraḥ vandhyā sutasya iva avidyamāna tvāt  api ca ayam ātmā upādānāt upādānam saṃsaran vibhavaḥ  bhavet  vibhavaḥ ca anupādānaḥ kaḥ sa kim saṃsariṣyati bhavatu kāmam ātmanaḥ saṃsāraḥ yadi anupādānasya sataḥ  asya saṃsāraḥ  yuktaḥ syāt  katham punar asya anupādāna tā prasajyata iti pratipādayan  āha upādānāt upādānam saṃsaran vibhavaḥ  bhavet  iti iha hi manuṣya upādānāt deva upādānam gacchan parityajya vā manuṣya upādānam deva upādānam gacchet aparityajya vā yadi tāvat parityajya gacchati iti ucyate tadā pūrva upādānasya parityāgāt uttarasya ca anupādānāt tad antarāle vibhavaḥ syāt  vigataḥ  bhavaḥ  vibhavaḥ bhavaḥ pañca upādāna skandhāḥ tad rahitaḥ syāt  yaḥ ca vibhavaḥ  anupādānaḥ sa skandha rahita tvāt  prajñapti upādānakāraṇa rahita tvāt nirhetukaḥ syāt  yaḥ ca anupādānaḥ  nirañjanaḥ  avyaktaḥ  nirhetukaḥ kaḥ saḥ na kaścid  saḥ na asti eva sa iti arthaḥ tasmin  ca asati tad abhāvāt eva upādānam api nirupādātṛkam na asti iti kim saṃsariṣyati na asti eva tad  yad saṃsariṣyati iti arthaḥ athavā kim iti etad  saṃsaraṇa kriyā viśeṣaṇam tatas ca avidyamāna tvāt  na eva saṃsaraṇa kriyām kariṣyati evam tāvat pūrva upādāna parityāgena saṃsaraṇam ayuktam atha aparityāgena tathā api na upapadyate kim kāraṇam pūrvasya aparityāgāt uttarasya ca grahaṇāt  yasmāt ekasya ātmanaḥ  dvaya ātmaka tā syāt  na ca etad iṣyata iti tasmāt aparityāgena api saṃsaraṇam na asti atha pūrva uttarayoḥ bhavayoḥ madhye āntarābhavika skandha saṃbhavāt taiḥ ca sa upādāna tvāt  sa upādānam saṃsarataḥ  api na vibhavatā prasaṅga iti tad api na yuktam pūrva bhava parityāga aparityāga abhyām āntara āmavika skandha saṃsāre api tulya prasaṅga tvāt  yugapad tyāgopādānāt adoṣa  iti ced  ucyate kim eka deśena pūrva upādānam tyajate eka deśena antarā abhava upādānam saṃcarati atha sarva ātmanā tatra yadi avayavena iti parikalpyate tadā dvaya ātmaka tā prasaṅgāt iti ukta doṣaḥ atha sarva ātmanā evam api sa eva vibhavatā prasaṅga āpadyate etāvān  tu viśeṣaḥ yad antarābhava saṃcāre atisāmīpyāt  sūkṣmam kālam anupādānaḥ syāt  na ca sarva ātmanā ekasya padārthasya abhinnapadārthasya viṣaye yugapad  tyāga upādāne dṛṣṭe na hi ekasya devadattasya sarva ātmanā gṛhāt gṛham saṃcarataḥ ekadā tyāga upādāna kriye dve saṃbhavataḥ atha ekena pādena ekasya parityāgāt aparasya ca upādānāt  yugapad tyāgopādāne parikalpyete nanu evam sati pāda dvayavat  dvaya ātmaka tā ātmanaḥ syāt  aṃśena pūrvatra avasthānāt aṃśena ca uttaratra avasthānāt aneka avayava tā prasajyeta tasmāt  yaugapadyena api tyāga upādāne na saṃbhavataḥ iti aparihāra eva ayam tasmāt antarā abhava upādāne api sa eva doṣa prasaṅga iti sarvathā ātmanaḥ  api na asti saṃsāraḥ yadā ca saṃskārāṇām ātmanaḥ ca saṃsāraḥ  na asti tadā na asti eva saṃsāra iti sthitam atra āha vidyata eva saṃsāraḥ pratidvandvi sadbhāvāt  iha yaḥ  na asti na tasya pratidvandvī vidyate tad yathā vandhyā sūnoḥ iti asti ca saṃsārasya pratidvandvi nirvāṇam tasmāt asti saṃsāra iti ucyate syāt saṃsāraḥ yadi tad pratidvandvi nirvāṇam syāt  na tu asti iti āha saṃskārāṇām na nirvāṇam kathaṃcid upapadyate sattvasya api na nirvāṇam kathaṃcid upapadyate yadi nirvāṇam nāma kiṃcid  syāt  tad  parikalpyamānam saṃskārāṇām nityānām vā parikalpyeta anityānām vā tatra nityānām avikāriṇām kim nirvāṇam kuryāt  anityānām api asaṃvidyamānānām kim nirvāṇam kuryāt iti sarvam pūrveṇa tulyam na kathaṃcid iti na kena api prakāreṇa iti arthaḥ atha sattvasya nirvāṇam parikalpyate tad api nityasya vā anityasya vā pūrvavat na upapadyate atha nitya anitya tvena avācyasya parikalpyate nanu evam sati nirvāṇe api ātmā asti iti abhyupeta bhavati saṃsāra iva api ca sa upādānasya eva ātmanaḥ avācya tā yujyate na ca nirvāṇe upādānam asti iti kutaḥ asya avācya tā bhavatu vā tattva anyatva avācya tā ātmanaḥ api tu kim asau nirvāṇe asti uta na asti yadi asti tadā mokṣe api tasya sadbhāvāt nitya tā syāt  atha na asti tadā anitya ātmā syāt  tatas ca tattva anyatva avācya tāvat nitya anitya tvena api ātmanaḥ avaktavyatā iti na syāt  atha nirvāṇe api ātmanaḥ astitvanā astitvena avācya tā eva iṣyate evam api kim asau vijñeyaḥ atha na yadi vijñeyaḥ na tarhi nirupādānaḥ  asau  ātmā nirvāṇe vijñeya tvāt  saṃsāra iva atha na vijñāyate tatra asau avijñeya svarūpa tvāt kha puṣpavat na asti eva iti kutaḥ asya avācya tā tad evam nirvāṇam api na asti tad abhāvāt na asti saṃsāra iti ata eva uktam bhagavatyām aṣṭa sāhasrikāyām nirvāṇam api āyuṣman subhūte māyā upamam svapna upamam buddha dharmā āyuṣman subhūte māyā upamāḥ svapna upamā ityādi saceta kula putra nirvāṇāt api adhika taraḥ  anyaḥ  dharmaḥ  abhaviṣyat  tam api aham māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadāmi tathā ārya samādhi rāja bhaṭṭārake parama artha satya supinena samam nirvāṇam svapna samotaratī mana evam otarati yena vidu mana saṃvaraḥ kathitu śreṣṭhu ayam tathā nirodha satyam supinam yathā eva svapna svabhāvām atha nirvṛtim ca yena iha vācā uttari bodhisattvaḥ  ayam khu saḥ  vuccati vāca saṃvaraḥ atra āha yadi api tvayā saṃsāra nirvāṇe pratiṣiddhe tathā api bandha mokṣau vidyete na ca avidyamānasya bhāva svabhāvasya bandha mokṣau saṃbhavataḥ tasmāt  bandha mokṣa sadbhāvāt  vidyata eva bhāvānām svabhāva iti ucyate syāt bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ yadi bandha mokṣau  eva syātām na tu staḥ iti āha na badhyante na mucyante udaya vyaya dharmiṇaḥ saṃskārāḥ pūrvavat sattvaḥ  badhyate na na mucyate iha ya ime rāga ādayaḥ kleśāḥ baddhānām asvatantrī karaṇe bandhanam iti vyapadiśyate yaiḥ ca baddhāḥ pṛthagjanāḥ traidhātukam na atikramanti iti vyavasthāpyate tad etad rāga ādikam bandhana tvena parikalpyamānam udaya vyaya dharmiṇām tāvat  kṣaṇikānām saṃskārāṇām utpāda anantara dhvaṃsinām naṣṭānām asattvāt na saṃbhavati rāga ādi bandhana viccheda lakṣaṇaḥ  api mokṣaḥ anityānām saṃskārāṇām avidyamāna tvāt na eva saṃbhavati pūrvavat  pūrva ukta vidhinā iti arthaḥ yathā ca pūrva ukta vidhinā saṃskārāṇām bandha mokṣau na saṃbhavataḥ evam pūrvavat eva sattvaḥ  api na badhyate na api mucyate iti evam bandha mokṣau  api na staḥ atra āha yadi api saṃskārāṇām sattvasya vā bandhaḥ na asti tathā api rāga ādikam upādāna ākhyam bandhana bhūtam asti tad sadbhāvāt bandhaḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate syāt upādānam bandhanam yadi kaṃcid padārtham badhnīyāt  na tu badhnāti yathā ca na badhnāti tathā pratipādayan  āha bandhanam ced upādānam sa upādānaḥ  na badhyate badhyate na anupādānaḥ kim avasthaḥ  atha badhyate tatra vidyamāna upādānaḥ sa upādānaḥ sa tāvat bhāvaḥ  na badhyate yaḥ  hi sa upādānaḥ sa baddha eva tasya punar api bandhana yogaḥ kim kuryāt  yaḥ ca api anupādānaḥ bandhana rahitaḥ asau  api bandhana rahita tvāt  tathāgatavat na badhyate anupādānaḥ bandhana rahitaḥ badhyata iti paraspara viruddha tvāt ca ayuktam etad  yaḥ ca evam nirūpyamāṇaḥ sa upādānaḥ  nirupādānaḥ  vā na badhyate sa idānīm kim avasthaḥ  badhyatām na asti eva asau kācid aparā asya avasthā yasyām badhyeta iti abhiprāyaḥ yadā ca evam nirūpyamāṇam bandhanam na kaṃcid api badhnāti tadā kaṃcid api abadhnata upādānasya rāga ādeḥ kutaḥ bandhana tvam iti tasmāt  bandhanam api na asti api ca badhnīyāt bandhanam kāmam bandhyāt pūrvam bhavet yadi na ca asti tad  iha bandhya vyatirekeṇa bandhanam nigaḍa ādikam pūrva siddham sat  bandhyam devadattam badhnāti iti dṛṣṭam evam yadi bandhyebhyaḥ saṃskārebhyaḥ pudgalāt vā bandhyāt pūrvam rāga ādikam bandhanam siddham syāt  tena pūrva siddhena bandhanam syāt  saṃskārāṇām pudgalasya vā tad ca etad na saṃbhavati nirāśrayasya rāga ādikasya asiddha tvāt  pūrva siddhasya ca bandhanasya paścāt  bandhyena saha saṃbandhasya niṣprayojana tvāt  bandhyasya ca bandhanāt pṛthak siddhasya pūva bandhana apekṣā niṣprayojana tvāt ca na asti bandhyāt bandhanasya pūrva siddhiḥ tasmāt na eva bandhanam kaṃcid api badhnāti na ca kaṃcid api abadhnataḥ  bandhana tvam yuktam iti na asti bandhanam bandhana abhāvāt ca bandhyaḥ  api na asti iti siddham yad punar atra śeṣam dūṣaṇam tad  śeṣa muktam gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ iti veditavyam śloka pāṭha parivartanena baddhaḥ  na badhyate tāvat abaddhaḥ  na eva badhyate baddha ābaddha vinirmuktaḥ  badhyamānaḥ  na badhyate ityādinā yojyam atra āha yadi api bhavatā bandhanam pratiṣiddham tathā api saṃsāra cāraka āgāra avabaddhānāmatrāṇānām sattvānām mahā kāruṇikaiḥ tathāgataiḥ śīla samādhi prajñā ātma kara kandha traya upadeśaḥ  yad artham uktaḥ sa tāvat mokṣaḥ  asti na ca abaddhasya puṃsaḥ mokṣaḥ tasmāt  bandhaḥ api asti iti ucyate syāt bandhayadi mokṣa eva syāt  iha ayam mokṣaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ baddhasya vā parikalpyeta abaddhasya vā kicātaḥ ubhayathā ca na yujyata iti āha baddhaḥ  na mucyate tāvat abaddhaḥ  na eva mucyate syātām baddhe mucyamāne yugapad bandha mokṣaṇe tatra baddhasya mokṣaḥ  na saṃbhavati baddha tvāt  atha baddhasya paścāt upāyena mokṣa iti kṛtvā baddha eva mucyate iti syāt  na tarhi baddhaḥ  mucyata iti vaktavyam kim tarhi mokṣyata iti vartamāna sāmīpyāt eva mucyata iti ced  yadi kadācid api mokṣaḥ saṃbhavet  tadā samīpe syāt  yadā tu kasyāṃcid api avasthāyām mokṣe iṣyamāṇe baddhasya mokṣa asaṃbhavena mokṣa abhāvaḥ pratipipādayiṣita tadā kutaḥ vartamāna samīpa tā evam tāvat  baddhaḥ  na mucyate iti sthitam idānīm abaddhaḥ  api na mucyate sa hi mukta eva tasya punar api mokṣaḥ kim kuryāt  muktānām ca arhatām punar api mokṣa apekṣa tvāt  baddha tā eva syāt  tatas ca arhataḥ  api bandhaḥ syāt  atha syāt  abaddhasya mokṣa asaṃbhavāt  baddha eva mucyate iti evam sati baddhe mucyamāne parikalpyamāne baddha tvāt mucyamāna tvāt ca yaugapadyena bandha mokṣaṇe syātām na ca paraspara viruddha tvāt āloka andhakāravat ekasmin kāle bandha mokṣaṇe upapadyete yatas ca evam baddha ābaddhayoḥ mokṣā saṃbhava tasmāt mokṣaḥ  api na asti tad abhāvāt ca bandhanam api na asti iti siddham atra āha yadi bhavatā eva saṃsāra nirvāṇe niṣiddhe bandha mokṣau ca pratiṣiddhau ya eṣa saṃsāra vinirmumukṣūṇām avidyā sāndra andhakāra vividha kudarśana kaṭhina ati dīrgha latā saṃchādita sat patham jāti ādi vividhā paryanta vyasana aniṣṭatara vipula vipāka phalada anuśaya viṣa vṛkṣa saṃkulam viṃśati śikhara samunnata tara ati pṛthu sat kāya dṛṣṭi mahā śaila pariveṣṭita sarva diṅmukham viṣaya sukha āśāti picchila vipula mahā taṭa vivara vāhi tṛṣṇā nadī mahā parikham saṃsāra mahā aṭavī kāntāram nistitīḥ ṣūṇām parama āśvāsa karaḥ kuśalaḥ  mahā dharma  chandaḥ kadā nu khalu aham anupādānaḥ  nirvāsyāmi kadā nu me nirvāṇam bhaviṣyati iti nanu sa vyarthaka eva saṃjāyate yaḥ ca api evam utpādita kuśala amala vipula dharma  chandānām kalyāṇa mitra saṃseva ādāna śīla śruta cintā bhāvana ādi kramaḥ  nirvāṇa prāptaye nanu tamyā api vaiyarthyam syāt iti ucyate yaḥ  hi evam niḥsvabhāveṣu sarva bhāveṣu pratibimba marīcikā jala alāta cakra svapna māyā indrajāla sadṛśeṣu ātma ātmīya svabhāva rahiteṣu viparyāsa mātra anugamāt tām eva sat kāya dṛṣṭim aham mama iti ahaṃkāram amakāra samudācāra parigraheṇa utpādya manyate nirvāsyāmi anupādānaḥ  nirvāṇam me bhaviṣyati iti yeṣām grahaḥ teṣām upādāna mahā grahaḥ aham anupādānaḥ sarva upādāna rahitaḥ  nirvāsyāmi mama ca evam pratipannasya nirvāṇam bhaviṣyati iti evam yeṣām mumukṣūṇām grāhaḥ  bhavati nanu tad eva ahaṃkāram amakāra ākhyam sat kāya dṛṣṭayupādānam eṣām mahā grahaḥ  bhavati na ca evaṃvidha mahā graha abhiniviṣṭānām śāntiḥ saṃbhāvyate niravaśeṣa graha prahāṇena eva mokṣa avāptaye yāvat ahaṃmam eti grāha abhiniveśaḥ yāvat ca nirvāṇam nāma asti iti grāha abhiniveśaḥ yāvat ca upādāna tyāga abhiniveśaḥ tāvat niyatam eva anupāyena nirvāṇam prārthayatām sarva eva ārambhā vyarthā bhavanti tasmāt mumukṣuṇā sarvam etad  parityājyam yathā uktam bhagavatā ārya dhyāyita muṣṭi sūtre atha khalu bhagavān mañju śriyam kumāra bhūtam etad avocat  caturṇām ārya satyānām yathābhūta artha adarśanāt caturbhiḥ viparyāsaiḥ viparyasta cittāḥ satvāḥ evam imam abhūtam saṃsāram na atikrāmanti evam ukte mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ  bhagavantam etad avocat  deśayatu bhagavān kasya upalambhataḥ sattvāḥ saṃsāram na atikrāmanti bhagavān āha ātma ātmīya upalambhāt mañjuśrīḥ sattvāḥ saṃsāram na atikrāmanti tad  kasya hetoḥ yaḥ  hi mañjuśrīḥ ātmānam param ca samanupaśyati tasya karma abhisaṃskārā bhavanti bālaḥ  mañju śrīraśrutavān pṛthagjanaḥ atyanta aparinirvṛtān sarva dharmānaprajā nānaḥ ātmānam param ca upalabhate upalabhya abhiniviśate abhiniviṣṭaḥ san rajyate duṣyate muhyate sa raktaḥ  duṣṭaḥ  mūḍhaḥ san trividham karma abhisaṃskaroti kāyena vācā manasā saḥ asat samāropeṇa vikalpayati aham raktaḥ aham dviṣṭaḥ aham mūḍhaḥ iti tasya tathāgata śāsane pravrajitasya evam bhavati aham śīlavān aham brahmacārī iti aham saṃsāram samatikramiṣyāmi aham nirvāṇam anuprāpsyāmi aham duḥkhebhyaḥ  mokṣyāmi sa vikalpayati ime kuśalā dharmāḥ ime akuśalā dharmāḥ ime dharmāḥ prahātavyāḥ ime dharmāḥ sākṣāt kartavyāḥ duḥkham parijñātavyam samudayaḥ prahātavyaḥ nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ mārgaḥ  bhāvayitavyaḥ sa vikalpayati anityāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ ādīptāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ yad nu aham sarva saṃskārebhyaḥ palāya iyam tasya evam avekṣamāṇasya utpadyate nirvitsaha gataḥ  manasikāraḥ animitta purogataḥ tasya evam bhavati eṣā sā duḥkha parijñā yā iyam eṣām dharmāṇām parijñā tasya evam bhavati yad nu aham samudayam prajaheyam sa ebhyaḥ  dharmebhyaḥ  ārtīyate jehrīyate vitarati vijugupsate uttrasyati saṃtrasyati saṃtrāsam āpadyate tasya evam bhavati iyam eṣām dharmāṇām sākṣātkriyā idam samudaya prahāṇam yadidamebhyaḥ  dharmebhyaḥ  artīyanā vijugupsanā tasya eva bhavati nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ samudayam kalpayitvā nirodhe saṃjānāti tasya evam bhavati eṣā sā nirodha sākṣāt kriyā tasya evam bhavati yad nūnam aham mārgam bhāvayeyam sa ekaḥ  rahaḥ gataḥ tān dharmān manasi kurvan śamatham pratilabhate tasya tena nirvitsaha gatena manasikāreṇa śamatha utpadyate tasya sarva dharmeṣu cittam pratilīyate prativahati pratyudāvartate tebhyaḥ ca ārtīyate jehrīyate anabhinandana acittam utpadyate tasya evam bhavati muktaḥ  asmi sarva duḥkhebhyaḥ na mama bhūya uttariṃ kiṃcitkaraṇīyam arhan  asmi iti ātmānam saṃjānāti sa maraṇa kāla samaye utpattim ātmanaḥ samanupaśyati tasya kāṅkṣā ca vicikitsā ca bhavati buddha bodhau sa vicikitsā patitaḥ kālagataḥ  mahānirayeṣu prapatati tad kasya hetoḥ yathā api idam anutpannān sarva dharmān vikalpayitvā tathāgate vicikitsām vimatim ca utpādayati atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ  bhagavantam etad avocat  katham punar bhagavan  catvāri ārya satyāni draṣṭavyāni bhagavān āha yena mañju śrīḥ anutpannāḥ sarva saṃskārā dṛṣṭāḥ tena duḥkham parijñātam yena asamutthitāḥ sarva dharmā dṛṣṭāḥ tasya samudayaḥ prahīṇaḥ yena atyanta parinirvṛtāḥ sarva dharmā dṛṣṭāḥ tena nirodhaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ yena atyanta śūnyāḥ sarva dharmā dṛṣṭāḥ tena mārgaḥ  bhāvitaḥ yena mañjuśrīḥ evam catvāri ārya satyāni dṛṣṭāni sa na kalpayati na vikalpayati ime kuśalā dharmāḥ ime akuśalā dharmāḥ ime dharmāḥ prahātavyāḥ ime dharmāḥ sākṣāt kartavyāḥ duḥkham parijñātavyam samudayaḥ prahātavyaḥ nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ mārgaḥ  bhāvayitavya iti tad kasya hetaḥ tathā hi sa tam dharmam na samanupaśyati yam parikalpayet  bāla pṛthagjanāḥ tu etān dharmān kalpayantaḥ  rajyanti ca dviṣanti ca muhyanti ca sa na kaṃcid dharmam āvyūhati nirvyūhati tasya evam anāvyūhataḥ  anirvyūhataḥ traidhātuke citta na sajjati ajāta sarva tra edhātukam samanupaśyati iti vistaraḥ ata eva asmāt āgamāt  parama artha satya ucyate na nirvāṇa samāropaḥ  na saṃsāra apakarṣaṇam yatra kaḥ tatra saṃsāraḥ  nirvāṇam kim vikalpyate yatra hi nāma parama artha satye na evam na nirvāṇa samāropaḥ na nirvāṇa adhyāropaḥ saṃbhavati anupalabhyamāna tvāt  na api saṃsāra apakarṣaṇam saṃsāra parikṣayaḥ na saṃbhavati kaḥ tatra saṃsāraḥ yaḥ  vikalpyate kṣaya artham kim vā tatra nirvāṇam yad prāpi artham vikalpyate athavā yatra nirvāṇe kasyacid  sattvasya saṃsārāt apakarṣaṇam apanayanam nirvāṇe ca samāropaṇam prayatnavatā api na śakyate kartum saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ api anupalabhyamāna tvāt  tatra kim nirvāṇam vikalpyate na eva hi kiṃcid vikalpayitum yuktam avikalpayataḥ ca niyatam yathā udita saṃsāra aṭavī kāntāra atikramaḥ  nirvāṇa pura prāptiḥ ca bhaviṣyati iti ata eva uktamārya mārada mana sūtre atha mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ tasyām velāyām tathārūpam samanvāhāram samanvāharati sma yad māraḥ pāpīyān indra kīla bandhana baddhaḥ  dharaṇī tala prapatitaḥ utkrośati sma gāḍha bandhana baddhaḥ  asmi mañjuśrīḥ āha asti pāpīyat   etasmāt bandhanāt gāḍhataram bandhanam yena tvam nitya baddhaḥ  na punar badhyase tad punar  katamat  yad idam asmi māna viparyāsa bandhanam tṛṣṇā dṛṣṭi bandhanam idam pāpīyan bandhanam atas  bandhanāt  gāḍhataram bandhanam na saṃvidyate tena tvam nitya baddhaḥ  na punar badhyase peyālam āha kim tvam pāpīyannāttamanā bhūyāḥ yadi mucyethāḥ āha ātta manā bhaveyam parama āttamanā bhaveyam atha khalu suyāmaḥ  deva putraḥ  mañju śriyam kumāra bhūtam etad avocat  utsṛja mañjuśrīḥ māram pāpīyāṃsam gacchatu sva bhavanam atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ  māram pāpīyāṃsam etad avocat  kena asi pāpīyan baddhaḥ  yadā ātmānam utsṛjasi āha na jāne mañjuśrīḥ kena asmi baddhaḥ iti āha yathā tvam pāpīyan abaddhaḥ  baddha saṃjñī evam eva sarva bāla pṛthagjanā anitye nitya saṃjñinaḥ duḥkhe aduḥkha saṃjñinaḥ aśubhe śubha saṃjñinaḥ anātmani ātma saṃjñinaḥ arūpe rūpa saṃjñinaḥ avedanāyām vedanā saṃjñinaḥ asaṃjñāyām saṃjñā saṃjñinaḥ asaṃskāre saṃskāra saṃjñinaḥ avijñāne vijñāna saṃjñinaḥ api tu khalu punar  pāpīyan yaḥ tvam mokṣyase kutaḥ mokṣyase āha na aham jāne kutaścid mokṣye āha evam eva pāpīyan ye api mokṣyante nate kutaścid vimokṣyante anyatra yā asau asat bhūta saṃjñā tām parijānanti tām parijñāya vimuktā iti ucyante iti ata eva āgamāt  asat viparyāsa kalpanā mātra latā bandhana vicchedaḥ  vimokṣaḥ  nirvāṇam iti ucyate svapna upalabdha dahana jvālā nirvāpaṇavat tad anila salilaiḥ iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau bandha mokṣa parīkṣā nāma ṣoḍaśamam prakaraṇam karma phala parīkṣā saptadaśamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyata eva saṃsāraḥ karma phala saṃbandha āśraya tvāt yadi iha saṃtāna aviccheda krameṇa janma maraṇa paraṃparayā hetu phala bhāva pravṛttyā saṃskārāṇām ātmanaḥ  vā saṃsaraṇam syāt  syāt tadānīm karma phala saṃbandhaḥ yathā āvarṇite saṃsāra abhāve tu utpatti anantara vināśi tvāt cittasya karma ākṣepa kāle ca vipākasya asadbhāvāt karma phala saṃbandha abhāva eva syāt  saṃsāra sadbhāve tu sati iha kṛtasya karmaṇe janmāntare api vipāka phala saṃbandhāt  karmaṇām phala saṃbandhaḥ  na virodhitaḥ  bhavati tasmāt vidyata eva saṃsāraḥ karma phala saṃbandha āśraya tvāt iti kāni punar tāni karmāṇi kim vā tad phalam iti tad prabheda vivakṣaya it am ucyate ātma saṃyamakam cetaḥ para anugrāhakam ca yad  maitram sa dharmaḥ tad bījam phalasya pretya ca iha ca tatra āhitaḥ utpāditaḥ ahaṃmānaḥ  asmin  iti ātmā skandhān upādāya prajñapyamānaḥ pudgalaātmā iti ucyate cinoti upacinoti śubham aśubham karma vipāka dāna sāmarthye niyamayati iti cetaḥ cittam manaḥ vijñānam iti tasya eva paryāyāḥ ātmānam saṃyamayati viṣayeṣu asvatantrayati rāga ādi kleśa vaśena pravṛttim nivārayati iti ātma saṃyamakam tad etad ātma saṃyamakam kuśalam cetaḥ prāṇa atipāta ādiṣu pravṛtti vidhārakam durgati gamanāt dhārayati iti dharma iti ucyate dharma śabdaḥ  ayam pravacane tridhā vyavasthāpitaḥ sva lakṣaṇa dhāraṇa arthena kugati gamana vidhāraṇa arthena pāñcagatika saṃsāra vidhāraṇa arthena tatra sva lakṣaṇa dhāraṇa arthena sarve sa āsravā anāsravāḥ ca dharmā iti ucyante kugati gamana vidhāraṇa arthena daśa kuśala ādayaḥ  dharmā iti ucyante dharma cārī sukham śete asmin  loke paratra ca pāñcagatika saṃsāra gamana vidhāraṇa arthena nirvāṇe dharma iti ucyate dharmam śaraṇam gacchati iti atra iha tu kugati gamana vidhāraṇa arthena eva dharma śabdaḥ  abhipretaḥ kim punar ātma saṃyamakam eva ekam cetaḥ dharma iti na iti āha kim tarhi para anugrāhakam ca maitram ca yad cetaḥ asau  api dharmaḥ maitram iti atra caśabdaḥ  lupta nirdiṣṭaḥ  veditavyaḥ tatra param anugṛhṇāti iti para anugrāhakam cetaḥ catur saṃgraha vastu pravṛttam bhaya paritrāṇa pravṛttam ca yad cetaḥ asau  api dharmaḥ mitre bhavam aviruddham sattveṣu yad cetaḥ tad maitram cetaḥ maitram yad cetaḥ tad maitra cetaḥ maitram evam vā yad ca etad  trividham cetaḥ  nirdiṣṭam sa dharma iti ucyate viparyayāt adharmaḥ  yojyaḥ yad ca etad nirdiṣṭa prabhedam cetaḥ tad bījam phalasya asādhāraṇam phala abhinirvṛttau yad kāraṇam tad eva bījam iti ucyate tad yathā śāli aṅkurasya śāli bījam yad tu sādhāraṇam kṣiti ādi na tad bījam kāraṇam etad  yathā etad evam iha api iṣṭasya vipākasya abhinirvṛttau trividham cetaḥ  bhavati bījam puruṣakāra ādayaḥ tu kāraṇam eva kasmin punar  kāle bījasya phala niṣpattiḥ iti āha pretya ca iha ca pretya iti adṛṣṭe janmani iha iti dṛṣṭe janmani iti arthaḥ etad ca āgamāt vistareṇa boddhavyam evam tāvat  citta ātmakam eva ekam dharmam vyavasthāpya punar api dvividham bhagavatā cetanā cetayitvā ca karma uktam parama ṛṣiṇā parama artha darśanāt ṛṣiḥ paramaḥ ca asau ṛṣiḥ ca iti parama ṛṣiḥ sarva ākāra tayā parama artha gamanāt  śrāvaka pratyekabuddhabhyaḥ  api utkṛṣṭa tvāt  parama ṛṣiḥ saṃbuddhaḥ  bhagavān tena parama ṛṣiṇā cetanā karma cetayitvā ca karma iti uktam sūtre yad ca etad  dvividham karma uktam tasya anekavidhaḥ bhedaḥ karmaṇaḥ parikīrtitaḥ katham kṛtvā tatra yad cetanā iti uktam karma tad mānasam smṛtam cetayitvā ca yad tu uktam tad tu kāyika vācikam manasi bhavam mānasam manaḥ dvāreṇa eva niṣṭhā gamanāt  kāya vāc pravṛtti nirapekṣa tvāt ca manaḥ vijñāna saṃprayuktā eva cetanā mānasam karma iti ucyate tatraśabdaḥ  nirdhāraṇe yad tu dvitīyam cetayitvā ca karma iti uktam tad punar  kāyikam vācikam ca veditavyam evam ca evam ca kāya vāgbhyām pravartiṣye iti evam cetasā saṃcintya yad  kriyate tad cetayitvā karma iti ucyate tad punar dvividham kāyikam vācikam ca kāya vācoḥ bhava tvāt  tad dvāreṇa ca niṣṭhā gamanāt  evam ca trividham kāyikam vācikam mānasam ca etad api trividham karma punar bhidyamānam saptavidham saṃjāyate iti evam tasya karmaṇaḥ  bhagavatā bahu prakāraḥ  bhedaḥ  anuvarṇitaḥ katham kṛtvā vāc viṣpandaḥ  aviratayaḥ  yāḥ ca avijñapti saṃjñitāḥ avijñaptaya eva anyāḥ smṛtā viratayaḥ tathā paribhoga anvayam puṇyam apuṇyam ca tathāvidham cetanā ca iti saptā ete dharmāḥ karma añjanāḥ smṛtāḥ tatra vyakta varṇa uccāraṇam vāc  viṣpandaḥ śarīraṃceṣṭā tatra kuśala akuśalā vā vāc  sarvā eva virati avirati lakṣaṇā vijñapti samutthāpikā sāmānyena vāc iti gṛhyate evam kuśalaḥ  akuśalaḥ  vā virati avirati lakṣaṇaḥ  vijñapti samutthāpa kaḥ  viṣpandaḥ sāmānyena gṛhyate yathā ca etad vijñapteḥ dvidhā bhedaḥ evam avijñapteḥ api avirati lakṣaṇā avijñaptayaḥ virati lakṣaṇāḥ ca iti kṛtvā tatra avirati lakṣaṇā avijñaptayaḥ tad yathā adya prabhṛti mayā prāṇinam hatvā cauryam kṛtvā jīvikā parikalpayitavyā iti pāpa karma abhyupagamāt prabhṛti tad akāriṇaḥ  api akuśala karma abhyupagama hetukāḥ satata samitam avijñaptayaḥ samupajāyante kaivarta ādīnāṃca jāla ādi parikarma kālāt prabhṛti tad akāriṇām api yā avijñaptaya upajāyante tā etā avirati lakṣaṇā avijñaptaya iti ucyante yathā ca etāḥ tathā anyāḥ virati lakṣaṇāḥ kuśala svabhāvā avijñaptayaḥ tad yathā adya prabhṛti prāṇa atipāta ādibhyaḥ prativiramāmi iti kāya vāc vijñapti parisamāptikā lakṣaṇāt prabhṛti tad uttara kālam pramatta ādi avasthasya api yāḥ kuśala upacaya svabhāvā avijñaptaya upajāyante tā etā virati lakṣaṇā avijñaptaya iti ucyante etā rūpa kriyā svabhāvā api satyaḥ  vijñaptivat  parān na vijñāpayanti iti avijñaptayaḥ tathā paribhoga anvayam puṇyam kuśalam iti arthaḥ paribhogena anvayaḥ asya iti paribhoga anvayam paribhogaḥ parityaktasya vastunaḥ saṃgha ādibhiḥ upabhogaḥ anvayaḥ anugamaḥ dāyaka saṃtāna jaḥ kuśala upacaya iti arthaḥ apuṇyam ca tathāvidham paribhoga anvayam iti arthaḥ tad yathā devakula ādi pratiṣṭhāpanam yatra sattvā hanyante yathā yathā hi tad kīrtau prāṇinaḥ  hanyante tathā tathā tad deva kula ādi upabhogāt tad kartṛṇām saṃtāne paribhoga an vayam apuṇyam api jāyate iti evam apuṇyam ca tathāvidham bhavati citta abhisaṃskāra manaskarma lakṣaṇā cetanā ca iti saṃkṣepeṇa etad saptavidham karma bhavati kuśala akuśalā vāc  kuśala akuśalaḥ  viṣpandaḥ kuśalam avijñapti lakṣaṇam akuśalam avijñapti lakṣaṇam paribhoga anvayam puṇyam paribhoga anvayam apuṇyam cetanā ca iti ete ca sapta dharmāḥ karma añjanāḥ karma tvena abhivyaktāḥ karma lakṣaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ atra eke paricodayanti yad etad  karma bahuvidham uktam tad  kimā vipāka kālāt avatiṣṭhate atha na tiṣṭhati utpatti anantara vināśi tvāt  yadi tāvat  tiṣṭhatyā pāka kālāt ced karma tad nitya tām iyāt niruddham ced niruddham sat kim phalam janayiṣyati yadi utpannam sat  karma āvipāka kālam svarūpeṇa avatiṣṭhate iti parikalpyate tad  iyantam kālam asya nitya tā āpadyate vināśa rahita tvāt  paścāt vināśa sadbhāvāt na nitya tvam iti ced  na etad evam pūrvam vināśa rahitasya ākāśa ādivat  paścāt api vināśena saṃbandha abhāvāt  vināśa rahitasya ca asaṃskṛtatva prasaṅgāt  asaṃskṛtānām ca vipāka adarśanāt  avipāka tvena sadā eva avasthānāt nitya tā abhyupagama eva karmaṇām upapadyate iti evam tāvat nitya tve doṣaḥ atha utpāda anantara vināśi tvam eva karmaṇām abhyupetam nanu evam sati niruddham ced niruddham sat  kim phalam janayiṣyati abhāvībhūtam sat  karma avidyamāna svabhāva tvāt na eva phalam janayiṣyati iti abhiprāyaḥ tatra eke nikāya antarīyāḥ parihāram varṇayanti utpatti anantara vināśi tvāt saṃskārāṇām anityatva doṣaḥ tāvat asmākam na upapadyate yad ca api uktam niruddham ced niruddham sat  kim phalam janayiṣyati iti atra api parihāram brūmaḥ yaḥ  aṅkura prabhṛtiḥ bījāt saṃtānaḥ  abhipravartate tatas  phalam ṛte bījāt sa ca na abhipravartate iha bījam kṣaṇikam api sat  sva jātīya bhāvi phala viśeṣa niṣpatti sāmarthya viśeṣa yuktasya eva saṃtānasya aṅkura kāṇḍa nāla patra ādi abhidhānasya hetu bhāvam api upagamya nirudhyate yaḥ ca ayam aṅkura prabhṛtiḥ bījāt saṃtānaḥ pravartate tasmāt  krameṇa sahakāri kāraṇa vaikalye sati su alpāt api hetoḥ vipula phala pracaya upajāyate ṛte bījāt  vinā bījāt  sa ca aṅkura ādi saṃtānaḥ na abhipravartate tad evam tad bhāve bhāvi tvena tad abhāve ca abhāvi tvena bīja hetuka tvam aṅkura ādi saṃtānasya phalasya upadarśitam bhavati tad evam bījāt ca yasmāt saṃtānaḥ saṃtānāt ca phala udbhavaḥ bīja pūrvam phalam tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam yadi iha bījam aprasūya aṅkura ādi saṃtānam jvālā aṅgāra ādi virodhi pratyaya sāṃnidhyāt nirudhyeta tadā tatra kārya saṃtāna pravṛtti adarśanāt syāt uccheda darśanam yadi ca bījam na nirudhyeta aṅkura ādi saṃtānaḥ ca pravarteta tadā bījasya anirodha abhyupagamāt śāśvata darśanam syāt  na ca etad evam iti atas  na asti bījasya śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ yathā ca bīje ayam kramaḥ  anuvarṇitaḥ evam yaḥ tasmāt citta saṃtānaḥ cetasaḥ  abhipravartate tatas  phalam ṛte cittāt sa ca na abhipravartate tasmāt  kuśala akuśala cetanā viśeṣa saṃprayuktāt cittāt  yaḥ citta saṃtānaḥ tad hetukaḥ pravartate tasmāt  kuśala akuśala cetanā paribhāvitāt citta saṃtānāt sahakāri kāraṇa saṃnidhāna avaikalye sati iṣṭam aniṣṭam phalam upajāyate sugati durgatiṣu ṛte tu tad citāt  cittam antareṇa sa ca na abhipravartate tad evam cittāt ca yasmāt saṃtānaḥ saṃtānāt ca phala udbhavaḥ karma pūrvam phalam tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam yadi arhat carama cittam iva tad hetu phala pāraṃparya avicchinna krama vartinaḥ  bhāvinaḥ citta saṃtānasya hetu bhāvam anupagamya kuśalam cittam nirudhyeta tadā ucchinnam tad karma syāt  atha api anāgata saṃtānasya hetu bhāvam upagamya svarūpāt apracyutam syāt  syāt tadānīm karma śāśvatam na ca etad evam iti tasmāt  kṣaṇika karma abhyupagame api na asti uccheda śāśvata darśana dvaya prasaṅga iti tad atra yathā udita karma prabheda vyākhyāne daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathā vyākhyātāḥ te ca dharmasya sādhana upāyāḥ śuklāḥ karma pathā daśa phalam kāma guṇāḥ pañca dharmasya pretya ca iha ca ta ete daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathā dharmasya sādhana upāyā niṣpatti hetu bhūtā iti arthaḥ kaḥ punar asau kuśala karma patha vyatiriktaḥ  dharmaḥ  nāma yasya ete sādhana upāya tvena vyavasthāpyante ucyate citta viśeṣa eva kaścid  dharma śabdena uktaḥ ātma saṃyamakam cetaḥ para anugrāhakam ca yad  maitram sa dharmaḥ iti anena athavā pariniṣṭhita rūpā ete daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathā dharma śabda vācyā bhavanti kriyamāṇa rūpāḥ tu kuśala karma patha vācyā bhavanti tad asya ukta lakṣaṇasya ete daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathā niṣpattau hetu tvena vyavasthāpyante katham punar atra prakrānte karma vibhāge daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathā iti ucyate vāc viṣpandaḥ  aviratayaḥ  yāḥ ca avijñapti saṃjñitāḥ ityādinā kāyikā srayaḥ karma pathāḥ vācikāḥ catvāraḥ  vyākhyātāḥ cetanā ca iti anena abhidhyā vyāpāt samyak dṛṣṭayā ākhya asrayaḥ mānasā vyākhyātāḥ iti evam daśā api kuśalāḥ karma pathā atra vyākhyātāḥ te ca yathā uditasya dharmasya niṣpatti hetavaḥ  bhavanti asya ca dharmasya rūpa śabda gandha rasa spraṣṭavya lakṣaṇāḥ pañca kāma guṇāḥ pretya ca adṛṣṭe para loke iti arthaḥ iha ca iti ihaloke iti arthaḥ phalam upabhujyate iti evam tāvat aika nikāyikaiḥ ākṣepa parihāre varṇite sati tān prati apare doṣam udbhāvya anya ākṣepa parihāram varṇayantaḥ āhuḥ bahavaḥ ca mahāntaḥ ca doṣāḥ syuḥ api kalpanā yadi eṣā tena na eva eṣā kalpanātra upapadyate yadi bīja aṅkura sādharmyeṇa citta saṃtāne śāśvata uccheda darśana dvaya doṣa prasaṅga parihāraḥ syāt  tadā bahavaḥ ca doṣāḥ saṃkhyā bahu tvena mahāntaḥ ca dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa virodhena para pakṣe prāpruvanti katham kṛtvā yadi hi bīja saṃtāna dṛṣṭāntena śāli bījāt  śāli aṅkura ādi saṃtāna eva pravartate na vijātīyaḥ śāli aṅkura ādi saṃtānāt ca śāli phalam eva upajāyate na bilva phalam bhinna jātīya tvāt  evam iha api kuśala cittāt  kuśala citta saṃtāna eva syāt  samāna jātīya tvāt na akuśala avyākṛta citta saṃtānaḥ vijātīya tvāt  evam akuśala avyākṛta cittāt akuśala avyākṛta citta saṃtāna eva syāt na anyaḥ bhinna jātīya tvāt  kāmarūpā rūpya avacarān āsrava cittebhyaḥ sadṛśānām eva cittānām kāmarūpā rūpya avacarān āsravāṇām utpādaḥ syāt  na bhinna jātīyānām manuṣya cittān manuṣya cittam eva syāt na deva nāraka tiryak ādi anya cittam tatas ca yaḥ  devaḥ sa deva eva syāt  yaḥ  manuṣyaḥ sa manuṣya eva syāt ityādi tatas ca akuśalam api kurvatām deva manuṣyāṇām gati yoni varṇa buddhīndriya bala rūpa bhoga ādi vaicitryam na syāt apāya patanam ca iṣyate ca etad sarvam iti evam bahavaḥ ca mahāntaḥ ca doṣā yasmāt bīja saṃtāna sādharmya kalpanāyām prasajyante tasmāt na eṣā kalpanā atra upapadyate imām punar  pravakṣyāmi kalpanām yātra yojyate buddhaiḥ pratyekabuddhaiḥ ca śrāvakaiḥ ca anuvarṇitām kā ca asau kalpanā iti āha patram yathā vipraṇāśaḥ tathā ṛṇam iva karma ca caturvidhaḥ  dhātutaḥ sa prakṛtyā vyākṛtaḥ ca saḥ iha kuśalam karma kṛtam sat  utpāda anantaram eva nirudhyate na ca tasmin niruddhe phala abhāva prasaṅgaḥ yasmāt  yadā eva tad karma utpadyate tadā etasya karmaṇaḥ  avipraṇāśaḥ  nāma viprayuktaḥ  dharmaḥ kartuḥ saṃtāne samupajāyate ṛṇa patra sthānīyaḥ tad evam patram yathā avipraṇāśaḥ tathā veditavyaḥ yasya ca asau avipraṇāśa ākhyaḥ  dharma utpadyate ṛṇam iva tad karma veditavyam yathā ca ṛṇa patra avasthānāt prayukte api dhane dhaninaḥ na dhana nāśaḥ  bhavati saṃbadhyata eva sa kāla antareṇa pañcamena dhana skandhena tathā vinaṣṭe api karmaṇi avipraṇāśa ākhya dharma antara avasthānāt tad nimittakena phalena abhisaṃbadhyata eva kartā yathā ca ṛṇa patram dātuḥ dhana abhyāgamam kṛtvā nirmuktam sat  punar api vidyamānam vā avidyamānam vā na dhana abhyāgame samartham evam avipraṇāśaḥ  api datta vipākaḥ san vidyamānaḥ  vā avidyamānaḥ  vā na śaknoti nirmukta patravat  kartuḥ punar api vipāka saṃbandham kartum yaḥ ca ayam avipraṇāśaḥ  asmābhiḥ uktaḥ sūtra antara uktaḥ caturvidhaḥ  dhātutaḥ sa kāmarūpā rūpya avacara an āsrava bhedāt  prakṛtyā avyākṛtaḥ ca saḥ kuśala akuśala tvena avyākaraṇāt avyākṛta eva avipraṇāśaḥ yadi asau akuśalānām karmaṇā ām akuśalaḥ syāt  tadā kāmam vīta rāgāṇām na syāt  yadi ca kuśalānām kuśalaḥ syāt  samucchinna kuśala mūlānām sa na syāt  tasmāt  prakṛti avyākṛta eva asau kim ca prahāṇataḥ  na praheyaḥ  bhāvanā āheya eva vā sa ca ayam avipraṇāśaḥ prahāṇataḥ  na praheyaḥ pārthak janikāni karmāṇi darśana mārgeṇa eva prahīyante mā bhūt āryaḥ pṛthagjana karma samanvāgata iti avipraṇāśaḥ tu tad karma prahāṇe api darśana mārgeṇa na prahīyate kim tu bhāvanā mārgeṇa vā tasyāḥ  prahāṇam bhavati dhātu samatikramaṇa praheya eva iti vā śabdaḥ  vikalpa arthaḥ yatas ca evam avipraṇāśaḥ karma vināśe api na naśyati karma prahāṇe api na prahīyate tasmāt avipraṇāśena jāyate karmaṇām phalam yadi punar api asya avipraṇāśasya karmaṇaḥ prahāṇena prahāṇāt prahāṇataḥ prahāṇam syāt  karmaṇaḥ ca saṃkrameṇa karmaṇaḥ  vināśena karma antara saṃmukhībhāvena vināśaḥ syāt  kaḥ  doṣaḥ syāt iti ucyate prahāṇataḥ praheyaḥ syāt karmaṇaḥ saṃkrameṇa vā yadi doṣāḥ prasajyeran  tatra karma vadha ādayaḥ yadi darśana mārgeṇa pārthagjanika karmavat avipraṇāśaḥ prahīyeta tadā karmaṇaḥ  vināśa eva syāt  karma vināśāt ca āryāṇām iṣṭa aniṣṭa karma phala vipākaḥ pūrva karma phala hetu kaḥ  na syāt  akṛtasya eva karmaṇaḥ phala udayaḥ syāt  karma phala abhāva darśanāt ca mithyā darśanam syāt iti evam karma vadha āt ayaḥ  doṣāḥ prasajyante prahāṇataḥ praheyatva abhyupagame sati avipraṇāśasya evam karmaṇaḥ saṃkrame api yojyam sarveṣām viṣa bhāgānām sabhāgānām ca karmaṇām pratisaṃdhau sa dhātūnām eka utpadyate tu saḥ bhinna jātīyāni karmāṇi viṣa bhāgāni sadṛśāni sa bhāgāni teṣām sarveṣām eva sabhāgānām ca viṣa bhāgānām ca karmaṇām kāmarūpa ārūpya dhātu pratisaṃdhiṣu sarva karma apamardanaḥ eka eva avipraṇāśa utpadyate sa ca api sa dhātūnām samāna dhātukānām eva utpadyate na viṣa bhāga dhātukānām karmaṇaḥ karmaṇaḥ  dṛṣṭe dharma utpadyate tu saḥ dvi prakārasya sarvasya vipakke api ca tiṣṭhati sa ca ayam avipraṇāśa ākhyaḥ  dharmaḥ sarvasya eva karmaṇaḥ cetanā cetayitvā svabhāvasya sa āsravānāsrava bhedena vā dvi prakāra bhinnasya dṛṣṭe dharme iha eva janmani karmaṇaḥ karmaṇaḥ ekaikaḥ  avipraṇāśa utpadyate sa ca ayam avipraṇāśaḥ  vipakke api vipāke na avaśyam nirudhyate nirbhukta patravat ca vidyamānaḥ  api san na śaknoti punar api vipaktum phala vyatikramāt vā sa maraṇāt vā nirudhyate anāsravam sa āsravam ca vibhāgam tatra lakṣayet  tatra phala vyatikramāt nirudhyate yathā uktam bhāvanā āheya eva iti maraṇāt nirudhyate yathā uktam pratisaṃdhau sa dhātūnām eka utpadyate tu saḥ iti sa ca ayam sa āsravāṇām sa āsravaḥ anāsravāṇām anāsravaḥ iti evam vibhāgam lakṣayet  tad evam śūnyatā ca na ca ucchedaḥ saṃsāraḥ ca na śāśvatam karmaṇaḥ  avipraṇāśaḥ ca dharmaḥ  buddhena deśitaḥ yasmāt  karma kṛtam sat  nirudhyate na svabhāvena avatiṣṭhate tasmāt  karmaṇaḥ svabhāvena avasthānāt śūnyatā ca upapadyate na ca evam karmaṇaḥ  anavasthānāt uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ avipraṇāśa parigraheṇa karma vipāka sadbhāvāt vipāka abhāve hi karmaṇaḥ uccheda darśanam syāt  avipraṇāśa dharma sadbhāvāt bīja saṃtāna sādharmya parikalpanā bhāvāt ca nānā gati jāti yoni dhātu bheda bhinnaḥ ca pāñcagatikaḥ saṃsāraḥ  vicitraḥ siddhaḥ  bhavati na ca śāśvata vāda prasaṅgaḥ karmaṇaḥ sva rūpeṇa avasthāna anabhyupagamāt karmaṇām ca avipraṇāśaḥ avipraṇāśa sadbhāvāt  iti evam niravaśeṣa avidyā nidrā apagamāt vibuddhena bhagavatā yasmāt ayam dharmaḥ  deśitaḥ tasmāt  yad pūrvaṃmuktam pareṇa tiṣṭhatyā pāka kālāt ced  karma tad nitya tām iyāt niruddham ced niruddham sat  kim phalam janayiṣyati iti tad asmad pakṣe na upapadyate iti tasmāt asmābhiḥ upavarṇita kalpanā eva nyāyyā iti atra ucyate kim iha bhavantaḥ  gandharvanagara prākāra patana atiśaṅkitayā atīva udvignāḥ tad parirakṣā pariśramāyāsam āpannāḥ ye nāma yūyam karmaṇi anupapadyamāne tad phala nimittam vipra vadadhvam yadi hi karmaṇaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva utpādaḥ syāt  tasya āvipākam avasthānāt nitya tvam syāt  vināśāt ucchedaḥ syāt  yadā tu karma na eva utpadyate svabhāva śūnyatvāt tadā tasya kutaḥ avasthānam vināśaḥ  vā yata eṣā cintā syāt  atra āha karma na utpadyate kasmāt  ācārya āha niḥsvabhāvam yatas tatas  yasmāt niḥsvabhāvam karma tasmāt na utpadyate yadi khalu evam niḥsvabhāva tvāt karma na utpadyate tad  katham evam uktam bhagavatā na praṇaśyanyi karmāṇi kalpa koṭi śataiḥ api sāmagrīm prāpya kālam ca phalanti khalu dehinām iti ucyate yasmāt ca tad anutpannam na tasmāt vipraṇaśyati iti evam bhagavataḥ  abhiprāya iti atas  na ayam asmākam bādhakaḥ  vidhiḥ iti avaśyam ca etad evam vijñeyam niḥsvabhāvam karma iti anyathā hi karma svabhāvataḥ ced syāt śāśvatam syāt asaṃśayam akṛtam ca bhavet karma kriyate na hi śāśvatam yadi hi karma svabhāvataḥ syāt  mukta saṃśayam tad śāśvatam syāt  svabhāvasya anyathā bhāva abhāvāt  tatas ca akṛtam eva karma bhavet  kartuḥ svatantrasya kriyayā yadīpsitatamam tad karma etad ca na yujyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt  kriyate na hi śāśvatam śāśvatam hi nāma tad  yad vidyamāna sattākam yad ca vidyamānam tasya karaṇa anupapatteḥ tad na eva kāraṇam apekṣata iti śubha aśubhe karmaṇi akṛta eva sakalasya lokasya vipākaḥ  yasmāt  tatas ca akṛta abhyāgam bhayam syāt karma akṛtakam yadi abrahmacarya vāsaḥ ca doṣaḥ tatra prasajyate yadi hi akṛtam karma bhavet  tadā akṛta abhyāgam bhayam syāt  yena api hi prāṇa atipāta ādikam na kṛtam tasya api akṛtam api sat  tad  karma asti eva iti tena api asya saṃbandhāt akṛta abhyāgam bhayam syāt  abrahmacarya vāsaḥ ca tatra pakṣe prāpnoti kim kāraṇam pariśuddha brahmacarya vāsān na kasyacid nirvāṇena bhavitavyam syāt  kim ca atas  vyavahārā virudhyante sarva eva na saṃśayaḥ puṇya pāpa kṛtoḥ na eva pravibhāgaḥ ca yujyate ye hi ete kṛṣi vāṇijya gorakṣa ādayaḥ kriyā ārambhāḥ phala artham ārabhyante teṣām sarveṣām akṛtānām eva vidyamāna tvāt  prārambha vaiyarthyam syāt  ghaṭam kuru paṭam kuru iti evamādayaḥ ca sarva eva laukika vyavahārā virudhyante ghaṭa ādīnām sarveṣām eva vidyamāna tvāt  puṇya kṛt ayam pāpa kṛt ayam iti ca pravibhāgaḥ  na prāpnoti ubhayoḥ api puṇya pāpa kṛtoḥ akṛtayoḥ api puṇya pāpayoḥ pratyekam vidyamāna tvāt  kim ca tad vipakva vipākam ca punar eva vipakṣyati karma vyavasthitam yasmāt tasmāt svābhāvikam yadi vipakva vipākasya api karmaṇaḥ punar vipāka dānam āpadyate sva rūpāt apracyuta tvāt avipakva vipāka avasthāyām iva tad evam yadi karma svābhāvikam iti manyase yasmāt  tad karma vyavasthitam asti tasmāt niḥsaṃśayam yathā upavarṇitā doṣāḥ prāpnuvanti sa svabhāva tve tasmāt niḥsvabhāvam karma yatas ca niḥsvabhāvam karma tasmāt śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ  na eva asmākam evam vyācakṣamāṇānām āpadyate iti atra āha vidyata eva svabhāvataḥ karma tad kāraṇa sadbhāvāt iha yad na asti na tasya kāraṇam asti [kūrma] romakūpa prāvārasya iva asti ca karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam kleśāḥ avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ upādāna pratyayaḥ bhavaḥ iti vacanāt  tasmāt vidyata eva karma svabhāvataḥ iti ucyate ayuktam eva kim kāraṇam yasmāt  karma kleśa ātmakam ca idam te ca kleśā na tattvataḥ na ced te tattvataḥ kleśāḥ karma syāt tattvataḥ katham iha idam karma kleśa ātmakam kleśa hetukam te ca kleśāḥ tattvataḥ  na santi vakṣyati hi śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya ye te svabhāvāt na vidyante tasmāt kleśā na tattvataḥ iti tad evam tāvat  na tattvataḥ kleśāḥ tad hetukam karma tadānīm kutas tattvataḥ  bhaviṣyati tasmāt na asti karma svabhāvataḥ atra āha vidyanta eva kleśā karmāṇi ca tad kārya sadbhāvāt iha hi kleśa karmaṇām deha ākhyam kāryam upalabhyate yasya ca kāryam upalabhyate tad asti avidyamānasya kha puṣpa ādeḥ kārya adarśanāt  iti ucyate syuḥ kleśāḥ karmāṇi ca yadi tad kāryam dehā vidyeran na tu vidyante iti āha karma kleśāḥ ca dehānām pratyayāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ karma kleśāḥ ca te śūnyā yadi deheṣu kā kathā yathā karma kleśāḥ ca śūnyāḥ tathā pratipāditam tatas ca karma kleśā yadā na santi tadā tad kāryāṇām dehānām asattve kā kathā bhaviṣyati na astitvam teṣām pūrvam eva siddham yasmāt  tasmāt na anna kaścid vaktavya viśeṣaḥ  asti iti abhiprāyaḥ atra āha vidyata eva svabhāvataḥ karma tad phala bhoktṛ sadbhāvāt yad na asti na tasya phala upabhoktā asti tad yathā gagana cūta phalasya iti asti ca karmaṇaḥ phala upabha uktā avidyā nivṛtaḥ  jantuḥ tṛṣṇā saṃyojanaḥ ca saḥ sa bhoktā sa ca na kartuḥ anyaḥ  na ca sa eva saḥ tatra avidyā ajñānam tamaḥ saṃmoha iti paryāyāḥ avidyayā nivṛtaḥ chāditaḥ pāñcagatika saṃsāre punar  punar jāyata iti jantuḥ sattvaḥ pudgalaḥ prāṇi iti tasya eva paryāyāḥ tṛṣṇā rāgaḥ saktiḥ visaktiḥ ca iti paryāyāḥ saṃyojanam bandhanam tṛṣṇā saṃyojanam asya iti tṛṣṇā saṃyojanaḥ tṛṣṇā bandhana iti arthaḥ yathā uktam sūtre avidyā nivṛtāḥ sattvāḥ tṛṣṇā saṃyojanāḥ iti atha ca punar idam pāpam karma svayam eva kṛtam asya svayam eva vipākaḥ pratyanubhavitavyaḥ iti vacanāt  sa ca bhoktā karma phalasya sa ca na kartuḥ anyaḥ na ca sa eva saḥ tattva anyatva avācya tvāt tasmāt  phala upabhoktṛ sadbhāvāt asti eva karma iti atra ucyate syāt karmaṇaḥ kartā karma phalasya ca upabhoktā yadi karma eva syāt  na tu asti katham kṛtvā na pratyaya samutpannam na apratyaya samutthitam asti yasmāt idam karma tasmāt kartā api na asti atas  karma ced na asti kartā ca kutas  syāt karma jam phalam asati atha phale bhoktā kuta eva bhaviṣyati yadi karma nāma kiṃcid syāt  tad  pratyaya samutpannam vā bhavet  apratyaya samutpannam vā yadi tāvat  pratyaya samutpannam iṣyate tad na yuktam pratyaya parīkṣāyām ukta doṣa tvāt atha apratyaya janitam nirhetukam tad api hetau  asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca ityādinā karma kāraka parīkṣāyām vistareṇa pratipāditam yatas ca evam pratyaya samutpannam vā apratyaya samutpannam vā karma idam na saṃbhavati tasmāt asya karmaṇaḥ kartā api na saṃbhavati yadā ca evam karma ca kartā ca na asti tadā nirhetukam karma jam phalam kutaḥ bhaviṣyati iti asati ca phale kuta eva phala bhoktā bhaviṣyati iti sarvam etad  svabhāvataḥ  asaṃvidyamānam eva iti vijñeyam atra āha yadi evam naiḥsvābhāvyam bhāvānām vyavasthāpitam bhavati yad tarhi etad uktam bhagavatā svayam kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ svayam eva vipākaḥ pratyanubhavitavyaḥ iti tad etad sarvam amunā nyāyena apākṛtam bhavati karma phala apavādāt ca pradhāna nāstikaḥ  bhavān iti ucyate na vayam nāstikāḥ astitva nā astitva dvaya vāda nirāsena tu vayam nirvāṇa pura gāmi nam advaya patham vidyotayāmaḥ na ca karma kartṛ phala ādikam na asti iti brūma kim tarhi niḥsvabhāvam etad iti vyavasthāpayāmaḥ atha manyase niḥsvabhāvānām bhāvānām vyāpāra karaṇa anupapatteḥ tad avastha eva doṣa iti etad api na asti sa svabhāvānām eva vyāpāra adarśanāt  niḥsvabhāvānām eva vyāpāra darśanāt  tathā hi niḥsvabhāvā eva santaḥ  ghaṭa ādayaḥ loke sva kārya kṛt  upalabhyante api ca amuṣmād dṛṣṭāntāt  spaṣṭatarāt ayam arthaḥ  avasīyatām yathā nirmitakam śāstā nirmimīta ṛddhi saṃpadā nirmitaḥ  nirmimīta anyam sa ca nirmitakaḥ punar  tad yathā ekam nirmitakam śāstā buddhaḥ  bhagavān ṛddhi saṃpadā ṛddhi prabhāveṇa nirmimīta sa ca api nirmitakaḥ punar  yaḥ  ayam buddhena bhagavatā nirmitaḥ sa punar bhūyaḥ anyam aparam nirmitakam nirmimīta tatra ya eṣa nirmitakaḥ aparasya nirmitakasya nirmātā sa śūnyaḥ niḥsvabhāvaḥ tathāgata svabhāva rahita iti arthaḥ yaḥ ca ayam aparaḥ  nirmitakaḥ yoniḥ mitakena nirmitaḥ asau  api śūnyaḥ  nisvabhāvaḥ tathāgata svabhāva rahita iti arthaḥ yathā atra niḥsvabhāvānām nisvabhāva kārya kṛt tvam karma kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ ca bhavati tathā nirmitaka ākāraḥ kartā karma ca tad kṛtam tad yathā nirmitena anyaḥ  nirmitaḥ  nirmitaḥ tathā yaḥ  hi atra karmaṇaḥ kartā sa nirmitaka ākāraḥ svabhāva śūnyaḥ tena ca svabhāva śūnyena svatantra kartrā yad  kiṃcid  karma kriyate tad api svabhāva śūnyam tad yathā nirmitakena anyaḥ  nirmitakaḥ  nirmitaḥ tathā veditavyam yathoktam āgame ekasya bhāṣamāṇasya sarve bhāṣanti nirmitāḥ ekasya tūṣṇīṃbhūtasya sarve tūṣṇīṃbhavanti hi tasmāt advaya vādinām mādhyamikānām kutaḥ mithyā darśanam uktam ca ārya samādhi rāje yada sugatu kathām kathā iti nāthaḥ  vīthi gatān manujān kṛpāyamānaḥ nirmita jinu tatra nirminitva vicarati teṣu praṇīta buddha dharmān prāṇi śata sahasra tam śruṇitvā praṇidadhayiṃsu vara agra buddha jñāne kada vaya labhi jñānam eva rūpam āśaya jñātva jinaḥ asya vyākaroti raśmi śata sahasra aprameyān avasiri pāda talehi dharmarājā sarvi niraya śītalā bhavanti dukham apanīya sukham ca vedayanti dharma daśa bala prabhāṣite atra marum anujāna viśuddha bhoti cakṣuḥ ityādi keci spṛha janenti tatra kāle parama  acintya tehi labdha lābhā yehi jinu nimantritaḥ  narendraḥ  na ca pariyanta teṣu dakṣiṇāyā ityādi vistaraḥ tathā ārya vimala kīrti nirdeśe tad nirmita bodhisattvena gandha sugandhāyām lokadhātau samantabhadra tathā gata upabhukta śeṣam bhojanam ānītam nānā vyañjana kha ādya ādi saṃprayuktam pṛthak pṛthak vividha rasam eka bhojanena sarvam tad śrāvaka bodhisattva saṃgha rāja rāja amātya purohita antaḥ pura dauvārika sārthavāha ādi janapadam saṃtarpya prīti ākāram nāma mahā samādhim lambhayāmāsa iti vinaye ca paṭhayate pāpa bhikṣuḥ apratirūpa kaḥ bhagavatā bhikṣuḥ abhinirmitaḥ tad vacanena śīlavataḥ  api viśuddhi pratijñā saṃvāsaḥ prajñaptaḥ iti na ca kevalam nirmāṇa dṛṣṭāntena naiḥsvabhāvya darśanam upapadyamāna rūpam api ca amībhyaḥ  dṛṣṭāntebhyaḥ sphuṭam naiḥsvabhāvyam bhāvānām pratīyatām iti pratipādayan  āha kleśāḥ karmāṇi dehāḥ ca kartāraḥ ca phalāni ca gandharvanagara ākārā marīci svapna saṃnibhāḥ tatra kleśā rāga ādayaḥ kliśnanti sattva citta saṃtānāni iti kṛtvā karmāṇi kuśala akuśalāneñjyāni dehāḥ śarīrāṇi kartāraḥ ātmānaḥ phalāni vipāka ādhipatya niṣyanda ādīni ta ete kleśāt ayaḥ  arthāḥ gandharvanagara ādivat niḥsvabhāvāḥ veditavyāḥ tasmāt mādhyamikānām eva bhāvānām svabhāva anabhyupagamāt śāśvata uccheda darśana dvaya prasaṅgaḥ  na asti iti vijñeyam atra ca karma phala saṃbandha vicāre kuca udya śeṣa ākṣepa parihāraḥ  madhyamaka avatārāt vistareṇa avaseyaḥ yathā uktam ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre pañca ca bhikṣu śatāni dhyāna lābhīni utthāya āsanebhyaḥ prakrāntāni imām gambhīrām dharma deśa nāmanavabudhyamānāni anavataranti anavagāhamānāni anadhimucyamānāni bhagavān āha tathā hi ete kāśyapa bhikṣavaḥ ābhimānikāḥ imām anāsravān śīla viśuddhim na avataranti na avagāhante na adhimucyante uttrasyanti saṃtrasyanti saṃtrāsam āpadyante gambhīraḥ kāśyapa gāthā abhinirhāraḥ  gambhīrā ca buddhānām bhagavatām bodhiḥ sā na śakyā anavaropita kuśala mūlaiḥ sattvaiḥ pāpa mitra parigṛhītaiḥ anadhi mukti bahulaiḥ adhimoktum api ca etāni kāśyapa pañca bhikṣu śatāni kāśyapasya tathāgatasya pravacane anya tīrthika śrāvakā abhūvan taiḥ eva tasya kāśyapasya tathāgatasya antikāt upālambha abhiprāyaiḥ eṣā dharma deśanā śrutā śrutvā ca ekacitta prasādaḥ  labdhaḥ evaṃtaiḥ vāc  bhāṣitā āścaryam yāvat  madhurapriyamāṇī kāśyapaḥ tathāgataḥ  arhan samyaksaṃbuddha iti ta etena eka citta prasādena pratilabdhena kālagatāḥ trāyastriṃśeṣu deveṣu upapannāḥ te tatas cyutāḥ samānāḥ iha upapannāḥ tena eva ca hetunā iha mama śāsane pravrajitāḥ tāni etāni kāśyapa pañca bhikṣu śatāni dṛṣṭi praskandhāni imām gambhīrām dharma deśanām na avataranti na avagāhante na adhimucyante uttrasyanti saṃtrasyanti saṃtrāsam āpadyante kṛtam punar eṣām anayā dharma deśanayā parikarma na bhūyaḥ durgati vinipātam gamiṣyanti ebhiḥ eva ca skandhaiḥ parinirvāsyanti atha khalu bhagavān āyuṣmantam subhūtim āmantrayate sma gaccha subhūte etān bhikṣūn saṃjña patha subhūtiḥ āha bhagavata eva tāvat ete bhāṣitam vilomayanti kaḥ punarvādaḥ  mama atha bhagavān  tasyām velāyām yena mārgeṇa ete bhikṣāvaḥ  gacchanti sma tasmin mārge drau bhikṣū nirmimīte sma atha tāni pañca bhikṣu śatāni yena mārgeṇa tau dvau bhikṣū nirmitakau tena upasaṃkrāmanti sma upasaṃkramya etad avocan kutra āyuṣmantau gamiṣyathaḥ tau  avocatām gamiṣyāva āvām araṇya āyataneṣu tatra dhyāna sukha saṃsparśa vihāraiḥ vihariṣyāvaḥ tāni api pañca bhikṣu śatāni etad avocan vayam api āyuṣmantau bhagavataḥ  dharma deśanām na avatarāmaḥ  na avagāhāmahe na adhimucyāmahe uttrasyāmaḥ saṃtrasyāmaḥ saṃtrāsam āpadyāmahe tena vayam araṇya āyataneṣu dhyāna sukha saṃsparśa vihāraiḥ vihariṣyāma iti nirmitakau  avocatām tena hi āyuṣmantaḥ saṃgāsyāmaḥ  na vivadiṣyāmaḥ avivāda paramaḥ  hi śramaṇa dharmaḥ yad idam āyuṣmanta ucyate parinirvāṇam iti katamaḥ sa dharmaḥ  yaḥ parinirvāsyati kaścid punar atra kāyaḥ ātmā vā sattvaḥ  vā jīvaḥ  vā jantuḥ vā poṣaḥ  vā puruṣaḥ  vā pudgalaḥ  vā manujaḥ  vā mānavaḥ  va yaḥ parinirvāsyati kasya vā kṣayāt  parinirvāṇam te avocan rāga dveṣa moha kṣayāt parinirvāṇam nirmitakau  avocatām kim punar āyuṣmatām saṃvidyante rāga dveṣa mohā yān kṣayiṣyatha te avocan na te adhyātmam na bahirdhā na ubhayam antareṇa upalabhyante na api te aparikalpitā utpadyante iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau karma phala parīkṣā nāma saptadaśamam prakaraṇam ātma parīkṣā aṣṭādaśamam prakaraṇam atra āha yadi kleśāḥ karmāṇi ca dehāḥ ca kartāraḥ ca phalāni ca sarvam etad na tattvam kevalaṃtu gandharvanagara ādivadatta tvam eva sat  tattva ākāreṇa pratibhāsate bālānām kim punar atra tattvam katham vā tattvasya avatāraḥ iti ucyate ādhyātmika bāhya aśeṣa vastu anupalambhena adhyātmam bahis ca yaḥ sarvathā ahaṃkāra m amakāra parikṣayaḥ idam atra tattvam tattva avatāraḥ punar  sat kāya dṛṣṭi prabhavān aśeṣān kleśān  ca doṣān  ca dhiyā vipaśyan ātmānam asya viṣayam ca buddhā yogī karoti ātma niṣedham eva ityādinā madhyamaka avatārāt vistareṇa avaseyaḥ kāya dṛṣṭi mūlakam eva saṃsāram anupaśyan ātma anupalambhāt ca sat kāya dṛṣṭi prahāṇam tad prahāṇāt ca sarva kleśa vyāvṛttim samanupaśyan prathamataram ātmānam eva upaparīkṣate kaḥ  ayam ātmā nāma iti yaḥ  ahaṃkāra viṣayaḥ sa ca ayam ahaṃkārasya viṣayaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ skandha svabhāvaḥ  vā bhavet skandha vyatiriktaḥ  vā ādhāra ādheya tadvat pakṣāṇām api ekatva anyatva pakṣe eva antar bhāvāt  saṃkṣepeṇa eva ca vivakṣita tvāt ekatva anyatva pakṣa dvaya pratiṣedhena eva ātma niṣedham ārabdhu kāma ācārya āha ātmā skandhā yadi bhavet udayavyaya bhāj bhavet  skandhebhyaḥ  anyaḥ  yadi bhavet bhavet askandha lakṣaṇaḥ kimartha punar anyatra tathāgata parīkṣāyām agni in dhana parīkṣāyām ca pañca pañca pakṣā upanyastāḥ iha tu punar  pakṣa dvayam eva iti ucyate yena eva tatra prakaraṇa dvaye pañca pañca pakṣā nirdiṣṭāḥ ata eva anyatra nirdiṣṭa tvāt na punar iha nirdiśyante saṃkṣepeṇa tu pakṣa dvayam upanyasyate iti tatra yadi skandhā ātmā iti parikalpyate tadā udaya vyaya bhāj  utpādī ca vināśī ca ātmā prāpnoti skandhānām udaya vyaya bhāktvāt na ca evam iṣyate ātma aneka [tva] doṣa prasaṅgāt  vakṣyati hi na api abhūtvā samutpannaḥ  doṣaḥ  hi atra prasajyate kṛtakaḥ  vā bhavet ātmā saṃbhūtaḥ  vā api ahetukaḥ iti tathā na ca upādānam eva ātmā vyeti tad samudeti ca katham hi nāma upādānam upādātā bhaviṣyati iti kim ca skandhā ātmā ced atas tad bahu tvāt  ātmānaḥ syuḥ te api bhūyāṃsa eva dravyam ca ātmā prāpnuyāt tādṛśaḥ ca dravye vṛttau vaiparītye ca na syāt  ātma ucchedaḥ  nirvṛtau syāt avaśyam nāśa utpādau nirvṛteḥ prāk  kṣaṇeṣu kartuḥ nāśāt tad phala abhāva eva bhuñjīta anyena arjitam karma ca anyaḥ ityādinā madhyamaka avatāre vistareṇa vihita vicārāt api pakṣaḥ  boddhavya iti na iha punar vistara prapañca ārabhyate evam tāvat  skandhā ātmā na bhavati skandha vyatiriktaḥ  api na yujyate yadi hi skandhebhyaḥ  anya ātmā bhavet  askandha lakṣaṇaḥ  bhavet  yathā hi goḥ anyaḥ  aśvaḥ na gaḥ lakṣaṇe bhavati evam ātmā api skandha vyatiriktaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ askandha lakṣaṇaḥ  bhavet  tatra skandhāḥ saṃskṛta tvāt  hetu pratyaya saṃbhūtā utpāda sthiti bhaṅga lakṣaṇāḥ tatra askandha lakṣaṇa ātmā bhavan bhavat matena utpāda sthiti bhaṅga lakṣaṇa āyuktaḥ syāt  yaḥ ca evam bhavati saḥ avidyamāna tvāt asaṃskṛta tvāt vā kha puṣpavat nirvāṇa badvā na eva ātma vyapadeśam pratilabhate na api ahaṃkāra viṣaya tvena yujyate iti skandha vyatiriktaḥ  api ātmā na yujyate athavā ayam anyaḥ arthaḥ yadi ātmā skandha vyatiriktaḥ syāt  saḥ askandha lakṣaṇa syāt  rūpaṇa anubhava nimitta udgahaṇa abhisaṃskaraṇa viṣaya prativijñapti lakṣaṇāḥ pañca skandhāḥ ātmā ca rūpāt iva vijñānam skandhebhyaḥ  vyatirikta iṣyamāṇaḥ pṛthak lakṣaṇa siddhaḥ syāt  pṛthak lakṣaṇa siddhaḥ ca gṛhyeta rūpāt iva cittam na ca gṛhyate tasmāt  skandha vyatiriktaḥ  api na asti nanu ca tīrthikāḥ skandhebhyaḥ  vyatiriktam ātmānam pratipannā bhinna lakṣaṇam ācakṣate tasmāt teṣām abādhaka eva ayam vidhiḥ iti yathā ca tīrthikā ātmanaḥ  bhinna lakṣaṇam ācakṣate tathā uktam madhyamaka avatāre ātmā tīrthyaiḥ kalpyate nitya rūpaḥ  akartā bhoktā nirguṇaḥ  niṣkriyaḥ ca kaṃcid kaṃcid vedam āśritya tasya bhedam yātā prakriyā tīrthikānām iti anena ucyate satyam bruvanti tīrthikāḥ skandha vyatiriktasya lakṣaṇam na punar te svarūpata ātmānam upalabhya tasya lakṣaṇam ācakṣate kim tarhi yathāvat upādāya prajñapti anavagamena nāma mātrakam eva ātmānam trāsāt apratipadyamānāḥ saṃvṛti satyāt api paribhraṣṭā mithyā kalpanayā eva kevalam anumāna ābhāsa mātra vipralabdhāḥ santaḥ mohāt  parikalpayanti ātmānam tasya ca lakṣaṇam ācakṣate teṣām ca karma kāraka parīkṣā ādiṣu ātma upādānayoḥ paraspara āpekṣikīm siddhim bruvatā saṃvṛtya api pratiṣedhaḥ  vihita eva uktam ca yathā ādarśam upādāya sva mukha pratibimbakam dṛśyate nāma tad ca eva na kiṃcid api tattvataḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tathā skandhān upādāya upalabhyate na ca kaścid sa tattvena sva mukha pratibimbavat yathā ādarśam anādāya sva mukha pratibimbakam na dṛśyate tathā skandha ānanādāya aham iti api evaṃvidha artha śravaṇāt dharma cakṣuḥ avāptavān ārya ānandaḥ svayam ca eva bhikṣubhyaḥ  abhīkṣṇam uktavān iti atas  na punar tad pratipādana artham yatna ārabhyate upādāya prajñapyamāna eva avidyā viparyāsa anugatānām ātma abhiniveśa āspada bhūtaḥ  mumukṣubhiḥ vicāryate yasya idam skandha pañcakam upādāna tvena pratibhāsate kim asau skandha lakṣaṇaḥ uta askandha lakṣaṇaḥ iti sarvathā ca vicārayantaḥ  mumukṣavaḥ  na enam upalabhante bhāva svabhāvataḥ tadā eṣām ātmani asati ca ātmīyam kuta eva bhaviṣyati ātma anupalambhāt ātma prajñapti upādānam skandha pañcakam ātmīyam iti sutarām na upalabhante yathā eva hi dagdhe rathe tad aṅgāni api dagdha tvāt na upalabhyante evam yoginaḥ  yadā eva ātmanairātmyam pratipadyante tadā eva ātmīya skandha vastu nairātmyam api niyatam pratipadyante yathā uktam ratnāvalyām ahaṃkāra udbhavāḥ skandhāḥ saḥ  ahaṃkāraḥ  anṛtaḥ  arthataḥ bījam yasya anṛtam tasya prarohaḥ satyataḥ kutas  skandhān asatyān dṛṣṭvā evam ahaṃkāraḥ prahīyate ahaṃkāra prahāṇāt ca na punar  skandha saṃbhavaḥ iti yathā eva hi grīṣme madhyāhna kāla avasānam āsāditasya vidhana nabhaḥ madhya deśam āci kraṃsoḥ īṣat paribhramyamāna paṭu tara hutabhuj vitata sphuliṅgān iva virūkṣatara mahī maṇḍala uttāpana parān pradīpta kiraṇasya kiraṇān pratītya virūkṣataram avanideśam ca āsādya viparītam ca darśanam apekṣya salila ākārā marīcaya upalabhyamānā vidūra deśa avasthitānām janmavatām ati prasanna abhinīla jala ākāram pratyayam ādadhati na tu tad samīpa gatānām evam iha api yathā avasthita ātma ātmīya padārtha tattva darśana vidūra deśa antara sthitānām saṃsāra adhvani vartamānānām avidyā viparyāsa anugamāt mṛṣā artha eva skandha samāropaḥ satyataḥ pratibhāsamānaḥ padārtha tattva darśana samīpa sthānām na pratibhāsate yathā uktam ācārya pādaiḥ dūrāt ālokitam rūpam āsannaiḥ dṛśyate sphuṭam marīciḥ yadi vāri syāt āsannaiḥ kim na gṛhyate dūrībhūtaiḥ yathābhūtaḥ  lokaḥ  ayam dṛśyate yathā na dṛśyate tad āsannaiḥ ānimittaḥ  marīcivat  marīciḥ toya sadṛśī yathā na ambhona ca arthataḥ skandhāḥ tathā ātma sadṛśā na ātmānaḥ  na api te arthataḥ iti ata eva ca ātma ātmīya anupalambhāt parama artha darśana samīpa sthaḥ  yogī niyatam bhavati nirmamaḥ  nirahaṃkāraḥ śamāt ātmā ātmanīnayoḥ ātmani hitam ātmanīnam skandha pañcakam ātmīyam iti arthaḥ ātmanaḥ  ahaṃkāra viṣayasya ātmanīnasya ca skandha ādeḥ vastunaḥ mamakāra viṣayasya śamāt anutpādāt anupalambhāt nirmamaḥ  nirahaṃkāraḥ ca jāyate yogī nanu ca yaḥ  asau  evam nirmamaḥ  nirahaṃkāraḥ ca yogī bhavati sa tāvat asti sati ca tasmin siddha ātmā skandhāḥ ca iti na etad evam yasmāt  nirmamaḥ  nirahaṃkāraḥ  yaḥ ca saḥ  api na vidyate nirmamam nirahaṃkāram yaḥ paśyati na paśyati ātmani skandheṣu ca sarvathā anupalabhyamāna svarūpeṣu kutas ta dvayatiriktaḥ  apara padārthaḥ  bhaviṣyati yaḥ  asau nirmamaḥ  nirahaṃkāraḥ ca iti yaḥ tu evam asaṃvidyamāna svarūpam nirmamam nirahaṃkāram ca paśyati sa tattvam na paśyati iti vijñeyam yathā uktam bhagavatā śūnyam ādhyātmikam paśya paśya śūnyam bahis gatam na vidyate saḥ  api kaścid yaḥ bhāvayati śūnyatām tathā yaḥ  api ca cintayi śūnyaka dharmān saḥ  api ku mārga papanna ku bālaḥ akṣara kīrtita śūnyaka dharmāḥ te ca anakṣara akṣara uktāḥ śānta paśānta ya cintayi dharmān saḥ  api ca cittu na jātu na bhūtaḥ citta vitarkiṇa sarvi papañcāḥ tasya acintiya budhyatha dharmān iti tathā skandha sabhāvatu śūnya vivikta bodhi sabhāvatu śūnya vivikta yaḥ  api caret sa pi śūnya sa bhāvaḥ  jñānavataḥ  na tu bāla janasya iti tad evam mama iti aham iti kṣīṇe bahirdhā adhyātmam eva ca nirudhyata upādānam tad kṣayāt janmanaḥ kṣayaḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi mūlakāḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi samudayāḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi hetukāḥ sarva kleśāḥ sūtre uktāḥ sā ca sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ ātma ātmīya anupalambhāt prahīyate tad prahāṇāt ca kāma dṛṣṭi śīla vrata ātma vāda upādāna catuṣṭayam prahīyate upādāna kṣayāt ca janmanaḥ punarbhava lakṣaṇasya kṣayaḥ  bhavati yatas ca ayam janma nivṛtti kramaḥ evam vyavasthāpitaḥ tasmāt  karma kleśa kṣayāt mokṣaḥ iti sthitam upādāne hi kṣīṇe tad pratyayaḥ bhavaḥ  na bhavati bhave niruddhe kutaḥ jāti jarā maraṇa ādikasya saṃbhava iti evam karma kleśa kṣayāt mokṣaḥ  bhavati iti sthitam karma kleśānām tarhi kasya kṣayāt parikṣaya iti vaktavyam ucyate karma kleśā vikalpataḥ te prapañcāt prapañcaḥ tu śūnyatāyām nirudhyate ayaḥ niśaḥ hi rūpa ādikam vikalpayataḥ  bāla pṛthagjanasya kleśa upajāyate rāga ādikaḥ vakṣyati hi saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ  rāgaḥ  dveṣaḥ  mohaḥ ca kathyate śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya hi uktam ca sūtre kāma jānāmi te mūlam saṃkalpāt kila jāyase na tvām saṃkalpayiṣyāmi tatas  me na bhaviṣyasi iti evam tāvat  karma kleśā vikalpataḥ pravartante te ca vikalpāḥ anādimat saṃsāra abhyastād jñāna jñeya vācya vācaka kartṛ karma karaṇa kriyā ghaṭa paṭa mukuṭa ratha rūpa vedanā strī puruṣa lābha alābha sukha duḥkha yaśaḥ  ayaśaḥ nindā praśaṃsā ādi lakṣaṇāt vicitrāt prapañcāt upajāyate sa ca ayam laukikaḥ prapañcaḥ  niravaśeṣa śūnyatāyām sarva svabhāva śūnyatā darśane sati nirudhyate katham kṛtvā yasmāt sati hi vastunam upalambhe syāt  yathā udita prapañca jālam na hi anupalabhya vandhyā duhitaram rūpa lāvaṇya yauvanavatīm tad viṣayam prapañcam avatārayanti rāgiṇaḥ na ca anavatārya prapañcam tad viṣayam ayoniśaḥ vikalpam avatārayanti na ca anavatārya kalpanā jālam ahaṃmama iti abhiniveśāt  sat kāya dṛṣṭi mūlakān kleśa gaṇān utpādayanti na ca anutpādya satkāya dṛṣṭayā ātmakān kleśa gaṇān karmāṇi śubha aśubhāniñjyāni kurvanti na ca akurvāṇāḥ karmāṇi jāti jarā maraṇa śoka parideva duḥkha daurmanasya[upāyāsa ādi rūpaṃ] ekajālībhūtam saṃsāra kāntāram anubhavanti evam yoginaḥ  api śūnyatā darśana avasthā niravaśeṣa skandha dhātu āyatanāni svarūpataḥ  na upalabhante na ca anupalabhamānā vastu svarūpam tad viṣayam prapañcam avatārayanti na ca anavatārya tad viṣayam prapañcam vikalpam avatārayanti na ca anavatārya vikalpam ahaṃmama iti abhiniveśāt  sat kāya dṛṣṭi mūlakam kleśa gaṇam utpādayanti na ca anutpādya satkāya dṛṣṭayā ādikam kleśa gaṇam karmāṇi kurvanti na ca akurvāṇāḥ jāti jarā maraṇa ākhyam saṃsāram anubhavanti tad evam aśeṣa prapañca upaśama śiva lakṣaṇām śūnyatām āgamya yasmāt aśeṣa kalpanā jāla prapañca vigamaḥ  bhavati prapañca vigamāt ca vikalpa nivṛtiḥ vikalpa nivṛttyā ca aśeṣa karma kleśa nivṛtti karma kleśa nivṛttyā ca janma nivṛttiḥ tasmāt  śūnyatā eva sarva prapañca nivṛtti lakṣaṇa tvāt nirvāṇam iti ucyate yathā uktam śatake dharmam samāsatas  ahiṃsām varṇayanti tathāgatāḥ śūnyatām eva nirvāṇam kevalam tad iha ubhayam iti ācārya bhāva vivekaḥ tu śrāvaka pratyekabuddhānām yathā udita śūnyatā adhigamam apratipadyamānaḥ evam varṇayati apara utpanna pratikṣaṇa vinaśvara saṃskāra kalāpa mātram anātmā anātmīyam avalokayataḥ ārya śrāvakasya api ātma ātmīya vastu abhāvāt  dharma mātram idam jāyate mriyate ca iti darśanam utpadyate ahaṃkāra viṣayaḥ  hi ātmā [tad abhāvāt tasya api abhāvaḥ] tad abhāvāt eva na kvacid ādhyātmikam bāhyam vā vastu asti iti mamakārānutpatteḥ nirmamaḥ  nirahaṃkāraḥ  aham iti na svarūpa viniścitiḥ upajāyate anyatra vyavahāra saṃketāt  prāk eva ajāta sarva saṃskāra darśinām nirvikalpa prajñācāra vihāriṇām mahābodhisattvānām iti ata āha nirmamaḥ  nirahaṃkāraḥ  yaḥ ca saḥ  api na vidyate iti tad ayam ācāryaḥ  yathā evaṃvidhe viṣaye na ācārya pāda mata anuvartī tathā pratipāditam madhyamaka avatāre dūraṃgamāyām tu dhiyā adhikaḥ iti atra iti na punar tad dūṣaṇe yatna āsthīyate ata eva uktam bhagavatā ārya aṣṭa sāhasrikāyām bhagavatyām śrāvaka bodhim abhisaṃboddhu krāmena subhūte asyām eva prajñāpāramitāyām śikṣitavyam pratyeka bodhim abhisaṃboddhu kāmena subhūte asyām eva prajñāpāramitāyām śikṣitavyam anuttarām samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃboddhu kāmena subhūte bodhisattvena mahāsattvena asyām eva prajñāpāramitāyām śikṣitavyam ityādi āha ca yaḥ  icchatī sugata śrāva ku ham bhaveyam pratyekabuddhu bhavijā tatha dharmarājaḥ  imu kṣānti na āgatya na śakyati pāpuṇotum yatha āra pāra gamanīyam atīradarśī iti atra āha yadi evam ādhyātmika bāhya vastu anupalambhāt adhyātmam bahis ca ahaṃmameti kalpanā jālānām anutpādaḥ tattvam iti vyavasthāpitam yad tarhi etad uktam bhagavatā ātmā hi ātmanaḥ  nāthaḥ kaḥ  nu nāthaḥ paraḥ  bhavet  ātmanā hi su dāntena svargam prāpnoti paṇḍitaḥ ātmā hi ātmanaḥ  nāthaḥ kaḥ  nu nāthaḥ paraḥ  bhavet  ātmā hi ātmanaḥ sākṣī kṛtasya apakṛtasya ca tathā ārya samādhi rāje kṛṣṇa śubham ca na naśyati karma ātmana kṛtva ca vedayitavyam naḥ pi ca saṃkrama karma phalasya naḥ ca ahetuka pratyanubhoti iti vistaraḥ tad katham na virudhyata iti ucyate idam api kim na uktam bhagavatā na asti iha sattva ātmā vā dharmāḥ tu ete sa hetukāḥ iti tathā hi rūpam na ātmā rūpavān na api ca ātmā rūpe na ātmā na ātmani rūpam evam yāvat  vijñānam na ātmā vijñānavān na ātmā vijñāne na ātmā na ātmani vijñānam iti tathā anātmānaḥ sarva dharmā iti tad katham idānīm anena āgamena pūrvakasya āgamasya virodhaḥ  na syāt  tasmāt deśa nābhi prāyaḥ  bhagavataḥ  anveṣyaḥ sāmānyena tu bhagavadbhiḥ buddhaiḥ pravacane na iya nīta artha vistara prabhede aśeṣa jagat vineya buddhi padma ākara vibodhana paraiḥ āditya kalpa eḥ anastaṃgataiḥ mahā karuṇa upāya vijñāna gabhasti vistaraiḥ ātmā iti api prajñapitam anātmā iti api deśitam buddhaiḥ na ātmā na ca anātmā kaścid iti api deśitam atra ca ayam abhiprāyaḥ iha ye [a ātmā abhāva viparyāsa] kudarśana dhana timira paṭala avacchādita aśeṣa buddhi nayana tayā laukika avadāta darśana viṣayān atikrāntam api bhāva jātam apaśyantaḥ  vyavahāra satya avasthitā eva santaḥ kṣiti salila jvalana pavana abhidhāna tattva mātra anuvarṇana parā mūlaudana udaka kiṇva ādi dravya viśeṣa paripāka mātra pratyaya utpanna mada murcchā ādi sāmarthya viśeṣa anugata madya pāna upalambhavat kalala ādi mahābhūta paripāka mātra saṃbhūtā eva buddhīḥ anuvarṇayantaḥ pūrva anta aparānta apavāda pravṛttāḥ santaḥ para lokam ātmānam ca apavat ante na asti ayam lokaḥ na asti para lokaḥ na asti sukṛta duṣkṛtānām karmaṇām phala vipākaḥ na asti sattva upapādukaḥ ityādinā tad apavādāt ca svarga apavarga viśiṣṭa iṣṭa phala viśeṣa ākṣepa parāṅmukhāḥ satata samitam akuśala karma abhisaṃskaraṇa pravṛttā naraka ādi mahā prapāta patana abhimukhāḥ teṣām tad asadṛṣṭi nivṛtti artha caturaśīti citta carita sahasra bheda bhinnasya sattva dhātoḥ yathā āśaya anuvartakaiḥ aśeṣa sattva dhātu uttāraṇa ākṣipta pratijñā saṃpādana tatparaiḥ prajñā upāya mahā karuṇā saṃbhāra puraḥ saraiḥ nirupamaiḥ eka jagat bandhubhiḥ niravaśeṣa kleśa mahā vyādhi cikitsakaiḥ mahā vaidya rāja bhūtaiḥ hīna madhya utkṛṣṭa vineya jana anujidhṛkṣayā hīrnānām vineyānām akuśala karma kāriṇām akuśala ādi nivartayitum buddhaiḥ bhagavadbhiḥ kvacid ātmā iti api prajñapitam loke vyavasthāpitam ahetuvāda pratiṣedha upapattiḥ ca karma kāraka parīkṣātaḥ na api ahetutaḥ iti atas  madhyamaka avatārāt ca vistareṇa veditavyā iti tad pratiṣedha artha  na iha punar yatna āsthīyate ye tu sat bhūta ātma dṛṣṭi kaṭhina ati dīrgha śithila mahā sūtra baddhā vihaṃgamā iva su dūram api gatāḥ kuśala karma kāriṇaḥ  akuśala karma patha vyāvṛttā api na śaknuvanti traidhātuka bhava upapattim ati vāhya śivam ajaram amaraṇam nirvāṇa puram abhigantum teṣām madhyānām vineyānām sat kāya darśana abhiniveśa śithilīkaraṇāya nirvāṇa abhilāṣa saṃjanana artham buddhaiḥ bhagavadbhiḥ vineya jana anugraha cikīrṣubhiḥ anātmā iti api deśitam ye tu pūrva abhyāsa viśeṣa anugata gambhīra dharma adhimokṣa labdha bīja paripākāḥ pratyāsanna vartini nirvāṇe teṣām utkṛṣṭānām vineyānām vigata ātma snehānām parama gambhīramauni indra pravacana artha tattva avagāhana samarthānām adhimukti viśeṣam avadhārya buddhaiḥ ātmā na ca anātmā kaścid iti api deśitam yathā eva hi ātma darśanam atattvam evam tad pratipakṣa bhūtam api anātma darśanam na eva tattvam iti evam na asti ātmā kaścid  na ca api anātmā kaścid asti iti deśitam yathā uktam ārya ratna kūṭe ātmā iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ  antar  nairātmyam iti ayam dvitīyaḥ  antar  yad etad anayoḥ antayoḥ madhyam tad arūpyam anidarśanam apratiṣṭham anābhā sam avijñaptikam aniketam iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā pratipada dharmāṇām bhūta pratyavekṣā iti uktam cārya ratna āvalyām na evam ātmā na ca anātmā yathābhūtena labhyate ātmānātma kṛte dṛṣṭī vavāra asmān mahā muniḥ dṛṣṭa śruta ādyam muninā na satyam na mṛṣā uditam pakṣāt hi pratipakṣaḥ syāt ubhayam tad ca na arthataḥ iti yatas ca evam hīna madhya utkṛṣṭa vineya jana āśaya nānātvena ātmā anātma tad ubhaya pratiṣedhena buddhānām bhagavatām dharma deśanā pravṛttā tasmāt na asti āgama bādhaḥ  mādhyamikānām ata eva uktam ārya deva pādaiḥ vāraṇam prāk apuṇyasya madhye vāraṇam ātmanaḥ sarvasya vāraṇam paścāt yaḥ  jānīte sa buddhimān iti tathā ācārya pādaiḥ uktam yathā eva vaiyākaraṇaḥ  mātṛkām api pāṭhayet  buddhaḥ  avadat tathā dharma vineyānām yathākṣamam keṣāṃcid avadat dharmam pāpebhyaḥ  vinivṛttaye keṣāṃcid puṇya siddhayartham keṣāṃcid  dvaya niścitam dvayāniśritam ekeṣām gambhīram bhīru bhīṣaṇam śūnyatā karuṇā garbham keṣāṃcid  bodhi sādhanam iti athavā ayam anyaḥ arthaḥ ātmā iti api prajñapitam sāṃkhya ādibhiḥ pratikṣaṇa vinaśvarāṇām saṃskārāṇām karma phala saṃbandha abhāvam utprekṣya anātmā iti api prajñapitam lokāyatikaiḥ upapattyā ātmānam saṃsartāram apaśyadbhiḥ etāvān eva puruṣaḥ  yāvān indriya gocaraḥ bhadre vṛka padam hi etad  yad vadanti bahu śrutāḥ ityādinā taimirika upalabdha keśa maśaka ādiṣu iva vitaimirikaiḥ iva bāla jana parikalpita ātmānātma ādi vastu svarūpam sarvathā eva apaśyadbhiḥ buddhaiḥ na ātmā na ca anātmā kaścid iti api deśitam yathā uktam ārya tathāgata guhya sūtre atha khalu śānta matiḥ bodhisattvaḥ  bhagavantam etad avocat  upaśama upaśama iti bhagavan  ucyate ka eṣa upaśamaḥ  nāma kasya ca upaśamāt upaśama iti ucyate bhagavān āha upaśama iti kula putra ucyate kleśa upaśamasya etad adhivacanam kleśa upaśama iti saṃkalpa vikalpa parikalpa upaśamasya etad adhivacanam saṃkalpa vikalpa parikalpa upaśama iti saṃjñā manasikāra upaśamasya etad adhivacanam saṃjñā manasikāra upaśama iti viparyāsa upaśamasya etad adhivacanam viparyāsa upaśama iti hetu ārambaṇa upaśamasya etad adhivacanam hetu ārambaṇa upaśama iti avidyā bhava tṛṣṇā upaśamasya etad adhivacanam avidyā bhava tṛṣṇā upaśama iti ahaṃkāram amakāra upaśamasya etad adhivacanam ahaṃkāra m amakāra upaśama iti uccheda śāśvata dṛṣṭayupaśamasya etad adhivacanam uccheda śāśvata dṛṣṭayupaśama iti satkāya dṛṣṭayupaśamasya etad adhivacanam iti śānta mate ye kecid ārambaṇa hetu dṛṣṭi saṃyuktāḥ saṃkleśāḥ pravartante sarve te satkāya dṛṣṭeḥ utpadyante satkāya dṛṣṭayupaśamāt sarva dṛṣṭayupaśama iti sarva dṛṣṭayupaśamāt sarva praṇidhāna upaśama iti sarva prāṇi dhānā upaśamāt sarva kleśa upaśamaḥ tad yathā api nāma śānta mate vṛkṣasya mūle chinne sarva śākhā patra phalāni śuṣyanti evam eva śānta mate satkāya dṛṣṭayupaśamāt sarva kleśā upaśāmyante sat kāya dṛṣṭau śānta mate aparijñātāyām sarva upādāna upakleśā utpadyante sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñātaḥ  api sarva upādāna upakleśā na utpadyante na bādhante śānta matiḥ āha kā punar bhagavan sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā bhagavān āha ātmā samutthānam śānta mate sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā sattva asamutthānam jivāsam utthānam pudgalāsamutthānam dṛṣṭayasam utthānam sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā na khalu punar  śānta mate sā dṛṣṭiḥ adhyātmam pratiṣṭhitā na bahirdhā pratiṣṭhitā sā dṛṣṭiḥ sarvatas  apratiṣṭhitā yad tasyāḥ  apratiṣṭhitāyāḥ  dṛṣṭeḥ apratiṣṭhitā iti jñānam iyam śānta mate sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā iti śānta mate śunyatāyā etad adhivacanam yad śūnyatā anulomikyā kṣāntyā tām dṛṣṭi na udgṛhṇāti iyam api śānta mate sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā satkāya iti śānta mate śūnyatā nimitta apraṇihita anabhisaṃskāra ajāta anutpāda dṛṣṭayā tām dṛṣṭim na udgṛhṇāti iyam api śānta mate sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā satkāya iti śānta mate akāya eṣaḥ na kasati na vikasati na cinoti na upacinoti ādita eva tad abhūtam parikalpitam yad ca abhūtam parikalpitam tad na parikalpitam na parikalpyate na vikalpyate tad na kriyate na viṭhapyate na utthāpyate na adhyavasyate tad ucyate upaśama iti śānta matiḥ āha upaśānta upaśānta iti bhagavan  ucyate kasya upaśamāt upaśānta iti ucyate bhagavān āha ārambaṇataḥ śānta mate cittam jvalati yad na bhūya ālambanīkaroti tad na jvalati ajvalan upaśānta iti ucyate tad yathā api nāma śānta mate agniḥ upādānataḥ  jvalati anupādānataḥ śāmyati evam eva ālambanataḥ cittam jvalati anālambanataḥ śāmyati tatra śānta mate upāya kuśalaḥ  ayam bodhisattvaḥ prajñāpāramitā pariśuddhaḥ ālambana sama tām ca prajānāti kuśala mūla ālambanam ca śamayati ityādi atra āha yadi buddhaiḥ bhagavadbhiḥ na ātmā iti deśitam na anā ātmā iti kim tarhi deśitam iti ucyate nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare anutpannā aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharmatā iha yadi kiṃcid abhidhātavyam vastu syāt  tad deśyeta yadā tu abhidhātavyam nivṛttam vācām viṣayaḥ  na asti tadā kiṃcid api na eva deśyate buddhaiḥ kasmāt punar abhidhātavyam na asti iti āha nivṛtte citta gocare iti cittasya gocaraḥ citta gocaraḥ gocaraḥ  viṣayaḥ ārambaṇam iti arthaḥ yadi cittasya kaścid  gocaraḥ syāt  tatra kiṃcid nimittam adhyāropya syāt  vācām pravṛttiḥ yadā tu cittasya viṣaya eva anupapannaḥ tadā kva nimitta adhyāropaḥ yena vācām pravṛttiḥ syāt  kasmāt  punar citta viṣayaḥ  na asti iti pratipādayan  āha anutpannā aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharmatā yasmāt anutpanna aniruddhā nirvāṇam iva dharmatā dharma svabhāvaḥ dharma prakṛtiḥ vyavasthāpitā tasmāt na tatra cittam pravartate cittasya apravṛttau ca kutaḥ nimitta adhyāropaḥ tad abhāvāt kutaḥ vācām pravṛttiḥ atas ca na kiṃcid  buddhaiḥ bhagavadbhiḥ deśitam iti sthitam avikalam ata eva ca vakṣyati sarva upalambha upaśamaḥ prapañca upaśamaḥ śivaḥ na kvacid kasyacid kaścid dharmaḥ  buddhena deśitaḥ iti evam ca etad  athavā ayam anyaḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ yad uktam prapañcaḥ śūnyatāyām nirudhyate iti katham punar  prapañcasya śūnyatāyām nirodha iti ucyate yasmāt nivṛttam abhidhātavyam ityādi pūrvavat  vyākhyeyam athavā yad etad uktam prāc ādhyātmika bāhyavastu anupalambhena adhyātmam bahis ca yaḥ sarvadā ahaṃkāra m amakāra parikṣayaḥ idam atra tattvam iti kīdṛśam tad  kiṃvat  vaktum vā śakyate tasmāt  nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare tatra tattvataḥ iti vākya śeṣaḥ kim punar  kāraṇam tatra tattve nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare iti āha anutpannā aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharmatā iti pūrvakam eva vyākhyānam yojyam ata eva uktam ārya tathā gata guhya sūtre yām ca śānta mate rātriṃ tathāgataḥ  anuttarām samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbuddhaḥ yām ca rātrim anupādāya parinirvāsyati asmin  antare tathāgatena eka akṣaram api na udāhṛtam na pravyāhṛtam na pravyāhariṣyati katham tarhi bhagavatā sakala sura asura nara kiṃnara siddha vidyādhara uraga prabhṛti vineya janebhyaḥ  vividha prakārebhyaḥ  dharma deśanā deśitā eka kṣaṇa vāc udāhāreṇa eva tad tad jana manaḥ ta maḥ haraṇī bahuvidha buddhi nalinī vana vibodhinī jarā maraṇa sarit sāgara ucchoṣiṇī kalpa kāla anala sapta arka raśmi visara hrepiṇī śarad aruṇa mahā prabhā iti tad evam sūtre yathā yantra kṛtam tūryam vādyate pavana īritam na ca atra vādakaḥ kaścid niścaranti atha ca svarāḥ evam pūrva su śuddha tvāt sarva sattva āśaya īritā vā agniḥ carati buddhasya na ca asya asti iha kalpanā pratiśrutka ādayaḥ śabdā na adhyātmam na bahis  sthitāḥ vāc api evam narendrasya na adhyātmam na bahis  sthitāḥ iti tathā devataḥ  codani dundubhi divya karma vipāka nivṛtta marūṇam deva pamatta vihāriṇa ñātvā dundubhi ghoṣa pamuñci nabhātaḥ  sarva anitya aśāśvata kāmā itvara adhruva phenasa bhāvāḥ māya marīci samā daka candrāḥ sarvi bhavāḥ su pina anta sa bhāvāḥ dundubhi vādita śakra marudbhiḥ sārddhaya saṃkrami dharma sabhāyām dharma kathām pakaroti marūṇām yā katha śānta virāga nukūlā tathā ārya samādhi rāje buddhaḥ  yadā bheṣyati dharmarājaḥ sarvāṇa dharmāṇa pakāśa kaḥ  muniḥ tṛṇa gulma vṛkṣa oṣadhi śaila parvata abhāva dharmāṇa ravaḥ  bhaviṣyati yāvanti śabda astahi lokadhātau sarve hi abhāvā na hi kaści bhāvaḥ tāvantu khaḥ tasya tathāgatasya svaru niścarī loka vināyakasya iti vistaraḥ tathā eka svarā tu tava loka hitaḥ  nānā adhimukti svaru niścarati ekaikam anvimama bhāṣi jinaḥ brūhi smitam prakṛtakasya kṛte iti atra eke paricodayanti nāstikā viśiṣṭā mādhyamikāḥ yasmāt  kuśala akuśalam karma kartāram ca phalam ca sarvam ca lokam bhāva svabhāva śūnyam iti bruvate nāstikā api hi etad na asti iti bruvate tasmāt nāstikā viśiṣṭā mādhyamikā iti na evam kutas  pratītyasamutpāda vādinaḥ  hi mādhyamikāḥ hetu pratyayān prāpya pratītya samutpanna tvāt  sarvam eva ihaloka para lokam niḥsvabhāvam varṇayanti yathā svarūpa vādinaḥ  na eva nāstikāḥ pratītyasamutpanna tvāt  bhāva svabhāva śunyatvena na para loka ādi abhāvam pratipannāḥ kim tarhi aihalaukikam vastu jātam upalabhya svabhāvataḥ tasya para lokāt iha āgamanam ihalokāt ca para loka gamana paśyantuḥ ihaloka upalabdha padārtha sadṛśa padārtha antara apavādam kurvanti tathā api vastu svarūpeṇa avidyamānasya eva te na astitvam pratipannāḥ iti amunā tāvat darśanena sāmyam asti iti ced  na hi kutas  saṃvṛtyā mādhyamikaiḥ astitvena abhyupagamāt na tulya tā vastutas tulya tā iti ced  yadi api vastu tas  asiddhiḥ tulyā tathā api pratipatṛ bhedāt atulya tā yathā hi kṛta caurya puruṣam ekaḥ samyak aparijñāya eva tad amitra preritaḥ tam mithyā vyācaṣṭe cauryam anena kṛtam iti aparaḥ tu sākṣāt  dṛṣṭvā dūṣayati tatra yadi api vastu tas  na asti bhedaḥ tathā api parijñātṛ bhedāt ekaḥ tatra mṛṣāvādī iti ucyate aparaḥ tu satya vādī iti ekaḥ ca ayaśasā ca apuṇyena ca samyak  parīkṣyamāṇaḥ  yujyate na aparaḥ evam iha api yathāvat vidita vastu svarūpāṇām mādhyamikānām bruvatām avagacchatām ca vastu svarūpa abhede api yathāvat avidita vastu svarūpaiḥ nāstikaiḥ saha jñāna abhidhānayoḥ na asti sāmyam yathā eva hi upekṣā sāmānye api apratisaṃkhyāya pratisaṃkhyāya upekṣakayoḥ iva pṛthagjana arhatoḥ jāti andha cakṣuṣmatoḥ ca viṣama prapāta pradeśa viniścita sāmānye api yathā asti mahān viśeṣaḥ tathā nāstikānām mādhyamikānām ca viśeṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti pūrva ācāryāḥ iti alam prasaṅgenaḥ prakṛtam eva vyākhyāsyāmaḥ atra āha yadi api evam anutpannā aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharmatā tasyām ca na asti vāc cittayoḥ pravṛttiḥ tathā api na eva asau adeśyamānā śakyā janaiḥ vijñātum iti avaśyam tasyām avatāraṇa artham vineya janānām saṃvṛti satya apekṣayā kadācid deśana ānupūrvyā bhavitavyam iti atas  sā kathyatām iti ucyate iyam atra buddhānām bhagavatām tattva amṛta avatāra deśana ānupūrvī vijñeyā yad uta sarvam tathyam na vā tathyam tathyam ca atathyam eva ca na eva atathyam na eva tathyam etad buddha anuśāsanam tatra yad yad yasya priyam pūrvam tad tad tasya samācaret  na hi pratihataḥ pātram saddharmasya kathaṃcana iti tathā ca bhagavatā uktam lokaḥ  mayā sārdham vivadati na aham lokena sārdham vivadāmi yad loke asti saṃmatam tad mama api asti saṃmatam yad loke na asti saṃmatam mama api tad na asti saṃmatam iti āgamāt ca na anyayā bhāṣayā mlecchaḥ śakyaḥ  grāhayitum yathā na laukika mṛte lokaḥ śakyaḥ  grāhayitum tathā iti ādita eva tāvat bhagavatā sva prasiddha padārtha meda sva rūpa vibhāga śravaṇa saṃjāta abhilāṣasya vineya janasya yad etad  skandha dhātu āyatana ādikam avidyā taimirikaiḥ satyataḥ parikalpitam upalabdham tad eva tāvat  satyam iti upavarṇitam bhagavatā tad darśana apekṣayā ātmani lokasya gaurava utpādana artham vidita niravaśeṣa loka vṛttāntaḥ  ayam bhagavān sarvajñaḥ sarva darśī yaḥ evam bhava agra paryantasya vāyu maṇḍala ādeḥ ākāśa dhātu paryavasānasya bhājana lokasya sattva lokasya ca aviparītam sthiti utpāda pralaya ādikam sā ati vicitra prabhedam sa hetukam saphalam sa āsvādam sa ādīnavam ca upadiṣṭavān iti tad evam bhagavati utpanna sarvajña buddhi vineya janasya uttara kālam tad eva sarvam na vā tathyam iti upadeśitam tatra tathyam nāma yasya anyathātvam na asti vidyate ca pratikṣaṇa vināśi tvāt  saṃskārāṇām anyathā bhāvaḥ tasmāt anyathā bhāva sadbhāvāt na vā tathyam vā
