śabdaḥ cakāra arthaḥ  deśanā samuccaye draṣṭavyaḥ sarvam tathyam na ca tathyam iti keṣāṃcid  sarvam etad  tathyam ca atathyam ca iti deśitam tatra bāla jana apekṣayā sarvam etad  tathyam ārya jñāna apekṣayā tu sarvam etad mṛṣā taiḥ evam anupalambhāt iti keṣāṃcittu ati cira abhyasta tattva darśanānām kiṃcid mātrā nutkhāta āvaraṇa tarū mūlānām na eva atathyam na eva tathyaṃtat iti deśitam tasya api kiṃcid mātrasya āvaraṇasya prahāṇa artham vandhyā sutasya avadāta śyāma tā pratiṣedhavat ubhayam etad  pratiṣiddham etad ca buddhānām bhagavatām anuśāsanam unmārgāt apanīya samyak mārga pratiṣṭhāpanam śāsanam evam ānupūrvyā śāsanam anuśāsanam vineya jananurūpyeṇa vā śāsanam anuśāsanam sarvāḥ ca etāḥ  deśanā buddhānām bhagavatām mahā karuṇa upāya jñānavatām tattva amṛta avatāra upāya tvena vyavasthitāḥ na hi tathāgatāḥ tattva amṛta avatārān upāya bhūta vākyam udāharanti vyādhi anurūpa bhaiṣajya upasaṃhāravat te vineya jana anujighṛkṣayā yathā anurūpam dharmam deśayanti yathā uktam śatake sat asat sadasat ca iti na ubhayam ca iti kathyate nanu vyādhi vaśāt pathyam auṣadham nāma jāyate iti kiṃlakṣaṇam punar  tad  tattvam yasya etā deśanā avatāra artham upadiśante bhagavantaḥ uktam etad asmābhiḥ nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare iti yadā ca etad evam tadā kim aparam pṛcchayate yadi api evam tathā api vyavahāra satya anurodhena laukika tathya ādi abhyupagamavat tasya api samāropataḥ lakṣaṇam ucyatām iti tad ucyate apara pratyayam śāntam prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam nirvikalpa manāna artham etad tattvasya lakṣaṇam tatra na asmin para pratyayaḥ asti iti apara pratyayam para upadeśa agamyam svayam eva adhigantavyam iti arthaḥ yathā hi taimirikā vitatham keśa maśaka makṣikā ādi rūpam paśyantaḥ  vitimira upadeśena api na śaknuvanti keśānām yathāvat avasthitam sva rūpam adarśana nyāyena adhigantavyam ataimirikā iva adhigantum kim tarhi ataimirika upadeśāt mithyā etad iti etāvat mātrakam eva pratipadyante yadā tu timira upaghāti aviparīta śūnyatā darśana añjanān jita buddhi nayanāḥ santaḥ samutpanna tattva jñānā bhavanti tadā tad  tattvam anadhigamana yogena svayam adhigacchanti iti evam apara pratyayam bhāvānām yad  svarūpam tad  tattvam etad ca śānta svabhāvam ataimirika keśa adarśanavat svabhāva virahitam iti arthaḥ ata eva tad  prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam prapañcaḥ  hi vāc  prapañcayati arthān iti kṛtvā prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam vāgbhiḥ avyāhṛtam iti arthaḥ nirvikalpam ca tad  vikalpaḥ citta pracāraḥ tad rahita tvāt  tad  tattvam nirvikalpam yathā uktam sūtre parama artha satyam katamat  yatra jñānasya api apracāraḥ kaḥ punarvādaḥ  akṣarāṇām iti evam nirvikalpam nānā arthaḥ  asya iti nānā artham bhinna artham na nānā arthaḥ anāna artham abhinna artham iti arthaḥ yathā uktam ārya satya dvaya avatāra sūtre deva putra āha katamaḥ punar mañjuśrīḥ samyak prayogaḥ mañjuśrīḥ āha yad samā deva putra paramārthataḥ tathatā dharmadhātuḥ atyanta ajātiḥ ca tad samāni paramārthataḥ pañca ānantaryāṇi yad samāni pañca ānantaryāṇi tad samāni dṛṣṭi kṛtāni yad samāni dṛṣṭi kṛtāni tad samāḥ pṛthagjana dharmāḥ yad samāḥ pṛthagjana dharmāḥ tad samāḥ śaikṣa dharmāḥ yad samāḥ śaikṣa dharmāḥ tad samā aśaikṣa dharmāḥ yad samā aśaikṣa dharmāḥ tad samāḥ samyaksaṃbuddha dharmāḥ yad samāḥ samyaksaṃbuddha dharmāḥ tad samam nirvāṇam yad samam nirvāṇam tad samaḥ saṃsāraḥ yad samaḥ saṃsāraḥ tad samaḥ paramārthataḥ saṃkleśaḥ yad samaḥ paramārthataḥ saṃkleśaḥ tad samam paramārtha taḥ  vyavadānam yad samam paramārtha taḥ  vyavadānam tad samāḥ paramārthataḥ sarva dharmāḥ evam paramārthataḥ sarva dharma samatā prayuktaḥ  deva putra bhikṣuḥ samyak prayukta iti ucyate deva putra āha katamayā punar mañjuśrīḥ samatayā yāvat  paramārtha taḥ  yad samam vyavadānam tad samāḥ sarva dharmāḥ paramārtha ta iti mañjuśrīḥ āha paramārthataḥ sarva dharma anutpāda sama tayā paramārthataḥ sarva dharma atyantā jāti samatayā paramārthataḥ samāḥ sarva dharmāḥ tad  kasmāt hetoḥ paramārtha taḥ  nirvāṇa anānā akaraṇā hi deva putra sarva dharmā atyanta nirutpāda tām upādāya tad yathā api nāma deva putra yad ca mṛddhājanasyāmi antaram ākāśam yad ca ratna bhājanasya ākāśam ākāśa dhātuḥ eva eṣaḥ tad  paramārtha taḥ  na kiṃcid nānā karaṇam evam eva deva putra yaḥ saṃkleśaḥ sa paramārtha taḥ  atyantān utpādatā yad api vyavadānam tad api paramārtha taḥ  atyantān utpādatā saṃsāraḥ  api paramārtha taḥ  atyantān utpādatā yāvat nirvāṇam api paramārtha taḥ  atyantān utpādatā na atra kiṃcid paramārtha taḥ  nānā karaṇam tad  kasmāt hetoḥ paramārtha taḥ  atyanta an utpāda tvāt sarva dharmāṇām iti tad evam anān ārtha tā tattvasya lakṣaṇam veditavyam śūnyatā eka rasa tvāt uttarottara vyākhyānam ca atra veditavyam evam tāvat āryāṇām jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāra parikṣayāya kṛta kāryāṇām tattva lakṣaṇam laukikam tu tattva lakṣaṇam adhikṛtya ucyate pratītya yad yad bhavati na hi tāvat tad eva tad  na ca anyat api tad tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam yad  kāraṇam pratītya yad  kāryam utpadyate tad yathā śāli bījam pratītya pṛthivī ādi sāmagrīm ca śāli aṅkura upajāyate na hi tāvat  tad eva tad iti śakyate vaktum na eva yad eva bījam sa eva aṅkuraḥ janya jana kayoḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt  tatas ca pitāputrayoḥ api eka tvam syāt  ananya tvāt ca aṅkura avasthāyām aṅkuravat bīja grahaṇam api syāt  bījavat ca aṅkurasya api grahaṇam syāt  nitya tvam ca evam bījasya syāt  avināśa abhyupagamāt tatas ca śāśvata vāda prasaṅgāt mahā doṣa rāśiḥ syāt  karma phala ādi bhāva prasaṅgāt  evam tāvat  yad eva bījam sa eva aṅkuraḥ iti na yujyate na ca anyat api tad tasmāt  na api bījāt aṅkurasya anya tvam bījam antareṇa api aṅkura udaya prasaṅgāt  yadi anyat anyat anyasmāt anyasmāt api ṛte bhavet  iti vacanāt aṅkura avasthāne api bīja anuccheda prasaṅgāt  tatas ca satkārya vāda doṣaḥ syāt  yatas ca evam yad  kāraṇam pratītya yad  kāryam utpadyate na eva tad  kāraṇam kāryam bhavati na ca tasmāt kāraṇāt tad kāryam anyat  tasmāt na kāraṇam ucchinnam na api śāśvatam iti śakyate vyavasthāpayitum yathā uktam ārya deva pādaiḥ yasmāt pravartate bhāvaḥ tena ucchedaḥ  na jāyate yasmāt nivartate bhāvaḥ tena nityaḥ  na jāyate iti uktam ca ārya lalita vistara sūtre bījasya sataḥ  yathā aṅkuraḥ  na ca yaḥ  bīja sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas  na ca eva tad evam anuccheda aśāśvata dharmatā iti tad evam yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena aneka artha manāna artham anucchedam aśāśvatam etad tad loka nāthānām buddhānām śāsana amṛtam mahā karuṇa upāya mahā megha paṭala nirantara avacchādita ākāśa dhātu paryanta diś maṇḍalānām rāga ādi kleśa gaṇa samudācāra ati tīkṣṇatara āditya maṇḍala upatāpita jagat jāti jarā maraṇa duḥkha dahana saṃtāpa upaśama tatparāṇām satata avirata yatha anurūpa carita pratipakṣa sat dharma deśana amṛta dhārā pātaiḥ yathā anurūpa vineya jana kuśala mūla śasya oṣadhi phala phulla latā utpanna ati vṛddha yanuji dhṛkṣūṇām saddharma amṛta mahā varṣa varṣiṇām samyaksaṃbuddha mahā nāgānāmatrāṇālaukika trāṇānām anātha nāthānām sakala loka nāthānām etad  tad saddharma amṛtam sakala traidhātuka bhava duḥkha kṣaya svabhāvam yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena ekatva anyatva rahitam śāśvata uccheda vāda vigatam ca vijñeyam etad dharma tattva amṛta pratipannānām śrāvakāṇām śruta cintā bhāvanā kramāt pravartamānānām śīla samādhi prajñā ātmaka skandha traya amṛta rasasya upayogāt niyatam eva jarā maraṇa kṣaya svabhāva nirvāṇa adhigamaḥ  bhavati atha api kathaṃcid iha aparipakva kuśala mūla tayā śrutvā api etad saddharma amṛtam dṛṣṭa eva dharme na mokṣam āsādayanti tathā api janmāntare api avaśyam eṣām pūrva hetu balāt eva niyatā siddhiḥ saṃpadyate yathā uktam śatake iha yadi api tattva jñaḥ  nirvāṇam na adhigacchati prāpnoti ayatnataḥ avaśyam punar janmani karmavat  iti atha api kathaṃcid  saṃbuddhānām anutpāde śrāvakāṇām punar  kṣaye sati ārya mārga upadeśaka kalyāṇa mitra pratyaya vaikalyāt  na syāt  dharma tattva amṛta adhigamaḥ tathā api pūrva janma antara dharma tattva śravaṇa hetu balāt eva aihalaukikā upadeśa nirapekṣāṇām api praviveka sevā mātra upanata pratyayānām svāyaṃbhuvam jñānam pratyekabuddhānām asaṃsargāt pravartate kāya cetasoḥ pravivekaḥ  asaṃsargaḥ kalyāṇa mitra aparyeṣaṇam vā tasmāt asaṃsargāt hetoḥ pratyekabuddhānām asaṃbuddhake api kāle yasmāt bhavati eva dharma tattva adhigamaḥ tasmāt abandhyā siddhiḥ asya saṃbuddha mahā vaidya rāja praṇītasya saddharma tattva amṛta bhaiṣajyasya iti vijñeyam yatas ca etad evam atas  arhati prājñaḥ prāṇān api parityajya saddharma tattvam paryeṣitum iti yathā uktam bhagavatā ārya aṣṭa sāhasrikāyām bhagavatyām katham ca bhagavan sadā praruditena bodhisattvena mahāsattvena iyam prajñāpāramitā paryeṣitā evam uktaḥ  bhagavān āyuṣmantam subhūtim sthaviram etad avocat  sadā praruditena bodhisattvena mahāsattvena pūrvam prajñāpāramitām paryeṣamāṇena kāye anarthikena jīvita nirapekṣeṇa lābha satkāra ślokeṣu aniśritena paryeṣamāṇena paryeṣitā tena prajñāpāramitām paryeṣamāṇena araṇya gatena antarīkṣān nirghoṣaḥ śrutaḥ  abhūt  gaccha kula putra pūrvasyām diśi tatra prajñāpāramitām śroṣyasi tathā ca gaccha yathā na kāya klamatha manasikāram utpādayasi na styānam iddha manasikāram utpādayasi na bhojana manasikāram utpādayasi yāvat  mā kvacid cittam praṇidhā adhyātmam vā bahirdhā vā mā ca kula putra vāmena avalokayan gāḥ mā dakṣiṇena [mā pūrveṇa] mā paścimena mā uttareṇa mā urdhvam mā adhas  mā ca anuvidiśam avalokayan gāḥ tathā ca kula putra gaccha yathā [nā ātmato] na satkāyataḥ calasi na rūpataḥ  na vedanātaḥ  na saṃjñātaḥ  na saṃskārebhyaḥ  na vijñānataḥ calasi yaḥ  hi atas calati sa vitiṣṭhate [kutaḥ vitiṣṭhate ] buddha dharmebhyaḥ  vitiṣṭhate yaḥ  buddha dharmebhyaḥ  vitiṣṭhate sa saṃsāre carati yaḥ saṃsāre carati sa prajñāpāramitāyām na carati na ca tām anuprāpnoti iti yāvat māreṇa pāpīyasā udake antar dhāpite atha asya etad abhūt  yad nu aham ātmanaḥ kāyam viddhā ime pṛthivī pradeśam rudhireṇa siñcā iyam tad kasya hetoḥ ayam pṛthivī pradeśa uddhata rajaskaḥ mā rajaḥ dhāturitaḥ  dharma udgatasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya śarīre nipatet  kim aham ātma bhāvena kariṣyāmi avaśyam bhedana dharmiṇā varam khalu punar mama evaṃrūpayā kriyayā ātma bhāvasya vināśaḥ kṛtaḥ  bhavet  na tu evam niḥsāmarthya kriyayā bahūni ca mama ātma bhāva sahasrāṇi kāma hetoḥ kāma nidānam bhinnāni punar  punar  saṃsāre saṃsarataḥ na punar evaṃbhūteṣu sthāneṣu atha khalu sadā praruditaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ  mahāsattvaḥ tīkṣṇam śastram gṛhītvā samantāt ātmānam viddhā samantatas tam pṛthivī pradeśam svakena rudhireṇa āsiñcat ityādi atha khalu sadā praruditaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ  mahāsattvaḥ saha darśanāt eva dharma udgatasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya evaṃrūpam sukham pratyalabhata tad yathā api nāma prathama dhyāna samāpannasya bhikṣoḥ ekāgra manasikārasya bhikṣoḥ tatra iyam dharma udgatasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya prajñāpāramitā deśanā yad uta sarva dharma sama tayā prajñāpāramitā sama tā sarva dharma vivikta tayā prajñāpāramitā vivikta tā sarva dharma acala tayā prajñāpāramitā acala tā sarva dharma āmanana tayā prajñāpāramitā mananatā sarva dharma astambhita tayā prajñāpāramitā stambhita tā sarva dharma eka rasa tayā prajñāpāramitā eka rasa tā sarva dharma aparyanta tayā prajñāpāramitā paryanta tā sarva dharma anutpāda tayā prajñāpāramitā anutpāda tā sarva dharma anirodha tayā prajñāpāramitā nirodha tā gagana aparyanta tayā prajñāpāramitā paryanta tā yāvat  sarva dharma asaṃbhedana tayā prajñāpāramitā saṃbhedana tā sarva dharma anupalabdhi tayā prajñāpāramitā anupalabdhi tā sarva dharma abhibhāvanā samatayā prajñāpāramitā abhibhāvanā sama tā sarva dharma niśceṣṭa tayā prajñāpāramitā niśceṣṭa tā sarva dharma acintya tayā prajñāpāramitā acintya tā veditavyā iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau ātma parīkṣā nāma aṣṭādaśamam prakaraṇam kāla parīkṣā ekonaviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyata eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ kāla traya vijñapti hetutvāt iha atīta anāgata pratyutpanna asrayaḥ kālā bhagavatā upadiṣṭāḥ te ca bhāva āśrayāḥ yasmāt utpannaḥ niruddhaḥ  hi bhāva svabhāvaḥ atīta iti vyapadiśyate utpannaḥ  aniruddhaḥ  hi vartamānaḥ alabdha ātma bhāvaḥ  anāgata iti evam bhāva svabhāva nibandhana asrayaḥ kālā upadiṣṭāḥ te ca santi tasmāt  tad nibandhanaḥ  api bhāva svabhāvaḥ  asti iti ucyate syāt  kāla traya prajñapti hetuḥ bhāva svabhāvaḥ yadi kāla trayam eva bhavat abhimatam bhavet  na tu asti yathā ca na asti tathā pratipādayan  āha pratyutpannaḥ  anāgataḥ ca yadi atītam apekṣya hi pratyutpannaḥ  anāgataḥ ca kāle atīte bhaviṣyataḥ iha tāvat  yadi vartamāna anāgatau syātām tau  apekṣya atītam kālam bhavetām anapekṣya vā tatra yadi atītam apekṣya sidhyete tathā niyatam atīte kāle bhaviṣyataḥ yasmāt  yasya hi yatra asattvam tad  tena na apekṣyate tad yathā vandhyā srī sva tanayena gagana māla tīla tā sva kusumena sikatā sva tailena avidyamānam api andhakāram pradīpena pradīpaḥ  api andhakāreṇa pratidvandvi tvena apekṣyate iti ced  na etad evam asya api sādhya sama tvāt  tad atra yadi atīte kāle vartamāna anāgatau kālau iṣyete apekṣā siddhayartham evam sati atīte kāle vidyamāna tvāt  atīta kāla ātmavat  tayoḥ api atīta tvam syāt  tatas ca atītaḥ  api na syāt  yasmāt  vartamāna avasthā atikrāntaḥ  hi atītaḥ asaṃprāptaḥ anāgata iti syāt  yadā tu vartamāna anāgatayoḥ asaṃbhava eva tadā kutas  kasyacid atīta tvam syāt  iti atas  atītaḥ  api na syāt  atha yathā ukta doṣa parijihīrṣayā pratyutpannaḥ  anāgataḥ ca na staḥ tatra punar yadi pratyutpannaḥ  anāgataḥ ca syātām kaśram apekṣya tam tatra atīte kāle yadi vartamāna anāgatau kālau na staḥ iti parikalpyate evam api tatra avidyamāna tvāt  gagana indīvaravat na asti apekṣā atha api syāt  kāla vādinām vidyate eva kālaḥ tatra kim apekṣayā prayojanam iti ucyate evam api anapekṣya punar  siddhiḥ na atītam vidyate tayoḥ pratyutpannaḥ  anāgataḥ ca tasmāt kālaḥ  na vidyate pratyutpanna anāgatayoḥ asattvam atīta anapekṣa tvāt khara viṣāṇavat  yatas ca evam pratyutpannaḥ  anāgataḥ ca tasmāt kālaḥ  na vidyate iti vijñeyam yadā ca evam atītam apekṣya vā anapekṣya vā pratyutpanna anāgatayoḥ na asti siddhiḥ evam pratyutpanna apekṣayā vā anapekṣayā vā atīta anāgatayoḥ anāgata apekṣayā vā anapekṣayā vā pratyutpanna atītayoḥ asiddhau iṣyamāṇāyām tena eva pratyutpanna āgatayoḥ atīta apekṣayā vā anapekṣayā asiddhi krameṇa dūṣaṇa sāmyam atidiśan  āha etena eva avaśiṣṭau dvau krameṇa parivartakau uttama adhama madhyādīn ekatva ādīn  ca lakṣayet  katham kṛtvā yadi atītaḥ  anāgataḥ ca pratyutpannam apekṣya hi kālaḥ  atītaḥ  anāgataḥ ca pratyutpanne bhaviṣyataḥ kālaḥ  atītaḥ  anāgataḥ ca na staḥ tatra punar yadi kālaḥ  atītaḥ  anāgataḥ ca syātām katham apekṣya tam anapekṣya punar  siddhiḥ na jātam vidyate tayoḥ tena atītaḥ  anāgataḥ ca kālaḥ  nāma na vidyate eṣa tāvat ekaḥ kāla parivartaḥ atītaḥ  vartamānaḥ ca yadi ajātam apekṣya hi atītaḥ  vartamānaḥ ca kāle ajāte bhaviṣyataḥ atītaḥ  vartamānaḥ ca na staḥ tatra punar yadi atītaḥ  vartamānaḥ ca syātām katham apekṣya tam anapekṣya punar  siddhiḥ na ajātam vidyate tayoḥ atītaḥ  vartamānaḥ ca tasmāt kālaḥ  na vidyate eṣa dvitīyaḥ kāla parivarta iti vyākhyāna kārikā iti evaṃdvau kāla parivartau boddhavyau yatas ca evam vicāraṇe kāla trayam na asti tasmāt  kālaḥ  na vidyate kāla abhāvāt ca bhāva sadbhāvaḥ  api na asti iti siddham yathā ca etad kāla trayam vicāritam evam uttama adhama madhyādīn ekatva ādīn  ca lakṣayet  uttama adhama madhyamān iti ādi śabdena kuśala akuśala avyākṛtāni utpāda sthiti bhaṅgāḥ pūrva anta apara anta madhya antāḥ kāmarūpa ārūpya dhātavaḥ śaikṣā śaikṣana eva śaikṣana eva āśaikṣādayaḥ  yāvantaḥ padārthāḥ tri padārtha saṃbandha vyavasthitāḥ te sarve gṛhyante ekatva ādīn  ca iti anena ādi śabdena dvitva bahu tvayaḥ grahaṇāt  te eva uttama ādayaḥ ekatva ādayaḥ ca kāla traya vyākhyānena vyākhyātā veditavyāḥ atra āha vidyata eva kālaḥ parimāṇavat tvāt  iha yad na asti na tasya parimāṇavat tvam vidyate tad yathā khara viṣāṇasya asti ca kālasya parimāṇavat tvam kṣaṇa lava muhūrta divasa rātrī ahorātra pakṣa māsa saṃvatsara ādi bhedena tasmāt  parimāṇavat tvāt  vidyata eva kālaḥ iti ucyate yadi kālaḥ  nāma kaścid  syāt  syāt tasya parimāṇavat tvam na tu asti yasmāt  na āsthitaḥ  gṛhyate kālaḥ sthitaḥ kālaḥ  na vidyate yaḥ  gṛhyeta agṛhītaḥ ca kālaḥ prajñapyate katham iha yadi kālaḥ  nāma kaścid avasthitaḥ kṣaṇa ādi vyatiriktaḥ syāt  sa kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ parimāṇavat tvāt  gṛhyeta na tu avasthitaḥ kūṭasthaḥ kaścid  kālaḥ  nāma asti yaḥ kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ gṛhyeta tad evam na āsthitaḥ  gṛhyate kālaḥ asthita tvāt na gṛhyate iti arthaḥ atha api syāt  nitya eva avasthita svabhāvaḥ kālaḥ  nāma asti kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ abhivyajyate tathā hi kālaḥ pacati bhūtāni kālaḥ saṃharate prajāḥ kālaḥ supteṣu jāgarti kālaḥ  hi duratikramaḥ iti yaḥ ca evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ saḥ  avasthita svabhāvaḥ  asti iti ucyate evam api sthitaḥ kālaḥ  na vidyate yaḥ kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ abhivyajyamānaḥ  gṛhyeta kasmāt  punar  sthitaḥ kālaḥ  na asti iti ced  kṣaṇa ādi vyatirekeṇa āgṛhyamāṇa tvāt  api ca ayam kālaḥ saṃskṛta svabhāvaḥ san asti iti asaṃskṛta svabhāvaḥ  vā ubhayam ca saṃskṛta parīkṣāyām pratiṣiddham utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām asiddhau na asti saṃskṛtam saṃskṛtasya api asiddhau ca katham setsyati asaṃskṛtam iti anena tad evam na asti vyavasthitaḥ kālaḥ yaḥ  gṛhyeta yaḥ ca idānīm kālaḥ  na gṛhyate asthita tvāt avidyamāna svarūpa tvāt saḥ  agṛhyamāṇaḥ san katham kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ prajñapayitum bhāvataḥ pāryata iti āha agṛhītaḥ ca kālaḥ prajñapyate katham iti tasmāt na asti eva kālaḥ atra āha satyam na asti nityaḥ kālaḥ  nāma kaścid  rūpa ādi vyatiriktaḥ svabhāva siddhaḥ kim tarhi rūpa ādīn eva sa saṃskārān upādāya prajñaptaḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇa ādi vācyaḥ  bhavati tasmāt adoṣa iti ucyate evam api bhāvam pratītya kālaḥ ced kālaḥ  bhāvāt ṛte kutas  yadi evam bhāvam pratītya kālaḥ  bhavati iti bhavatā vyavasthāpyate yadā khalu bhāvaḥ na asti tadā niyatam tad hetukaḥ api kālaḥ  na asti iti pratipādayan  āha na ca kaścana bhāvaḥ asti iti pūrvam vistareṇa pratipādita tvāt vakṣyamāṇa pratiṣedhāt ca yadā ca evam na kaścid bhāvaḥ  asti bhāvataḥ tadā kutas  kālaḥ  bhaviṣyati kāla abhāvāt ca na santi kṣaṇa lava muhūrta ādayaḥ kāla bhedāḥ tad pariṇāma bhūtāḥ iti atas  kutas  pariṇāmavat tvena kāla siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati tasmāt na asti eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ iti uktam hi bhagavatā ārya hasti kakṣya sūtre yadi koci dharmāṇa bhavet svabhāvaḥ tatra eva gaccheya jinaḥ sa śrāvakaḥ  kūṭastha dharmāṇa siyā na nirvṛtī na niṣprapañcaḥ  bhavi jātu paṇḍitaḥ iti tathā buddha sahasra śatā ya atītā dharma sahasra śatāni bhaṇitvā na eva ca dharma na ca akṣara kṣīṇā na asti samudbhavu tena akṣīṇā iti tathā utpāda kāle hi tathāgatasya maitreya nāmā tu iha yaḥ  bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyati iyam kanaka āvṛtā mahī tasyāḥ  idānīm kuta āgamaḥ  asau ullāpanāḥ kāmaguṇā hi pañca vibhrāmaṇā mohana moṣa dharmiṇaḥ madhyāhna kāle hi yathā eva grīṣme jalam marīcyām hi tathā eva kāmāḥ ekena kalpena bhavet hi lokaḥ  ākāśa bhūtaḥ  gagana svabhāvaḥ  dāham vināśam ca payānti bhe[bhī ]ravaḥ kuta āgamaḥ kutra gatiḥ ca teṣām iti tad yathā pañca imāni bhikṣavaḥ saṃjñā mātram pratijñā mātram vyavahāra mātram saṃvṛti mātram yad uta atītaḥ  adhvā anāgataḥ  adhvā ākāśam nirvāṇam pudgalaḥ ca iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau kāla parīkṣā nāma ekonaviṃśam prakaraṇam sāmagrī parīkṣā viṃśatitamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyate kālaḥ phala pravṛttau sahakāri kāraṇa bhāvāt yaḥ  na asti na asau sahakāri kāraṇa bhāvena pratipadyate vandhyā tanayavat  tasmāt asti kālaḥ sahakāri kāraṇa bhāvāt iha bīja avani salila jvalana pavana gagana abhidhāna hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm pratītya ayam aṅkura upajāyamānaḥ satyām api bīja ādi pratyaya sāmagryām ṛtu viśeṣa asaṃnidhānāt na upajāyate yathā ca bāhyeṣu evam ādhyātmikeṣu api yathā uktam bhagavatā na praṇaśyanti karmāṇi kalpa koṭi śataiḥ api sāmagrīm prāpya kālam ca phalanti khalu dehinām iti yasmāt ca evam asti kāla apekṣā tasmāt asti asau kālaḥ  nāma yaḥ aṅkura ādi pravṛttau sahakāri kāraṇam bhavati iti ucyate syāt  sahakārikāraṇa tā kālasya yadi aṅkura ādi phalasya pravṛttiḥ eva syāt  na tu asti katham kṛtvā iha bīja ādi hetu pratyaya sāmagrītaḥ  aṅkura ādi phala udaye parikalpyamāne vyavasthitasya vā phalasya sāmagryām satyāṃtata utpādaḥ parikalpyeta avyavasthitasya vā kim ca atas  yadi tāvat  vyavasthitasya parikalpyate tad na yujyate iti pratipādayan  āha hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryā jāyate yadi phalam asti ca sāmagryām sāmagryā jāyate katham yadi hetu pratyaya sāmagryām tvad matena phalam asti nanu evam sati yasmāt  sāmagryām asti katham tayā tad janyate na hi kuṇḍe dadhi vidyamānam kuṇḍena janyate api ca yad vidyate tad niṣpanna tvāt  niṣpanna purovasthita ghaṭavat  na punar janma apekṣate abhivyaktiḥ sthaulyam vā sūkṣma ātmanā vidyamānasya kriyata iti ced  tasya api pakṣasya pūrvam eva āgacchati anyatas  na agniḥ indhane agniḥ na vidyate iti atra uktam uttaram atha na asti eva sāmagryām phalam iti parikalpyate etad api na upapadyate iti pratipādayan  āha hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryā jāyate yadi phalam na asti ca sāmagryām sāmagryā jāyate katham yadi hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryām na asti tad phalam katham tarhi hetu pratyaya sāmagryā phalam janyate tatra avidyamāna tvāt  sikatābhiḥ iva tailam ata eva asaṃbhāvayan  āha phalam na asti ca sāmagryām sāmagryā jāyate katham na tad phalam sāmagrītaḥ  jāyate iti abhiprāyaḥ kim ca anyat  hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryām asti ced phalam gṛhyeta nanu sāmagryām sāmagryām ca na gṛhyate yad  yatra asti tad  tatra gṛhyate tad yathā kuṇḍe dadhi yad ca yatra na asti na tad tatra gṛhyate tad yathā sikatāsu tailam maṇḍūka jaṭāyām śiromaṇiḥ atha syāt  vidyamānā api padārthāḥ ati saukṣmyāt  ati saṃnikarṣāt  ati viprakarṣāt  indriya upaghātāt mūrtivat dravya vyavadhānāt  mūrti antardhānāt  manaḥ navasthānāt  paramāṇuvat  akṣa stha añjana śalākāvat āditya gativat  taimirika ekaika keśavat  andha badhira ādi rūpa śabda ādivat  kuḍaya ādi vyavahita ghaṭa ādivat  siddha deva piśāca ādi śarīravat viṣaya antara vyāpṛtasya viṣaya antaravat na gṛhyate iti ced  kim khalu eṣā ām agṛhyamāṇānām astitve liṅgam yena eṣām astitve sati anupalabdhiḥ iti syāt  anumāna upamāna āgamaiḥ grahaṇāt eṣām astitvam iti ced  na tarhi teṣām anupalabdhiḥ iti vaktavyam anumāna ādibhiḥ upalabhyamāna tvāt  yad  rūpi indriya grāhyam tad  ebhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ vidyamānam api sanna gṛhyate iti ced  ucyate kim asmābhiḥ evam uktam rūpi indriyaiḥ vidyamānam sat  gṛhyeta iti kim tarhi sāmānyena eva yad  brūmaḥ gṛhyeta nanu sāmagryām iti atha api manyase yad  yatra na asti na tad  tasmāt utpadyate sikatābhyaḥ tailavat  utpadyate ca sāmagrītaḥ phalam tasmāt anumānataḥ sāmagryām phalasya astitvam iti ucyate yad  yatra asti na tad  tasmāt utpadyate tad yathā kuṇḍād dadhi iti asmāt api anumānāt astitvam asya ayuktam iti kṛtvā na asti eva sāmagryām phalam iti kim na gṛhyate atha api syāt  ubhyoḥ api pakṣayoḥ anumāna virodhāt  yathā astitvam na yuktam evam na astitvam api iti ucyate na vayam asya asattvam pratipādayāmaḥ kim tarhi para parikalpitam sattvam asya nirākurmaḥ evam na vayam asya sattvam pratipādayāmaḥ kim tarhi para parikalpitam asattvam asya apākurmaḥ anta dvaya parihāreṇa madhyamāyāḥ pratipadaḥ pratipādayitum iṣṭa tvāt iti uktam ca ārya devapādīye śatake stambha ādīnām alaṃkāraḥ  gṛhasya arthe nirarthakaḥ satkāryam eva yasya iṣṭam yasya asat kāryam eva ca iti tad evam na sāmagrītaḥ phalam utpadyate vidyamānasya grahaṇa prasaṅgāt  iti vyavasthitam atha manyase na asti eva sāmagryām phalam iti evam api hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryām na asti ced phalam hetavaḥ pratyayāḥ ca syuḥ ahetu pratyayaiḥ samāḥ yathā hi jvālā aṅgāra ādiṣu aṅkuraḥ na asti iti kṛtvā tasya te hetu pratyayā na bhavanti eva vivakṣitānām api bīja ādīnām hetu pratyaya tā na syāt  teṣu aṅkuraḥ na asti iti kṛtvā na ca ahetu pratyayebhyaḥ phala pravṛttiḥ yuktā iti na asti svabhāvataḥ phala pravṛttiḥ atra āha na eva hi sāmagryāḥ phala utpādana sāmarthyam asti yatas  iyam cintā syāt  kim sāmagryām phalam asti uta ahaḥ na asti iti kim tarhi hetoḥ phala utpādana sāmarthyam sāmagrī tu hetoḥ anugraha mātram karoti sa hetuḥ phalasya utpatti artham hetum datvā nirudhyate tena ca hetunā anugṛhyamāṇam phalam utpadyate iti ucyate na eva hi ajātasya phalasya hetoḥ anugrahaṇam asti na ca api ajātasya bandhyā tanayasi eva kenacid kiṃcid mātram kartum śakyam iti ayuktā eṣā kalpanā api ca hetukam phalasya datvā yadi hetuḥ nirudhyate yad dattam yad niruddham ca hetoḥ ātma dvayam bhavet  yadi hetuḥ phalasya utpatti artham hetukam kāraṇam datvā nirudhyata iti parikalpyate evam sati yad dattam yad niruddham ca tad ātma bhāva dvayam hetoḥ syāt  na ca etad  yuktam ardha śāśvata prasaṅgāt  nitya anityayoḥ ca paraspara viruddhayoḥ ekatva abhāvāt atha hetoḥ ātma bhāva dvaya prasaṅga parihāra artham sarva ātmanā nirodha iṣyate phalasya utpatti artham kiṃcid api adatvā evam api hetum phalasya ādatvā ca yadi hetuḥ nirudhyate hetau niruddhe jātam tad phalam āhetukam bhavet  yadi phalasya kiṃcid api adatvā sarva ātmanā hetuḥ nirudhyate nanu tasmin hetau niruddhe yad phalam utpadyate tad  āhetukam syāt  na ca āhetukam asti iti ayuktā eṣā kalpanā atra āha yadi evam phalasya hetoḥ utpattau doṣaḥ evam sati saha utpanna eva sāmagrī phalasya janikā astu tad yathā pradīpa prabhāyāḥ  iti eṣā api kalpanā na upapadyate iti pratipādayan  āha phalam saha eva sāmagryā yadi prādurbhavet punar  eka kālau prasajyete janakaḥ  yaḥ ca janyate na ca eka kālayoḥ savya itara gaḥ viṣāṇayoḥ janya janaka tvam dṛṣṭam vāma dakṣiṇa karayoḥ caraṇayoḥ vā iti ayuktā eṣā kalpanā iti ayuktam etad  atra āhuḥ eke na eva hi abhūtvā bhāvānām utpattiḥ yuktā ākasmikatva prasaṅgāt  tasmāt  hetu pratyaya sāmagrītaḥ pūrvam eva tad  phalam anāgata avasthāyām vyavasthitam anāgata ātmanā tasya hetu pratyaya sāmagryā vartamāna avasthā janyate dravyam tu vyavasthitam eva iti tān pratyucyate pūrvam eva ca sāmagryāḥ phalam prādurbhavet yadi hetu pratyaya nirmuktam phalam āhetukam bhavet  yadi bhavatām abhīpsitam sāmagrītaḥ pūrvam eva phalam svarūpataḥ syāt iti tad  hetu pratyaya nirapekṣam syāt  tatas ca āhetukam syāt  na ca āhetukānām padārthānām astitvam yuktam khara turaga uraga viṣāṇa ādīnām api astitva prasaṅgāt  pūrva siddhasya ca punar  hetu pratyaya apekṣayā niṣprayojanatva āditi yuktam etad  anye punar varṇayanti hetuḥ eva phalam janayati na sāmagrī na ca ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ yasmāt  na hi anyohetuḥ anyat  phalam yatas  kim hetum datvā phalasya hetuḥ nirudhyate uta adatvā eva iti vicāraḥ syāt  api tu hetuḥ eva niruddhaḥ phala ātmanā vyavasthitaḥ iti ucyate evam api niruddhe ced phalam hetau hetoḥ saṃkramaṇam bhavet  pūrva jātasya hetoḥ ca punarjanma prasajyate yadi niruddhe hetau bhavat matena phalam utpadyate tad ca phalam hetu ātmakam eva bhavati iti parikalpyate evam sati hetoḥ saṃkramaṇam bhavet  naṭasya veṣa antara parityāgena veṣa antara saṃcāravat hetoḥ saṃkramaṇa mātram eva syāt  na tu apūrvasya phalasya utpādaḥ tatas ca hetoḥ nityatā eva syāt  na ca nityānām astitvam kvacid asti yathā uktam śatake apratītya astitā na asti kadācid kasyacid kvacid  na kadācid kvacid kaścid vidyate tena śāśvataḥ iti kim ca etasyām kalpanāyām pūrva jātasya ca hetoḥ punarjanma prāpnoti na ca jātasya punar api [janma] yujyate niṣprayojana tvāt  anavasthā prasaṅgāt ca atha manyase yena ātmanā vidyamānaḥ  na tena eva ātmanā jāyate yena ca ātmanā avidyamānaḥ tena eva jāyata iti etad api na yuktam aparityakta hetu svabhāvasya hetu svarūpasya phalam iti saṃjñā mātra bhedāt avasthā bhedāt ca dravya abhedasya sādhayitum aśakyatvāt  phala avasthāyām ca parityakta hetu svabhāvasya phala śabda vācya tvāt  hetuḥ phala ātmanā tiṣṭhati iti yad kiṃcid etad  kim ca anyat  yadi hetuḥ phalam janayet  niruddhaḥ  vā janayet aniruddhaḥ  vā phalam api utpannam vā janayet anutpannam vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti pratipādayan  āha janayet phalam utpannam niruddhaḥ  astaṃgataḥ katham tiṣṭhan  api katham hetuḥ phalena janayet hṛtaḥ [yadi tāvata niruddhaḥ astaṃgataḥ hetuḥ utpannam sat  vidyamānam phalam janayati iti parikalpyate tad na upapadyate kasmāt iti ced  katham niruddhaḥ asaṃvidyamānaḥ hetuḥ phalam janayet  yadi janayati vandhyā putraḥ  api putram janayiṣyati phalam ca sat  vidyamānam api janma nirapekṣam api katham hetuḥ janayi ṣyati atha manyase śakti abhāvāt niruddhaḥ  na janayati kim tu tiṣṭhan  eva hetuḥ phalam janayiṣyati iti ucyate ] tiṣṭhan  api hetuḥ avikṛta rūpaḥ  vidyamānena phalena vṛtaḥ saṃbaddhaḥ katham janayet  iha hi kāraṇam vikṛtim gacchat jāyate anyasya kāraṇam iti kāraṇa abhāvam pratipadyamānasya hetoḥ avaśyam vikāreṇa bhavitavyam yaḥ tu na vikriyate sa hetu lakṣaṇa yukta eva na bhavati iti phalena ca saṃbaddhaḥ katham janayet  phalasya vidyamāna tvāt  atha manyase vidyamānasya phalasya punar janayitum aśakyatvāt  avṛta eva asaṃbaddha eva hetuḥ phalena phalam janayiṣyati iti etad api ayuktam iti āha atha āvṛtaḥ phalena asau katamat janayet phalam yadi hetuḥ phalena asaṃbaddha eva iṣyate tadā katamat idānīm phalam janayet  sarvam eva vā phalam janayet asaṃbaddha tvāt  na vā kiṃcid janayet asaṃbaddha tvāt eva iti abhiprāyaḥ kim ca anyat  yadi hetuḥ phalam janayet  sa dṛṣṭvā phalam janayet adṛṣṭvā vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha na hi adṛṣṭvā vā dṛṣṭvā vā hetuḥ janayate phalam tatra yadi hetuḥ dṛṣṭvā janayati iti parikalpyate tad na yujyate yasmāt vidyamānam eva draṣṭum pāryate na avidyamānam vidyamānam ced  tad na janyate vidyamāna tvāt iti evam tāvat  hetuḥ phalam dṛṣṭvā na janayati adṛṣṭvā api na janayati sarvasya phalasya hetoḥ janakatva prasaṅgāt  atha kim idam darśanam kim vā adarśanam iti ucyate prasiddham etad loke upalabdhiḥ darśanam iti nanu etad  bīja ādiṣu nirindriyeṣu na saṃbhavati saṃbhavatu mā vā na asmāka mayam paryanuyogaḥ kim tarhi tasya utpāda vādinaḥ tatra yaḥ utpāda vādī brūyāt  dṛṣṭvā janayati iti sa vaktavyaḥ na dṛṣṭam etad loke yad bīja ādikam paśyati iti tasmāt ayuktā eṣā kalpanā atha adṛṣṭvā kalpayet  evam api yad kiṃcid adṛṣṭam saṃbhavati tad sarvam utpādayet  na ca utpādayati tasmāt  na adṛṣṭvā api janayati aniṣṭa āpattyā hi vayam para kalpanām vicārayāmaḥ saṃsāra aṭavīkāntāragiridarīprapāta duḥkham ālā samākulāmā tāmīva buddhi pūrva kartṛkam ca puruṣa ādikāraṇinaḥ jagat abhyupagacchantaḥ  nirgranthāḥ ca eka indriyam bīja ādikam pratipannāḥ prasaṅgāt na vyativartanta iti tasmāt na asti doṣaḥ kim ca anyat  yadi yuṣmad abhimatam hetoḥ phalasya ca anyonya ḍhaukana lakṣaṇam saṃgamanam syāt  syāt tadānīm tayoḥ janya janaka bhāvaḥ yasmāt  na hi paraspara asaṃgatayoḥ āloka andhakārayoḥ saṃsāra nirvāṇa yoḥ janya janaka bhāvaḥ  dṛṣṭa iti atas  avaśyam hetu phala bhāvayoḥ janya janaka bhāvam icchatā pareṇa saṃgatiḥ abhyupeyā sā ca kāla traye api vicāryamāṇā na saṃbhavati atas  hetuḥ phalam na janayati yathā ca saṃgatiḥ na asti tathā pratipādayan  āha na atītasya hi atītena phalasya saha hetunā na ajātena na jātena saṃgatiḥ jātu vidyate atītasya tāvat  phalasya atītena hetunā saha jātu kadācid api saṃgatiḥ na asti atīta tvena ubhayoḥ api avidyamāna tvāt  na api ajātena hetunā atītasya phalasya saṃgatiḥ jātu vidyate naṣṭa ajāta tvena ubhayoḥ api avidyamāna tvāt  bhinna kāla tvāt ca na api jātena vartamānena hetunā saha atītasya phalasya saṃgatiḥ saṃbhavati bhinna kāla tvāt naṣṭasya ca phalasya avidyamāna tvāt vandhyā putreṇa iva devadattasya iti abhiprāyaḥ yathā ca atītasya phalasya atītena anāgata vartamānena hetunā saha na kadācid  saṃgatiḥ asti evam vartamānasya api phalasya traikālikena hetunā saha na asti saṃgatiḥ iti tad  pratipādayan  āha na jātasya hi ajātena phalasya saha hetunā na atītena na jātena saṃgatiḥ jātu vidyate jātasya phalasya bhinna kāla tvāt ajātena ca atītena ca hetunā saha saṃgamanam na asti na api vartamānasya vartamānena hetunā saha saṃgatiḥ asti hetu phalayoḥ yaugapadya abhāvāt tayoḥ ca saṃgatiḥ vaiyarthyāt  kim hi vidyamānayoḥ paraspara nirapekṣayoḥ punar  saṃgatyā prayojanam iti na asti saṃgatiḥ idānīm anāgatasya api phalasya yathā atīta anāgata pratyutpannena hetunā saha saṃgamanam na asti tathā pratipādayan  āha na ajātasya hi jātena phalasya saha hetunā na ajātena na naṣṭena saṃgatiḥ jātu vidyate ajātam hi phalam asaṃvidyamānam tasya bhinna kālena vartamānena atītena ca hetunā saha na asti saṃgamanam bhinna kāla tvāt anāgatena api hetunā saha na asti saṃgamanam ubhayoḥ avidyamāna tvāt  yadā ca evam sarvathā hetu phalayoḥ saṃgatiḥ na asti tadā asatyām saṃgatau hetuḥ katham janayate phalam na eva hetuḥ phalam janayati saṃgateḥ avidyamāna tvāt  vandhyā putram iva iti abhiprāyaḥ atha api syāt  satyām eva saṃgatau hetuḥ phalam janayati iti tad api na yuktam kāla traye api saṃgati anupalabdheḥ atha api kathaṃcid  hetu phalayoḥ saṃgatiḥ parikalpyate evam api satyām vā saṃgatau hetuḥ katham janayate phalam saṃnihitasya phalasya punar janma vaiyarthyāt  asaṃhitānām ca saṃgateḥ ayukta tvāt  iti abhiprāyaḥ kim ca anyat  hetuḥ phalena śūnyaḥ ced katham janayate phalam hetuḥ phalena aśūnyaḥ ced katham janayate phalam yaḥ  ayam phalasya hetuḥ phalasya janaka iṣyate sa tena śūnyaḥ  vā bhavan phalam utpādayet  aśūnyaḥ  vā tatra hetuḥ śūnyaḥ phalena rahitaḥ phalam na janayati ahetuvat  phala śūnya tvāt  phalena aśūnyaḥ  api hetuḥ phalam na janayati vidyamāna tvāt  phalasya vidyamāna putram devadatta iva evam tāvat  phala śūnyaḥ  vā phala aśūnyaḥ  vā hetuḥ phalam na janayati yad ca api phalam utpadyate tad ca api aśūnyam vā samutpadyate śūnyam vā tatra tāvat  phalam na utpatsyate aśūnyam aśūnyam na nirotsyate aniruddham anutpannam aśūnyam tad bhaviṣyati aśūnyam hi phalam apratītya samutpannam svabhāva vyavasthitam tad evaṃvidham phalam na eva utpatsyate svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt ca na nirotsyate tatas ca aśūnyam tad iṣyamāṇam aniruddham anutpannam ca syāt  na ca etad iṣṭam iti atas  aśūnyam tad phalam na bhavati utpāda nirodha abhyupagamāt idānīm śūnyam api tad phalam na saṃbhavati anudaya avyayavattva prasaṅgāt  iti pratipādayan  āha katham utpatsyate śūnyam katham śūnyam nirotsyate śūnyam api aniruddham tad anutpannam prasajyate tatra śūnyam ucyate yad svabhāvena na asti yad ca vastu svabhāvena na asti tad  katham utpatsyate katham vā nirotsyate na hi svabhāvena avidyamānasya ākāśa ādeḥ udaya vyayau dṛṣṭau tasmāt śūnyam api tad phalam iṣyamāṇam aniruddham anutpannam ca prasajyate kim ca anyat  yadi hetuḥ phalam janayet  sa phalāt avyatiriktaḥ  vā janayet  vyatiriktaḥ  vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha hetoḥ phalasya ca eka tvam na hi jātu upapadyate hetoḥ phalasya ca anya tvam na hi jātu upapadyate tad etad pratijñā mātrakam iti pratipādayan  āha ekatve phala hetvoḥ syāt aikyam janaka janyayoḥ pṛthaktve phala hetvoḥ syāt tulyaḥ  hetuḥ ahetunā yadi hetoḥ phalasya ca eka tvam syāt  tadā janya janakayoḥ eka tvam abhyupetam syāt  na ca anayoḥ eka tvam pitāputrayoḥ cakṣuḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānayoḥ bīja aṅkurayoḥ ca aikya prasaṅgāt  evam tāvat  hetoḥ phalasya ca eka tvam na asti idānīm anya tvam api na asti kim kāraṇam yadi hetoḥ phalasya ca bhavat matena abhimatam anya tvam syāt  tadā paratra nirapekṣa tvāt  hetu nirapekṣam eva phalam syāt  na ca etad evam iti atas  anya tvam api hetoḥ phalasya ca na saṃbhavati yayoḥ ca evam vicāryamāṇayoḥ tattva anya tve na staḥ tayoḥ na kadācid janya janaka bhāvaḥ iṣyate atas  na eva hetuḥ phalam janayati kim ca anyat  yadi hetuḥ phalam janayet  sa tad phalam svabhāvena sadbhūtam vā janayet  asat bhūtam vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha phalam svabhāva sadbhūtam kim hetuḥ janayiṣyati phalam svabhāva asat bhūtam kim hetuḥ janayiṣyati tatra yad  phalam svabhāvena sadbhūtam svabhāvena vidyamānam tad na punar janyate vidyamāna tvāt  vidyamāna ghaṭavat  yad api svabhāvena asat bhūtam phalam tad api hetuḥ na janayati svabhāvena asat bhūta tvāt  khara viṣāṇavat  pratibimbena anaikāntika tā iti ced  bhavatu anaikāntika tā naiḥsvābhāvyam tu siddham bhāvānām tatas ca sa svabhāva vāda tyāgaḥ syāt  asmad vāda anuvarṇanam eva syāt  sa svabhāvaḥ ca na kaścid  padārthaḥ  nāma asti iti pratidvan dvaya bhāvāt  niḥsvabhāvaḥ  api padārthaḥ  na asti iti kutaḥ anaikāntika tā na hi asmākam pratibimba kam sa svabhāvam na api niḥsvabhāvam dharmiṇam antareṇa tad dharmayoḥ api abhāvāt na hi āryāḥ pratibimba kam nāma kiṃcid  niḥsvabhāvam sa svabhāvam vā upalabhanta iti tatra pūrvam phalam na utpatsyate ityādinā śloka dvayena sākṣāt utpatti kriyā kartṛ tvam phalasya niṣiddham idānīm hetoḥ phala utpatti kriyā prayojaka tvam pratiṣiddham iti ayam asya pūrvakāt viśeṣa iti vijñeyam atra āha yadi api hetoḥ phala utpatti kriyā prayojaka tvam niṣiddham tathā api hetuḥ tāvat  svabhāvataḥ  asti na ca asati phale hetoḥ hetu tvam sidhyati tasmāt  phalam api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate syāt hetuḥ yadi ajanayataḥ  asya hetu tvam syāt  na ca ajanayamānasya hetu tvam upapadyate atha syāt  yadi api evam hetoḥ hetu tvam na asti tathā api phalam tāvat asti na ca hetum antareṇa phalam yuktam iti phala sadbhāvāt  hetuḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate yadā ajanayamānasya hetoḥ hetu tvam na asti iti uktam tadā hetutva anupapattau ca phalam kasya bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt  phalam api na asti iti atra āha na eva hi kevalasya hetoḥ phala utpatti kriyāyāḥ prayojaka tvam kim tarhi hetu pratyaya sāmagryā phalam janyate iti ucyate ukta doṣa tvāt  na yuktam etad  api ca iyam hetu pratyaya sāmagrī yadi phalasya janikā iti kalpyate kim sa asvayam eva tāvat ātmānam janayati uta ahaḥ na yadi janayati iti kalpyate tad na yujyate na hi alabdha ātma bhāvasya prayojaka tvam dṛṣṭam iti atas  sāmagryā avaśyam labdha ātma bhāvayā bhavitavyam na ca labdha ātma bhāvāyāḥ punar  sva ātma utpāde prayojaka tvam yuktam iti atas  na sāmagrī sva ātmānam utpādayati yā ca ātmānam na utpādayati sā katham phalam utpādayitum śaknoti iti pratipādayan  āha na ca pratyaya hetūnām iyam ātmānam ātmanā yā sāmagrī janayate sā katham janayet phalam pratyayānām hetūnām ca yā iyam sāmagrī sā tāvat ātmanā eva ātmānam na utpādayati sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt  satyāḥ punar utpāda vaiyarthyāt ca yā ca evam ātmānam eva tāvat na janayati sā katham phalam janayiṣyati na hi bandhyā duhitā ātmānam janayitum aśaktā satī putram janayiṣyati iti yujyate evam sāmagrī api sva ātmā ajanikā phalam janayati iti na yujyate tasmāt  na sāmagrīkṛtam phalam atha api syāt  yadi sāmagrīkṛtam phalam na saṃbhavati evam tarhi asāmagrīkṛtam bhaviṣyati iti ced  ucyate na āsām agrīkṛtam phalam yadā sāmagrīkṛtam phalam na saṃbhavati tadā katham atyanta viruddham asām agrīkṛtam bhaviṣyati asāmagrīkṛtam phalam na saṃbhavati atha syāt  yadi api na asti phalam svabhāvataḥ tathā api hetu pratyaya sāmagrī tāvat asti na ca phalam antareṇa hetu pratyaya sāmagrī saṃbhavati iti phalam api saṃbhaviṣyati iti ucyate syāt hetu pratyaya sāmagrī yadi phalam eva bhavet  yadā tu yathā uditena nyāyena phalam eva na asti tadā asti pratyaya sāmagrī kuta eva phalam vinā phala abhāve sati nirhetukā hetu pratyaya sāmagrī api na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ uktam hi ārya lalita vistara sūtre kaṇṭha uṣṭha pratītya tālukam jihva parivarti ravanti akṣarāḥ na ca kaṇṭha gatā na tāluke akṣara eka ekaśa na upalabhyate sāmagri pratītyatas ca sā vāca mana buddhi vaśena niścarī mana vāca adṛśya rūpiṇī bāhyatas  abhyantari na upalabhyate utpāda vyayam vipaśyataḥ  vācaruta ghoṣa svarasya paṇḍitaḥ kṣaṇikām vaśikām tadā dṛśī sarva vāca pratiśrutakopamā tathā ārya upāli paripṛcchāyām uktam bhagavatā iha śāsani sūramaṇīye pravrajathā gṛhiliṅga jahitvā phalavantu bhaviṣyatha śreṣṭhā eṣu nideśitu kāruṇikena pravrajitva gṛhiliṅga jahitvā sarva phalasya bhaviṣyati prāptiḥ puna dharma sabhāva tulitvā sarva phalāna phalāna ca prāptiḥ alabhanta phalam tatha prāptim āścariyam puna jāyati teṣām ahaḥ ati kāruṇikaḥ  narasiṃhaḥ  suṣṭupadeśita yukti jinena iti tathā ārya prajñāpāramitāyām aṣṭa sāhasrikāyām tena hi kauśika bodhisattvena mahāsattvena mahā saṃnāha saṃnaddhena na rūpe sthātavyam na vedanāyām na saṃjñāyām na saṃskāreṣu na vijñāne sthātavyam na srotaāpatti phale na sakṛdāgāmi phale na anāgāmi phale na arhat tve na pratyekabuddha tve na samyaksaṃbuddha tve sthātavyam iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau sāmagrī parīkṣā nāma viṃśatitamam prakaraṇam saṃbhava vibhava parīkṣā ekaviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyata eva svabhāvataḥ kālaḥ saṃbhava vibhava nimitta tvāt  iha kaṃcid  kāla viśeṣam apekṣya aṅkura utpattiḥ bhāvānām utpādaḥ  bhavati kaṃcid kāla viśeṣam apekṣya vibhavaḥ  vināśaḥ  bhavati na sarvadā vidyamānāyām api hetu pratyaya sāmagryām iti atas  vidyata eva kālaḥ saṃbhava vibhava nimittattvāt  ucyate syāt  saṃbhava vibhava nimitta tā kālasya yadi saṃbhava vibhavau  eva syātām na tu staḥ yathā ca na staḥ tathā pratipādayan  āha vinā vā saha vā na asti vibhavaḥ saṃbhavena vai vinā vā saha vā na asti saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavena vai iha yadi saṃbhava vibhavau syātām tau anyonyam sahabhāvena vā syātām vinā abhāvena vā ubhayathā ca vicāryamāṇau na saṃbhavataḥ katham kṛtvā tatra tāvat  yathā vinā saṃbhavena utpādena vibhavaḥ  vināśaḥ  na asti tathā pratipādayan  āha bhaviṣyati katham nāma vibhavaḥ saṃbhavam vinā vinā eva janma maraṇam vibhavaḥ  na udbhavam vinā saṃbhavam vinā katham nāma vibhavaḥ  vināśaḥ  bhaviṣyati katham nāma iti anena prasiddham atyanta asaṃbhavam darśayati katham nāma bhaviṣyati na eva etad saṃbhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ yadi punar vinā eva saṃbhavam vibhavaḥ syāt  kaḥ  doṣaḥ syāt  ucyate vinā eva janma maraṇam syāt  ajātasya maraṇam syāt  na ca ajātasya maraṇam dṛṣṭam iti tasmāt vibhavaḥ  na udbhavam vinā bhavitum arhati ādyena atra ślokasya ardhena pratijñā madhyena pādena prasaṅga āpādanam antyena nigamanam iti vijñeyam evam tāvat vinā saṃbhavena vibhavaḥ  na yuktaḥ iti pratipādya idānīm saha saṃbhavena api vibhavaḥ  na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha saṃbhavena eva vibhavaḥ katham saha bhaviṣyati na janma maraṇam ca evam tulya kālam hi vidyate yadi hi saṃbhavena saha yugapad  tulya kālam vibhavaḥ syāt  evam sati janma maraṇe yugapad  syātām na ca evam paraspara viruddhe āloka andhakāravat ekasmin kāle vidyete iti tasmāt  saha api saṃbhavena vibhavasya na asti siddhiḥ iti sthitam yadā ca evam saṃbhavena vinā vā saha vā vibhavasya na asti siddhiḥ evam saṃbhavasya api vinā vā saha vā vibhavena na asti siddhiḥ iti pratipādayan  āha bhaviṣyati katham nāma saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavam vinā anitya tā hi bhāveṣu na kadācid na vidyate na eva hi saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavena vinā yujyate yasmāt anitya tā hi bhāveṣu bhavana dharmakeṣu utpāda dharmakeṣu na kadācid na vidyate kim tarhi sarvadā eva vidyate uktam hi jarā maraṇa dharmeṣu sarva bhāveṣu sarvadā tiṣṭhanti katame bhāvā ye jarā maraṇam vinā iti yadā ca evam nityam anitya tā anugatāḥ sarve bhāvāḥ tadā kutas  sā kācid avasthā yā vināśa rahitā syāt iti atas  na asti vibhavena vinā utpāda iti evam tāvat vinā vibhavena na asti saṃbhavaḥ śeṣam atra saṃskṛta parīkṣāyām vicāri tattvāt na vicāryate yaḥ tu sa hetukaḥ  vināśaḥ saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvāt  utpādavat  iti sādhanam utkṣipya antya citta caittakṣaṇaiḥ anaikāntika tām āha sa na yuktam āha tad vināśasya api jāti pratyaya tvena sa hetuka tvāt  sādhya sama tvāt ca anaikāntika tā bhāvāt yad api nirdiṣṭam bhāva ātma bhāva eva abhūtvā bhāvāt utpāda ucyate tasmāt  dravya sat utpāda siddheḥ vyavahārataḥ  dṛṣṭānta bhāva iti tad api na yuktam adravya satām pratibimba ādīnām sa hetukatva abhyupagamāt yathā uktam ācārya pādaiḥ hetutaḥ saṃbhavaḥ  yeṣām tad abhāvāt na santi ye katham nāma na te spaṣṭam pratibimba samā matāḥ iti asmāt ā[gamāt] kutaḥ vyavahārataḥ  dṛṣṭānta asiddhiḥ yadi ca bhāvāt  yad  tattva anya tvena na śakyate vaktum tad  saṃvṛtya api na asti iti ucyate nīla ādikam api na asti iti ucyate yathā uktam ratnāvalyām rūpasya abhāva mātra tvāt ākāśam nāma mātrakam bhūtaiḥ vinā kutaḥ rūpam nāma mātrakam api atas  iti api ca kutaḥ mādhyamikānām svabhāva rūpam siddha sattākam yasya avasthā viśeṣa utpādaḥ syāt  atas  ayuktam eva dṛṣṭānta asiddha tā udbhāvanam yad ca uktam na sa hetukaḥ  vināśaḥ avināśavat tvāt  yathā asaṃskṛtam iti tasya evam bruvataḥ  mahāntam virodha mayam hetuḥ ābhavati yathā hi ayam hetuḥ vināśasya nirhetuka tvam sādhayati evam saṃskṛta lakṣaṇatva abhāvam api sādhayati tathā saṃskāra skandha saṃgraha pratītya samutpāda aṅga saṃgraha ādikam api sarvam virodhayati iti na yuktam etad matam tathā na vijñānam viṣaya svarūpa  chedakam avijñānavat tvāt  asaṃskṛtavat  ityādinā sarva niṣedhāt mahatī aniṣṭāpattiḥ upapadyate asya iti na astheyam etad  idānīm vibhavena saha yathā saṃbhavasya na asti siddhiḥ tathā pratipādayan  āha saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavena eva katham saha bhaviṣyati na janma maraṇam ca eva tulya kālam hi vidyate yadi hi saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavena eva saha syāt  tadā janma maraṇayoḥ tulya kālatā syāt  na ca [sā] saṃbhavati tasmāt  sahabhāvena api saṃbhava vibhavayoḥ na asti siddhiḥ atha syāt  yadi api janma maraṇayoḥ ekībhāvena vā nānā bhāvena vā na asti siddhiḥ tathā api vidyete eva saṃbhava vibhavau vācya tvāt vijñānavat  iti ucyate yadi vācya tvena anayoḥ siddhiḥ iṣyate vandhyā putrasya api iṣyatām api ca saha anyonyena vā siddhiḥ vinā anyonyena vā yayoḥ na vidyate tayoḥ siddhiḥ katham nu khalu vidyate sahabhāva asahabhāva rahitam na asti pakṣa antaram yatas  saṃbhava vibhavayoḥ siddhiḥ syāt  avācya tayā siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced  kā iyam avācya tā nāma yadi miśrībhāvaḥ saḥ  anupapannaḥ pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayaḥ miśrībhāva abhāvāt  anirdhāryamāṇau svarūpa tvāt  bandhyā putra śyāma gaura tā ādivat na staḥ eva saṃbhava vibhavau  iti yadā ca evam saṃbhava vibhavau na staḥ tadā tad hetuḥ api kālaḥ  na asti iti siddham kim ca anyat  iha imau saṃbhava vibhavau parikalpyamānau kṣaya dharmiṇaḥ  vā bhāvasya parikalpyeyātām kṣaya dharmiṇaḥ  vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti pratipādayan  āha kṣayasya saṃbhavaḥ  na asti na akṣayasya api saṃbhavaḥ kṣayasya vibhavaḥ  na asti vibhavaḥ  na akṣayasya ca tatra kṣayasya kṣaya lakṣaṇasya bhāvasya virodhi dharma sadbhāvāt saṃbhavaḥ  na yuktaḥ akṣayasya api bhāva lakṣaṇa viyukta tvāt  khara viṣāṇasya iva saṃbhavaḥ  na yuktaḥ evam kṣayasya vibhavaḥ  na asti kṣaya dharmaḥ  hi avidyamānaḥ tasya nirāśrayaḥ  vibhavaḥ  na yuktaḥ tathā vibhavaḥ  na akṣayasya ca akṣaya dharmaḥ  hi bhāva abhāva lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇaḥ tasya avidyamānasya kutaḥ vibhavaḥ  bhaviṣyati yau ca saṃbhava vibhavau na kṣaya dharmiṇaḥ  na akṣaya dharmiṇaḥ  bhāvasya saṃbhavataḥ tau na saṃbhavataḥ iti na staḥ saṃbhava vibhavau atra āha vidyete eva bhāvānām saṃbhava vibhavau tad āśrayi dharmi sadbhāvāt iha bhāva āśrayau saṃbhava vibhavau sa ca tāvat  bhāvaḥ asti tad sadbhāvāt tad āśritau  api dharmau bhaviṣyataḥ iti ucyate syātām bhāva āśritau  etau dharmau yadi bhāvaḥ syāt  yadā tu bhāvaḥ na asti tadā saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavaḥ ca eva vinā bhāvam na vidyate kasmāt punarbhāvaḥ  na asti iti ced  yasmāt  saṃbhavam vibhavam ca eva vinā bhāvaḥ na vidyate bhāvasya hi lakṣaṇa bhūtau saṃbhava vibhavau tau ca svarūpataḥ  na staḥ iti pratiṣiddhau yadā ca tau bhāvataḥ pratiṣiddhau tadā bhāva lakṣaṇam saṃbhavam vibhavam ca vinā kutaḥ bhāva lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇaḥ  bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati bhāvam ca vinā na staḥ saṃbhava vibhavau apare tu pūrva ardham paścimam kṛtvā vyācakṣate staḥ eva saṃbhava vibhavau bhāva dharma tvāt  iha yad na asti na tasya asti bhāva dharma tvam tad yathā maṇḍūka jaṭā śiromaṇeḥ bhāva dharmau ca saṃbhava vibhavau tasmāt  staḥ eva tau iti yadi kasyacid  paramārthataḥ saṃbhava vibhavau syātām sa bhāva iti yuktam syāt abhidhātum tau ca na staḥ iti saṃbhavam vibhavam ca eva vinā bhāvaḥ na vidyate bhāvasya saṃbhava vibhava sattve vidyamāna tvāt  iti bhāvaḥ tad asattve ca hetoḥ asiddhārtha tā tathā saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavaḥ ca eva vinā bhāvam na vidyate āśrayasya abhāvāt āśritasya asiddhiḥ iti abhisaṃdhiḥ iti kim ca anyat  iha imau saṃbhava vibhavau parikalpamānau śūnyasya vā bhāvasya parikalpyeyātām aśūnyasya vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti pratipādayan  āha saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavaḥ ca eva na śūnyasya upapadyate avidyamāna āśraya tvāt ākāśa citravat iti abhiprāyaḥ tathā saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavaḥ ca eva na aśūni asya upapadyate aśūnyasya asattvāt  nirāśrayau saṃbhava vibhavau na upapadyataḥ kim ca anyat  iha yadi saṃbhava vibhavau syātām tau eka tvena vā syātām anya tvena vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavaḥ ca eva na eka iti upapadyate paraspara viruddhayoḥ āloka andhakārayoḥ iva ekatva anupapatteḥ saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavaḥ ca eva na nānā iti upapadyate ubhayoḥ parasparam avyabhicāri tvāt  na hi saṃbhava rahitasya vināśaḥ na vibhava rahitasya saṃbhavaḥ  dṛṣṭa iti evam ubhayoḥ parasparam avyabhicāri tvāt  saṃbhavaḥ  vibhavaḥ ca eva na nānā iti upapadyate atha syāt  kim anayā sūkṣma īkṣikayā āgopāla aṅganā ādikaḥ  hi janaḥ yasmāt  saṃbhavam vibhavam ca paśyati tasmāt  staḥ saṃbhava vibhavau na hi avidyamānaḥ  vandhyā tanayaḥ śakyaḥ  draṣṭum iti evam api dṛśyate saṃbhavaḥ ca eva vibhavaḥ ca eva te bhavet  ucyate anaikāntikam etad  na hi yad  yad  lokena upalabhyate tasya tasya astitvam tathā hi āgopāla aṅganā ādikaḥ  janaḥ gandharvanagara māyāsvapna alāta cakra marīcikā salila ādikam avidyamānam api paśyati indriya upaghātāt evam imau  api saṃbhava vibhavau asantau mohāt eva paśyati iti āha dṛśyate saṃbhavaḥ ca eva mohāt vibhava eva ca atha kasmāt  punar etad evam niścīyate avidyamāna svarūpau  imau saṃbhava vibhavau mohāt eva vāra lokena dṛśyete iti yuktyā hi etad evam niścīyate kā punar atra yuktiḥ iha yadi kaścid  bhāvaḥ nāma bhavet  niyatam sa bhāvāt vā jāyeta abhāvāt vā tathā yadi abhāvaḥ  nāma kaścid  saḥ  api bhāvāt vā jāyeta abhāvāt vā ubhayathā ca ubhayoḥ api asaṃbhavaḥ iti āha na bhāvāt jāyate bhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ abhāvāt na jāyate na abhāvāt jāyate abhāvaḥ  abhāvaḥ  bhāvān na jāyate bhāvāt  tāvat  saṃbhava ākhyād bhāvasya saṃbhava ākhyasya utpādaḥ  na vidyate kārya kāraṇayoḥ yaugapadya abhāvāt utpādasya ca labdhajanmanaḥ punar utpāda vaiyarthyāt  abhāvāt api bhāvaḥ na jāyate kim kāraṇam abhāvaḥ  hi nāma vibhavaḥ  vināśaḥ sa ca bhāva viruddhaḥ tasmāt bhāva viruddhāt  katham bhāvaḥ syāt  yadi syāt  tadā vandhyāduhituḥ api putraḥ syāt  na ca etad evam iti tasmāt abhāvāt api bhāvaḥ na bhavati idānīm abhāvaḥ  api abhāvāt na bhavati bhāva nivṛtti rūpaḥ  hi abhāvaḥ tatas  kutaḥ asya kārya karaṇa sāmarthyam yadi syāt  nirvāṇasya api kārya karaṇa sāmarthyam syāt  yadi ca abhāvāt abhāvaḥ syāt  tadā vandhyāduhituḥ api putraḥ syāt  na ca etad evam iti tasmāt abhāvāt api abhāvaḥ  na bhavati idānīm bhāvāt api abhāvaḥ  na bhavati bhāva viruddhaḥ  hi abhāvaḥ sa katham bhāvāt bhavet  yadi bhavet  pradīpāt andhakāraḥ syāt  yatas ca evam vicāryamāṇau saṃbhava vibhavau na staḥ tasmāt mohāt eva lokena dṛśyete iti vijñeyam athavā ayam anyaḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ iha hi yadi saṃbhava vibhavau syātām tau bhāva āśrayau vā syātām abhāva āśrayau vā tau ca bhāva abhāvau sarvathā vicāryamāṇau na saṃbhavataḥ tatas ca kutaḥ nirāśrayau saṃbhava vibhavau  iti atas  dṛśyate saṃbhavaḥ ca eva mohāt vibhava eva ca iti vijñeyam yathā ca bhāva abhāvau na saṃbhavataḥ tathā pratipādayan  āha na bhāvāt jāyate bhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ abhāvāt na jāyate na abhāvāt jāyate abhāvaḥ  abhāvaḥ  bhāvān na jāyate asya arthaḥ pūrvavat  api ca yadi kaścid  bhāvaḥ nāma syāt  tasya udaya vyayavat tvāt  saṃbhava vibhavau syātām na ca kaścid  bhāvaḥ svarūpataḥ  asti khara viṣāṇavat  svabhāva an utpanna tvāt  anutpanna tvam asiddham iti ced  tad  siddham yasmāt  na svatas  jāyate bhāvaḥ paratas  na eva jāyate na svatas  paratas ca eva jāyate jāyate kutas  etad ca ādya eva prakaraṇe vyākhyā tattvāt na punar vyākhyāyate yaḥ ca evam yathā ukta prakāreṇa jāyate sa idānīm kutaḥ jāyate na eva kutaścid jāyate iti abhiprāyaḥ avaśyam ca etad evam abhyupeyam sarvathā na asti bhāvasya utpāda iti bhāva sadbhāvatā abhyupagame ca bhavataḥ śāśvata uccheda darśanam āpadyate bauddha mata anugasya iti āha bhāvam abhyupapannasya śāśvata uccheda darśanam prasajyate yasmāt  sa bhāvaḥ hi nityaḥ  anityaḥ  atha vā bhavet  yaḥ  hi yathā udita padārtha vyavasthām atikramya bhāva sadbhāva darśanam abhyupaiti tasya avaśyam pravacana atyanta viruddham śāśvata uccheda darśana dvayam āpadyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt  sa bhāvaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ nityaḥ  vā bhavet anityaḥ  vā yadi nityaḥ tadā niyatam śāśvata vādaḥ atha anityaḥ tadā niyatam uccheda iti atra āha bhāvam abhyupapannasya na eva ucchedaḥ  na śāśvatam kim kāraṇam yasmāt  udaya vyaya saṃtānaḥ phala hetvorbhavaḥ sa hi yaḥ  hi hetu phalayoḥ udaya vyaya anuprabandhaḥ sa hi asmākam bhavaḥ saṃsāraḥ tatra yadi hetuḥ nirudhyeta tad hetukam phalam na utpadyeta tadā syāt uccheda vāda doṣaḥ yadi ca hetuḥ na nirudhyeta svarūpeṇa avatiṣṭhet  tadā syāt śāśvata vāda darśana doṣaḥ na ca etad evam iti tasmāt  bhāva abhyupagame api na asti śāśvata uccheda darśana doṣa dvaya prasaṅgaḥ sa eva saṃsāraḥ yaḥ  ayam hetu phalā vicchinna krama vartī utpāda vyaya anuprabandhaḥ saṃskārāṇām iti atas  na asti asmāka mayam doṣa iti ucyate udaya vyaya saṃtānaḥ phala hetvorbhavaḥ sa ced  nanu evam api vyayasya apunarutpatteḥ hetu ucchedaḥ prasajyate yaḥ  hi hetu kṣaṇaḥ phalasya utpattau hetu bhāvam upetya nirudhyate nanu tasya vyayavataḥ  hetu kṣaṇasya punar anutpādāt uccheda darśanam āpadyate tava ayam katham na doṣa iti ced  bhāvam abhyupapannasya ayam doṣaḥ na ca mayā bhāvaḥ abhyupagataḥ svabhāva an utpanna tvāt  sarva dharmāṇām yatra api mayā pratītya yad yad bhavati na hi tāvat tad eva tad  na ca anyat api tad tasmāt na ucchedaḥ  na api śāśvatam iti uktam tatra api amunā nyāyena naiḥsvābhāvyam eva bhāvānām pratipāditam anyathā hi sati bhāva svarūpe bīja aṅkurayoḥ katham anya tvam na syāt  tasmāt na ayam prasaṅgaḥ  asmākam bādhaka iti evam tāvat  bhāvam abhyupapannasya hetoḥ punar anutpādāt uccheda darśana prasaṅgam udbhāvya idānīm śāśvata vāde doṣa prasaṅgam udbhāvayan  āha sadbhāvasya svabhāvena na asadbhāvaḥ ca yujyate yadi hi hetoḥ sadbhāvaḥ svabhāvataḥ syāt  tasya paścāt asadbhāvaḥ  na syāt  svabhāvasya napāyi tvāt  tatas ca śāśvata darśana prasaṅgaḥ tad avastha eva kim ca anyat  nirvāṇa kāle ca ucchedaḥ praśamāt bhava saṃtateḥ yadi api hetu phalayoḥ udaya vyaya saṃtāna pravṛttyā śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ parihriyate tathā api yatra asya saṃtānasya punar api apravṛttiḥ tatra nirvāṇe niyatam uccheda darśanam āpadyate uccheda darśanam ca prahātavyam iti uktam bhagavatā evaṃvidham uccheda darśanam na bhaviṣyati iti ced  anyat api kimartham bhavatā bhaviṣyati iti bhāva viccheda ālambana tvāt nirvāṇa kāle bhāva viccheda ālambanavat iti abhiprāyaḥ yad ca uktam udaya vyaya saṃtānaḥ phala hetvorbhavaḥ sa hi iti tad api na upapadyate katham kṛtvā iha hi caramaḥ  bhavaḥ  nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ prathamaḥ  gati pratisaṃdhi lakṣaṇaḥ tatra caramaḥ  bhavaḥ  nirudhyamānaḥ  hetu tvena avatiṣṭhate upapatti lakṣaṇaḥ tu prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ phala rūpa tvena vyavatiṣṭhate anayoḥ ca bhavayoḥ saṃsāra iti saṃjñā kṛtā atra ca idam vicāryate ya eṣa prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ phala rūpa tvena vyavasthāpyate sa kim carame bhave niruddhe upajāyate atha aniruddhe uta nirudhyamāne yatas  hetu phala anuprabandhāt saṃsāraḥ syāt  sarvathā ca vicāryamāṇaḥ  na saṃbhavati iti pratipādayan  āha carame na niruddhe ca prathamaḥ  yujyate bhavaḥ carame na aniruddhe ca prathamaḥ  yujyate bhavaḥ tatra yadi carame bhave niruddhe prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ  jāyate iti parikalpyate tadā nirhetuka syāt  dahana dagdha bījāt api aṅkura udayaḥ syāt  na ca etad iṣṭam tasmāt carame niruddhe prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ  na yujyate idānīm aniruddhe api carame bhave prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ  na yujyate yadi syāt  nirhetukaḥ syāt  dvi rūpa tā ca ekasya sattvasya syāt  apūrva sattva prādurbhāvaḥ ca pūrvasya ca nitya tā syāt  avinaṣṭe ca bīje aṅkura udayaḥ syāt  na ca etad evam iṣṭam iti atas  carame na aniruddhe ca prathamaḥ  yujyate bhavaḥ iti sthitam idānīm nirudhyamāne api carame bhave prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ  yathā na upapadyate tathā pratipādayan  āha nirudhyamāne carame prathamaḥ  yadi jāyate nirudhyamāna ekaḥ syāt jāyamānaḥ  aparaḥ  bhavet  tatra nirudhyamānaḥ  vartamānaḥ  vartamāna pratyaya anta vācya tvāt jāyate iti api vartamāna eva ucyate vartamāna śabda vācya tvāt athavā nirudhyamānaḥ  nirodha kriyā kārakaḥ yaḥ ca api jāyate asau  api jani kriyā kārakaḥ tau ca eka kāla āviṣyamāṇau yaugapadyena eva staḥ tatas ca nirudhyamānaḥ ekaḥ  bhavaḥ syāt  jāyamānaḥ ca apara iti yaugapadyena eva dvau bhavau prāpnutaḥ na ca ekasya yugapad  dvau bhavau saṃbhavataḥ iti uktam etad  tad evam yathā uktena vicāra kameṇa na ced nirudhyamānaḥ ca jāyamānaḥ ca yujyate sārdham ca mriyate yeṣu teṣu skandheṣu jāyate caśabdaḥ samuccaya arthaḥ pṛthak pṛthak  ca iti etad saṃnidhāpayati yadā evam yathā udita nyāyena niruddhe carame prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ  na saṃbhavati aniruddhe api carame prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ  na saṃbhavati sārdham ca ekasmiḥ ca kāle caramena bhavena saha prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ  na saṃbhavati tad  kim idānīm yeṣu eva skandheṣu mriyate teṣu eva jāyate iti syāt  yeṣu skandheṣu sthitaḥ  mriyate teṣu eva jāyate iti atyanta viruddham etad  na hi mriyamāṇaḥ  jāyate iti dṛṣṭam tad  evam triṣu api kāleṣu na yuktā bhavat abhimatā bhava saṃtatiḥ carame bhave niruddhe aniruddhe nirudhyamāne yasmāt  prathamaḥ  bhavaḥ  na saṃbhavati tasmāt  triṣu api kāleṣu bhavasaṃtirnā asti triṣu kāleṣu yā na asti sā katham bhava saṃtatiḥ yā ca idānīm triṣu kāleṣu na asti kutas  sā anyena ātmanā bhaviṣyati iti sarvathā na asti bhavat matā bhava saṃtatiḥ tatas ca yad uktam udaya vyaya saṃtānaḥ phala hetvorbhavaḥ sa hi iti tad na yuktam tatas ca bhāva abhyupagame sati sa eva śāśvata uccheda vāda prasaṅgaḥ  durnivāraḥ  bhavatām iti atas  na asti eva bhāvānām svabhāvata utpattiḥ iti siddham yathā uktam ārya samādhi rāja bhaṭṭārake tathā bījasya sataḥ  yathā aṅkuraḥ  na ca yaḥ  bīju sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas  na ca eva tad evam anuccheda aśāśvata dharmatā mudrāt pratimudra dṛśyate mudra saṃkrānti na ca upalabhyate na ca tatra na ca eva sa anyatas  evam saṃskāra anuccheda śāśvatāḥ ata eva uktam ārya nāgārjuna pādaiḥ svādhyāya dīpa mudrā darpaṇa ghoṣa arka kānta bījāmraiḥ skandha pratisaṃdhiḥ asaṃkramaḥ ca vidvadbhiḥ avadhāryau iti tathā bhagavān jāyate cyavate ca api na ca jātiḥ na ca cyutiḥ yasya vijānata eṣa samādhiḥ na asya durlabhaḥ iti tathā sū sukhitā sada te nara loke yehi acintiya jñātibhi dharmāḥ na ca dharma adharma vikalpaḥ  citta papañca vibhāvita sarvi bhāva abhāva vibhāvayi jñānam sarvam acintayi sarvam abhūtam ye puna citta vaśa anuga bālāḥ te dukhitā bhava koṭi śateṣu yaḥ  api ca cintayi śūnyaka dharmān saḥ  api ku mārga papanna ku bālaḥ akṣara kīrtita śūnyaka dharmāḥ te ca anakṣara akṣara uktāḥ śānta paśānta ya cintayi dharmān saḥ  api ca cittu na jātu na bhūtaḥ citta vitarkaṇa sarvi papañcāḥ sūkṣma acintiya budhyatha dharmān iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau saṃbhava vibhava parīkṣā nāma ekaviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam tathāgata parīkṣā dvāviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyata eva bhava saṃtatiḥ tathāgata sadbhāvāt iha hi bhagavatā mahā karuṇa upāya prajñā dvaya dhāriṇā sakala traidhātuka aśeṣa sattva jāti ādi duḥkha vyupaśama eka manasā tribhiḥ kalpa asaṃkhyeyaiḥ saptabhiḥ vā nairantarya krameṇa udyacchatā taiḥ taiḥ niratiśayaiḥ ati vicitraiḥ puṇya kriyā prārambhaiḥ sakala jagat hita udaya eka kriyā lakṣaṇaiḥ priya eka putrāt api adhikatara niravaśeṣa jagat anugraha tatpareṇa mahā karuṇā para vaśena tatra tatra upapatti āyatane kṣiti salila jvalana pavana sādhāraṇa bhaiṣajya mahā mahīruhavat janānām sva icchāta upabhogya tām ātmānam upagamayatā mahākālena sārvajñam sarva ākāra paricchedi padam adhigatam sa evam adhigata sarvajña jñānaḥ  bhagavān yathā dharmāṇām tattvam vyavasthitam tathā eva aśeṣatas  gata tvāt  buddha tvāt  tathāgata iti ucyate yadi bhava saṃtatiḥ na syāt  tadā tathāgataḥ  api na syāt  na hi ekena janmanā śakyam tathāgata tvam anuprāptum tasmāt vidyata eva bhava saṃtatiḥ tathāgata sadbhāvāt iti ucyate bhavadīyam eva hi idam ati mahat ajñānam bhava saṃtānasya aviccheda vartitām ca ati dīrgha kālam ca gamayati yasya nāma bhavataḥ ati mahat ajñāna dhana andhakāram eva vicitraiḥ upapatti śarad candra jñāna ālokaiḥ vidhvasyamānam api ati ciratara kāla abhyāsa vāsanā vistara abhivṛddham adya api na vidhvasyate na nivartate yadi hi tathāgataḥ  nāma kaścid  syāt  svabhāvataḥ tadā tasya mahatā kālena abhiniṣpatteḥ bhava saṃtatiḥ syāt  na ca tathāgataḥ  nāma kaścid  bhāva svabhāvata upalabhyate kevalam tu bhavān avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā dvi candra keśa maśaka ādivat mithyā tathāgatam nāma svabhāvata upalabhate yathā ca tathāgataḥ  na asti svabhāvataḥ tathā pratipādayan  āha skandhā na na anyaḥ skandhebhyaḥ  na asmin skandhā na teṣu saḥ tathāgataḥ skandhavān na katamaḥ  atra tathāgataḥ yadi hi tathāgataḥ  nāma kaścid  padārthaḥ  amalaḥ  niṣprapañcaḥ syāt  sa skandha svabhāvaḥ  vā bhavet  rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñāna ākhya skandha pañcaka svabhāvaḥ  vā bhavet  yadi vā śīla samādhi prajñā vimukti vimukti jñāna darśana ākhya pañca skandha svabhāvaḥ tad vayatiriktaḥ  vā bhavet  pūrvakā eva pañca skandhāḥ sattva prajñapti nimitta tvāt iha vicāre parigṛhyante na uttare avyāpaka tvāt eṣām pūrvakaiḥ antar bhāvita tvāt iti yadi vā pañca skandha vyatiriktaḥ  bhavet  tatra tathāgate vā skandhāḥ syuḥ skandheṣu vā sa bhavet  tathāgataḥ  vā skandhavān bhavet  dhanavān iva devadattaḥ sarvathā ca vicāryamāṇaḥ  na saṃbhavati katham kṛtvā tatra tāvat  skandhā eva na tathāgataḥ kim kāraṇam uktam hi yad indhanam sa ced agniḥ eka tvam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ bhavet iti tad iha api yojyam sa buddhaḥ  yaḥ  hi upādānam eka tvam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ bhavet iti tathā ātmā skandhā yadi bhavet udayavyaya bhāj bhavet  iti uktam tad iha api yojyam buddhaḥ skandhā yadi bhavet udayavyaya bhāj bhavet  iti evam tāvat  skandhā na tathāgataḥ idānīm na anyaḥ skandhebhyaḥ tathāgata iti kim kāraṇam uktam hi anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ indhanāt aṣi ṛte bhavet  tathā paratra nirapekṣa tvāt apradīpana hetukaḥ punar ārambha vaiyarthyam evam ca akarmakaḥ sati iti tathā iha api yojyam buddhaḥ  anyaḥ ced upādānāt upādānam vinā bhavet  tathā paratra nirapekṣa tvāt anupādāna hetukaḥ punar ārambha vaiyarthyam evam ca akarmakaḥ sati tathā skandhebhyaḥ  anyaḥ  yadi bhavet bhavet askandha lakṣaṇaḥ iti anyatva abhāvāt ca skandha ādīnām tathāgatasya ca tathāgate skandhā na upapadyante na api skandheṣu tathāgata iti upapadyate uktam ca etad madhyamaka avatāre pakṣa dvaya vyākhyānam skandheṣu ātmā vidyate na eva cāmī santi skandhā ātmani iti iha yasmāt  sati anya tve syāt iyam kalpanā vai tad ca anya tvam na asti atas  kalpanā eṣā skandhavān api tathāgataḥ  yathā na bhavati tathā tatra eva uktam iṣṭaḥ  na ātmā rūpavān na asti yasmāt ātmā vattva artha upayogaḥ  hi na atas  bhede gomān rūpa vān aṣya bhede tattva anya tve arūpataḥ  na ātmanaḥ staḥ tattva anyatva pakṣe eva tu pañca api pakṣā antargatā vastutas  sat kāya dṛṣṭi pravṛtti apekṣayā tu pañca pakṣāḥ samupavarṇyante ācāryeṇa iti vijñeyam yaḥ ca evam skandheṣu pañcadhā vicāryamāṇaḥ  na asti tathāgataḥ sa kena anyena ātmanā bhaviṣyati iti sarvathā na saṃbhavati eva tathāgata iti bhāva svabhāvāt apaśyanta ācārya pādāḥ prāhuḥ katamaḥ  atra tathāgata iti na asti eva sa kaścid  sakala trailokya vastu vipaḥ cit bhāva svabhāva iti abhiprāyaḥ tathāgata abhāvāt ca bhava saṃtatiḥ api dravya saṃtatiḥ na asti iti siddham atra eke vadanti na eva hi skandhāḥ tathāgata iti brūmaḥ yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgāt  na api skandha vyatiriktaḥ na api tathāgate anāsravān skandhān varṇayāmaḥ himavati parvate iva taru khaṇḍam na api skandheṣu taru khaṇḍe eva siṃham na api skandhavantam varṇayāmaḥ lakṣaṇavantam iva cakravartinam ekatva anyatva anabhyupagamāt eva kim tarhi skandhān amalān upādāya tattva anyatva ādi avācyam tathāgatam vyavasthāpayāmaḥ tasmāt na ayam vidhiḥ asmākam bādhaka iti atra ucyate buddhaḥ skandhān upādāya yadi na asti svabhāvataḥ svabhāvataḥ ca yaḥ  na asti kutas  sa para bhāvataḥ yadi hi buddhaḥ  bhagavān amalān skandhān upādāya tattva anya tvena āvaktavyaḥ prajñapyate na tarhi svabhāvataḥ saḥ  asti iti vyaktam āpadyate pratibimbavat upādāya prajñapyamāna tvāt  yaḥ ca idānīm svabhāvataḥ  na asti ātmīyena sva rūpeṇa sa katham avidyamānaḥ svabhāvataḥ skandhān upādāya para bhāvataḥ  bhaviṣyati iti na hi avidyamānaḥ  vandhyā tanayaḥ para bhāvam apekṣya bhavati iti yujyate atha syāt  yathā eva hi pratibimba kam svabhāvataḥ  asaṃvidyamānam api para bhāvam mukha ādarśa ādikam apekṣya bhavati evam ca tathāgataḥ  api svabhāvataḥ  asaṃvidyamānaḥ anāsravān pañca skandhān upādāya para bhāvataḥ  bhaviṣyati iti evam api pratītya para bhāvam yaḥ saḥ  anātmā iti upapadyate yaḥ ca anātmā sa ca katham bhaviṣyati tathāgataḥ yadi pratibimbavat  para bhāvam pratītya tathāgataḥ iṣyate evam sati pratibimbavat eva sa tathāgataḥ  anātmā iti upapadyate na tu svabhāvata iti yujyate ātma śabdaḥ  ayam svabhāva śabda paryāyaḥ yaḥ ca anātmā niḥsvabhāvaḥ pratibimbavat eva sa katham tathāgataḥ svabhāva rūpataḥ  bhaviṣyati aviparīta mārga gataḥ  na bhaviṣyati iti abhiprāyaḥ kim ca anyat  iha yadi tathāgatasya kaścid  svabhāvaḥ syāt  tadā tad svabhāva apekṣayā skandha svabhāvaḥ para bhāva iti syāt  tam ca para bhāvam pratītya tathāgataḥ syāt  yadā tu tathāgatasya svabhāva eva na asti tadā kutas  skandhānām para tvam syāt iti pratipādayan  āha yadi na asti svabhāvaḥ ca para bhāvaḥ katham bhavet  yadā ca evam svabhāva para bhāvau na staḥ tadā svabhāva para bhāvābhyām ṛte kaḥ sa tathāgataḥ padārthaḥ  hi bhavan svabhāvaḥ  bhavet  para bhāvaḥ  vā tābhyām tu vinā kaḥ  asau aparaḥ padārthaḥ  asti yaḥ tathāgata iti vyavasthāpyate tasmāt na asti svabhāvataḥ tathāgata iti kim ca anyat  skandhān yadi anupādāya bhavet kaścid tathāgataḥ sa idānīṃm upādadyāt upādāya tatas  bhavet  yadi manyase skandhebhyaḥ tattva anya tvena avaktavyaḥ tathāgataḥ skandhān upādāya prajñapyate iti tad  kadā yujyate yadi skandhān anupādāya agṛhītvā pūrvam kaścid tathāgataḥ  nāma bhavet  sa skandha anupādadyāt  vyatirikta eva hi pūrva siddhaḥ  dhanāt  devadattaḥ  dhanasya upādānam kurute tadvat etān skandhān anupādāya yadi kaścid  tathāgataḥ syāt  sa idānīm skandha anupādadyāt  tatas ca tān skandhān upādāya tatas  bhavet  vicāryamāṇaḥ tu sarvathā skandhān  ca api anupādāya na asti kaścid tathāgataḥ nirhetukatva prasaṅgāt  yaḥ ca na asti anupādāya sa upādāsyate katham avidyamāna tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ yadā ca evam na kiṃcid api upādatte tadā skandhān upādāya tathāgataḥ  nāma bhaviṣyati iti na upapadyate yadā ca evam tathāgataḥ upādānāt pūrvam avidyamāna tvāt  na kiṃcid upādatte tadā tad upādānasya api kenacid api anupādīyamānasya upādāna tvam na saṃbhavati eva iti pratipādayan  āha na bhavati anupādattam upādānam ca kiṃcana yadā ca evam upādānam kenacid api anupādīyamāna tvāt upādānam na bhavati iti tadā upādāna abhāvāt upādātā api kaścid na asti iti pratipādayan  āha na ca asti nirupādānaḥ kathaṃcana tathāgataḥ iti tad evam yathā upapādita nyāyena tattva anya tvena yaḥ  na asti mṛgyamāṇaḥ ca pañcadhā upādānena sa katham prajñapyeta tathāgataḥ yaḥ  hi tathāgataḥ  vicāryamāṇaḥ  mṛgyamāṇaḥ tattvena skandhebhya eka tvena na asti anya tvena skandhebhyaḥ pṛthaktvena ca yaḥ  na asti evam tattva anyatva asa tvāt ādhāra ādheya tadvat pakṣa pañca prakāraiḥ mṛgyamāṇaḥ  yaḥ  na asti sa katham atyantaḥ  asaṃvidyamānaḥ tathāgataḥ upādānena śakyaḥ prajñapayitum iti atas  api na asti tathāgataḥ  nāma svabhāvataḥ na kevalam anena vicāreṇa tathāgata eva na asti yad api idam upādānam tad svabhāva tvāt na vidyate yad api idam upādānam rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñāna ākhyam skandha pañcakam tad api svabhāvena na vidyate pratītyasamutpanna tvāt  skandha parīkṣāyām ca vistareṇa pratiṣiddha tvāt  atha api syāt  yadi api svabhāvataḥ upādānam na asti tathā api hetu pratyaya ātmakāt para bhāvā dbhaviṣyati iti tadā api na upapadyate iti pratipādayan  āha svabhāvataḥ ca yad na asti kutas tad para bhāvataḥ na hi bandhyā sūnuḥ svabhāvataḥ  asaṃvidyamānaḥ śakyaḥ para bhāvena prajñapayitum iti atas  upādānam api na asti athavā yad api idam upādānam tad svabhāvān na vidyate upādātṛ sāpekṣa tvāt upādātṛ nirapekṣasya ca upādānatva abhāvāt na asti svabhāva siddham upādānam atha yadi api upādātṛ nirapekṣam upādānam svabhāva siddham na saṃbhavati evam tad upādātrapekṣam eva bhavatu iti ucyate evam api svabhāvataḥ ca yad na asti kutas tad para bhāvataḥ svabhāvataḥ  yad upādānam na siddham tad avidyamāna svabhāvam katham upādātuḥ para bhāvataḥ  bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt upādānam api na asti iti idānīm yathāprasādhitam eva artham upadarśayan  āha evam śūnyam upādānam upādātā ca sarvaśas  sarveṇa prakāreṇa vicāryamāṇam śūnyam upādānam niḥsvabhāvam upādātā ca śūnyaḥ svabhāva rahitaḥ tena idānīm upādānena prajñapyate ca śūnyena katham śūnyaḥ tathāgataḥ na eva tad saṃbhavati yad avidyamānena avidyamānasya tathāgatasya prajñaptiḥ syāt iti tasmāt  skandhān upādāya tathāgataḥ prajñapyate iti na upapadyate atra āhuḥ ahaḥ vata hatā pratyāśā asmākam ye hi nāma vayam sva vikalpa vikalpita ati kaṭhina kudarśana mālu tā la tā jāla avabaddheṣu nirvāṇa pura gāmi aviparīta mārga gamana paribhraṣṭeṣu anatikrānta saṃsāra aṭavī kāntāra durgeṣu kaṇa bhakṣa akṣa pāda digambara jaimi ninaiyāyika prabhṛtiṣu tīrthakareṣu aviparīta svarga apavarga mārga upadeśa abhimāniṣu spṛhām parityajya niravaśeṣa anya tīrthya mata andhakāra upaghātakam svarga apavarga anugāmya viparīta mārga saṃprakāśakam sat dharma deśanā ati paṭutara kiraṇa vyāpta aśeṣa āśā mukham vividha vineya janam ati kamala kuṅmala vibodhana tad param yathāvat avasthita padārtha tattva artha bhājanānām amala eka cakṣuḥ bhūtam sakala jagat śaraṇya bhūtam advitīyam daśa bala vaiśāradyā veṇika buddha dharma amala maṇḍalam mahāyāna mahānaya sārathi varam sapta bodhi aṅga uttuṅga turaṃga padāti yojitam sakala tribhuvana jana jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāra kāntāra sarit ucchoṣaṇa tad param catura sama mārāra ati samara śara saṃpāta vijayinam sakala jagat asat grāha rāhu graha vigraha udgraha nirāsinam tathāgata savitāram ajñāna dhana gahana andhakāra nirākaraṇāya mokṣa arthinaḥ  atuttara samyaksaṃbodhi arthinaḥ śaraṇam pratipannāḥ tasya ca tvayā evam śūnyam upādānam upādātā ca sarvaśas  prajñapyate ca śūnyena katham śūnyaḥ tathāgataḥ ityādinā svabhāvataḥ  asattvam vruvatā bhavatā hatā asmākam mokṣa pratyāśā anuttara samyaksaṃbodhya āgama abhilāṣaḥ iti tad alam bhavatā tathāgata mahā āditya pracchādakena ākālika dhana dhana āvalī visaraṇena jagat andhakāra upamena iti ucyate asmākam eva hatā pratyāśā bhavadvidheṣu abudha janeṣu ye hi nāma bhavantaḥ mokṣa kāma tayā anya tīrthya matāni parityajya bhagavantam tathāgatam api aviparītam parama śāstāram pratipadya parama gambhīram anuttaram sarva tīrthya vāda asā dhāraṇam nairātmya siṃhanādam asahamānāḥ kuraṅgamā iva svādhi mukti daridra tayā vividha kudṛṣṭi vyāla mālā ākulam viparyasta jana anuyātam tam eva mahā ghora saṃsāra aṭavī kāntāra cāraka anuga mārgam avagāhante na hi tathāgatāḥ kadācid api ātmanaḥ skandhānām vā astitvam prajñapayanti yathā uktam bhagavatyām buddhaḥ  api āyuṣman subhūte māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ buddha dharmā api āyuṣman subhūte māyā upamāḥ svapna upamāḥ iti tathā dharma svabhāvatu śūnya viviktaḥ  bodhi svabhāvatu śūnya viviktā yaḥ  hi caret sa pi śūnya svabhāvaḥ  jñānavataḥ  na tu bāla janasya iti na ca vayam sarvathā eva niṣprapañcānām tathāgatānām na astitvam brūmaḥ yad asmākam tad apavāda kṛtaḥ  doṣaḥ syāt  api ca niḥsvabhāvam hi tathāgatam vyācakṣāṇena aviparīta artha abhidhitsunā yoginām satā sarvathā śūnyam iti na vaktavyam aśūnyam iti vā bhavet  ubhayam na ubhayam ca iti sarvam etad na vaktavyam asmābhiḥ kim tu anukte yathāvat avasthitam svabhāvam pratipattā pratipattum na samartha iti atas  vayam api āropataḥ vyavahāra satye eva sthitvā vyavahāra artham vineya jana anurodhena śūnyam iti api brūmaḥ aśūnyam iti api śūnyāśūnyam iti api na eva śūnyam na aśūnyam iti api brūmaḥ ata eva āha prajñapti artham tu kathyate iti yathā uktam bhagavatā śūnyāḥ sarva dharmā niḥsvabhāva yogena nirnimittāḥ sarva dharmā nirnimitta tām upādāya apraṇihitāḥ sarva dharmā apraṇidhāna yogena prakṛti prabhāsvarāḥ sarva dharmāḥ prajñāpāramitā pariśuddhayā iti anyatra aśūnyam uktam atītam ced bhikṣavaḥ  rūpam na abhaviṣyat na śrutavān ārya śrāvakaḥ  atītam rūpam abhyanandiṣyat  yasmāt tarhi bhikṣavaḥ asti atītam rūpam tasmāt ārya śrāvakaḥ śrutavān atītam rūpam abhinandati iti anāgatam ced bhikṣavaḥ ityādi evam yāvat  atītam ced bhikṣavaḥ  vijñānam na abhaviṣyat ityādi pūrvavat  tathā sautra antika mate atīta anāgatam śūnyam anyat aśūnyam viprayuktā vijñaptiḥ śūnyā vijñāna vāde api kalpita svabhāvasya śūnya tvam apratītya samutpanna tvāt  taimirika dvi candra ādi darśanavat  na śūnyam na api ca aśūnyam tasmāt sarvam vidhīyate [tathā] sattvāt asattvāt ca madhyamā pratipad ca sā iti yena tu abhiprāyeṇa śūnyatva ādikam upadiśyate sa ātma parīkṣātaḥ  boddhavyaḥ yathā uktam sūtre māyā upamam jagat idam bhavatā naṭaraṅga svapna sadṛśam vihitam na ātmā na sattva na ca jīva gatī dharmā marīci daka candra samāḥ śūnyam ca śāntam anupāda mayam avijānadeva jagat udbhramatī teṣām upāya naya yukti śataiḥ avatārayasi api kṛpālu tayā rāga ādibhiḥ ca bahu roga śataiḥ saṃtrāsitam sakalam īkṣi jagat  vaidya upamaḥ  vicarase apratimaḥ  parimocayam sugata sattva śatān ratha cakravat  bhramati sarva jagat  tiryakṣu preta nirayeṣu gatāḥ mūḍhā adeśika anātha gatāḥ teṣām pradarśayasi mārga varam iti sarvāḥ tu etāḥ kalpanā niṣprapañce tathāgate na saṃbhavanti na ca kevalam śūnyatva ādikam eva catuṣṭayam tathāgate na saṃbhavati api ca śāśvata aśāśvata ādyā kutas  śānte catuṣṭayam anta ananta ādi ca api atra kuntaḥ śānte catuṣṭayam iha caturdaśa avyākṛta vastūni bhagavatā nirdiṣṭāni tad yathā śāśvataḥ  lokaḥ aśāśvataḥ  lokaḥ śāśvataḥ ca aśāśvataḥ ca lokaḥ na eva śāśvataḥ  na aśāśvataḥ ca lokaḥ iti catuṣṭayam antavān lokaḥ anantavān lokaḥ antavān  ca anantavān  ca lokaḥ na eva antavān na anantavān  ca lokaḥ iti dvitīyam bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt  na bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt  bhavati ca na bhavati ca tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt  na eva bhavati na na bhavati ca tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt  iti tṛtīyam sa jīvaḥ tad śarīram anyaḥ  jīvaḥ  anyat śarīram iti tāni etāni caturdaśa vastūni avyākṛta tvāt avyākṛta vastūni iti ucyante tatra yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena yathā śūnyatva ādikam catuṣṭayam prakṛtyā śānte niḥsvabhāve tathāgate na saṃbhavati evam śāśvata aśāśvata ādikam api catuṣṭayam atra na saṃbhavati asaṃbhavāt eva ca catuṣṭayam vandhyā putrasya śyāma gauratva ādivat  na vyākṛtam bhagavatā lokasya yathā ca etad catuṣṭayam tathāgate na saṃbhavati evam anta ananta ādikam api śānte tathāgate na saṃbhavati idānīm bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt  iti ādikasya api kalpanā catuṣṭayasya pravṛtti asaṃbhava mudbhau  ayan  āha yena grāhaḥ  gṛhītaḥ tu ghanaḥ  asti iti tathāgataḥ na asti iti sa vikalpayat nirvṛtasya api kalpayet  yena hi ghana taraḥ mahatā abhiniveśena asti tathāgataḥ iti grāhaḥ  gṛhītaḥ parikalpa utpāditaḥ saḥ niyatam parinirvṛte tathāgate na bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt  maraṇāt uttara kālam na bhavati ucchinnaḥ tathāgataḥ na saṃvidyate iti parikalpayet  tasya evam vikalpayataḥ syāt  dṛṣṭi kṛtam yasya tu na kasyāṃcid api avasthāyām svabhāva śūnyatvāt tathāgatasya astitva nāstitvam tasya pakṣe svabhāvataḥ ca śūnye asmin  cintā na eva upapadyate param nirodhāt bhavati buddhaḥ  na bhavati iti vā ākāśe citra rūpa kalpanāvat eṣā kalpanā na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ tad evam prakṛti śānte niḥsvabhāve tathāgate sarva prapañca atīte manda buddhi tayā śāśvatā śāśvata ādikayā nitya anityāsti nāsti śūnyā śūnya sarvajñā sarva jña ādikayā kalpanayā prapañcayanti ye buddham prapañca atītam avyayam te prapañca hatāḥ sarve na paśyanti tathāgatam vastu nibandhanā hi prapañcāḥ syuḥ avastukaḥ ca tathāgataḥ kutas  prapañcānām pravṛtti saṃbhava iti atas  prapañca atītaḥ tathāgataḥ anutpāda svabhāvā vāt ca svabhāva antarāgamanāt avyayaḥ tam itthaṃvidham tathāgatam sva utprekṣita mithyā parikalpa mala malina māna satayā vividhaiḥ abhūtaiḥ parikalpa viśeṣaiḥ ye buddham bhagavantam prapañcayanti te svakaiḥ eva prapañcaiḥ hatāḥ santaḥ tathāgata guṇa samṛddheḥ atyanta parokṣa vartinaḥ  bhavanti tatas ca śava bhūtāḥ etasmin pravacane na paśyanti tathāgatam jāti andhā iva ādityam ata eva āha bhagavān ye mām rūpeṇa adrākṣuḥ ye mām ghoṣeṇa anvayuḥ mithyā prahāṇa prasṛtā na mām drakṣyanti te janāḥ dharmataḥ  buddhā draṣṭavyā dharmakāyā hi nāyakāḥ dharmatā ca api avijñeyā na sā śakyā vijānitum iti tad atra tathāgata parīkṣāyām sattva lokaḥ sakalaḥ sa sura asura nara ādiḥ parīkṣitaḥ yathā ca ayam sattva lokaḥ  niḥsvabhāvaḥ tathā bhājana lokasya api vāyu maṇḍala āderakaniṣṭha vitāna bhavana paryantasya naiḥsvābhāvyam udbhāvayan  āha tathāgataḥ  yad svabhāvaḥ tad svabhāvam idam jagat  idam jagat iti ayam bhājana loke  iti arthaḥ kiṃsvabhāvaḥ tathāgataḥ punar iti āha tathāgataḥ  niḥsvabhāvaḥ  niḥsvabhāvam idam jagat  iti yathā ca jagataḥ  naiḥsvābhāvyam tathā pratyaya parīkṣā ādibhiḥ pratipāditam ata eva uktam sūtre anupāda dharmaḥ satatam tathāgataḥ sarve ca dharmāḥ sugatena sādṛśāḥ nimitta grāheṇa tu bāla buddhayaḥ asatsu dharmeṣu caranti loke tathāgataḥ  hi pratibimba bhūtaḥ kuśalasya dharmasya anāsravasya na eva atra tathatā na tathāgataḥ  asti bimbam ca saṃdṛśyati sarva loke iti uktam ca bhagavatyām prajñāpāramitāyām atha khalu te deva putrāḥ āyuṣmantam subhūtim sthaviram etad avocan kim punar ārya subhūte māyā upamāḥ te sattvāḥ na te māyā evam ukte āyuṣmān subhūtiḥ tān deva putrān etad avocat  māyā upamāḥ te deva putrāḥ sattvāḥ svapna upamāḥ te deva putrāḥ sattvāḥ iti hi māyā ca sattvāḥ ca advayam eta dadvaidhīkāram iti hi svapnaḥ ca sattvāḥ ca advayam etad ad vaidhīkāram sarva dharmā api deva putrā māyā upamāḥ svapna upamāḥ strotaāpannaḥ  api māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ strotaāpatti phalam api māyā upamam svapna upamam evam sakṛdāgāmi api sakṛdāgāmi phalam api anāgāmi api anāgāmi phalam api arhan  api māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ arhattva phalam api māyā upamam svapna upamam pratyekabuddhaḥ  api māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ pratyekabuddha tvam api māyā upamam svapna upamam samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ  api māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ iti samyaksaṃbuddha tvam api māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadāmi atha khalu deva putrā āyuṣmantam subhūtim etad avocan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ  api māyā upamaḥ svapna upama iti samyaksaṃbuddha tvam api māyā upamam svapna upamam iti ārya subhūte vadasi subhūtiḥ āha nirvāṇam api deva putrā māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadāmi kim punar anyam dharmam deva putrā āhuḥ nirvāṇam api ārya subhūte māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadasi subhūtiḥ āha yadi api deva putrā nirvāṇāt api anyaḥ kaścid dharmaḥ  viśiṣṭataraḥ syāt  tam api aham māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadeyam iti hi māyā ca nirvāṇam ca advayam etad ad vaidhīkāram iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau tathāgata parīkṣā nāma dvāviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam viparyāsa parīkṣā trayoviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam atra āha vidyata eva bhava saṃtatiḥ tad kāraṇa sadbhāvāt iha hi kleśebhyaḥ karma pravartate karma kleśa hetukā janma maraṇa paraṃparā upajāyate sā ca bhava saṃtatiḥ vyapadiśyate tasyāḥ ca pradhānam kāraṇam kleśāḥ prahīṇa kleśānām bhava saṃtateḥ abhāvāt  te ca rāga ādayaḥ kleśāḥ santi tasmāt  kārya bhūtā api janma maraṇa paraṃparā aviccheda prabandhena bhava saṃtatiḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate syāt  bhava saṃtatiḥ yadi tad hetu bhūtāḥ kleśāḥ syuḥ na tu santi katham kṛtvā iha bhagavadbhiḥ buddhaiḥ sakala tribhuvana jana saṃkleśa śatru vidhvaṃsibhiḥ catur māra arāti samara parājayaiḥ saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ  rāgaḥ  dveṣaḥ  mohaḥ ca kathyate śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya hi saṃkalpaḥ  vitarkaḥ saṃkalpāt  prabhavati iti saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ kāma jānāmi te mūlam saṃkalpāt kila jāyase na tvām saṃkalpayiṣyāmi tatas  me na bhaviṣyasi iti gāthā abhidhānāt saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ  rāgaḥ  dveṣaḥ  mohaḥ ca kathyate etad mūlaka tvāt anyeṣām kleśānām mukhya tvāt eṣām eva upādānam trayāṇām ete ca trayaḥ kleśāḥ śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya hi tatra hi śubham ākāram pratītya rāga utpadyate aśubham pratītya dveṣaḥ viparyāsān pratītya moha utpadyate saṃkalpaḥ tu eṣām trayāṇām api sādhāraṇa kāraṇam utpattau katham punar mohaḥ saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ ucyate uktam hi pratītyasamutpāde bhagavatā avidyā api bhikṣavaḥ sa hetukā sa pratyayā sa nidānā kaḥ ca bhikṣavaḥ avidyāyāḥ  hetuḥ ayaḥ niśaḥ bhikṣavaḥ  manaskāraḥ  avidyāyāḥ  hetuḥ āvilaḥ  moha jaḥ  manaskāraḥ  bhikṣavaḥ  avidyāyāḥ  hetuḥ iti atas  avidyā saṃkalpa prabhavā bhavati tatas ca śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya ye te svabhāvāt na vidyante tasmāt  kleśā na tattvataḥ iti yadi rāga ādayaḥ svabhāva siddhāḥ syuḥ na eva te śubha aśubha viparyāsān pratītya saṃbhaveyuḥ svabhāvasya akṛtrima tvāt  para nirapekṣa tvāt ca bhavanti ca śubha aśubha viparyāsān pratītya tasmāt niḥsvabhāvā eva te tattvataḥ  na vidyante paramārthataḥ svabhāvataḥ  na vidyante iti arthaḥ api ca ātmanaḥ  astitva nāstitvena kathaṃcid ca sidhyataḥ tam vinā asti tvana astitve kleśānām sidhyataḥ katham ātmanaḥ  yathā astitvanā astitve na staḥ tathā uktam vistareṇa tatas ca tad āśritasya dharmasya kutaḥ astitvana astitve bhaviṣyataḥ atha syāt  yadi astitvanā astitve ātmanaḥ  na staḥ tadā kim atra kleśānām āyātam yatas teṣām api astitvanā astitve na staḥ iti ucyate kasyacid hi bhavanti ime
