kleśāḥ sa ca na sidhyati kaścid āhaḥ vinā kaṃcid santi kleśā na kasyacid  iha amī rāga ādayaḥ kuḍayam citravat  phalam pakva tā ādivat ca utpattau āśrayam apekṣante tatas ca kasyacid ete bhavanti na vinā kaṃcid āśrayam sa ca āśrayaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ ātmā vā cittam vā bhavet  sa ca eṣām āśrayaḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣiddha tvāt na asti tam ca kaṃcid āśrayam vinā kasya kleśā bhavantu na eva kasyacid bhavanti tasya avidyamāna tvāt  āhaḥ vinā kaṃcid  santi kleśā na kasyacid  atra āha na eva hi kleśānām kaścid āśrayaḥ pūrvam siddhaḥ  abhyupagamyate na ca ātmā nāma kaścid asti yaḥ āśraya tvena vyavasthāpyeta nirhetuka tvāt  vyoma cūta taruvat  kim tarhi kliṣṭam cittam pratītya kleśā upajāyante tad ca cittam saha eva kleśaiḥ upajāyata iti etad api na yuktam iti āha sva kāya dṛṣṭivat  kleśāḥ kliṣṭe santi na pañcadhā sva kāya dṛṣṭivat  kliṣṭam kleśeṣu api na pañcadhā sva kāyaḥ  hi nāma rūpa ādi lakṣaṇa saṃhatiḥ sva kāya dṛṣṭiḥ sva kāye ātma dṛṣṭiḥ ātmīya ākāra grahaṇa pravṛttā yathā iyam pañcadhā vicāryamāṇā sva kāye na saṃbhavati skandhā na na anyaḥ skandhebhyaḥ  na asmin skandhā na teṣu saḥ tathāgataḥ skandhavān na katamaḥ  atra tathāgataḥ iti anena evam kliṣṭe api kleśā vicāryamāṇāḥ pañcadhā na saṃbhavanti tatra kliśyanti iti kleśā kliśyate iti kliṣṭam tatra yad eva kliṣṭam tad eva kleśā iti na yujyate dagdhṛ dāhyayoḥ api ekatva prasaṅgāt  anyat  kliṣṭam anye kleśā iti na yujyate paratra nirapekṣa tvāt  akliṣṭa hetuka kleśa prasaṅgāt  ata eva ca ekatva anyatva abhāvāt ādhāra ādheya tadvat pakṣāṇām ca abhāvāt na kleśeṣu kliṣṭam na kliṣṭe kleśāḥ na api kleśavat  kliṣṭam iti evam kliṣṭe pañcadhā vicāryamāṇāḥ kleśā na saṃbhavanti yathā ca kliṣṭa hetukāḥ kleśā na saṃbhavanti evam kleśa hetukam api kliṣṭam kleśeṣu vicāryamāṇam pañcadhā na saṃbhavati na hi kleśā eva kliṣṭam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt  na anye kleśā anyat  kliṣṭam nirapekṣatva prasaṅgāt  na ca kliṣṭe kleśāḥ na ca kleśeṣu kliṣṭam na kliṣṭavantaḥ kleśāḥ iti evam sva kāya dṛṣṭivat eva kliṣṭam kleśeṣu api pañcadhā na asti yatas ca evam atas  paraspara apekṣayā api kleśa akliṣṭayoḥ na asti siddhiḥ atra āha yadi api tvayā kleśāḥ pratiṣiddhāḥ tathā api kleśa hetavaḥ śubha aśubha viparyāsāḥ tāvat  santi tad sadbhāvāt ca kleśāḥ santi iti ucyate syuḥ kleśāḥ yadi śubha aśubha viparyāsā eva syuḥ yāvatā ete api pratītya sa sutpanna tvāt vakṣyamāṇa pratiṣedhāt ca yadā ca te na santi svabhāvataḥ tadā svabhāvataḥ  na vidyante śubha aśubha viparyayāḥ pratītyasamutpanna tvāt vakṣyamāṇa pratiṣedhāt ca yadā ca te na santi svabhāvataḥ tadā pratītya katamān kleśāḥ śubha aśubha viparyayān na eva santi kleśāḥ tad hetu śubha aśubha viparyaya abhāvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ atra āha vidyanta eva kleśāḥ tad ālambana sadbhāvāt iha hi yad na asti na tasya ālambana masti tad yathā vandhyā sūnoḥ asti ca rūpa śabda gandha rasa spraṣṭavya dharma ākhyam ṣaḍvidham ālambanam tasmāt ālambana sadbhāvāt vidyanta eva kleśā iti ucyate asti etad  yad  bhavadbhiḥ rūpa śabda rasa sparśā gandhā dharmāḥ ca ṣaḍvidham vastu rāgasya dveṣasya mohasya ca vikalpyate tatra vastu ālambanam vasati iti vā asmin rāga ādikam tad utpatteḥ iti kṛtvā tad ca tad ālambanam ṣoḍhā bhavati indriyāṇām ṣaṇṇām pariccheda karāṇām anyonya bhedāt  rūpam śabdā gandhā rasāḥ spraṣṭavyāni dharmāḥ ca iti tatra idam iha amutra iti nirūpaṇāt  rūpaṇāt ca rūpam tena śabdena śabdyante prakāśyante padārthā iti śabdaḥ gandhyante hiṃsyante yatra prāptāḥ tatas  anyatra āgamanāt  gandhāḥ rasyate āsvādyate iti rasaḥ spṛśyate iti sparśaḥ sva lakṣaṇa asā dhāraṇāt nirvāṇa agra dharma ādhāraṇāt dharmāḥ tad etad ṣaḍvidham vastu bhavati kasya rāgasya dveṣasya mohasya tatra rañjanam rāgaḥ  raktiḥ adhyavasānam rajyate vā anena cittam iti rāgaḥ dūṣaṇam doṣaḥ āghātaḥ sattva viṣayaḥ  asattva viṣayaḥ  vā dūṣyate vā anena citam iti doṣaḥ mohanam mohaḥ saṃmohaḥ padārtha svarūpa aparijñānam muhyate vā anena cittam iti mohaḥ tad eṣām kleśānām rūpa ādikam ṣaḍvidham vastu ālambanam bhavati tatra śubha ākāra adhyāropeṇa yathā rūpa ādibhyaḥ  rāga upajāyate aśubha ākāra adhyāropeṇa dveṣaḥ nitya ātma ādi adhyāropeṇa mohaḥ saṃbhavati iti satyam vikalpyate etad bāla janaiḥ ṣaḍvidham vastu kim tu avidyamāna svabhāva sattākam etad  rāga ādīnām ālambana tvena parikalpyate bhavatā taimirikaiḥ iva asat keśa maśaka makṣikāt vi candra ādikam iti pratipādayan  āha rūpa śabda rasa sparśā gandhā dharmāḥ ca kevalāḥ kevalā iti parikalpita mātrā niḥsvabhāvā iti arthaḥ yadi niḥsvabhāvāḥ katham tarhi upalabhyante iti ucyate gandharvanagara ākārā marīci svapna saṃnibhāḥ iti ete upalabhyante yathā gandharvanagara ādi prakhyā ete kevalam viparyāsāt upalabhyante tadā aśubham vā śubham vā api kutas teṣu bhaviṣyati māyā puruṣa kalpeṣu pratibimba sameṣu ca tad anena mithyā āśraya samutpanna tvāt śubha aśubhayoḥ api nimittayoḥ mṛṣā tvam eva bhavati yathā uktam ahaṃkāra udbhavāḥ skandhāḥ saḥ  ahaṃkāraḥ  anṛtaḥ  arthataḥ bījam yasya anṛtam tasya prarohaḥ satyataḥ kutas  skandhān asatyān dṛṣṭvā evam ahaṃkāraḥ prahīyate ahaṃkāra prahāṇāt ca na punar  skandha saṃbhavaḥ iti na ca kevalam āśraya mithyā tve śubha aśubhayoḥ nimittayoḥ mithyātvam api ca anayā api upapattyā anayoḥ mithyātvam iti pratipādayan  āha anapekṣya śubham na asti aśubham prajñapayemahi yad pratītya śubham tasmāt śubham na eva upapadyate iha yadi śubham nāma kiṃcid  syāt  niyatam tad aśubham apekṣya bhavet  pārāvāravat  bīja aṅkuravat  hrasva dīrghavat vā śubhasya saṃbandhi antara padārtha sāpekṣa tvāt tad ca api apekṣaṇīyam aśubham śubhena vinā na asti [anapekṣya śubham na asti aśubhaṃ] śubham nirapekṣya aśubham na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ yad aśubham pratītya yad aśubham apekṣya śubham prajñapayemahi vyavasthāpayemahi yad śabdena anantarasya aśubhasya parāmarśaḥ prajñapayemahi iti anena uttarasya śubhasya saṃbandhaḥ yatas ca evam śubhasya prajñaptau saṃbandhi antaram apekṣaṇīyam aśubha ākhyam padārtha antaram na asti tasmāt śubham na eva upapadyate hrasva asaṃbhavāt iva dīrgham pāra asaṃbhavāt iva avāram iti abhiprāyaḥ idānīm aśubham api yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha anapekṣya aśubham na asti śubham prajñapayemahi yad pratītya aśubham tasmāt aśubham na eva vidyate yadi hi aśubham nāma kiṃcid  syāt  niyatam eva tad śubham apekṣya bhavet  pārāvāravat  hrasva dīrghavat vā aśubhasya saṃbandhi antara padārtha sāpekṣa tvāt tad ca api apekṣaṇīyam śubham aśubhena vinā na asti anapekṣya aśubham na asti śubham aśubham nirapekṣya śubham na saṃbhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ yad śubham pratītya yad śubham apekṣya aśubham prajñapayemahi aśubham vyavasthāpayemahi atra api yad śabdena anantarasya śubhasya parāmarśaḥ prajñapayemahi iti anena ca uttarasya aśubhasya saṃbandhaḥ yatas ca evam aśubhasya prajñaptau saṃbandhi antaram apekṣaṇīyam śubha ākhyam padārtha antaram na asti tasmāt aśubham na eva vidyate yatas ca evam śubha aśubhayoḥ asaṃbhavaḥ atas  avidyamāne ca śubhe kutaḥ rāgaḥ  bhaviṣyati aśubhe avidyamāne ca kutaḥ dveṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati śubha aśubha nimittaka yaḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ śubha aśubha nimitta abhāve sati nirhetuka tvāt na asti saṃbhava iti abhiprāyaḥ tad evam śubha aśubha nimitta abhāvena rāga dveṣayoḥ abhāvam upapādya viparyāsa svabhāva abhāva pratipādanena mohasya api adhunā svabhāva abhāvam pratipādayan  āha anitye nityam iti evam yadi grāhaḥ  viparyayaḥ na anityam vidyate śūnye kutaḥ grāhaḥ  viparyayaḥ iha catvāraḥ  viparyāsā ucyante tad yathā anitye pratikṣaṇa vināśini skandha pañcake yaḥ  nityam iti grāhaḥ sa viparyāsaḥ tathā anityasya dhruvā pīḍā pīḍā yasya na tad sukham tasmāt anityam yad sarvam duḥkham tad iti jāyate iti amunā nyāyena yad anityam tad duḥkham sarva saṃskārāḥ ca anityāḥ tasmāt duḥkha ātmake skandha pañcake yaḥ sukham iti viparītaḥ  grāhaḥ saḥ  aparaḥ  viparyāsaḥ tathā śukra śoṇita saṃparka bījam viṣ mūtra vardhitam amedhya rūpam ājānan rajyase atra kaya icchayā amedhya puñja pracchanne tad kleda ārdreṇa carmaṇā yaḥ śayīta sa nārīṇām śayīta jaghana udare ityādi evam idam śarīram sarva ātmanā satatam aśuci svabhāvam tatra yaḥ  mohāt śuci tvena grāhaḥ  abhiniveśaḥ sa viparyāsaḥ tathā pañca skandhakam ātma lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇam asthira tvāt udaya vyaya dharmi tvāt ca nirātmakam ātma svabhāva śūnyam tasmin ya ātma grāhaḥ  abhiniveśaḥ anātmani ātma abhiniveśaḥ sa viparyāsaḥ iti ete catvāraḥ  viparyāsāḥ saṃmohasya hetu bhūtāḥ atra idānīm vicāryate yadi nitya tvam nitya darśanam svabhāva śūnyeṣu nitya grāhaḥ  viparyāsa iti evam vyavasthāpyate nanu ca svabhāva śūnyeṣu skandheṣu anitya tvam api na asti iti na anityam vidyate śūnye kutaḥ grāhaḥ  viparyayaḥ anitya tvam hi viparītam apekṣya nitya tvam viparyāsa iti vyavasthāpyate na ca anitya tvam vidyate śūnye yadā anitya tvasya abhāvaḥ tadā kutas tad virodhi nitya tvam nitya darśana viparyāsaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti bhāvaḥ tasmāt na asti viparyāsaḥ yathā ca anitya tvam śūnye na saṃbhavati bhāva svabhāva rahite sa svabhāvena anutpanne evam duḥkha tvam api na saṃbhavati aśuci tvam api na asti anātmaka tvam api na asti yadā ca svabhāva śūnya tvāt duḥkhatva ādikam na asti tadā kutas tad vipakṣa bhūtā nitya sukha śucī ātma viparyāsā bhaviṣyanti tasmāt  santi viparyāsāḥ svarūpataḥ tad abhāve kutaḥ bhaviṣyati avidyā hetu abhāvāt  yathā uktam bhagavatā avidyayā na eva kadāci vidyate avidyata pratyaya saṃbhavaḥ ca avidyamānā iyam avidya loke tasmāt mayā ukta avidya eṣā tathā katham bhagavan mohaḥ  dhāraṇī padam bhagavān āha atyanta muktaḥ  hi mañjuśrīḥ mohaḥ tena ucyate mohaḥ ityādinā viparyaya iti vyavasthāpyate nanu evam sati svabhāvena avidyamāne padārthe anityam iti api grāhaḥ  na saṃbhavati iti asau  api kasmāt na viparyāsa iti vyavasthāpyate iti pratipādayan  āha anitye nityam iti evam yadi grāhaḥ  viparyayaḥ anityam iti api grāhaḥ śūnye kim na viparyayaḥ yadā ca ubhayasya api vaiparītyam nityasya anityasya ca tadā tadvayatiriktam tṛtīyam aparam na asti yad na viparyayaḥ syāt  yadā ca aviparyāsaḥ  na asti tadā kim apekṣaḥ  viparyāsaḥ syāt iti tasmāt amunā api nyāyena na asti viparyayaḥ tasya abhāvāt ca na asti avidyā svarūpataḥ yathā ca anitye nityam iti evam grāhaḥ  viparyāsaḥ  na saṃbhavati evam śeṣa viparyāsa asaṃbhave api yojyam ata eva uktam bhagavatā ārya dṛḍha āśaya paripṛcchāyām bhagavān āha kim etad  kula putra tasya bhavati yaḥ  mārgeṇa niḥsaraṇam paryeṣate na kula putra tathāgatena rañjanīyān dharmān parivarjya rāga prahāṇam prajñaptam evam na doṣaṇīyān mohanīyāna dharmān parivarjya tathāgatena doṣa moha prahāṇam prajñaptam tad  kasmāt hetoḥ na kula putra tathāgatāḥ kasyacid dharmasya utsargāya vā pratilambhāya vā dharmam deśayanti na parijñāyai na prahāṇāya na sākṣātkriyāyai nābhi samayāya na saṃsāra caraṇa tāyai na nirvāṇa gamana tāyai na utkṣepāya na prabhedāya na hi kula putra dvaya prabhāvitā tathāgata dharma tā tatra ye dvaye caranti na te samyak prayuktāḥ mithyā prayuktāḥ te vaktavyāḥ katamat ca kula putra dvayam aham rāgam prahāsyāmi iti dvayam etad  aham dveṣam prahāsyāmi iti dvayam etad  aham moham prahāsyāmi iti dvayam etad  ye evaṃprayuktāḥ na te samyak prayuktā mithyā prayuktāḥ te veditavyāḥ tad yathā api nāma kula putra kaścid eva puruṣaḥ  māyākāra nāṭake pratyupasthite māyā kāra nirmitām striyam dṛṣṭvā rāga cittam utpādayet  sa rāga parīta cittaḥ parṣad śāradya bhayena utthāya āsanāt apakramet  saḥ  apakramya tām eva striyam aśubha taḥ  manasi kuryāt anityatas  duḥkhataḥ śūnyataḥ  anātmataḥ  manasi kuryāt  bhagavān āha evam eva kula putra iha eke bhikṣubhikṣuṇī upāsa kopāsikā draṣṭavyāḥ ye anutpannān dharmān ajāta an aśubha taḥ manasi kurvanti anityataḥ  duḥkhataḥ  anātmataḥ  manasi kurvanti na aham teṣām moha puruṣāṇām mārga bhāvanām vadāmi mithyā prayuktāḥ te veditavyāḥ tad yathā api nāma kula putra kaścid eva puruṣaḥ suptaḥ svapna antare sva gṛhe rāja bhāryām paśyet  sa tayā sārdham śayyām kalpayet  smṛti saṃmoṣāt ca evam kalpayet  viruddhaḥ  asmi iti sa bhīta srastaḥ palāyet  mā mām rājā vidhyet  sa mā mām jīvitāt  vyavaropayet  tad  kim manyase kula putra api nu sa puruṣaḥ  bhīta srastaḥ palāyamānaḥ tatas  rāja bhāryā nidāna bhayāt parimucyeta āha naḥ bhagavan tad kasya hetoḥ tathā hi bhagavan  tena puruṣeṇa astriyām strī saṃjñā utpāditā abhūtam ca parikalpitam bhagavān āha evam eva kula putra iha eke bhikṣubhikṣuṇī upāsa kopāsikā draṣṭavyāḥ ye arāge rāga saṃjñām utpādya rāga bhaya bhītā rāga niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante evam adoṣe doṣa saṃjñām utpādya doṣa bhaya bhītā doṣa niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante amohe moha saṃjñām utpādya moha bhaya bhītā moha niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante na aham teṣām moha puruṣāṇām mārga bhāvanām vadāmi mithyā prayuktāḥ te veditavyāḥ tad yathā api nāma kula putra sa puruṣaḥ abhaye bhaya saṃjñām utpādayet asat samāropeṇa evam eva kula putra sarva bāla pṛthagjanā rāga koṭim virāga koṭim aprajā anantaḥ  rāga koṭi bhaya bhītā virāga koṭim niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante doṣa koṭim akiṃcana koṭim aprajā anantaḥ  doṣa koṭi bhaya bhītā akiṃcana koṭim niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante moha koṭim śūnyatā koṭim aprajā anantaḥ  moha koṭi bhaya bhītāḥ śūnyatā koṭim niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante na aham teṣām kula putra moha puruṣāṇām mārga bhāvanām vadāmi mithyā prayuktāḥ te veditavyāḥ iti vistaraḥ atra āha yadi api anitye nityam iti evam grāhaḥ  viparyayaḥ  na saṃbhavati tathā api eṣa tāvat  grāhaḥ  asti grāhaḥ ca nāma saṃgrahaṇam bhāva rūpaḥ tasya ca avaśyam sādhanena karaṇena bhavitavyam sādhakatamena nityatva ādinā kartrā ca bhavitavyam svatantreṇa nitya ātmanā cittena vā karmaṇā ca kartuḥ īpsitatamena viṣayeṇa rūpa ādinā satyām ca bhāva karaṇa kartṛ karmaṇām siddhau sarva siddheḥ iṣṭa siddhiḥ syāt asmākam iti ucyate alīkā iyam pratyāśā nanu ca yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena yena gṛhṇāti yogrāhaḥ  grahītā yad ca gṛhyate upaśāntāni sarvāṇi tasmāt grāhaḥ  na vidyate iha hi kaścid  grahītā yena viśeṣeṇa nityatva ādinā karaṇa bhūtena kiṃcid  karma bhūtam rūpa śabda ādikam vastu gṛhṇāti tad yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pūrvam pratipāditam katham kṛtvā anitye nityam iti evam yadi grāhaḥ  viparyayaḥ ityādinā yathā nityatva ādikam karaṇam na saṃbhavati tathā pratipāditam grahītā api yathā na asti tathā ātmanaḥ  astitvana astitve na kathaṃcid ca sidhyataḥ iti anena pratipāditam yad ca gṛhyate tad api na asti tathā rūpa śabda rasa sparśā gandhā dharmāḥ ca kevalāḥ iti anena pratipāditam yadā ca evam kartṛ karaṇa karmāṇi na siddhāni tadā kutaḥ nirhetukaḥ  grāhaḥ  bhaviṣyati tatas ca yena gṛhṇāti yaḥ  grāhaḥ  grahītā yad ca gṛhyate upaśāntāni sarvāṇi svabhāvena anutpannatva anirvṛtāni sarvāṇi iti arthaḥ yatas ca evam evam tasmāt  grāhaḥ  na vidyate athavā pratyaya parīkṣā ādibhiḥ prakaraṇaiḥ yasmāt  sarveṣām eva karaṇa kartṛ karmaṇām sarvathā anutpādaḥ pratipāditaḥ tasmāt  sarvāṇi etāni bhāva svarūpa virahāt upaśāntāni atas ca grāhaḥ  na vidyate atra āha vidyanta eva viparyayāḥ viparīta sadbhāvāt  iha hi viparyāsa anugataḥ  devadattaḥ  nāma vidyate na ca vinā viparyāsaiḥ sa viparyāsa anugataḥ saṃbhavati tasmāt  santi viparyāsāḥ viparyasta sadbhāvāt iti ucyate iha asmābhiḥ karaṇa kartṛ karmaṇām abhāvāt sarvathā grāha eva na asti iti pratipāditam tatas ca avidyamāne grāhe ca mithyā vā samyak eva vā bhavet viparyayaḥ kasya bhavet kasya aviparyayaḥ samyak vā mithyā vā kasyacid  kiṃcid api agṛhṇataḥ kutaḥ viparīta tvam aviparīta tvam vā iti tasmāt na santi viparyayāḥ api ca ime viparyayāḥ kasyacid iṣyamāṇāḥ viparītasya parikalpyeran aviparītasya vā viparyasyamānasya vā sarvathā ca na upapadyante iti pratipādayan  āha na ca api viparītasya saṃbhavanti viparyayāḥ na ca api aviparītasya saṃbhavanti viparyayāḥ na viparyasyamānasya saṃbhavanti viparyayāḥ vimṛśasva svayam kasya saṃbhavanti viparyayāḥ tatra tāvat viparītasya viparyayā na saṃbhavanti kim kāraṇam yasmāt  yaḥ  hi viparīta sa viparīta eva kim tasya punar api viparyaya saṃbandhaḥ kuryāt  niṣprayojana tvāt  aviparītasya api viparyayā na yujyante vibuddha buddhi nayanānām api ajñāna nidrā timira upaśamāt  buddhānām viparyaya prasaṅgāt  tathā viparyasyamānasya api na santi viparyayāḥ viparyasyamānasya bhāvasya abhāvāt  kaḥ  hi nāma asau  aparaḥ padārthaḥ yaḥ  viparīta aviparīta vinirmuktaḥ  viparyasyamānaḥ  nāma bhaviṣyati ardha viparītaḥ  viparyasyamāna iti ced  ardha viparītaḥ  hi nāma yasya kiṃcid viparītam kiṃcid aviparītam tatra yad asya kiṃcid viparītam tad viparyāsaḥ  na viparyāsayati viparyasta tvāt  yad api asya aviparītam tad api viparyāsaḥ  na viparyāsayati aviparyasta tvāt  tasmāt viparyasyamānasya api kasyacid viparyāsā na saṃbhavanti yadā ca evam viparīta aviparīta viparyasyamānā na saṃbhavanti bhavān idānīm vimṛśatu svayam prajñayā madhyasthaḥ san kasya saṃbhavanti viparyāsā iti tad evam āśrayasya abhāvāt na santi viparyayāḥ kim ca anyat  anutpannāḥ katham nāma bhaviṣyanti viparyayāḥ viparyayeṣu ajāteṣu viparyaya gataḥ kutas  tatra na svatas  jāyate bhāvaḥ paratas  na eva jāyate na svatas  paratas ca iti viparyaya gataḥ kutas  kutaḥ viparīta iti arthaḥ tatas ca yad uktam santi viparyayāḥ viparyaya gata sadbhāvāt iti tad na yuktam yasya api kathaṃcid viparyāsa catuṣṭayam asti eva iti abhyupagamyate tathā api tasya viparīta tvam aśakyam āsthātum kim kāraṇam yasmāt  ātmā ca śuci nityaṃna sukham ca yadi vidyate ātmā ca śuci nityam ca sukham ca na viparyayaḥ yadi etāni ātma śuci niti asukhāni viparyāsā iti vyavasthāpyante kim etāni santi atha na santi yadi vidyante na tarhi viparyāsāḥ vidyamāna tvāt anātma ādivat  atha na vidyante tadā eṣām avidyamāna tvāt na kevalam na asti viparyāsa tvam viparyāsa pratibandhya bhāvāt anātma ādīnām api aviparyāsa ādīnām na asti sadbhāva iti pratipādayan  āha na ātmā ca śuci nityam ca sukham ca yadi vidyate anātma aśuci anityam ca na eva duḥkham ca vidyate yadi ātmā ca śuci nityam ca na vidyate iti manyase viparyāsa asaṃbhavāt evam sati ātma ādīnām api abhāvāt  yadi etad anātma ādikamaviparyāsa tvena gṛhītam tad api tarhi tyajyatām pratiṣedhya abhāve pratiṣedhasya abhāvāt  yadā ca evam anātma ādikam na saṃbhavati tadā tad api svarūpataḥ  avidyamāna tvāt  ātma ādivat  katham na viparyāsaḥ syāt  tasmāt  jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāra cāraka āgāra bandhanāt mumukṣubhiḥ aṣṭau  api ete viparyāsāḥ tyājyāḥ asya ca yathā upavarṇita viparyāsa vicārasya avidyā ādi prahāṇa hetu tvena mahārtha tām pratipādayan  āha evam nirudhyate avidyā viparyaya nirodhanāt  avidyāyām niruddhāyām saṃskāra ādyam nirudhyate yadā ayam yogī yathā uditena nyāyena viparyāsān na upalabhate tadā evam viparyāsān upalambhanena tad hetukā avidyā nirudhyate tad nirodhāt ca saṃskāra ādayaḥ avidyā hetukā jarā maraṇa śoka parideva duḥkha daurmanasya upāyāsa paryantā dharmā nirudhyante avidyā hi sakalasya eva saṃkleśa gaṇasya jāti ādi duḥkhasya ca hetu bhūtā yathā hi kāya indriya hetukāni sarvāṇi rūpi indriyāṇi kāya indriye nirudhyamāne nirudhyante evam avidyā hetukāni saṃskāra ādīni bhava aṅgāni pravartamānāni niyatam avidyāyām niruddhāyām nirudhyante iti pratipādayan  āha avidyāyām niruddhāyām saṃskāra ādyam nirudhyate iti atra āha yadi viparyāsa nirodhāt avidyā nirudhyate asti tarhi avidyā yasyāḥ  evam viparyāsa nirodhāt nirodhaḥ  bhavati na tarhi avidyamānāyāḥ  gagana cūta latāyāḥ prahāṇa upāya anveṣam asti tasmāt vidyate eva avidyā tad nirodha upāya anveṣaṇa sadbhāvāt tatas ca santi tad hetukā rāga ādayaḥ kleśāḥ kleśa asadbhāvāt ca asti eva saṃsāre bhava saṃtatiḥ ucyate atra hi nāma ati mahat anartha pāṇḍityam parasya yaḥ  hi nāma sarva ātmanā atyanta duḥkha āyāsa kleśa asamañjase saṃsāre nirantara phulla phala prada saṃkleśa viṣa vṛkṣe parārtha udaya saṃbaddha kakṣaiḥ sādhubhiḥ prajñā upāya mahā anila balaiḥ niḥśeṣam tad unmūlyamānaiḥ na kevalam na sāhāyyena avatiṣṭhante api khalu tad unmūla kānām ati mahā anila balānām iva bhāva sadbhāva vāda mahā śailāyamāna iva ati virodhi tayā avasthitaḥ  bhavān āhopuruṣikayā tasya eva kleśa viṣa vṛkṣasya jāti jarā maraṇa śoka āyāsa visara duḥkha eka phalasya sutarām bhāva abhiniveśa toya āsravaiḥ āropaṇam ādriyate api ca yadi avidyā ādīnām saṃkleśānām prahāṇam saṃbhavet  syāt  tad prahāṇa upāya anveṣaṇam na ca teṣām prahāṇam saṃbhavati yadi syāt  tadā tattva rūpa taḥ  vidyamānānām vā syāt  avidyamānānām vā kim ca atas  tatra yadi svarūpataḥ sat bhatānām kleśānām prahāṇam iṣyate tad na upapadyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt  yadi bhūtāḥ svabhāvena kleśāḥ kecid hi kasyacid  katham nāma prahīyeran kaḥ svabhāvam prahāsyati svabhāvataḥ  vidyamānānām bhāvānām na śakyaḥ svabhāvaḥ  vinivartayitum na hi kṣiti ādīnām kaṭhinatva ādi svabhāvaḥ  nivartate evam yadi ime kleśāḥ svabhāvataḥ sadbhūtāḥ syuḥ kecid iti avidyā ādayaḥ kasyacid iti pudgalasya katham nāma prahīyeran na eva te kasyacid  kathaṃcid nāma prahīyeran kasmāt punar  na te prahīyante iti āha kaḥ svabhāvam prahāsyati iti svabhāvasya vinivartayitum aśakyatvāt  ākāśānāvaraṇa vinivartana asaṃbhavavat iti abhiprāyaḥ atha svabhāvena asat bhūtā iti vikalpyate evam api prahāṇa asaṃbhava eva iti āha yadi abhūtāḥ svabhāvena kleśāḥ kecid hi kasyacid  katham nāma prahīyeran kaḥ  asadbhāvam prahāsyati abhūtā api kleśāḥ svabhāvena avidyamānāḥ aśakyā eva prahātum na hi agneḥ śaityam asaṃvidyamānam śakyam apākartum evam ime api kleśāḥ kecid  yadi kasyacid  svabhāvataḥ  na vidyante kaḥ tān prahāsyati na eva kaścid  prahāsyati tad evam ubhaya pakṣe api prahāṇa asaṃbhavān na asti prahāṇam kleśānām prahāṇa abhāvāt ca kutas  kleśa prahāṇa upāya anveṣaṇam iti atas  yad uktam vidyanta eva avidyā ādayaḥ kleśāḥ tad prahāṇa upāya anveṣaṇāt iti tad ayuktam iti yathā uktam ārya samādhi rāje yaḥ  rajyeta yatra vā rajyeta yena vā rajyeta yaḥ  duṣyeta yatra vā duṣyeta yena vā duṣyeta yaḥ  muhyeta yatra vā muhyeta yena vā muhyeta sa tam dharma na samanupaśyati tam dharmam na upalabhate sa tam dharmam asam anupaśyan anupalabhamānaḥ  araktaḥ  aduṣṭaḥ  amūḍhaḥ  aviparyasta cittaḥ samāhita iti ucyate tīrṇaḥ pāraga iti ucyate kṣema prāpta iti ucyate iti vistaraḥ tathā ādarśa pṛṣṭhe tatha taila pātre nirīkṣate nārimukham su alaṃkṛtam saḥ  tatra rāgam janayitva bālaḥ  pradhāvitaḥ  kāmi gaveṣamāṇaḥ  mukhasya saṃkrānti yadā na vidyate bimbe mukham na eva kadāci labhyate mūḍhaḥ  yathā saḥ  janayeta rāgam tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān ityādi tathā rūpeṇa darśitā bodhī bodhaye rūpa darśitam viṣa bhāgena śabdena uttaraḥ  dharmu deśitaḥ śabdena uttaram rūpam gambhīram ca svabhāvataḥ samam rūpam ca bodhiḥ ca nānā tvam na sa labhyate yathā nirvāṇu gambhīram śabdena saṃprakāśitam labhyate na ca nirvāṇam sa ca śabdaḥ  na labhyate śabdaḥ ca api nirvāṇam ca ubhayam tad na labhyate evam śūnyeṣu dharmeṣu nirvāṇam saṃprakāśitam nirvāṇam nivṛttiḥ eva nirvāṇam ca na labhyate apravṛttiḥ hi dharmāṇām yathā paścāt tathā purā sarva dharmāḥ svabhāvena nirvāṇa sama sādṛśāḥ jñātā naiṣkramya sārehi ye yuktā buddha bodhaye tathā jñānena jānāmi ahu skandha śūnyatām jñātvā ca kleśa ihi na saṃvasāmi vyāhāra mātreṇa hi vyāharāmi parinirvṛtaḥ  lokam imam carāmi tathā parinirvṛta loki te śūrā yehi svabhāvata jñātibhi dharmāḥ kāma guṇaiḥ hi caranti asaṅgāḥ saṅgu vivarjiya sattva vinenti iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau viparyāsa parīkṣā nāma trayoviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam ārya satya parīkṣā caturviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam atra āha yadi śūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ  na asti na vyayaḥ caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ te prasajyate yadi yuktyā na upapadyate iti kṛtvā sarvam idam bāhyam ādhyātmikam bhāva jātam śūnyam iti pratipāditam nanu ca evam sati bahavaḥ ca mahāntaḥ ca doṣā bhavata āpadyante katham kṛtvā yadi sarvam idam śūnyam syāt  tadā yad śūnyam tad na asti yad ca na asti tad avidyamāna tvāt  vandhyā putravat na eva utpadyate na ca api nirudhyate iti na kasyacid padārthasya udayaḥ vyayaḥ ca tad abhāvāt ca caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ te śūnya vādinaḥ prasajyate katham kṛtvā iha hi pūrva hetu janitāḥ pratītyasamutpannāḥ pañca upādāna skandhāḥ duḥkha duḥkha tayā vipariṇāma duḥkha tayā saṃskāra duḥkha tayā ca pratikūla varti tvāt ca pīḍā ātmaka tvena duḥkham iti ucyate etad ca duḥkham āryā eva viparyāsa prahāṇe sati duḥkham iti saṃjānate na anāryāḥ viparyāsa anugata tvāt yathādarśanam ca padārtha svabhāva vyavasthānāt yathā hi viparyasta indriyāṇām madhura svabhāvam api guḍa śarkarā ādikam tikta tayā upalabhamānānām jvara ādi roga āturāṇām tikta tā eva satyam tad jñāna apekṣayā mādhuryam tena ātmanā tasya vastunaḥ  anupalabhyamāna tvāt  evam iha api yadi api pañca upādāna skandhā duḥkha svabhāvā bhavanti tathā api ye etān duḥkha ātmakān paśyanti teṣām eva duḥkham vyavasthāpyate na viparyāsa anugamāt anyathā upalabhamānānām iti atas  āryāṇām eva duḥkha ātma tā satyam iti kṛtvā duḥkham ārya satyam iti ucyate nanu ca anāryaiḥ duḥkhā vedanā duḥkham iti paricchidyate iti evam tad katham duḥkham āryāṇām eva satyam satyam na hi duḥkhā eva vedanā kevalam duḥkha satyam kim tarhi pañca api upādāna skandhāḥ iti atas  āryāṇām eva tad  satyam iti kṛtvā ārya satyam iti vyavasthāpyate yathā uktam ūrṇā pakṣma yathā eva hi kara tala saṃstham na vi ve dyate puṃbhiḥ akṣi gatam tu tad eva hi janayati aratim ca pīḍām ca kara tala sadṛśaḥ  bālaḥ  na vetti saṃskāra duḥkha tā pakṣma akṣi sadṛśaḥ tu vidvān tena eva udvejate gāḍham iti tasmāt āryāṇām eva tad duḥkha satyam iti duḥkham ārya satyam iti vyavasthāpyate kadā ca tad duḥkham ārya satyam yujyate yadā saṃskārāṇām udaya vyayau saṃbhavataḥ yadā tu śūnya tvāt na kiṃcid utpadyate na api kiṃcid nirudhyate tadā na asti duḥkham asati ca duḥkhe kutas  samudaya satyam yatas  hi hetoḥ duḥkham samudeti samutpadyate sa hetuḥ tṛṣṇā karma kleśa lakṣaṇaḥ samudaya iti ucyate yadā tu phala bhūtam duḥkha satyam na asti tadā phala rahitasya hetukatva anupapatteḥ samudayaḥ  api na asti duḥkhasya ca vigamaḥ apunarutpādaḥ nirodha iti ucyate yadā tu duḥkham eva na asti tadā kasya nirodhaḥ syāt iti atas  duḥkha nirodhaḥ  api na saṃbhavati asati hi duḥkhe nirodha satyasya api abhāvaḥ asati ca duḥkha nirodhe kutaḥ duḥkha nirodha gāminī ārya aṣṭa aṅga mārga anugā pratipad  bhaviṣyati iti mārga satyam api na asti iti tad evam śūnya tvam bhāvānām bruvataḥ caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ prasajyate tatas ca kaḥ  doṣa iti ucyate parijñā ca prahāṇam ca bhāvanā sākṣi karma ca caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvāt na upapadyate caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāva prasaṅge sati yad etad anitya ādibhiḥ ākāraiḥ duḥkha satya parijñānam duḥkha samudayasya ca prahāṇam duḥkha nirodha gāminyāḥ ca pratipadaḥ  bhāvanā duḥkha nirodhasya ca sākṣi karma sākṣātkaraṇam tad na upapadyate yadi duḥkha ādīnām ārya satyānām abhāve sati parijñāna ādikam na asti tadā kaḥ  doṣa iti ucyate tad abhāvāt na vidyante catvāri ārya phalāni ca phala abhāve phala sthā naḥ na santi pratipannakāḥ saṃghaḥ  na asti na ced santi te aṣṭau puruṣa pudgalāḥ abhāvāt ca ārya satyānām saddharmaḥ  api na vidyate dharme ca asati saṃghe ca katham buddhaḥ  bhaviṣyati yadā ca evam duḥkha parijñāna ādikam na asti tadā asmin  asati srotaāpatti sakṛdāgāmi anāgāmī arhat phala ākhyam phala catuṣṭayam na upapadyate katham kṛtvā iha kleśānām prahāṇam saṃpiṇḍitam phala ākhyam pratilabhate tad yathā saṃyojana traya prahāṇe sati ṣoḍaśe mārge anvayajñāna kṣaṇe yad  kleśa prahāṇam tad  srotaāpatti phalam kāma avacarāṇām bhāvanā prahāta vyānām kleśānām adhimātra madhya mṛdūnām prakārāṇām punar adhimātra madhya mṛdu prakāra bhedena pratyekam bhidyamānānām nava prakārā bhavanti tatra kāma avacara ṣaṣṭha kleśa prakāra parikṣaye vimukti mārge yad  prahāṇam tad  sakṛdāgāmi phalam teṣām eva kāma avacarāṇām navama prakāra kleśa parikṣaye vimukti mārge yad  kleśa prahāṇam tad anāgāmi phalam rūpārūpya avacarāṇām kleśānām bhāvanā prahāta vyānām bhūmau bhūmau nava prakāra bheda bhinnānām yāvat na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā yatana bhūmikanavam akleśa prakāra parikṣaye vimukti mārge yad  prahāṇam tad arhat phalam iti etāni catvāri phalāni tāni etāni katham yujyante yadi duḥkhasya parijñānam saṃbhavati samudayasya prahāṇam nirodhasya sākṣātkaraṇam ārya mārgasya ca bhāvanā bhavati yadā tu duḥkha ādīnām ārya satyānām abhāve sati duḥkha parijñāna ādikam na asti tadā na santi tāni catvāri phalāni caturṇā ca phalānām abhāve sati ye teṣu vyavasthitāḥ phala sthāḥ catvāra ārya pudgalāḥ te na santi ata eva ca pratipannakā api catvāra ārya pudgalā na saṃvidyante iha hi ṣoḍaśāt  mārge anvaya jñāna kṣaṇāt  pūrve ye pañcadaśa kṣānti jñā na kṣaṇāḥ tad yathā traidhātuka duḥkha abhisamaye duḥkha satya ālambanāḥ catvāraḥ kṣānti jñā na kṣaṇāḥ tatra katame traidhātuka duḥkha abhisamaye catvāraḥ kṣānti jñā na kṣaṇāḥ tad yathā kāma avacara duḥkha darśana prahātavyasat kāya anta grāha mithyā dṛṣṭi dṛṣṭi parāmarśa śīla vrata parāmarśa vicikitsā rāga pratighamāna avidyā ākhya daśa anu anitya duḥkha śūnyān ātma ākāra utpannaḥ kāma avacara duḥkha satya ālambanaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ duḥkhe dharma jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ tad ālambana ākāra eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ duḥkhe dharma jñānakṣaṇaḥ dvitīyaḥ evam rūpa ārūpya avacara duḥkha satya ālambanaḥ pratigha varjita anantara ukta aṣṭādaśa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ duḥkha ādi ākāra utpannaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ duḥkhe anvayajñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tad ālambana ākāra eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ duḥkhe anvayajñānakṣaṇaḥ caturthaḥ yathā ca ete traidhātuka avacara duḥkha satya abhisamaye kṣānti jñā na kṣaṇāḥ catvāraḥ evam kāma avacara samudaya darśana prahāta vyamithyā dṛṣṭi dṛṣṭi parāmarśa vicikitsā rāga pratighamāna avidyā ākhya sapta anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ hetu samudaya prabhava pratyaya ākāra utpannaḥ kāma avacara sam udaya sati ālambanaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ samudaye dharma jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ tad ālambana ākāra eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ samudaye dharma jñāna kṣayaḥ  dvitīyaḥ evam rūpārūpya avacara samudaya sati ālambanaḥ pratigha varjita anantara ukta dvādaśa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ samudaya sati ākāra utpannaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ samudaye anvaya jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tad ālambana ākāra eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ samudaye anvayajñānakṣaṇaḥ caturthaḥ iti ete traidhātuka avacara duḥkha samudaya satya abhisamaye catvāraḥ kṣaṇāḥ yathā ca ete catvāraḥ kṣaṇāḥ traidhātuka duḥkha samudaya satya abhisamaye evam kāma avacara duḥkha nirodha darśana prahātavya sam udaya ukta sapta anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ nirodha śānta praṇīta niḥsaraṇa ākāra utpannaḥ kāma avacara duḥkha nirodha satya ālambanaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ nirodhe dharma jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ tad ālambana ākāra eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ nirodhe dharma jñānakṣaṇaḥ dvitīyaḥ etaiḥ eva ākāraiḥ rūpa ārūpya avacara duḥkha nirodha satya ālambanaḥ pratigha varjita dvādaśa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ nirodhe anvayajñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tad ālambana ākāra eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ nirodhe anvayajñānakṣaṇaḥ caturthaḥ iti ete traidhātuka avacara duḥkha nirodha satya abhisamaye catvāraḥ kṣaṇāḥ evam kāma avacara duḥkha nirodha gāmi mārga darśana prahāta vya nirodha ukta anuśayeṣu śīla vrata parāmarśam aṣṭamam prakṣipya aṣṭa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ mārga nyāya pratiā upad naiḥ yāṇika ākāra utpannaḥ kāma avacara duḥkha nirodha gāmi mārga ālambanaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ mārge dharma jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ tad ālambana ākāra eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ mārge dharma jñānakṣaṇaḥ dvitīyaḥ etaiḥ eva ākāraiḥ rūpa ārūpya avacara duḥkha nirodha gāmi mārga ālambanaḥ pratigha varjita caturdaśa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ  mārge anvaya jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti ete pañcadaśa kṣaṇāḥ darśana mārga abhidhānāḥ evam vyavasthitaḥ āryaḥ srotaāpatti phala sākṣāt kriyāyai pratipannakaḥ iti ucyate ṣoḍaśe tu mārge anvaya jñāna sthitaḥ sa srotaāpanna iti ucyate ta ete aṣṭāśītiḥ anuśayāḥ satyānām darśana mātreṇa bhāvanām anapekṣya eva prahīyante iti kṛtvā darśana prahātavyā iti ucyante yathā dṛṣṭa satya ākāra bhāvanayā tu ye paścāt prahīyante te bhāvanā prahātavyāḥ te ca daśa anuśayā bhavanti kāmāvacarā rāga pratighamāna avidyāḥ rūpāvacarā eva pratigha varjita asrayaḥ ārūpya avacarāḥ ca trayaḥ ete eva iti daśa bhavanti ete ca yathā uktena nyāyena bhūmau bhūmau navadhā bhidyante kāmadhātau caturṣu dhyāneṣu caturṣu ārūpyeṣu ekaikasya ca kleśa prakārasya prahāṇa artham ānantarya vimukti mārga bhedena dvau dvau jñā nakṣaṇau vyavasthā apyete kleśa kṣaṇa viparyayeṇa adhimātra adhimātraḥ  hi kleśa prakāraḥ mṛdu mṛdubhyām ānantarya vimukti mārgābhyām prahīyate yāvat mṛdu mṛdu kleśa prakāraḥ  adhimātra adhimātrābhyām jñāna kṣaṇābhyām prahīyate sthūlam hi malam alpa prayatna sādhyam sūkṣmam tu mahā āyatna sādhyam rajaka vastra dhāvana sādharmyeṇa iti vijñeyam tatra darśana mārgāt ūrdhvam kāma avacara bhāvanā prahātavya ṣaṣṭha kleśa prakāra pratipakṣa vimukti mārga ākhya jñā nakṣaṇāt arvāk  jñāna kṣaṇa avasthitaḥ āryaḥ sakṛdāgāmi phala pratipannaka iti ucyate sakṛt imam lokam āgatya parinirvāṇāt  sakṛdāgāmi iti ucyate tad phala arthaṃpratipannakaḥ prayoga sthaḥ sakṛdāgāmi phala pratipannaka iti ucyate ṣaṣṭhe tu kṣaṇe sakṛdāgāmi iti ucyate ṣaṣṭhāt  kṣaṇāt ūrdhva navama kleśa prakāra prahāṇa vimukti mārga kṣaṇāt arvāk jñā na kṣaṇeṣu vartamānaḥ āryaḥ anāgāmi phala pratipannaka iti ucyate anāgatya imam lokam tatra eva parinirvāṇāt anāgāmī iti ucyate tad phala artham pratipannakaḥ prayoga sthaḥ anāgāmi phala pratipannaka iti ucyate navame tu kṣaṇe anāgāmī iti ucyate kāma avacara navamavimukti mārga kṣaṇāt ūrdhvam na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā tayana bhūmi kanavam akleśa prakāra prahāṇa vimukti mārga kṣaṇāt arvāk jñā na kṣaṇeṣu vartamānaḥ āryaḥ arhat phala pratipannakaḥ iti ucyate sa deva mānuṣa asurāt lokāt  pūjā arha tvāt arhan  iti ucyate tad phala artham pratipannakaḥ prayoga sthaḥ arhat phala pratipannakaḥ iti ucyate bhava agrika navam akleśa prakāra prahāṇāt tu navama vimukti mārge vyavasthitaḥ arhan bhavati ta ete catvāraḥ pratipannakāḥ pudgalāḥ catvāraḥ ca phala sthāḥ iti ete aṣṭau mahāpuruṣa pudgalā bhavanti parama dakṣiṇa arhā uktā bhagavatā yathā uktam sūtre pṛṣṭaḥ sa devarājena śakreṇa vaśavartinā kṛṣatām yajamānānām prāṇinām puṇya kāṅkṣiṇām kurvatām śraddhat dadhānānām puṇyam aupadhikam sadā su kṣetram te pravakṣyāmi yatra dattam mahat phalam pratipannakāḥ catvāraḥ catvāraḥ ca phala sthitāḥ eṣa saṃghaḥ  dakṣiṇīyaḥ  vidyā caraṇa saṃpadā iti yadi catvāri ārya satyāni na santi teṣām ca parijñānāni tadā satya darśana bhāvanā labhyānām phalānām abhāvāt pratipannaka phala stha pudgalānām abhāva eva atas ca saṃghaḥ  na asti tatra adhigama dharmeṇa pratyakṣa dharma tayā sarva māraiḥ api buddhe bhagavati abhedya tvāt avetya prasāda lābhena saṃghaḥ sa na syāt  na ced  santi te aṣṭau puruṣa pudgalāḥ ārya satyānām ca abhāvāt  saddharmaḥ  api na saṃbhavati satām āryāṇām dharmaḥ saddharmaḥ tatra nirodha satyam phala dharmaḥ mārga satyam tu phala avatāra dharmaḥ eṣa tāvat adhigama dharmaḥ tad saṃprakāśikā deśanā āgama dharmaḥ sarva eṣa ārya satyānām abhāve sati na asti iti abhāvāt ca ārya satyānām saddharmaḥ  api na vidyate dharme ca asati saṃghe ca katham buddhaaḥ  bhaviṣyati yadi hi yathā uktaḥ  dharmaḥ syāt  tadā tad dharma pratipattyā sarva ākāra sarva dharma abhisaṃbodhāt  buddhaḥ  bhavati iti yuktam syāt  yadi ca saṃghaḥ syāt  tadā tad upadeśaiḥ upacīyamāna jñāna saṃbhāraḥ tad dāna māna śaraṇa gamana ādibhiḥ ca upacīyamāna puṇya saṃbhāraḥ kramāt  buddhaḥ  bhavet  athavā asati saṃghe srotaāpatti phala pratipannaka ādīnām abhāvaḥ syāt  na ca pratipannaka ādi tvam aprāpya buddha tvam āpyate avaśyam hi pūrvam bhagavatā kasmiṃścid  phale vyavasthātavyam tatra ca phale vyavasthitaḥ saṃgha antar pāti ā iva bhagavān bhavati saṃghe ca asati niyatam na asti bhagavān buddhaḥ atha bhagavān api aśaikṣa antar bhāvāt saṃgha antargata eva tathā ca buddha pramukhaḥ  bhikṣu saṃghaḥ iti abhidhānāt  saṃgha antargata eva bhagavān iti kecid varṇayanti teṣām matena spaṣṭam eva etad  dharme ca asati saṃghe ca katham buddhaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti madhya uddeśikāḥ ca mahā vastu upadiṣṭa bhūmi vyavasthayā prathama bhūmi sthitam bodhisattvam utpanna darśana mārgam vyācakṣāṇāḥ saṃgha antaḥpātinam vyācakṣate tadā saṃghe ca asati bodhisattvaḥ  api na asti iti katham buddhaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti spaṣṭam eva etad  tad  evam trīṇi api ratnāni bruvāṇaḥ pratibādhase śūnyatām iti evam vadan buddha dharma saṃgha ākhyāni trīṇi api durlabha tvāt  kadācid eva utpattitaḥ alpa puṇyānām ca tad aprāpteḥ mahārgha mūlya tvāt  ratnāni pratibādhase kim ca anyat  śūnyatām phala sadbhāvam adharmam dharmam eva ca sarva saṃvyavahārān  ca laukikān pratibādhase śūnyatām bruvāṇa iti anena saṃbandhaḥ yadi sarvam idam śūnyam yadā sarvam eva na asti tadā sarva antaḥ pāti tvāt  dharma adharmau saha tad hetukena iṣṭa aniṣṭa phalena na saṃbhavataḥ sarva eva cāmī laukikā vyavahārāḥ kuru paca khāda tiṣṭha gaccha āgaccha iti evamādayaḥ  api sarva antargata tvāt sarva dharmāṇām ca śūnya tvāt na eva yujyante iti atas  na ayam yathā upavarṇitaḥ  nyāyaḥ  jyāyān iti atra brūmaḥ śūnyatāyām na tvam vetsi prayojanam śūnyatām śūnyatā artham ca tatas  evam vihanyase sa bhavān sva vikalpanayā eva na astitvam śūnyatā artha iti evam viparītam adhyāropya  yadi sarvam idam śūnyam udayaḥ na asti na vyayaḥ  ityādinā upālambham bruvāṇaḥ  asmāsu mahāntam khedam āpannaḥ  atīva vihanyate vividhaiḥ bhūtaiḥ parikalpaiḥ hanyate iti arthaḥ na tu ayam asmābhiḥ atra śāstre śūnyatā artham upavarṇitaḥ  yaḥ tvayā parigṛhītaḥ śūnyatā artham ca aja ānānaḥ śūnyatām api na jānāsi na ca api śūnyatāyāḥ  yad prayojanam tad vijānāsi tatas ca yathā avasthita vastu svarūpā parijñānena etad  tvayā bahu ca ayuktam asmad vaya ākhyāna asaṃbaddham eva upavarṇitam atha kim punar  śūnyatāyām prayojanam uktam eva tad ātma parīkṣāyām karma kleśa kṣayāt mokṣaḥ karma kleśā vikalpataḥ te prapañcāt prapañcaḥ tu śūnyatāyām nirudhyate iti atas  niravaśeṣa prapañca upaśama artham śūnyatā upadiśyate tasmāt sarva prapañca upaśamaḥ śūnyatāyām prayojanam bhavān  tu na astitvam śūnyatā artham parikalpayan prapañca jālam eva saṃvardhayamānaḥ  na śūnyatāyām prayojanam vetti atha kā punar  śūnyatā sā api tatra eva uktā apara pratyayam śāntam prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam nirvikalpa manāna artham etad tatvasya lakṣaṇam iti atas  prapañca nivṛtti svabhāvāyām śūnyatāyām kutaḥ nāstitvam iti śūnyatām apina jānāti bhavān yam ca artham upādāya śūnyatā śabdaḥ pravartate tam api iha eva pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ yaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ śūnyatām tām pracakṣmahe sā prajñaptiḥ upādāya pratipatsā eva madhyamā iti yaḥ pratyayaiḥ jāyati sa hi ajātaḥ  na tasya utpādu svabhāvataḥ  asti yaḥ pratyaya adhīnu sa śūnyu uktaḥ  yaḥ śūnyatām jānati saḥ  apramattaḥ iti bhagavataḥ  gāthā vacanāt  evam pratītyasamutpāda śabdasya yaḥ  arthaḥ sa eva śūnyatā śabdasya arthaḥ na punar abhāva śabdasya yaḥ  arthaḥ sa śūnyatā śabdasya arthaḥ abhāva śabda artham ca śūnyatā artham iti adhyāropya bhavān asmān upālabhate tasmāt śūnyatā śabda artham api na jānāti ajānānaḥ ca tvam evam upālambham kurvan niyatam vihanyase kaḥ ca asmākam yathā uktam upālambham karoti yaḥ  bhagavat pravacana upadiṣṭa aviparīta satya dvaya vibhāgam na jānāti kevalam grantha mātra adhyayana para eva iti ata ācāryaḥ karuṇayā parasya mithyā pravacana artha avabodha nirāsa artham bhagavat pravacana upadiṣṭa aviparīta satya dvaya vyavasthām eva tāvat adhikṛtya āha dve satye samupāśritya buddhānām dharma deśanā loka saṃvṛti satyam ca satyam ca paramārthataḥ iha hi bhagavatām buddhānām satya dvayam āśritya dharma deśanā pravartate katamat satya dvayam loka saṃvṛti satyam ca parama artha satyam ca tatra skandha ātmā loka ākhyātaḥ tatra lokaḥ  hi niśritaḥ iti vacanāt pañca skandhān upādāya prajñapyamānaḥ pudgalaḥ  loka iti ucyate samantāt varaṇam saṃvṛtiḥ ajñānam hi samantāt sarva padārtha tattva avacchādanāt saṃvṛtiḥ iti ucyate paraspara saṃbhavanam vā saṃvṛtiḥ anyonya samāśrayeṇa iti arthaḥ athavā saṃvṛtiḥ saṃketaḥ  loka vyavahāra iti arthaḥ sa ca abhidhāna abhidheya jñāna jñeya ādi lakṣaṇaḥ loke saṃvṛtiḥ loka saṃvṛtiḥ kim punar aloka saṃvṛtiḥ api asti yata evam viśiṣyate loka saṃvṛtiḥ iti yathā avasthita padārtha anuvāda eṣaḥ na atra eṣā cintā avatarati athavā timira kāmalā ādi upahata indriya viparīta darśana avasthānāḥ te alokāḥ teṣām yā saṃvṛti rasa avaloka saṃvṛtiḥ atas  viśiṣyate loka saṃvṛtiḥ iti etad ca madhyamaka avatāre vistareṇa uktam tatas  veditavyam loka saṃvṛtyā satyam loka saṃvṛti satyam sarva eva ayam abhidhāna abhidheya jñāna jñeya ādi vyavahāraḥ  aśeṣaḥ  loka saṃvṛti satyam iti ucyate na hi paramārtha ta ete vyavahārāḥ saṃbhavanti tatra hi nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare anutpannā aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharmatā iti kṛtvā kutas tatra parama arthe vācām pravṛttiḥ kutaḥ vā jñānasya sa hi parama arthaḥ  apara pratyayaḥ śāntaḥ pratyātma vedya āryāṇām sarva prapañca atītaḥ sa na upadiśyate na ca api jñāyate uktam hi pūrvam apara pratyayam śāntam prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam nirvikalpa manāna artham etad tattvasya lakṣaṇam iti paramaḥ ca asau  arthaḥ ca iti parama arthaḥ tad eva satyam parama artha satyam anayoḥ ca satyayoḥ vibhāgaḥ  vistareṇa madhyamaka avatārāt avaseyaḥ tad etad satya dvayam āśritya buddhānām bhagavatām dharma deśanā pravartate evam vyavasthite deśanā krame ye anayoḥ na vijānanti vibhāgam satyayoḥ dvayoḥ te tattvam na vijānanti gambhīram buddha śāsane atra āha yadi tarhi parama arthaḥ  niṣprapañca svabhāvaḥ sa eva astu tad kim anayā aparayā skandha dhātu āyata nāri asatya pratītyasamutpāda ādi deśanayā prayojanam aparama arthayā ata tvam hi parityājyam yad ca parityājyam kim tena upadiṣṭena ucyate satyam etad evam kim tu laukikam vyavahāram anabhyupagamya abhidhāna abhidheya jñāna jñeya ādi lakṣaṇam aśakya eva parama arthaḥ  deśayitum adeśitaḥ ca na śakyaḥ  adhigantum anadhigamya ca parama artham na śakyam nirvāṇam adhigantum iti pratipādayan  āha vyavahāram anāśritya parama arthaḥ  na deśyate parama artham anāgamya nirvāṇam na adhigamyate tasmāt nirvāṇa adhigama upāya tvāt avaśyam eva yathā avasthitā saṃvṛtiḥ ādau  eva abhyupeyā bhājanam iva salila arthinā iti tad evam yaḥ saṃvṛti parama artha lakṣaṇa satya dvayasya vyavasthām apākṛtya śūnyatām varṇayati tam tathāvidham pudgalam vināśayati durdṛṣṭā śūnyatā manda medhasam sarpaḥ  yathā durgṛhītaḥ  vidyā vā duṣprasādhitā saṃvṛti satyam hi ajñāna mātra samutthāpitam niḥsvabhāvam buddhā tasya parama artha lakṣaṇām śūnyatām pratipadyamānaḥ  yogī na anta dvaye patati kim tadā āsīt yad idānīm na asti iti evam pūrvam bhāva svabhāva anupalambhāt  paścāt api na astitām na pratipadyate pratibimba ākārāyāḥ ca loka saṃvṛteḥ abādhanāt  karma karma phala dharma adharma ādikam api na bādhate na ca api parama artham bhāva svabhāva tvena samāropayati niḥsvabhāvānām eva padārthānām karma phala ādi darśanāt  sa svabhāvanām ca adarśanāt  yaḥ tu evam satya dvaya vibhāgam apaśyan śūnyatām saṃskārāṇām paśyati sa śūnyatām paśyan mumukṣuḥ na astitām vā saṃskārāṇām parikalpayet  yadi vā śūnyatām kāṃcid bhāvataḥ satīm tasyāḥ ca āśraya artham bhāva svabhāvam api parikalpayet  ubhayathā ca asya durdṛṣṭā śūnyatā niyatam vināśayet  katham kṛtvā yadi tāvat sarvam idam śūnyam sarvam na asti iti parikalpayet  tadā asya mithyādṛṣṭiḥ āpadyate yathā uktam vināśayati durdṛṣṭaḥ  dharmaḥ  ayam avipaścitam na astita adṛṣṭi samale yasmāt asmin nimajjati atha sarva apavādam kartum na icchati tadā niyatam asya śūnyatāyāḥ pratikṣepa āpadyate katham hi nāma amī bhāvāḥ sakala sura asura nara lokaiḥ upalabhyamānā api śūnyā bhaviṣyanti tasmāt na niḥsvabhāva arthaḥ śūnyatā arthaḥ iti evam pratikṣipya saddharma vyasana saṃvartanīyena pāpakena karmaṇā niyatam apāya anvayāt yathā uktam ārya ratna āvalyām aparaḥ  api asya durjñānāt mūrkhaḥ paṇḍita mānikaḥ pratikṣepa vinaṣṭa ātmā yāti avīcim adhomukhaḥ iti evam tāvat abhāvena gṛhyamāṇā śūnyatā grahītāram vināśayati atha ayam bhāvena śūnyatām parikalpayet  tad āśrayāṇām ca saṃskārāṇām astitvam evam api nirvāṇa gāmini mārge vipratipanna tvāt śūnyatā upadeśa vihvalaḥ  jāyeta tad evam bhāva rūpeṇa api śūnyatā gṛhyamāṇā grahītāram vināśayati nanu ca yad upakārakam tad anyathā [kriyamāṇam akāla uptam iva bījam na phalāya kalpate kāla uptam ca mahate phala lābhāya jāyate evam eva maṇi mantra auṣadha ādibhi] rgṛhyamāṇaḥ [sarpaḥ] mahāntam dhana skandham āvahati śiraḥ maṇi grahaṇāt  tena ca vyāla grāhakāṇām jīvikā kalpanāt  yathā uddeśa tiraskāreṇa tu gṛhyamāṇaḥ  grahītāram eva vināśayati yathā ca yathā upadeśam prasādhitā vidyā sādhakam anugṛhṇāti upadeśa paribhraṣṭā tu sādhyamānā sādhakam eva vināśayati evam iha api yathā upadeśam śūnyatā mahatī vidyā sādhyamānā gṛhyamāṇā bhāva abhāva ādi grāha tiraskāreṇa madhyamayā pratipadā grahītāram parameṇa jāti jarā maraṇa ādi duḥkha hutāśana śamana eka rasena nirupadhi śeṣa nirvāṇa jala dhara dhārā varṣa mukhena yojayati yathā upadeśa viśeṣa vigamena tu gṛhyamāṇā niyatam yathā uditena nyāyena grahītāram eva vināśayati yatas ca evam śūnyatā durgṛhītā grahītāram vināśayati manda prajñaiḥ ca aśakyā samyak grahītum atas ca pratyudāvṛttam cittam deśayitum muneḥ dharmam matvā asya dharmasya mandaiḥ duravagāha tām yasmāt ayam śūnyatā lakṣaṇaḥ  dharmaḥ  manda medha samalpa prajñam sattvam viparyāsa grahaṇāt vināśayati ata eva asya dharmasya mandaiḥ duravagāha tām matvā anuttarām samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbudhya sarva sattva dhātum ca avalokya dharmasya ca atigāmbhīryam saddharmam deśayitum cittam pratinivṛttam muneḥ buddhasya bhagavataḥ  mahā upāya jñāna viśeṣa śālinaḥ yathā uktam sūtre atha bhagavataḥ  acira abhisaṃbuddhasya etad abhavat  adhigataḥ  mayā dharmaḥ  gambhīraḥ  gambhīra avabhāsaḥ  atarkaḥ  atarka avacaraḥ sūkṣmaḥ paṇḍita vijña vedanīyaḥ saced tam aham pareṣām ārocayeyam pare ca me na vibhāvayeyuḥ sa mama vighātaḥ syāt  klamathaḥ syāt  cetasaḥ  anudayaḥ syāt  yad nu aham ekāki araṇye pravivikte dṛṣṭa dharma sukha vihāram anuprāptaḥ  vihareyam iti vistaraḥ tad evam satya dvaya aviparīta vyavasthām avijñāya śūnyatāyām adhilayam yam punar  kurute bhavān doṣa prasaṅgaḥ  na asmākam sa śūnye na upapadyate yaḥ  ayam bhavatā mahān doṣa prasaṅgaḥ  asmāsu prakṣiptaḥ yadi śūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ  na asti na vyayaḥ ityādinā sa yasmāt  satya dvaya vyavasthā anabhijñena satā śūnyatām śūnyatā artham śūnyatā prayojanam ca yathāvat abuddhā upakṣiptaḥ saḥ  asmākam śūnye śūnyatā vāde na upapadyate yatas ca na upapadyate atas  yam bhavān doṣa prasaṅgam śūnyatāyām udbhāvayan śūnyatāyām adhilayam adhikṣepam nirākaraṇam pratikṣepam karoti saḥ  adhilayaḥ  asmākam na upapadyate abhāva artham hi śūnyatā artham adhyāropya prasaṅga udbhāvitaḥ  bhavatā na ca vayam abhāva artham śūnyatā artham vyācakṣmahe kim tarhi pratītyasamutpāda artham iti atas  na yuktam etad  śūnyatā darśana dūṣaṇam na ca kevalam yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ  asmad pakṣe na avatarati api khalu sarvam eva satyādi vyavasthānam sutarām upapadyate iti pratipādayan  āha sarvam ca yujyate tasya śūnyatā yasya yujyate sarvaṃna yujyate tasya śūnyam yasya na yujyate yasya hi sarva bhāva svabhāva śūnyatā iyam yujyate tasya sarvam etad  yathā upavarṇitam yujyate katham kṛtvā yasmāt  pratītyasamutpādam hi vayam śūnyatā iti vyācakṣmahe yaḥ pratyayaiḥ jāyati sa hi ajātaḥ  na tasya utpādu svabhāvataḥ  asti yaḥ pratyaya adhīnu sa śūnya uktaḥ  yaḥ śūnyatām jānati saḥ  apramattaḥ iti gāthā vacanāt   śūnyāḥ sarva dharmā niḥsvabhāva yogena  iti prajñāpāramitā abhidhānāt tasmāt yasya iyam śūnyatā yujyate rocate kṣamate tasya pratītyasamutpādaḥ  yujyate yasya pratītyasamutpādaḥ  yujyate tasya catvāri ārya satyāni yujyante katham kṛtvā yasmāt  pratītyasamutpannam hi duḥkham bhavati na apratītyasamutpannam tad ca niḥsvabhāva tvāt śūnyam sati ca duḥkhe duḥkha samudayaḥ  duḥkha nirodhaḥ  duḥkha nirodha gāminī ca pratipad  yujyate tatas ca duḥkha parijñānam samudaya prahāṇam nirodha sākṣāt karaṇam mārga bhāvanā ca yujyate sati ca duḥkha ādi satya parijñāna ādike phalāni yujyante satsu ca phaleṣu phala sthā yujyante satsu ca phala stheṣu pratipannakā yujyante satsu ca pratipannaka phala stheṣu saṃghaḥ  yujyate ārya satyānām ca sadbhāve sati saddharmaḥ  api yujyate sati ca saddharme saṃghe ca buddhaḥ  api yujyate tatas ca trīṇi api ratnāni yujyante laukika lokottarāḥ ca padārthāḥ sarve viśeṣa adhigamā yujyante dharma adharmam tad phalam sugati durgatiḥ laukikāḥ ca sarva saṃvyavahārā yujyante tad evam sarvam ca yujyate tasya śūnyatā yasya yujyate yasya sarva bhāva svabhāva śūnyatā yujyate tasya sarvam etad  yathā uditam yujyate saṃpadyate iti arthaḥ yasya tu śūnyatā yathā uditā na yujyate tasya pratītyasamutpāda abhāvāt sarvam na yujyate yathā ca na yujyate tathā vistareṇa pratipādayiṣyati tad evam āsmākīne su pariśuddhatare sarva vyavasthāsu aviruddhe vyavasthite atisthūle ati āsanne tad viruddhe ca svakīye pakṣe doṣavati atimoghaḥ  yathāvat avasthitau guṇa doṣau  apaśyan sa tvam doṣān ātmanīnānasmāsu paripātayan aśvam eva abhiruḍhaḥ san  aśvam eva asi vismṛtaḥ yathā hi kaścid  yam eva aśvam ārūḍhaḥ tam eva vismṛtaḥ san tad apahāra doṣeṇa parān upālabhate evam eva bhavān pratītyasamutpāda lakṣaṇa śūnyatā darśana aśvam ārūḍha eva atyanta vikṣepāt tam anupalambhamānaḥ  asmān parivadati ke punar te parasya doṣāḥ yān anupalabhamānaḥ śūnyatā vādinam eva upālabhate iti tān pratipādayan  āha svabhāvāt yadi bhāvānām sadbhāvam anupaśyasi ahetu pratyayān bhāvān  tvam evam sati paśyasi yadi tvam svabhāvena vidyamānān bhāvān paśyasi tadā svabhāvasya hetu pratyaya nirapekṣa tvāt ahetu pratyayān avidyamāna hetu pratyayān padārthān bāhya ādhyātmika bheda bhinnān nirhetukān tvam evam sati paśyasi sati ca ahetukatva abhyupagame kāryam ca kāraṇam ca eva kartāram karaṇam kriyām utpādam ca nirodham ca phalam ca pratibādhase katham kṛtvā yadi iha ghaṭaḥ svabhāvataḥ  asti iti parikalpayasi tadā asya svabhāvataḥ  vidyamānasya kim mṛd ādibhiḥ hetu pratyayaiḥ prayojanam iti teṣām abhāvaḥ syāt  nirhetukam ca kāryam ghaṭa ākhyam na upapadyate asati ca asmin  cakra ādikasya karaṇasya kartuḥ kumbhakārasya ghaṭa karaṇa kriyāyāḥ ca abhāvā dutpāda nirodhayoḥ abhāvaḥ asatoḥ ca utpāda nirodhayoḥ kutas  phalam iti sa svabhāva abhyupagame sati sarvam etad  kārya ādikam pratibādhase tad evam bhavataḥ sa svabhāva abhyupagame sati sarvam eva na yujyate asmākam tu bhāva svabhāva śūnyatā vādinām sarvam etad upapadyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt vayam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ śūnyatām tām pracakṣmahe sā prajñaptiḥ upādāya pratipatsā eva madhyamā yaḥ  ayam pratītyasamutpādaḥ  hetu pratyaya an apekṣya aṅkura vijñāna ādīnām prādurbhāvaḥ sa svabhāve na anutpādaḥ yaḥ ca svabhāvena anutpādaḥ  bhāvānām sā śūnyatā yathā bhagavatā uktam yaḥ pratyatyaiḥ jāyati sa hi ajātaḥ  na tasya utpādu svabhāvataḥ  asti yaḥ pratyaya adhīnu sa śūnya uktaḥ  yaḥ śūnyatām jānati saḥ  apramattaḥ iti tathā ārya laṅkā avatāre  svabhāva anutpattim saṃdhāya mahāmate sarva dharmāḥ śūnyā iti mayā deśitāḥ  iti vistareṇa uktam dvayardha śatikāyām  śūnyāḥ sarva dharmā niḥsvabhāva yogena  iti yā ca iyam svabhāva śūnyatā sā prajñaptiḥ upādāya sā eva śūnyatā upādāya prajñaptiḥ iti vyavasthāpyate cakra ādīni upādāya rathāṅgāni rathaḥ prajñapyate tasya yā sva aṅgāni upādāya prajñaptiḥ sā svabhāvena anutpattiḥ yā ca svabhāvena anutpattiḥ sā śūnyatā sā eva svabhāva anutpatti lakṣaṇā śūnyatā madhyamā pratipad iti vyavasthāpyate yasya hi svabhāvena anutpattiḥ tasya astitva abhāvaḥ svabhāvena ca anutpannasya vigama abhāvāt nāstitva abhāva iti atas  bhāva abhāva anta dvaya rahita tvāt  sarva svabhāva anutpatti lakṣaṇā śūnyatā madhyamā pratipad  madhyamaḥ  mārga iti ucyate tad evam pratītyasamutpādasya eva etā viśeṣa saṃjñāḥ śūnyatā upādāya prajñaptiḥ madhyamā pratipad  iti vicāryamāṇaḥ ca sarvathā apratītya samutpannaḥ  dharmaḥ kaścid na vidyate yasmāt tasmāt aśūn yaḥ  hi dharmaḥ kaścid na vidyate yaḥ  hi apratītya samutpannaḥ  dharmaḥ sa na saṃvidyate yathā uktam śatake apratītya astitā na asti kadācid kasyacid kvacid  na kadācid kvacid kaścid vidyate tena śāśvataḥ ākāśa ādīni kalpyante nityāni iti pṛthagjanaiḥ laukikena api teṣu arthān na paśyanti vicakṣaṇāḥ iti uktam ca bhagavatā pratītya dharmān adhigacchate vidū na ca anta dṛṣṭīya karoti niśrayam sa hetu sa pratyaya dharma jānati ahetu apratyaya na asti dharmatā evam apratītya samutpannaḥ  dharmaḥ kaścid na vidyate apratīsamutpannaḥ ca śūnyaḥ tasmāt aśūnyaḥ  dharmaḥ  na asti yata etad evam atas  asmākam sarva dharmāḥ ca śūnyāḥ na ca para ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ bhavataḥ tu sa svabhāva vādinaḥ yadi aśūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ  na asti na vyayaḥ tadā niyatam udaya vyayayoḥ abhāve sati caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ te prasajyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt  apratītya samutpannam kutaḥ duḥkham bhaviṣyati anityam uktam duḥkham hi tad svābhāvye na vidyate yad hi sa svabhāvam na tad pratītya utpadyate yad ca apratītya samutpannam na tad anityam bhavati na hi gagana kusumam avidyamānam anityam anityam ca duḥkham uktam bhava gatā yad anityam tad duḥkham iti tathā ca śataka śāstre anityasya dhruvā pīḍā pīḍā yasya na tad sukham tasmāt anityam yad sarvam duḥkham tad iti jāyate iti yad ca anityam svābhāvye sa svabhāva tve abhyupagamyamāne bhāvānām tad na vidyata iti evam tāvat  sa svabhāva tve sati bhāvānām duḥkham na yujyate na ca kevalam duḥkham eva na yujyate sati sa svabhāva abhyupagame samudayaḥ  api na yujyate iti pratipādayan  āha svabhāvataḥ  vidyamānam kim punar  samudeṣyate tasmāt samudayaḥ na asti śūnyatām pratibādhataḥ iha samudeti asmāt duḥkham iti duḥkhasya hetu [taḥ] samudaya iti ucyate tad asya duḥkhasya śūnyatām pratibādhamānasya sa svabhāvam duḥkham abhyupagacchataḥ tasya punar utpāda vaiyarthyāt  tad hetu kalpanā vaii arthyam eva iti evam śūnyatām pratibādhamānasya samudayaḥ  api bhavataḥ  na yujyate svābhāvikam eva duḥkham abhyupagacchataḥ  duḥkha nirodhaḥ  api na yujyate iti pratipādayan  āha na nirodhaḥ svabhāvena sataḥ  duḥkhasya vidyate svabhāva paryavasthānāt nirodham pratibādhase yadi hi svabhāvataḥ  duḥkham syāt  tadā svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt kutaḥ asya nirodha tvam iti evam svabhāva paryavasthānāt  svabhāvam gṛhītvā pratyavatiṣṭhamānaḥ  duḥkha nirodham api pratibādhase idānīm ārya mārgaḥ  api sa svabhāva vādinaḥ  yathā na upapadyate tathā pratipādayan  āha svābhāvye sati mārgasya bhāvanā na upapadyate atha asau bhāvyate mārgaḥ svābhāvyam te na vidyate yadi hi sa svabhāvā bhāvā bhaveyuḥ tadā mārgaḥ  api sa svabhāva eva iti kṛtvā abhāvita eva asau  asti tasya kim punar bhāvanayā iti evam svābhāvye sati mārgasya bhāvanā na upapadyate atha asya mārgasya bhāvanā abhyupagamyate bhavatā evam tarhi svabhāva tā ārya mārgasya na syāt  kāryatvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ api ca duḥkhasya nirodha prāpti artham samudayasya ca prahāṇa artham bhāvanā mārgasya iṣyate pūrva uktena tu nyāyena sa svabhāva vādinaḥ  bhavataḥ yadā duḥkham samudayaḥ  nirodhaḥ ca na vidyate mārgaḥ  duḥkha nirodha tvāt  katamaḥ prāpayiṣyati na asti eva asau duḥkha nirodhaḥ yad nirodhāt mārgaḥ  bhāvitaḥ san prāpayiṣyati tasmāt ārya mārgaḥ  api evam na upapadyata iti evam sa svabhāva vādinaḥ caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ prāpnoti idānīm duḥkha ādi parijñāna ādikam api yathā parasya na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha svabhāvena aparijñānam yadi tasya punar  katham parijñānam nanu kila svabhāvaḥ samavasthitaḥ yadi pūrvam duḥkham aparijñāta svabhāvam tad  paścāt  parijñāyata iti kalpyate tad ayuktam kim kāraṇam yasmāt nanu kila svabhāvaḥ samavasthitaḥ yaḥ  hi svabhāvaḥ sa kila loke samavasthitaḥ na eva anyathātvam āpadyate vahneḥ auṣṇyavat  yadā ca svabhāvasya anyathātvam na asti tadā pūrvam aparijñāta svabhāvasya duḥkhasya paścāt api parijñānam na upapadyata iti atas  duḥkha parijñānam api na saṃbhavati yadā ca etad duḥkha parijñānam api na saṃbhavati tadā prahāṇa sākṣāt karaṇe bhāvanā ca evam eva te parijñāvat na yujyante catvāri api phalāni ca yad etad  samudayasya prahāṇam nirodhasya ca sākṣātkaraṇam te ete dve prahāṇa sākṣāt karaṇe yā ca mārgasya bhāvanā eṣā api evam eva te duḥkha parijñāna asaṃbhavān na yujyante samudayasya svabhāvena aprahīṇasya svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt paścāt api prahāṇam na upapadyate evam bhāvanā sākṣātkaraṇe api yojyam na ca kevalam parijñāna ādikam eva na saṃbhavati sa svabhāva vāde api ca parijñāvat na yujyante catvāri api phalāni ca yathā svabhāvena aparijñātasya duḥkhasya parijñānam na yuktam evam svabhāvena avidyamānasya pūrvam srotaāpatti phalasya paścāt astitvam na saṃbhavati yathā srotaāpatti phalasya evam sakṛdāgāmi anāgāmi arhat phalānām abhāvaḥ  veditavyaḥ na ca kevalam etāni phalāni parijñāvat na yujyante kim tarhi adhigamaḥ  api eṣām na yujyata iti pratipādayan  āha svabhāvena anadhigatam yad phalam tad punar  katham śakyam samadhigantum syāt svabhāvam parigṛhṇataḥ svabhāvasya avijahana prakṛtika tvāt bhāva svabhāva vādam abhyupagacchataḥ pūrvam anadhigata svabhāvānām paścāt api adhigamaḥ  na upapadyate tatas ca phala abhāve phala sthā naḥ na santi pratipannakāḥ saṃghaḥ  na asti na ced santi te aṣṭau puruṣa pudgalāḥ abhāvāt ca ārya satyānām saddharmaḥ  api na vidyate dharme ca asati saṃghe ca katham buddhaḥ  bhaviṣyati anayoḥ ca ślokayoḥ pūrvavat eva arthaḥ  veditavyaḥ api ca sa svabhāva abhyupagame sati apratītya api bodhim ca tava buddhaḥ prasajyate apratītya api buddham ca tava bodhiḥ prasajyate yadi hi svabhāvataḥ  buddhaḥ  nāma kaścid  bhāvaḥ syāt  sa bodhim sarvajña jñānam apratītya api anapekṣya api syāt  akṛtrimaḥ svabhāvaḥ  hi nirapekṣaḥ paratra ca iti vacanāt  tathā vinā api buddhena bodhiḥ syāt  anapekṣya api buddham nirāśrayā bodhiḥ syāt  kim ca anyat  yaḥ ca abuddhaḥ svabhāvena sa bodhāya ghaṭan  api na bodhisattva caryāyām bodhim te adhigamiṣyati iha hi buddha tvāt pūrvam abuddha svabhāvasya sataḥ pudgalasya satyām api bodhisattva caryāyām bodhi artham ghaṭamānasya api na eva bodhiḥ syāt  abuddha svabhāvasya vyāvartayitum aśakyatvāt  kim ca anyat  na ca dharmam adharmam vā kaścid jātu kariṣyati kim aśūnyasya kartavyam svabhāvaḥ kriyate na hi sati hi svabhāva vāda abhyupagame dharma adharmayoḥ karaṇam na upapadyate kim hi aśūnyasya kartavyam na hi svabhāvasya aśūnyasya kāraṇam upapadyate vidyamāna tvāt  kim ca anyat  vinā dharmam adharmam ca phalam hi tava vidyate dharma adharma nimittam ca phalam tava na vidyate yad etad dharma adharma nimittakam iṣṭa aniṣṭa phalam yadi tad  svabhāvataḥ  asti tad  vinā api dharma adharmābhyām syāt  yadā ca vinā dharma adharmam phalam tava asti tadā dharma adharma jam phalam tava na saṃbhavati dharma adharma upārjana vaiyarthyam syāt  dharma adharma nimittam ca phalam tava na vidyate iti atha dharma adharma nimittakam phalam bhavati iti parikalpyate na tarhi tad phalam aśūnyam iti pratipādayan  āha dharma adharma nimittam vā yadi te vidyate phalam dharma adharma samutpannam aśūnyam te katham phalam śūnyam eva etad  pratītyasamutpanna tvāt  pratibimbavat  iti abhiprāyaḥ api ca sarva eva hi ete agaccha kuru paca paṭha tiṣṭha  iti evamādayaḥ  laukikā vyavahārāḥ pratītyasamutpannāḥ tān yadi sa svabhāvān icchati bhavān tadā bhavatā pratītyasamutpādaḥ  bādhitaḥ  bhavati tad bādhanāt ca sarva eva laukikā vyavahārā bādhitā bhavanti iti pratipādayan  āha sarva saṃvyavahārān  ca laukikān pratibādhase yad pratītyasamutpāda śūnyatām pratibādhase yad śabdaḥ kriyā viśeṣaṇam yad bādhase iti anena saṃbadhyate kim ca anyat  na kartavyam bhavet kiṃcid anārabdhā bhavet kriyā kārakaḥ syāt akurvāṇaḥ śūnyatām pratibādhataḥ yadi hi sva rūpa śūnyāḥ padārthā na bhaveyuḥ sa svabhāvā eva bhaveyuḥ tadā svabhāvasya vidyamāna tvāt na kenacid  kasyacid  kiṃcid  kartavyam syāt  na hi nabhasaḥ  anāvaraṇa tvam kenacid  kriyate akriyamāṇā ca kriyā syāt  kriyām ca akurvāṇasya kāraka tvam syāt  na ca etad evam iti tasmāt na aśūnyāḥ padārthāḥ kim ca anyat  ajātam aniruddham ca kūṭastham ca bhaviṣyati vicitrābhiḥ avasthābhiḥ svabhāve rahitam jagat  [vicitrābhiḥ avasthāmiḥ sva bhāva racitam svabhāvena eva racitam apratītya samutpannam jagat  svabhāva śūnya vādinām ] svabhāvena eva yadi bhāvāḥ [sa svabhāvāḥ] syuḥ tadā svabhāvasya akṛtrima tvāt avyāvartana tvāt ca sarvam idam jagat ajātam aniruddham ca syāt  ajāta aniruddha tvāt jagat  kūṭastham syāt  hetu pratyaya anapekṣam vicitrābhiḥ avasthābhiḥ  rahitam apratītya samutpannam jagat aśūn yavādinām syāt  yathā uktam pitāputra samāgame syāt yadi kiṃcid aśūnyam na vadet jinu tasya vyākaraṇam tathā hi sthitam tad  svake svake bhāve kūṭastham avikāram na tasya vṛddhiḥ na parihāṇiḥ iti tathā ārya hasti kakṣya sūtre yadi koci dharmāṇa bhavet svabhāvaḥ tatra eva gaccheya jinaḥ sa śrāvakaḥ kūṭastha dharmāṇa siyā na nirvṛtī na niṣprapañcaḥ  bhavi jātu paṇḍitaḥ iti na ca kevalam sa svabhāva vāda abhyupagame laukikā eva vyavahārā na upapadyante api ca lokottarā eva [api ] na upapadyante iti pratipādayan  āha asaṃprāptasya ca prāptiḥ duḥkha paryanta karma ca sarva kleśa prahāṇam ca yadi aśūnyam na vidyate yadi hi aśūnyam sa svabhāvam sarvam etad  syāt  tadā yad asaṃprāptam tad asaṃprāptam eva iti asaṃprāptasya ca phalasya prāptiḥ na syāt  tadā duḥkha paryanta kāraṇam ca pūrvam na abhūt iti sāṃpratam api na syāt  sarveṣām ca kleśānām pūrvam prahāṇam na abhūt iti paścāt api prahāṇam na syāt  tad evam yasmāt  sa svabhāva vāda abhyupagame sati sarvam etad na yujyate atas  yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam paśyati idam sa paśyati duḥkham samudayam ca eva nirodham mārgam eva ca yaḥ  hi sarva dharma pratītyasamutpāda lakṣaṇām svabhāva śūnyatām samyak  paśyati sa catvāri ārya satyāni paśyati yathābhūtāni tattvataḥ yathā uktam ārya mañjuśrī paripṛcchāyām yena mañju śrīḥ anutpādaḥ sarva dharmāṇām dṛṣṭaḥ tena duḥkham parijñātam yena na astitā sarva dharmāṇām dṛṣṭā tasya samudayaḥ prahīṇaḥ yena atyanta parinirvṛtāḥ sarva dharmā dṛṣṭāḥ tena nirodhaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ yena mañju śrīḥ bhāvaḥ sarva dharmāṇām dṛṣṭaḥ tena mārgaḥ  bhāvitaḥ iti vistaraḥ uktam ca ārya dhyāyita muṣṭi sūtre atha khalu bhagavān mañju śriyam kumāra bhūtam etad avocat  caturṇā mañjuśrīḥ ārya satyānām yathābhūta adarśanāt caturbhiḥ viparyāsaiḥ viparyasta cittāḥ sattvā evabhimama bhūtam saṃsāram na atikrāmanti evam ukte mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ  bhagavantam etad avocat  deśayatu bhagavān kasya upalambhataḥ sattvāḥ saṃsāram na atikrāmanti bhagavān āha ātma ātmīya upalambhataḥ  mañjuśrīḥ sattvāḥ saṃsāram na atikrāmanti tad  kasya hetoḥ yaḥ  hi mañjuśrīḥ ātmānam param ca samanupaśyati tasya karma abhisaṃskārā bhavanti bālaḥ  mañju śrīraśrutavān pṛthagjanaḥ  atyanta parinirvṛtān sarva dharmānaprajā nānaḥ ātmānam param ca upalabhate upalabhya abhiniviśate abhiniviṣṭaḥ san rajyate duṣyate muhyate sa raktaḥ  duṣṭaḥ  mūḍhaḥ san trividham karma abhisaṃskaroti kāyena vācā manasā saḥ asat samāropeṇa vikalpayati aham raktaḥ aham duṣṭaḥ aham mūḍhaḥ iti tasya tathāgata śāsane pravrajitasya evam bhavati aham śīlavān aham brahmacārī saṃsāram samatikrāmiṣyāmi aham nirvāṇam anuprāpsyāmi aham duḥkhebhyaḥ  mokṣyāmi sa kalpayati ime dharmāḥ kuśalāḥ ime dharmā akuśalā iti ime dharmāḥ prahātavyāḥ ime dharmāḥ sākṣāt kartavyāḥ duḥkham parijñātavyam samudayaḥ prahātavyaḥ nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ mārgaḥ  bhāvayitavyaḥ sa kalpayati anityāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ ādīptāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ yad nu aham sarva saṃskārebhyaḥ palāya iyam tasya eva mavekṣamāṇasya utpadyate nirvitsaha gataḥ  manasikāraḥ animitta purogataḥ tasya evam bhavati eṣā sā duḥkha parijñā yā iyam eṣām dharmāṇām parijñā tasya evam bhavati yad nu aham samudayam prajaheyam sa sarva dharmebhya artīyate jehrīyate vitarati vijugupsate uttrasyati saṃtrasyati saṃtrāsam āpadyate tasya evam bhavati iyam eṣām dharmāṇām sākṣātkriyā idam samudaya prahāṇam yadidamebhyaḥ  dharmebhyaḥ  artīyanā tasya evam bhavati nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ samudayam kalpayitvā nirodham saṃjānāti tasya evam bhavati eṣā sā nirodha sākṣāt kriyā tasya evam bhavati yad nūnam aham mārgam bhāvayeyam sa ekaḥ  rahaḥ gataḥ tān dharmān manasi kurvan śamatham pratilabhate tasya tena nirvitsaha gatena manasikāreṇa śamatha utpadyate tasya sarva dharmeṣu cittam na pralīyate prativahati pratyudāvartate tebhyaḥ ca ārtīyate jehrīyate anabhinandana acittam samutpadyate tasya evam bhavati muktaḥ  asmi sarva duḥkhebhyaḥ na mama bhūyas  uttariṃ kiṃcitkaraṇīyam arhan  asmi iti ātmānam saṃjānāti sa maraṇa kāla samaye utpattim ātmanaḥ  deveṣu paśyati tasya kāṅkṣā vicikitsā ca bhavati buddha bodhau sa vicikitsām āpatitaḥ kālagataḥ  mahānirayeṣu prapatati tad kasya hetoḥ yathā api idam anutpannān sarva dharmān vikalpayitvā tathāgate vicikitsām vimatim utpādayati atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ  bhagavantam etad avocat  katham punar bhagavan catvāri ārya satyāni draṣṭavyāni bhagavān āha yena mañju śrīḥ anutpannāḥ sarva dharmā dṛṣṭāḥ tena duḥkham parijñātam yena asamutthitāḥ sarva dharmā dṛṣṭāḥ tasya samudayaḥ prahīṇaḥ yena atyanta parinirvṛtāḥ sarva dharmā dṛṣṭāḥ tena nirodhaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ yena atyanta śūnyāḥ sarva dharmā dṛṣṭāḥ tena mārgaḥ  bhāvitaḥ yena mañjuśrīḥ evam catvāri ārya satyāni dṛṣṭāni sa na kalpayati ime dharmāḥ kuśalāḥ ime dharmā akuśalāḥ ime dharmāḥ prahātavyāḥ ime dharmāḥ sākṣāt kartavyāḥ duḥkham parijñātavyam samudayaḥ prahātavyaḥ nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ mārgaḥ  bhāvayitavyaḥ iti tad  kasya hetoḥ tathā hi sa tam dharmam na samanupaśyati na upalabhate yam parikalpayet  bāla pṛthagjanāḥ tu etān dharmān kalpayantaḥ  rajyanti ca dviṣyanti ca muhyanti ca sa na kaṃcid dharmam āvyūhati nirvyūhati tasya evam anāvyūhataḥ  anirvyūhataḥ traidhātuke cittam na sajjati ajātam sarva tra edhātukam samanupaśyati māyā upamam svapna upamam pratiśrutka upamam evaṃsvabhāvān sarva dharmān paśyan anunaya pratidhāpa gataḥ  bhavati sarva sattveṣu tad  kasya hetoḥ tathā hi sa tān dharmān na upalabhate yatra anunīyeta vā pratihanyeta vā sa ākāśa samena cittena buddham api na samanupaśyati dharmam api na samanupaśyati saṃdham api na samanupaśyati sarva dharmān śūnyān iti samanupaśyan na kvacid dharme vicikitsām utpādayati avicikitsan nirupādānaḥ  bhavati nirupādānaḥ  anupādāya parinirvāti iti vistaraḥ iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau ārya satya parīkṣā nāma caturviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam nirvāṇa parīkṣā pañcaviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam atra āha yadi śūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ  na asti na vyayaḥ prahāṇāt vā nirodhāt vā kasya nirvāṇam iṣyate iha hi bhagavatā uṣita brahmacaryāṇām tathāgata śāsana pratipanna annām dharma anudharma pratipatti yuktānām pudgalānām dvividham nirvāṇam upavarṇitam sa upadhi śeṣam nirupadhi śeṣam ca tatra niravaśeṣasya avidyā rāga ādikasya kleśa gaṇasya prahāṇāt  sa upadhi śeṣam nirvāṇam iṣyate tatra upadhīyate asmin  ātma snehaḥ iti upadhiḥ upadhi śabdena ātma prajñapti nimittāḥ pañca upādāna skandhā ucyante śiṣyata iti śeṣaḥ upadhiḥ eva śeṣaḥ upadhi śeṣaḥ saha upadhi śeṣeṇa vartate iti sa upadhi śeṣam kim tad  nirvāṇam tad ca skandha mātrakam eva kevalam sat kāya dṛṣṭayā ādi kleśa taskara rahitam avaśiṣyate nihata aśeṣa caura gaṇa grāma mātra avasthāna sādharmyeṇa tad  sa upadhi śeṣam nirvāṇam yatra tu nirvāṇe skandha pañcakam api na asti tad nirupadhi śeṣam nirvāṇam nirgataḥ upadhi śeṣaḥ  asmin  iti kṛtvā nihata aśeṣa caura gaṇasya grāma mātrasya api vināśa sādharmyeṇa tad eva ca adhikṛtya ucyate abhedi kāyaḥ  nirodhi saññā vedanā pi ti dahaṃsu sabbā vūpa samiṃsu saṃkhārā viññāṇam attham agamā ti tathā asaṃlīnena kāyena vedanām adhya vāsayat  pradyotasya iva nirvāṇam vimokṣaḥ tasya cetasaḥ iti tad evam nirupadhi śeṣam nirvāṇam skandhānām nirodhāt labhyate etad ca dvividham nirvāṇam katham yujyate yadi kleśānām skandhānām ca nirodhaḥ  bhavati yadā tu sarvam idam śūnyam na eva kiṃcid utpadyate na api kiṃcid nirudhyate tadā kutas  kleśāḥ kutaḥ vā skandhāḥ yeṣām nirodhe nirvāṇam syāt iti tasmāt vidyata eva bhāvānām svabhāva iti atra ucyate nanu evam api sa svabhāva abhyupagame yadi aśūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ  na asti na vyayaḥ prahāṇāt vā nirodhāt vā kasya nirvāṇam iṣyate svabhāvena hi vyavasthitānām kleśānām skandhānām ca svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt kutaḥ nivṛttiḥ yatas tad nivṛttyā nirvāṇam syāt iti tasmāt  svabhāva vādinām na eva nirvāṇam upapadyate na ca śūnyatā vādinaḥ skandha nivṛtti lakṣaṇam kleśa nivṛtti lakṣaṇam vā nirvāṇam icchanti yatas teṣām ayam doṣaḥ syāt iti atas  anupālambha eva ayam śūnya vādinām yadi khalu śūnyatā vādinaḥ kleśānām skandhānām vā nivṛtti lakṣaṇam nirvāṇam na icchanti kiṃlakṣaṇam tarhi icchanti ucyate aprahīṇam asaṃprāptam anucchinnam aśāśvatam aniruddham anutpannam etad nirvāṇam ucyate yad hi na eva prahīyate rāga ādivat  na api prāpyate śrāmaṇya phalavat  na api ucchidyate skandha ādivat  yad ca api na nityam aśūn yavat  tad  svabhāvataḥ  aniruddham anutpannam ca sarva prapañca upaśama lakṣaṇam nirvāṇam uktam tad  kutas tasmin  itthaṃvidhe niṣprapañce kleśa kalpanā yeṣām kleśānām prahāṇān nirvāṇam bhavet  kutaḥ vā skandha kalpanā tatra yeṣām skandhānām nirodhāt  tad bhavet yāvat hi etāḥ kalpanāḥ pravartante tāvat na asti nirvāṇa adhigamaḥ sarva prapañca parikṣayāt eva tad adhigamāt  atha syāt  yadi api nirvāṇe na santi kleśāḥ na ca api skandhāḥ tathā api nirvāṇāt arvāk vidyante tatas teṣām parikṣayāt nirvāṇam bhaviṣyati iti ucyate tyajyata āmayam grāhaḥ yasmāt nirvāṇāt arvāk  svabhāvataḥ  vidyamānānām na punar abhāvaḥ śakyate kartum tasmāt nirvāṇa abhilāṣiṇā tyājya eṣā kalpanā vakṣyati hi nivāṇasya ca yā koṭiḥ koṭiḥ saṃsaraṇasya ca na tayoḥ antaram kiṃcid su sūkṣmam api vidyate iti tad evam nirvāṇe na kasyacid  prahāṇam na api kasyacid nirodha iti vijñeyam tatas ca niravaśeṣa kalpanā kṣaya rūpam eva nirvāṇam uktam ca bhagavatā nirvṛtti dharmāṇa ca asti dharmā ye na iha astī na te jātu asti asti iti na asti iti ca kalpanāvatām evam carantāna na duḥkha śāmyati iti asyāḥ  gāthāyāḥ  ayam arthaḥ nivṛtau nirupadhi śeṣe nirvāṇa dhātau dharmāṇām kleśa karma janma lakṣaṇānām skandhānām vā sarvathā astaṃgamāt astitvam na asti evam ca sarva vādinām abhimatam ye tarhi dharmā iha nirvṛtau na santi pradīpa udayāt andhakāra upalabdha rajju sarpa bhaya ādivat  na te jātu asti na te dharmāḥ kleśa karma janma ādi lakṣaṇāḥ kasmiṃścid  kāle saṃsāra avasthāyām api tattvataḥ  vidyante na hi rajjuḥ andhakāra avasthāyām svarūpataḥ sarpaḥ  asti sadbhūta sarpavat  andhakāre api āloke api kāya cakṣuḥ bhyām agrahaṇāt  katham tarhi saṃsāraḥ iti ced  ucyate ātma ātmīya asat graha grastānām bāla pṛthagjanānām asat svarūpā api bhāvāḥ satyataḥ pratibhāsante taimirikāṇām iva asat keśam aśaka ādaya iva iti āha asti iti na asti iti ca kalpanāvatām evam carantāna na duḥkha śāmyati iti asti iti bhāva sadbhāva kalpanāvatām jaiminīya kāṇādakā pila ādīnām vaibhāṣika paryantānām na asti iti ca kalpanāvatām nāstikānām apāya gati niṣṭhānām tad anyeṣām ca atīta anāgata saṃsthānām vijñapti viprayukta saṃskārāṇām na astivādinām tad anyat asti vādinām parikalpita svabhāvasya na astivādinām paratantra pariniṣpanna svabhāvayoḥ asti vādinām evam asti nāstivādinām evam caratām na duḥkham saṃsāraḥ śāmyati iti tathā yatha śaṅkitena viṣa saṃjña abhyupeti naḥ ca api koṣṭha gantu āviṣṭa papadyate evam eva bālu apagataḥ  jāyi mriyate sadā abhūtaḥ  iti tad evam na kasyacid nirvāṇe prahāṇam na api kasyacid nirodha iti vijñeyam tatas ca sarva kalpanā kṣaya rūpam eva nirvāṇam yathā uktam ārya ratna āvalyām na ca abhāvaḥ  api nirvāṇam kuta eva asya bhāvanā bhāva abhāva parāmarśa kṣayaḥ  nirvāṇam ucyate iti ye tu sarva kalpanā upaśama rūpam nirvāṇam apratipadyamānāḥ bhāva abhāva tad ubhaya anubhaya rūpam nirvāṇam parikalpayanti tān prati ucyate bhāvaḥ tāvat na nirvāṇam jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇam prasajyeta asti bhāvaḥ hi na jarā maraṇam vinā tatra eke bhāvataḥ nirvāṇam abhiniviṣṭā evam ācakṣate iha kleśa karma janma saṃtāna pravṛtti niyata rodha bhūtaḥ  jala pravāha rodha bhūta setu sthānīyaḥ  nirodha ātmakaḥ padārthaḥ tad nirvāṇam na ca avidyamāna svabhāvaḥ  dharmaḥ evam kārya kārī dṛśyate nanu ca yaḥ  asyāḥ  nandī rāga sahagatāyāḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ kṣayaḥ  virāgaḥ  nirodhaḥ  nirvāṇam iti uktam na ca kṣaya mātram bhāvaḥ bhavitum arhati tathā pradyotasya iva nirvāṇam vimokṣaḥ tasya cetasaḥ iti uktam na ca pradyotasya nivṛttiḥ bhāva iti upapadyate ucyate na etad evam vijñeyam tṛṣṇāyāḥ kṣayaḥ tṛṣṇā kṣayaḥ iti kim tarhi tṛṣṇāyāḥ kṣayaḥ  asmin  iti nirvāṇa ākhye dharme sati bhavati sa tṛṣṇā kṣaya iti vaktavyam pradīpaḥ ca dṛṣṭānta mātram tatra api yasmin sati cetasaḥ  vimokṣaḥ  bhavati iti veditavyam iti evam bhāve nirvāṇa vyavasthāpite ācāryaḥ  nirūpayati bhāvaḥ tāvat na nirvāṇam kim kāraṇam yasmāt jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇam prasajyeta bhāvasya jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇa avyabhicāri tvāt tatas ca nirvāṇam eva tad na syāt  jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇa tvāt vijñānavat  iti abhiprāyaḥ tām eva ca jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇa vyabhicāritām spaṣṭayan  āha asti bhāvaḥ hi na jarā maraṇam vinā iti yaḥ  hi jarā maraṇa rahitaḥ sa bhāva eva na saṃbhavati kha puṣpavat  jarā maraṇa rahita tvāt kim ca anyat  bhāvaḥ ca yadi nirvāṇam nirvāṇam saṃskṛtam bhavet  na asaṃskṛtaḥ  hi vidyate bhāvaḥ kvacana kaścana yadi nirvāṇam bhāvaḥ syāt  tadā tad nirvāṇam saṃskṛtam bhavet  vijñāna ādivat  bhāva tvāt  yaḥ tu asaṃskṛtaḥ na asau bhāvaḥ tad yathā khara viṣāṇavat iti vyatirekam upadarśayan  āha na asaṃskṛtaḥ  hi vidyate bhāvaḥ kvacana kaścana kvacana iti adhikaraṇe deśe kāle siddhānte vā kaścana iti ādheye ādhyātmikaḥ bāhya ātmikaḥ  vā iti arthaḥ kim ca anyat  bhāvaḥ ca yadi nirvāṇam anupādāya tad katham nirvāṇam na anupādāya kaścid  bhāvaḥ hi vidyate yadi bhavat matena nirvāṇam bhāvaḥ syāt  tad upādāya bhavet  sva kāraṇa sāmagrīm āśritya bhavet iti arthaḥ na ca evam upādāya nirvāṇam iṣyate kim tarhi anupādāya tad yadi bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam anupādāya tad  katham nirvāṇam syāt  na eva anupādāya syāt  bhāva tvāt  vijñāna ādivat  vyatireka kāraṇam āha na anupādāya kaścid bhāvaḥ  hi vidyate iti atra āha yadi bhāvaḥ hi na nirvāṇam yathā udita doṣa prasaṅgāt  kim tarhi abhāva eva nirvāṇam kleśa janma nivṛtti mātra tvāt iti ucyate etad api ayuktam yasmāt  yadi bhāvaḥ na nirvāṇam abhāvaḥ kim bhaviṣyati nirvāṇam yatra bhāvaḥ na na abhāvaḥ tatra vidyate yadi bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam na iṣyate yadi nirvāṇam bhāva iti na iṣyate tadā kim abhāvaḥ  bhaviṣyati nirvāṇam abhāvaḥ  api na bhaviṣyati iti arthaḥ kleśa janmanoḥ abhāvaḥ  nirvāṇam iti ced  evam tarhi kleśa janmanoḥ anitya tā nirvāṇam iti syāt  anitya tā eva hi kleśa janmanoḥ abhāvaḥ  na anyat  iti atas  anitya tā eva nirvāṇam syāt  na ca etad iṣṭam ayatnena eva mokṣa prasaṅgāt iti uktam eva etad  kim ca anyat  yadi abhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam anupādāya tad katham nirvāṇam na hi abhāvaḥ  asti yaḥ  anupādāya vidyate tatra abhāvaḥ anitya tā vā bhāvam upādāya prajñapyate khara viṣāṇa ādīnām anitya tā anupalambhāt lakṣaṇam āśritya lakṣyam prajñapyate lakṣyam āśritya ca lakṣaṇam atas  paraspara apekṣikyām lakṣya lakṣaṇa pravṛttau kutaḥ lakṣyam bhāvam apekṣya anitya tā bhaviṣyati tasmāt abhāvaḥ  api upādāya prajñapyate tatas  yadi abhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam tad  katham anupādāya nirvāṇam bhavet  upādāya eva tad bhavet abhāva tvāt vināśavat  etad eva spaṣṭayan  āha na hi abhāvaḥ  asti yaḥ  anupādāya vidyate iti yadi tarhi abhāvaḥ anupādāya na asti kim idānīm upādāya bandhyā putrāt ayaḥ  abhāvā bhaviṣyanti kena etad uktam vandhyā putrāt ayaḥ  abhāvā iti uktam hi pūrvam bhāvasya ced aprasiddhiḥ abhāvaḥ  na eva sidhyati bhāvasya hi anyathābhāvam abhāvam bruvate janāḥ iti tasmāt na bandhyā putra ādīnām abhāva tvam yad ca api ucyate ākāśam śaśa śṛṅgam ca vandhyāyāḥ putra eva ca asantaḥ ca abhilapyante tathā bhāveṣu kalpanā iti tatra api bhāva kalpanā pratiṣedha mātram na abhāva kalpanā bhāvatva asiddheḥ eva iti vijñeyam vandhyā putra iti śabda mātram eva etad  na asya arthaḥ upalabhyate yasya arthasya bhāva tvam abhāva tvam vā syāt iti kutas  anupalabhyamāna svabhāvasya bhāva abhāva kalpanā yokṣyate tasmāt  na bandhyā putraḥ  abhāva iti vijñeyam tatas ca sthitam eva na hi abhāvaḥ  asti yaḥ  anupādāya vidyate iti atra āha yadi bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam na bhavati abhāvaḥ  api kim tarhi nirvāṇam iti ucyate iha hi bhagavadbhiḥ tathāgataiḥ ya ājavaṃjavībhāva upādāya pratītya vā saḥ  apratītya anupādāya nirvāṇam upadiśyate tatra ājavaṃjavībhāvaḥ āgamana gamana bhāva janma maraṇa paraṃparā iti arthaḥ sa ca ayam āja vaṃjavībhāvaḥ kadācid hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm āśritya asti iti prajñapyate dīrgha hrasvavat  kadācid utpadyata iti prajñapyate pradīpa prabhāva t  bīja aṅkuravat  sarvathā yadi ayam upādāya prajñapyate yadi vā pratītya jāyata iti vyavasthāpyate sarvathā asya janma maraṇa paraṃpara aprabandhasya apratītya vā anupādāya vā apravṛttiḥ tad nirvāṇam iti vyavasthāpyate na ca apravṛtti mātram bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ  vā iti parikalpitu pāryata iti evam na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ  nirvāṇam athavā yeṣām saṃskārāḥ saṃsaranti iti pakṣaḥ teṣām pratītya pratītya ya utpādaḥ ca vināśaḥ ca saḥ  apratītya apravartamānaḥ  nirvāṇam iti kathyate yeṣām tu pudgalaḥ saṃsarati teṣām tasya nitya anitya tvena avācyasya tad tad upādānam āśritya ya ājavaṃjavībhāvaḥ sa upādāya pravartate sa eva upādāya upādāya pravartayamānaḥ san  idānīm anupādāya apravartayamānaḥ  nirvāṇam iti vyapadiśyate na ca saṃskārāṇām pudgalasya vā apravṛtti mātrakam bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ  vā iti śakyam parikalpayitum iti atas  api na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ  nirvāṇam iti yujyate kim ca anyat  prahāṇam ca abravīt śāstā bhavasya vibhavasya ca tasmāt na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ  nirvāṇam iti yujyate tatra sūtra uktam ye kecid bhikṣavaḥ  bhavena bhavasya niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante vibhavena vā aparijñānam [tam ] tad teṣām iti ubhayam hi etad  parityājyam bhave tṛṣṇā vibhave tṛṣṇā ca na ca etad nirvāṇam prahātavyam uktam bhagavatā kim tarhi aprahātavyam tad yadi nirvāṇam bhāva rūpam syāt abhāva rūpam vā tad api prahātavyam bhavet  na ca prahātavyam tasmāt na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ  nirvāṇam iti yujyate yeṣām api kleśa janmanoḥ tatra abhāvāt abhāva rūpam nirvāṇam svayam ca bhāva rūpa tvāt bhāva rūpam iti ubhaya rūpam teṣām ubhaya rūpam iti nirvāṇam na upapadyate iti pratipādayan  āha bhavet abhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam ubhayam yadi bhavet abhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ ca mokṣaḥ tad ca na yujyate yadi bhāva abhāva ubhaya rūpam nirvāṇam syāt  tadā bhāvaḥ ca abhāvaḥ ca mokṣa iti syāt  tatas ca yaḥ saṃskārāṇām ātma lābhaḥ tasya ca vigamaḥ sa eva mokṣaḥ syāt  na ca saṃskārā eva mokṣa iti yujyate ata eva āha tad ca na yujyate iti kim ca anyat  bhavet abhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam ubhayam yadi na anupādāya nirvāṇam upādāya ubhayam hi tad  yadi bhāva abhāva rūpam nirvāṇam syāt  tadā hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm upādāya āśritya bhavet  na anupādāya kim kāraṇam yasmāt upādāya ubhayam hi tad  bhāvam upādāya abhāvaḥ abhāvam ca upādāya bhāvaḥ iti kṛtvā ubhayam etad  bhāvam ca abhāvam ca upādāya eva bhavati na anupādāya evam nirvāṇam bhavet  bhāva abhāva rūpam na ca etad evam iti na yuktam etad  kim ca anyat  bhavet abhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam ubhayam katham asaṃskṛtam ca nirvāṇam bhāva abhāvau ca saṃskṛtau bhāvaḥ hi sva hetu pratyaya sāmagrī saṃbhūta tvāt saṃskṛtaḥ abhāvaḥ  api [bhāvaṃ] pratītya saṃbhūta tvāt  jāti pratyaya jarā maraṇa vacanāt ca saṃskṛtaḥ tad yadi bhāva abhāva svabhāvam nirvāṇam syāt  tadā na asaṃskṛtam [kim tu] saṃskṛtam eva yasmāt na ca saṃskṛtam iṣyate tasmāt na bhāva abhāva svarūpam nirvāṇam yujyate atha api syāt  na eva hi nirvāṇam bhāva abhāva svarūpam kim tarhi nirvāṇe bhāva abhāvau  iti evam api na yuktam kutas  yasmāt  bhavet abhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇe ubhayam katham [tayoḥ ekatra na astitvam āloka tamasoḥ yathā] bhāva abhāvayoḥ api paraspara viruddhayoḥ ekatra nirvāṇe na asti saṃbhava iti atas  bhavet abhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇe ubhayam katham na eva bhavet iti abhiprāyaḥ idānīm yathā na eva bhāvaḥ na eva abhāvaḥ  nirvāṇam yujyate tathā pratipādayan  āha na eva abhāvaḥ  na eva bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti yā añjanā abhāve ca eva bhāve ca sā siddhe sati sidhyati yadi hi bhāvaḥ nāma kaścid  syāt  tadā tad pratiṣedhena na eva bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti eṣā kalpanā yadi kaścid abhāvaḥ syāt  tadā tad pratiṣedhena na eva abhāvaḥ  nirvāṇam syāt  yadā ca bhāva abhāvau  eva na staḥ tadā tad pratiṣedhaḥ  api na asti iti tasmāt na eva bhāvaḥ na eva abhāvaḥ  nirvāṇam iti yā kalpanā sā api na upapadyata eva iti na yuktam etad  kim ca anyat  na eva abhāvaḥ  na eva bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam yadi vidyate na eva abhāvaḥ  na eva bhāva iti kena tad ajyate yadi etad nirvāṇam na eva abhāva rūpam na eva bhāva rūpam asti iti kalpyate kena tadānīm tad itthaṃvidham na ubhaya rūpam nirvāṇam asti iti ajyate gṛhyate prakāśate vā kim tatra nirvāṇe kaścid evaṃvidhaḥ pratipattā asti atha na asti yadi asti evam sati nirvāṇe api tava ātmā syāt  na ceṣṭam nirupādānasya ātmanaḥ  astitva abhāvāt  atha na asti kena etad itthaṃvidham nirvāṇam asti iti paricchidyate saṃsāra avasthitaḥ paricchinatti iti ced  yadi saṃsāra avasthitaḥ paricchinatti sa kim vijñānena paricchinatti utta jñānena yadi vijñānena iti parikalpyate tad na yujyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt nimitta ālambanam vijñānam na ca nirvāṇe kiṃcid nimittam asti tasmāt na tad tāvat vijñānena ālambyate jñānena api na jñāyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt  jñānena hi śūnyatā ālambanena bhavitavyam tad ca anutpāda rūpam eva iti katham tena avidyamāna svarūpeṇa na eva abhāvaḥ  na eva bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti gṛhyate sarva prapañca atīta rūpa tvāt  jñānasya iti tasmāt na kenacid nirvāṇam na eva abhāvaḥ  na eva bhāva iti ajyate anajyamānam aprakāśyamānam agṛhyamāṇam tad evam asti iti na yujyate sarvathā yathā ca nirvāṇe etāḥ catasraḥ kalpanā na saṃbhavanti evam nirvāṇa adhigantarī api tathāgate etāḥ kalpanā na eva saṃbhavanti iti pratipādayan  āha param nirodhāt bhagavān bhavati iti eva na uhyate na bhavati ubhayam ca iti na ubhayam ca iti na uhyate uktam hi pūrvam ghana grāha gṛhītaḥ tu yena asti iti tathāgataḥ na asti iti vā kalpayan sa nirvṛtasya vikalpayet  evam tāvat  param nirodhāt bhavati tathāgataḥ  na bhavati ca iti na uhyate etad dvayasya abhāvāt
