ubhayam iti api na uhyate ubhayasya abhāvāt eva na ubhayam iti na uhyate na gṛhyate na ca kevalam param nirodhāt caturbhiḥ prakāraiḥ bhagavān na uhyate api ca tiṣṭhamānaḥ  api bhagavān bhavati iti eva na uhyate na bhavati ubhayaṃca iti na ubhayam ca iti na uhyate yathā na ājyam na cohyam tathā tathāgata parīkṣāyām pratipāditam ata eva na saṃsārasya nirvāṇāt kiṃcid asti viśeṣaṇam na nirvāṇasya saṃsārāt kiṃcid asti viśeṣaṇam yasmāt tiṣṭhan  api bhagavān bhavati iti evamādinā na uhyate parinirvṛtaḥ  api na uhyate bhavati iti evamādinā ata eva saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ parasparataḥ  na asti kaścid viśeṣaḥ vicāryamāṇayoḥ tulya rūpa tvāt yad ca api idam uktam bhagavatā anavara agraḥ  hi bhikṣavaḥ  jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāra iti tad api ata eva upapannam saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ viśeṣasya abhāvāt  tathā hi nirvāṇasya ca yā koṭiḥ koṭiḥ saṃsaraṇasya ca na tayoḥ antaram kiṃcid su sūkṣmam api vidyate na ca kevalam saṃsārasya nirvāṇena aviśiṣṭa tvāt  pūrva apara koṭi kalpanā na saṃbhavati yā api etāḥ param nirodhāt anta ādyāḥ śāśvata ādyāḥ ca dṛṣṭayaḥ nirvāṇam apara antam ca pūrva antam ca samāśritāḥ tā api ata eva na upapadyante saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ ubhayoḥ api prakṛti śānta tvena eka rasa tvāt tatra param nirodhāt itya nena upalakṣaṇena catasraḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ parigṛhyante tad yathā bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt  na bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāta bhavati ca na bhavati ca tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt  na eva bhavati na na bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt iti etāḥ catasraḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ  nirvāṇa parāmarśena pravṛttāḥ anta ādyā api dṛṣṭayaḥ tad yathā antavān lokaḥ anantavān  ca antavān  ca ānantavān  ca na eva antavān na anantavān lokaḥ iti etāḥ catasraḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ  apara antam samāśritya pravṛttāḥ tatra ātmanaḥ  lokasya vā anāgatam utpādam apaśyan antavān loka iti evam kalpayan apara antam ālambya pravartate evam anāgatam utpādam paśyan anantavān loka ioti pravartate paśyan  ca apaśyan  ca ubhayathā prātipadyate dvaya pratiṣedhena na eva antavān na anantavān iti pratipadyate śāśvataḥ  lokaḥ aśāśvataḥ  lokaḥ śāśvataḥ ca aśāśvataḥ ca na eva śāśvataḥ  na eva āśāśvātaḥ  lokaḥ iti etāḥ catasraḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ pūrva antam samāśritya pravartante tatra ātmanaḥ  lokasya vā atītam utpādam paśyan śāśvataḥ  loka iti pratipadyate apaśyan  aśāśvata iti pratipadyate paśyan  ca apaśyan  ca śāśvataḥ ca aśāśvataḥ ca iti pratipadyate na eva paśyat   aiva apaśyan na eva śāśvataḥ  na aśāśvataḥ ca iti pratipadyate pūrva antamāa śritya tāḥ ca etā dṛṣṭayaḥ katham yujyante yadi kasyacid padārthasya kaścid  svabhāvaḥ  bhavet  tasya bhāva abhāva kalpanāt  syuḥ etā dṛṣṭayaḥ yadā tu saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ pratipāditaḥ tadā śūnyeṣu sarva dharmeṣu kim anantam kim antavat  kim anantam antavat ca na anantam na antavat ca kim kim tad eva kim anyat kim śāśvatam kim aśāśvatam aśāśvatam śāśvatam ca kim vā na ubhayam api atas  caturdaśa api etāni avyākṛta vastūni asati bhāva svarūpe na eva yujyante yaḥ tu bhāva svarūpam adhyāropya tad vigama avigamataḥ etā dṛṣṭīḥ utpādya abhiniviśate tasya ayam abhiniveśaḥ  nirvāṇa pura gāminam panthānam niruṇaddhi sāṃsārikeṣu ca duḥkheṣu niyojayati iti vijñeyam atra āha yadi evam bhavatā nirvāṇam api pratiṣiddham nanu ca ya eṣa bhava gatā ananta carita sattva rāśi anuvartakena vidita aviparīta sakala jagat āśaya svabhāvena mahākarūṇa aparatantreṇa priya eka putra kaprema anugata aśeṣa tribhuvana janena carita pratipakṣa anurūpaḥ  dharmaḥ  deśitaḥ  lokasya nirvāṇa adhigama artham sa evam sati vyartha eva jāyate ucyate yadi kaścid dharmaḥ  nāma svabhāva rūpataḥ syāt  kecid ca sattvāḥ tasya dharmasya śrotāraḥ syuḥ kaścid vā deśitā buddhaḥ  bhagavān nāma bhāva svabhāvaḥ syāt  syāt etad evam yadā tu sarva upalambha upaśamaḥ prapañca upaśamaḥ śivaḥ na kvacid kasyacid kaścid dharmaḥ  buddhena deśitaḥ tadā kutaḥ asmākam yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iha hi sarveṣām prapañcānām nimittānām ya upaśamaḥ  apravṛttiḥ tad nirvāṇam sa eva ca upaśamaḥ prakṛtyā eva upaśānta tvāt śivaḥ vācām apravṛtteḥ vā prapañca upaśamaḥ cittasya apravṛtteḥ śivaḥ kleśānām apravṛttyā vā janmanaḥ  apravṛttyā śivaḥ kleśa prahāṇena vā prapañca upaśamaḥ  niravaśeṣa vāsanā prahāṇe śivaḥ jñeya anupalabdhyā vā prapañca upaśamaḥ  jñāna anupalabdhyā śivaḥ yadā ca evam buddhā bhagavantaḥ sarva prapañca upaśa anta rūpe nirvāṇe śive asthāna yogena nabhasi iva haṃsa rājāḥ sthitāḥ sva puṇya jñāna saṃbhāra pakṣa pāta vāte vāta gagane vā gaganasya akiṃcana tvāt  tadā sarva nimittān upalambhāt na kvacid deveṣu vā manuṣyeṣu vā na kasyacid devasya vā manuṣyasya vā na kaścid dharmaḥ sāṃkleśikaḥ  vā vaiyavadānikaḥ  vā deśita iti vijñeyam yathā uktam ārya tathāgata guhya sūtre  yām ca rātriṃ śānta mate tathāgataḥ  anuttarām samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbuddhaḥ yām ca rātrim anupādāya parinirvāsyati atra antare tathāgatena ekam api akṣaram na udāhṛtam na vyāhṛtam na api pravyāharati na api pravyāhariṣyati atha ca yathā adhimuktāḥ sarva sattvā nānā dhātvāśayāḥ tām tām vividhām tathāgata vācam niścarantīm saṃjānanti teṣām evam pṛthak  pṛthak bhavati ayam bhagavān asmabhyam imam dharmam deśayati vayam ca tathāgatasya dharma deśanām śṛṇumaḥ tatra tathāgataḥ  na kalpayati na vikalpayati sarva kalpa vikalpa jāla vāsanā prapañca vigataḥ  hi śānta mate tathāgataḥ  iti vistaraḥ tathā avāca anakṣarāḥ sarva śūnyāḥ śānta ādi nirmalāḥ ya evam jānati dharmān kumāraḥ  buddha sā ucyate yadi tarhi evam na kvacid kasyacid kaścid dharmaḥ  buddhena deśitaḥ tad katham ime ete vicitrāḥ pravacana vyavahārāḥ prajñāyante ucyate avidyā nidrā anugatānām dehinām svapnāyamānānām iva sva vikalpa abhyudaya eṣaḥ ayam bhagavān sakala tribhuvana sura asura nara nāthaḥ imam dharmam asmabhyam deśayati iti yathā uktam bhagavatā tathāgataḥ  hi pratibimba bhūtaḥ kuśalasya dharmasya anāsravasya na eva atra tathatā na tathāgataḥ  asti bimbam ca saṃdṛśyati sarva loke iti etad ca tathāgata vāc guhya parivarte vistareṇa vyākhyātam tatas ca nirvāṇa artham dharma deśanāyāḥ  abhāvāt  kutaḥ dharma deśanāyāḥ sadbhāvena nirvāṇasya astitvam bhaviṣyati tasmāt nirvāṇam api na asti iti siddham uktam ca bhagavatā anirvāṇam hi nirvāṇam lokanāthena deśitam ākāśena kṛtaḥ  granthiḥ ākāśena eva mocitaḥ iti tathā na teṣām bhagavan saṃsāra samatikramaḥ  ye nirvāṇam bhāvataḥ paryeṣante tad kasya hetoḥ nirvāṇam iti bhagavan yaḥ praśamaḥ sarva nimittānām uparatiḥ sarva in jita samiñjitānām tad ime bhagavan moha puruṣā ye su ākhyāte dharma vinaye pravrajya tīrthika dṛṣṭau nipatitā nirvāṇam bhāvataḥ paryeṣante tad yathā tilebhyaḥ tailam kṣīrāt sarpiḥ atyanta parinirvṛteṣu bhagavan sarva dharmeṣu ye nirvāṇam mārganti tān aham ā abhimānikān tīrthikān iti vadāmi na bhagavan yoga ācāraḥ samyak  pratipannaḥ kasyacid dharmasya utpādam vā nirodham vā karoti na api kasyacid dharmasya prāptim icchati nābhi samayam iti vistaraḥ iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau nirvāṇa parīkṣā nāma pañcaviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam dvādaśa aṅga parīkṣā ṣaḍviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam atra āha yad uktam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ śūnyatām tām pracakṣmahe sā prajñaptiḥ upādāya pratipatsā eva madhyamā iti kaḥ punar asau pratītyasamutpādaḥ yaḥ śūnyatā iti ucyate athavā yad etad uktam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam paśyati idam sa paśyati duḥkham samudayam ca eva nirodham mārgam eva ca iti tad katamaḥ  asau pratītyasamutpādaḥ iti atas tad aṅga prabheda vivakṣayā it amucyate punarbhavāya saṃskārān avidyā nivṛtaḥ tridhā abhisaṃskurute yān  taiḥ gatim gacchati karmabhiḥ tatra avidyā ajñānam tamaḥ  yathābhūta artha pracchādakam stimita tā avidyayā nivṛtaḥ chāditaḥ pudgalaḥ punarbhavāya punarbhava artham punarbhava utpatti artham abhisaṃskaroti utpādayati yān kuśala ādi cetanā viśeṣān  te punarbhava abhisaṃskārāt  saṃskārāḥ te ca trividhāḥ kuśalā akuśalā ānejyāḥ ca yadi vā kāyikā vācikā mānasāḥ ca iti tān  trividhān karma lakṣaṇān saṃskārān avidyā nivṛtaḥ pudgalaḥ karoti taiḥ ca saṃskāraiḥ abhisaṃskṛtaiḥ karmabhiḥ karma saṃjñitaiḥ tad hetukān gatim gacchati tatas  asya vijñānam saṃniviśate saṃskāra pratyayam gatau kṛta upacita saṃskārasya asya pudgalasya saṃskāra anurūpāyām gatau deva ādikāyām saṃskāra hetukam vijñānam saṃniviśate praviśati upapadyate saṃsāra anartha bīja bhūtam tatas  uttara kālam saṃniviṣṭe atha vijñāne nāma rūpam niṣicyate tatra karma kleśa āviddham tasmin  tasmin  upapatti āyatane nāmayati iti nāma saṃjñā vaśena vā artheṣu nāmayati iti nāma catvāraḥ  arūpiṇaḥ skandhā nāma iti vyapadiśyate rūpyata iti rūpam bādhyata iti arthaḥ idam ca rūpam pūrvakam ca nāma ubhayam etad abhisaṃkṣipya nāma rūpam iti vyavasthāpyate tatra bimba pratibimba nyāyena svādhyāya dīpa mudrā pratimudrā ādi nyāyena vā māraṇa antikeṣu skandheṣu nirudhyamāneṣu ekasmin  eva kṣaṇe tulā daṇḍa nāma unnāma nyāyena eva aupapattyā aṃśikāḥ skandhā yathā karma ākṣepata upajāyante evam ca bimba pratibimba mudrā pratimudrā nyāyena pratītyasamutpādaḥ sidhyati tulā daṇḍa nāma unnāma nyāyena tu yad vijñānam saṃniviśate iti uktam tad  bāla loka bodha anurodhena samāna kāla eva bhava pratisaṃdhiḥ iti tathā samānena samāna kālam lokasya duḥkham ca sukha udayam ca hartum ca kartum ca sadā astu śaktiḥ tamaḥ prakāśam ca yathā eva bhānoḥ iti na tu punar  pratītyasamutpāda svarūpa vicakṣaṇānām evam vaktum yujyate sāhacarya ādi tvam ekakṣaṇe tulā daṇḍa nāmā unnāma dṛṣṭāntena iti janma unmukham na sat idam yadi jāyamānaṃnāśa unmukham sat api nāma nirudhyamānam iṣṭam tadā katham idam tulayā samānam kartrā vinā janiḥ iyam na ca yukta rūpā ityādi vacanāt  yathā bimba pratibimba mudrā pratimudrā ādi nyāyena kṣaṇika tvam na iṣyate bhavadbhiḥ tathā anyasya api bhāvasya utpāda samanantara dhvaṃsinaḥ kṣaṇika tvam na yuktam yatas  jāti jarā sthiti anitya tā ākhyāni catvāri saṃskṛta lakṣaṇāni utpadyamānasya bhāvasya bāhyasya ādhyātmikasya vā ekasmin  eva kṣaṇe bhavanti iti abhidharma pāṭhaḥ tatra jāti jarayoḥ paraspara virodhāt  sthiti anitya tayoḥ ca ekasmin  eva bhāve na yugapad saṃbhava iṣyate sadbhiḥ kṣaṇike sarvathā bhāvāt kutas  kācid purāṇa tā sthairyāt akṣaṇike ca api kutas  kācid purāṇa tā yathā antaḥ asti kṣaṇasya evamādi madhyam ca kalpyatām antaka tvāt kṣaṇasya evam na lokasya kṣaṇa sthitiḥ ādi madhya avasānāni cintyāni kṣaṇavat punar  ādi madhya avasāna tvam na svatas  paratas  api vā iti madhyamaka siddhānta pāṭhāt  kṣaṇika padārtha asiddheḥ siddhiḥ avaseyā na ca jāti maraṇayoḥ paraspara bhinna lakṣaṇayoḥ ekasmin kṣaṇe saṃbhavaḥ  bhavet  saṃśaya niścaya jñānayoḥ āloka andhakārayoḥ jñāna ajñānayoḥ bīja aṅkurayoḥ maraṇa bhava upapatti bhavayoḥ bhinna lakṣaṇayoḥ iti ādivat  paraspara nirapekṣayoḥ eva sva hetu pratyaya siddhayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ  yujyate savya itara gaḥ viṣāṇayoḥ yuvati stanayoḥ nara karṇayoḥ iti ādivat  na tu punar  kadācid api paraspara viruddhayoḥ vināśa utpādayoḥ yathā uktam rāga rakta parīkṣāyām saha eva punar udbhūtiḥ na yuktā rāga raktayoḥ bhavetām rāga raktau hi nirapekṣau parasparam na ekatve sahabhāvaḥ  asti na tena eva hi tad saha pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ  atha kuta eva bhaviṣyati evam raktena rāgasya siddhiḥ na saha na asaha rāgavat sarva dharmāṇām siddhiḥ na saha na asaha iti pratiṣedhāt  kutas  samāna kāla tā bhāvānām maraṇa bhava upapatti bhavayoḥ iti atas  sahabhāvaḥ  vineya jana bodha anurodha pravṛtta eva iti lakṣyate tena na ekasmin  eva kṣaṇe nāma unnāmau tulāyāḥ saṃbhavataḥ nāma unnāmayoḥ kāla bhedāt  balavat puruṣāt chaṭā mātreṇa pañcaṣaṣṭiḥ kṣaṇā atikrāmanti iti pāṭhāt  utpala patra śata sahasra vedhavat sūcī agreṇa iti tathā api atra utpala patra śata sahasra vedhaḥ sūcī agreṇa kramaśas  vedhaḥ  avaseyaḥ kṣaṇānām ati sūkṣma tvāt  ekakṣaṇena śloka akṣara pada udāharaṇavat kim ca anirodham anutpādam anucchedam aśāśvatam aneka artha manāna artham anāgamam anirgamam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam prapañca upaśamam śivam iti pāṭhāt utpāda nirodhayoḥ asaṃbhava eva pratipāditaḥ śāstre madhyamake āgama sūtreṣu avināśam anutpannam dharmadhātu samam jagat  sattva dhātum ca deśa iti eṣā loka anuvartanā trīṣu adhvasu sattvānām prakṛtim na upalambhati sattva dhātum ca deśa iti eṣā loka anuvartanā ityādi tathā phena piṇḍa upamam rūpam vedanā budbuda upamā marīci sadṛśī saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ kadalī nibhāḥ māyā upamam ca vijñānam uktam āditya bandhunā evam dharmān vīkṣamāṇaḥ  bhikṣuḥ ārabdha vīryavān divā vā yadi vā rātrau saṃprajānan pratismṛtaḥ pratividhyet padam śāntam saṃskāra upaśamam śivam iti etāḥ ca gāthāḥ sarva nikāya śāstra sūtreṣu paṭhayante atas  phena piṇḍa ādīnām hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm prāpya pratītya samutpannānām sāra vastu vigatānām kutas  kṣaṇikā kṣaṇika cintā iti mahāyāna sūtreṣu ca su pinā upamā bhava gatī sakalā na hi kaści jāyati na ca u mriyate na ca karma naśyati kadāci kṛtam phalu deti kṛṣṇa śubha saṃsarataḥ  na ca śāśvatam na ca uccheda punaḥ na ca karma saṃcayu na ca api sthitiḥ na ca saḥ  api kṛtva punar āspṛśatī na ca anyu kṛtva puna vedayate yathā kumārī supina antarasmin sva putra jātam ca mṛtaṃca paśyati jāte ati tuṣṭā mṛti daurmanasyitā tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān yathā eva grāma antari lekha darśanāt  kriyāḥ pravartanti pṛthak  śubha aśubhāḥ na lekha saṃkrānti girāya vidyate tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān mudrāt pratimudra dṛśyate mudra saṃkrānti na ca upalabhyate na ca tatra na ca eva sa anyatas  evam saṃskāra anuccheda śāśvatāḥ bījasya sataḥ  yathā aṅkuraḥ  na ca yaḥ  bīju sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas  na ca eva tad  evam anuccheda aśāśvata dharmatā yatha muñja pratītya balbajam rajju vyāyāma balena vartitā ghaṭiyantra sa cakra vartate teṣu ekaikasu na asti vartanā tatha sarva bhava aṅga vartinī anyam anya upacayena niśritā ekaikeṣu teṣu vartanī pūrvam aparāntatu na upalabhyate ata eva uktam ācārya nāgārjuna pādaiḥ svādhyāya dīpa mudrā darpaṇa ghoṣa arka kānta bīja amlaiḥ skandha pratisaṃdhiḥ asaṃkramaḥ ca vidvadbhiḥ upadhāryau iti śataka śāstre ca ārya deva pādaiḥ mahā bodhi caryā sthira prasthāna sthitaiḥ alāta cakra nirmāṇa svapna māyā ambu candrakaiḥ dhūmikā antaḥ pratiśrutkā marī ci abhraiḥ samaḥ  bhavaḥ iti tad evam bimba pratibimba ādi nyāyena mātuḥ kukṣau vijñāne saṃmūrcchite vijñāna pratyayam nāma rūpam niṣicyate kṣarati prādurbhavati iti arthaḥ yadi iha gatau vijñānam na saṃmūrchitam syāt  tadā nāma rūpa prādurbhāvaḥ  na syāt  saced ānanda vijñānam mātuḥ kukṣim na avakrāmeta na tad  kalalam kalala tvāya saṃvarteta iti vacanāt  tad evam niṣikte nāma rūpe tu ṣaṣ āyatana saṃbhavaḥ duḥkha utpattyā āya dvāra bhāvena darśana śravaṇa ghrāṇa rasa sparśa manaa ākhyam ṣaṣ āyatanam nāma rūpa hetukam upajāyate sa cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭvā saumanasya sthānīyāni abhiniviśate abhiniviṣṭaḥ san rāga jam dvā iva jam moha jam karma karoti ityādinā duḥkha utpatta āvāya dvāra tvam ṣaṇṇām āyatanānām tad evam saṃbhūte ṣaṣ āyatane uttara kālam ṣaṣ āyatanam āgamya saṃsparśaḥ saṃpravartate kaḥ punar ayam saṃsparśaḥ katham vā saṃpravartate iti pratipādayan  āha cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpam ca samanvāhāram eva ca nāma rūpam pratītya evam vijñānam saṃpravartate saṃnipāta srayāṇām yaḥ  rūpa vijñāna cakṣuṣām sparśaḥ saḥ cakṣuḥ indriyam pratītya rūpāṇi ca samanvāhāram ca pratītya manaskāram viṣaya ādi vilakṣaṇam samanantara pratyayam vijñāna bīja bhūtam cakṣuḥ vijñānam utpadyate tatra cakṣuḥ ca rūpa āyatanam ca rūpam samanvāhāraḥ catur skandha lakṣaṇam nāma tad etad trayam pratītya utpadyamānam cakṣuḥ vijñānam nāma rūpam pratītya utpadyate tad evam eṣām indriya viṣaya vijñānānām trayāṇām yaḥ saṃnipātaḥ saha utpādaḥ anyonya upakāreṇa tulyam yā pravṛttiḥ sa spṛṣṭi lakṣaṇaḥ sparśaḥ tatas  uttara kālam tasmāt sparśāt ca vedanā saṃpravartate iṣṭa aniṣṭa ubhaya viparīta viṣaya anubhūtiḥ viṣaya anubhavaḥ  vedanam vittiḥ vedanā iti ucyate duḥkhā sukhā aduḥkha asukhā ca trividhā yathā ca eṣām rūpa vijñāna cakṣuṣām trayāṇām saṃnipāta lakṣaṇam sparśam āgamya vedanā uktā evam śeṣa indriya viṣaya vijñāna traya saṃnipāta lakṣaṇa sparśa hetukā vedanā vyākhyeyā tatas  uttara kālam vedanā pratyayā tṛṣṇā saṃpravartate iti vartate vedanā pratyayaḥ yasyāḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ sā vedanā pratyayā kiṃviṣayā punar  sā tṛṣṇā vedanā viṣayā eva kim kāraṇam yasmāt asau tṛṣṇāluḥ vedanā artham hi tṛṣyate vedanā nimittam eva abhilāṣam karoti iti arthaḥ katham kṛtvā yadi tāvat  sukhā vedanā asya upajāyate sa tasyāḥ punar  punar  saṃyoga artham paritṛṣyate atha duḥkhā tadā tasyāḥ  visaṃyoga artham paritṛṣyate atha aduḥkha asukhā tasyāḥ  api nityam aparibhraṃśa artham paritṛṣyate sa evam tṛṣyamāṇa  upādānam upādatte caturvidham sa evam vedanāsu abhiniviṣṭaḥ saktaḥ tṛṣṇā pratyayam kāma dṛṣṭi śīla vrata ātma vāda upādāna ākhyam caturvidham karma ākṣepa kāraṇam parigṛhṇāti tad evam asya tṛṣṇā pratyayam upādānam bhavati tatas  uttara kālam upādāne sati bhava upādātuḥ pravartate syāt hi yadi anupādānaḥ  mucyeta na bhavet bhavaḥ pañca skandhāḥ sa ca bhavaḥ caturvidhasya yathā uktasya upādānasya upādātā grahītā utpādayitā tasya upādātuḥ upādāna pratyayaḥ bhavaḥ upajāyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt  yaḥ  hi anutpādita vedanā tṛṣṇaḥ pratisaṃkhyāna balena tṛṣṇām asvīkurvan caturvidham upādānam pravihāya upādātā amala advaya jñāna saṃmukhībhāvāt syāt hi yadi anupādānaḥ  mucyeta saḥ tadānīm tasya na bhavet bhavaḥ kaḥ punar ayam bhavaḥ pañca skandhāḥ sa ca bhavaḥ yaḥ upādānāt  pravartate sa pañca skandha svabhāvaḥ  veditavyaḥ trividham api kāyikam vācikam mānasikam ca karma bhavati asmāt anāgatam skandha pañcakam bhavaḥ iti vyapadiśyate tatra kāyikam vācikam karma rūpa skandha svabhāvam karma vijñapti tvāt  mānasam tu catur skandha svabhāvam iti evam sa bhavaḥ pañca skandhā iti vijñeyam tasmāt  bhavāt jātiḥ pravartate anāgata skandha utpādaḥ  jātiḥ sā ca bhavāt  pravartate tatas  uttara kālam jarā maraṇa duḥkha ādi śokāḥ sa paridevanāḥ daurmanasyam upāyāsā jāteḥ etad pravartate jāti hetukā ete jarā maraṇa ādayaḥ pravartante eṣām ca yathāsūtram eva vyākhyānam veditavyam tatra skandha paripākaḥ  jarā jīrṇasya skandha bhedaḥ  maraṇam mriyamāṇasya vigacchataḥ saṃmūḍhasya sāmiṣaṅgaḥ  hṛdaya saṃtāpaḥ śokaḥ śoka samutthitaḥ  vāc pralāpaḥ paridevaḥ pañca indriya asāta nipātaḥ  duḥkham manaḥ niṣṭa nipātaḥ  daurmanasyam duḥkha daurmanasya bahutva saṃbhūtā upāyāsāḥ iti tad evam yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena kevalasya evam etasya duḥkha skandhasya saṃbhavaḥ kevalasya iti ātma ātmīya svabhāva vigatasya bāla pṛthagjana parikalpita mātrasya duḥkha ātmakasya sukha avyāmiśrasya eva iti arthaḥ evam iti hetu pratyaya mātra balena eva iti arthaḥ duḥkha skandhasya iti duḥkha samudāyasya duḥkha samūhasya duḥkha rāśeḥ iti arthaḥ yatas ca evam yathā upavarṇitādavidyā ādikāt eva bhava aṅgānām pravṛttiḥ atas  saṃsāra mūlān saṃskārān avidvān saṃskaroti atas  avidvān kārakaḥ tasmāt na vidvān  tattva darśanāt tatra saṃsārasya vijñāna ādi pravṛtti lakṣaṇasya mūlam pradhānam kāraṇam saṃskārāḥ tatas ca saṃsāra mūlān saṃskārān avidvān saṃskaroti avidyā anugataḥ  yaḥ pudgalaḥ  bhikṣavaḥ puṇyān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti apuṇyān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti āneñjyān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti iti bhagavat vacanāt  yatas ca evam avidvān kārakaḥ tasmāt avidvān eva pudgalaḥ kārakaḥ  bhavati saṃskārāṇām na vidvān  tattva darśī prahīṇa avidyaḥ kim kāraṇam tattva darśanāt tattva darśane hi sarva padārthanām ā iva anupalambhāt na asti kiṃcid  yad ā ālambya karma kuryāt iti yatas ca evam avidyāyām eva satyām saṃskārāḥ pravartante asatyām na pravartante atas  avidyāyām niruddhāyām saṃskārāṇām asaṃbhavaḥ hetu vaiyarthyāt  tasyāḥ punar avidyāyāḥ kutaḥ nirodhaḥ iti āha avidyāyāḥ  nirodhaḥ tu jñānena asya eva bhāvanāt  asya eva pratītyasamutpādasya yathāvat aviparīta bhāvanātaḥ avidyā prahīyate yaḥ  hi pratītyasamutpādam samyak  paśyati sa sūkṣmasya api bhāvasya na svarūpam upalabhate pratibimba sva prālāta cakra mudga ādivat tu svabhāva śūnyatām sarveṣām bhāvānām avatarati sa eva svabhāva śūnyatām sarveṣām bhāvānām avatīrṇaḥ  na kiṃcid vastu upalabhate bāhyam ādhyātmikam vā saḥ  anupalabhamānaḥ  na kvacid dharme muhyati amūḍhaḥ ca karma na karoti iti evam pratītyasamutpāda bhāvanayā tattvam avatarati tattva darśinaḥ yoginaḥ  niyatam eva avidyā prahīyate prahīṇa avidyasya saṃskārā nirudhyante yathā ca evam avidyā nirodhāt saṃskārā nirudhyante evam tasya tasya nirodhena tad tad na abhipravartate duḥkha skandhaḥ kevalaḥ  ayam evam samyak  nirudhyate pūrvasya pūrvasya aṅgasya nirodhena utarasya uttarasya aṅgasya nirodhaḥ  bhavati iti vijñeyam anayā ca ānupūrvyā ayam yogī ātma ātmīya ādya darśana āyāsa nirastaḥ kāraka vedaka vi rahitam bhāva svabhāva śūnyam duḥkha rāśim punar anutpattyā samyak nirodhayati yathā uktam ārya śāli stamba sūtre evam ādhyātmikaḥ  api pratītyasamutpādaḥ  dvābhyām eva kāraṇābhyām utpadyate katamābhyām dvābhyām hetu upanibandhataḥ pratyaya upanibandhataḥ ca tatra ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya hetu upanibandhaḥ katamaḥ yad idam avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃskāra pratyayam vijñānam vijñāna pratyayam nāma rūpam nāma rūpa pratyayam ṣaṣ āyatanam ṣaṣ āyatana pratyayaḥ sparśaḥ sparśa pratyayā vedanā vedanā pratyayā tṛṣṇā tṛṣṇā pratyayam upādānam upādāna pratyayaḥ bhavaḥ bhava pratyayā jātiḥ jāti pratyayā jarā maraṇa śoka parideva duḥkha daurmanasya upāyāsāḥ saṃbhavanti evam asya kevalasya mahataḥ  duḥkha skandhasya samudayaḥ  bhavati avidyā ced na abhaviṣyat   eva saṃskārāḥ prajñāsyante evam yāvat jātiḥ ced na abhaviṣyat jarā maraṇam na prajñāsyate athavā satyām avidyāyām saṃskārāṇām abhinirvṛttiḥ bhavati evam yāvat jātyām satyām jarā maraṇasya abhinirvṛttiḥ bhavati atra avidyāyā na evam bhavati aham saṃskārān abhinirvartayāmi iti saṃskārāṇām api na evam bhavati vayam avidyayā abhinirvartitā iti evam yāvat jāteḥ api na evam bhavati aham jarā maraṇam abhinirvartayāmi iti jarā maraṇasya api na evam bhavati aham jātyā abhinirvartitam iti atha ca satyām avidyāyām saṃskārāṇa abhinirvṛtti rbhavati prādurbhāvaḥ evam yāvat jātyām satyām jarā maraṇasya abhinirvṛttiḥ bhavati prādurbhāvaḥ evam ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya hetu upanibandhaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ katham ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya pratyaya upanibandhaḥ  draṣṭavya iti ṣaṇṇām dhātūnām samavāyāt  katameṣām ṣaṇṇām dhātūnām samavāyāt  yad idam pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśa vijñāna dhātūnām samavāyāt ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya pratyaya upanibandhaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ tatra ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya pṛthivī dhātuḥ katamaḥ yaḥ kāyasya saṃśleṣāt kaṭhina bhāvam abhinirvartayati ayam ucyate pṛthivī dhātuḥ yaḥ kāyasya anuparigraha kṛtyam karoti ayam ucyate ap dhātuḥ yaḥ kāyasya aśita bhakṣitam paripācayati ayam ucyate tejaḥ dhātuḥ yaḥ kāyasya āśvāsa praśvāsa kṛtyam karoti ayam ucyate vāyudhātuḥ yaḥ kāyasya antar  śauṣīryam abhinirvartayati ayam ucyate ākāśa dhātuḥ yaḥ  nāma rūpam abhinirvartayati naḍa kalāpa yogena pañca vijñāna kāya saṃyuktam sa āsravam ca manaḥ vijñānam ayam ucyate bhikṣavaḥ  vijñāna dhātuḥ tatra asatām eṣām pratyayānām kāyasya utpattiḥ na bhavati yadā tu ādhyātmikaḥ pṛthivī dhātuḥ avikalaḥ  bhavati evam ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśa vijñāna dhātavaḥ ca avikalā bhavanti tatas  sarveṣām samavāyāt kāyasya utpattiḥ bhavati tatra pṛthivī dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya kaṭhina bhāvam abhinirvartayāmi iti ap dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya anuparigraha kṛtyam karomi iti tejaḥ dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya aśita pīta khāditam paripācayāmi iti vāyu dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya āśvāsa praśvāsa kṛtyam karomi iti ākāśa dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya antar śauṣīryam abhinirvartayāmi iti vijñāna dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya nāma rūpam abhinirvartayāmi iti kāyasya api na evam bhavati aham emiḥ pratyayaiḥ janita iti atha ca punar  satām eṣām pratyayānām samavāyāt kāyasya utpatti rbhavati tatra pṛthivī dhātuḥ na ātmā na sattvaḥ  na jīvaḥ  na jantuḥ na manujaḥ  na mānavaḥ  na strī na pumān na napuṃsakam na ca aham na mama na ca anyasya kasyacid  evam ap dhātuḥ tejaḥ dhātuḥ vāyudhātuḥ ākāśa dhātuḥ vijñāna dhātuḥ na ātmā na sattvaḥ  na jīvaḥ  na jantuḥ na manujaḥ  na mānavaḥ  na strī na pumān na napuṃsakam na ca aham na mama na ca anyasya kasyacid  tatra avidyā katamā yā eṣām evam ṣaṇṇām dhātūnāyamaiksaṃjñā piṇḍa saṃjñā nitya saṃjñā dhruva saṃjñā śāśvata saṃjñā sukha saṃjñā ātma saṃjñā sattva saṃjñā jīva pudgalam anujamānava saṃjñā ahaṃkāra saṃjñā mamakāra saṃjñā evamādi vividham ajñānam iyam ucyate avidyā iti evam avidyāyām satyām viṣayeṣu rāga dveṣa mohāḥ pravartante tatra ye rāga dveṣa mohā viṣayeṣu amī saṃskārā iti ucyante vastu prativijñaptiḥ vijñānam vijñāna sahabhuvaḥ catvāraḥ skandhā arūpiṇaḥ upādāna ākhyāḥ tad nāma rūpam catvāri mahābhūtāni tāni ca upādāya rūpam tad ca nāma rūpam aikadhyam abhisaṃkṣipya tad nāma rūpam nāma rūpa saṃniśritāni indriyāṇi ṣaṣ āyatanam trayāṇām dharmāṇām saṃnipātaḥ sparśaḥ sparśa anubhavaḥ  vedanā vedanā adhyavasānam tṛṣṇā tṛṣṇā vaipulyam uipa ādānam upādāna nirjātam punarbhava janakam karma bhavaḥ bhava hetukaḥ skandha prādurbhāvaḥ  jātiḥ jātasya skandhasya paripākaḥ  jarā jīrṇasya skandhasya vināśaḥ  maraṇam mriyamāṇasya saṃmūḍhasya sa abhiṣvaṅgasya antardāhaḥ śokaḥ śoka uttham ālapanam paridevaḥ pañca vijñāna kāya saṃyuktam asātam anubhavanam duḥkham manasā saṃyuktam mānasam duḥkham dārmanasyam ye ca api anye evamādaya upakleśāḥ te upāyāsā iti tatra moha andhakāra arthena avidyā abhisaṃskāra arthena saṃskārāḥ vijñāpana arthena vijñānam anyonya upastambhana arthena nāma rūpam āya dvāra arthena ṣaṣ āyatanam sparśana arthena sparśaḥ anubhavana arthena vedanā paritarṣaṇa arthena tṛṣṇā upādāna arthena upādānam punarbhava arthena bhavaḥ janma arthena jātiḥ paripāka arthena jarā vināśa arthena maraṇam śocana arthena śokaḥ paridevana arthena paridevaḥ kāya paripīḍana arthena duḥkham citta saṃpīḍana arthena daurmanasyam upakleśa arthena upāyāsāḥ athavā tattve apratipattiḥ mithyāpratipattiḥ ajñānam avidyā evam avidyāyām satyām trividhāḥ saṃskārā abhinirvartante puṇya upagā apuṇya upagā ānen jya upagāḥ tatra puṇya upagānām saṃskārāṇām puṇya upagamā iva vijñānam bhavati apuṇya upagānām saṃskārāṇām apuṇya upagam ā iva vijñānam bhavati ānen jya upagānām saṃskārāṇāmāneñjya upagam eva vijñānam bhavati idam ucyate vijñānam vijñāna pratyayam nāma rūpam iti veda nādayaḥ  arūpiṇaḥ catvāraḥ skandhāḥ tatra tatra bhave nāmayanti iti nāma saha rūpa skandhena ca nāma rūpam ca iti nāma rūpam ucyate nāma rūpa vivṛddhayā ṣaḍbhiḥ āyatana dvāraiḥ kṛtya kriyāḥ pravartante prajñāyante tad nāma rūpa pratyayam ṣaṣ āyatanam iti ucyate ṣaḍbhyaḥ ca āyataṃebhyaḥ ṣaḍ  sparśakāyāḥ pravartante ayam ṣaṣ āyatana pratyayaḥ sparśa iti ucyate yad jātīyaḥ sparśaḥ  bhavati tad jātīyā vedanā pravartate iyam ucyate bhikṣavaḥ sparśa pratyayā vedanā iti yaḥ tām vedanām viśeṣeṇa āsvādayati abhinandati adhyavasyati adhyavasāya tiṣṭhati sā vedanā pratyayā tṛṣṇā iti ucyate āsvādana abhinandana adhyavasāna sthānāt ātma priya rūpa sāta rūpaiḥ viyogaḥ  mā bhūt nityam aparityāgaḥ  bhavet iti yā evam prārthanā idam ucyate bhikṣavaḥ tṛṣṇā pratyayam upādānam yatra vastuni sa tṛṣṇaḥ tasya vastunaḥ  arjanāya viṭhapanāya upādānam upādatte tatra tatra prārthayate evam prārthayamānaḥ punarbhava janakam karma samutthāpayati kāyena vācā manasā ca sa upādāna pratyayaḥ bhava iti ucyate tad karma nirjātānām skandhānām abhinirvṛtiḥ yā sā bhava pratyayā jātiḥ iti ucyate jātyā abhinirvṛttānām skandhānām upacayana paripākāt vināśaḥ  bhavati tad idam jāti pratyayam jarā maraṇam iti ucyate evam ayam dvādaśa aṅgaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ  anyonya hetukaḥ anyonya pratyayaḥ na eva anityaḥ  na eva nityaḥ  na saṃskṛtaḥ  na asaṃskṛtaḥ  na ahetukaḥ  na apratyayaḥ  na vedayitā na avedayitā na pratītyasamutpannaḥ  na apratītya samutpannaḥ  na kṣaya dharmaḥ  na akṣaya dharmaḥ  na vināśa dharmaḥ  na avināśa dharmaḥ  na nirodha dharmaḥ  na anirodha dharmaḥ  anādi kāla pravṛttaḥ  anucchinnaḥ anupravartate nadī srotavat yadi apyayam dvādaśa aṅgaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ  anucchinnaḥ anupravartate nadī srotavat atha ca imān yasya dvādaśa aṅgasya pratītyasamutpādasya catvāri aṅgāni saṃghāta kriyāyai hetu tvena pravartante katamāni catvāri yad uta avidyā tṛṣṇā karma vijñānam ca tatra vijñānam bīja svabhāva tvena hetuḥ karma kṣetra svabhāva tvena hetuḥ avidyā tṛṣṇā ca kleśa svabhāva tvena hetuḥ karma kleśā vijñāna bījam janayanti tatra karma vijñāna bījasya kṣetra kāryam karoti tṛṣṇā vijñāna bījam snehayati avidyā vijñāna bījam avakirati asatām teṣām pratyayānām vijñāna bījasi abhinirvṛttiḥ na bhavati tatra karmaṇaḥ  na evam bhavati aham vijñāna bījasya kṣetra kāryam karomi iti tṛṣṇāyāḥ  api na evam bhavati aham vijñānasya sneha kāryam karom iti avidyāyāḥ  api na evam bhavati aham vijñāna bījam avakirāmi iti vijñāna bījasya api na evam bhavati aham ebhiḥ pratyayaiḥ janitam iti atha ca vijñāna bījam karma kṣetra pratiṣṭhitam tṛṣṇā sneha abhiṣyanditam avidyayā su avakīrṇam vibhajyamānam virohati tatra tatra upapattyāṃyatana pratisaṃdhau mātuḥ kukṣau nāma rūpa aṅkuram abhinirvartayati sa ca nāma rūpa aṅkuraḥ  na svayam kṛtoa na para kṛtaḥ  na ubhaya kṛtaḥ  na īśvara kṛtaḥ  na kāla pariṇāmitaḥ  na prakṛti saṃbhūtaḥ  na ca eka kāraṇa adhīnaḥ  na api ahetu samutpannaḥ atha ca mātā pitṛ saṃyogāt  ṛtu samavāyāt  anyeṣām pratyayānām samavāyāt  āsvāda anuviddham vijñāna bījam mātuḥ kukṣau nāma rūpa aṅkuram abhinirvartayati asvāmikeṣu dharmeṣu aparigraheṣu amameṣu ākāśa sameṣu māyā lakṣaṇa svabhāveṣu hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt tad yathā pañcabhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānam utpadyate katamaiḥ pañcabhiḥ yad uta cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpam ca ālokam ca ākāśam ca tad jamana sikāram ca pratītya utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam tatra cakṣuḥ vijñānasya cakṣuḥ āśraya kṛtyam karoti rūpam ālambana kṛtyam karoti ālokaḥ  avabhāsa kṛtyam karoti ākāśam anāvaraṇa kṛtyam karoti tad ja manasikāraḥ samanvāharaṇa kṛtyam karoti asatām eṣām pratyayānām cakṣuḥ vijñānam na utpadyate yadā tu cakṣuḥ ādhyātmikam āyatanam avikalam bhavati evam rūpa āloka ākāśa tajja manasikārāḥ ca avikalā bhavanti tatas  sarveṣām samavāyāt cakṣuḥ vijñānam utpadyate tatra cakṣuṣaḥ  na evam bhavati aham cakṣuḥ vijñānasya āśraya kṛtyam karomi iti ālokasya api na evam bhavati aham cakṣuḥ vijñānasya avabhāsa kṛtyam karomi iti ākāśasya api na evam bhavati aham cakṣuḥ vijñānasya anāvaraṇa kṛtyam karom iti tad ja mana sikārasya api na evam bhavati aham cakṣuḥ vijñānasya samanvāharaṇa kṛtyam karomi iti cakṣuḥ vijñānasya api na evam bhavati aham ebhiḥ pratyayaiḥ janitam iti atha ca satām eṣām pratyayānām samavāyāt cakṣuḥ vijñānasya utpattiḥ bhavati evam śeṣāṇām indriyāṇām yathāyogam karaṇīyam tatra na kaścid dharmaḥ  asmāt lokāt para lokam saṃkrāmati asti ca karma phala prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt tad yathā bhikṣavaḥ su pariśuddhe ādarśa maṇḍale mukha pratibimba kam dṛśyate na ca tatra ādarśa maṇḍale mukham saṃkrāmati asti ca mukha prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt evam asmāt lokān na kaścid cyutaḥ  na api anyatra upapannaḥ asti ca karma phala prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt tad yathā bhikṣavaḥ candra maṇḍalam catvāriṃśat yojana śatam ūrdhvam vrajati atha ca punar  parītte api udaka bhājane candrasya pratibimbam dṛśyate na ca tasmāt sthānāt ūrdhvam nabhasaḥ cyutam parītte udakasya bhājane saṃkrāntam bhavati asti ca candra maṇḍala prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt evam asmāt lokān na kaścid cyutaḥ  na anyatra upapannaḥ asti ca karma phala prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt tad yathā agniḥ upādāna pratyaye sati jvalati upādāna vaikalyāt na jvalati evam eva bhikṣavaḥ karma kleśa janitam vijñāna bījam tatra tatra upapatti āyatana pratisaṃdhau mātuḥ kukṣau nāma rūpa aṅkuram abhinirvartayati asvāmikeṣu dharmeṣu aparigraheṣu māyā lakṣaṇa svabhāveṣu amameṣu kṛtrimeṣu hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt tatra ādhyātmikaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ pañcabhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ draṣṭavyaḥ katamaiḥ pañcabhiḥ na śāśvatataḥ na ucchedataḥ  na saṃkrāntitaḥ parītta hetu vipula phala abhinirvṛttitaḥ tad sadṛśa anuprabandhataḥ ca iti katham na śāśvatatas  yasmāt anye māraṇa antikāḥ skandhāḥ anye aupapatti aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ na tu ya eva māraṇa antikāḥ skandhāḥ ta eva aupapatti aṃśikāḥ api tu māraṇa antikāḥ skandhā nirudhyante tasmin  eva ca samaye aupapatti aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ prādurbhavanti atas  na śāśvatatas  katham na ucchedataḥ na ca pūrva niruddheṣu māraṇa antikeṣu skandheṣu aupapatti aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ prādurbhavanti na api aniruddheṣu api tu māraṇa antikāḥ skandhā nirudhyante tasmin  eva ca samaye aupapatti aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ prādurbhavanti tulā daṇḍa unnābha avanāmavat  candra bimba pratibimbavat  atas  na ucchedataḥ katham na saṃkrāntitaḥ visadṛśāḥ sattva nikāyāḥ sabhāgāyām jātyām jātim abhinirvartayanti atas  na saṃkrāntitaḥ katham parītta hetutaḥ vipula phala abhinirvṛttitaḥ parīttam karma kriyate vipulaḥ phala vipākaḥ  anubhūyate atas  parītta hetutaḥ vipula phala abhinirvṛttitaḥ katham tad sadṛśa anuprabandhataḥ yathāvedanīyam karma kriyate tathā vedanīyaḥ  vipākaḥ  anubhūyate atas tad sadṛśa anuprabandhataḥ ca iti vistaraḥ iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau dvādaśa aṅga parīkṣā nāma ṣaḍviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam dṛṣṭi parīkṣā saptaviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam yaḥ ca evam pratītyasamutpādam yathābhūtam samyak  paśyati sa na pūrva antam pratisarati na apara antam pratisarati ityādi sūtre paṭhayate tatra katamaḥ pūrva antaḥ katamaḥ  apara antaḥ katham na pratisarati iti tad vayutpati artham idam ārabhyate tatra vartamānam ātma bhāvam apekṣya atītā ātma bhāvāḥ pūrva anta iti ucyate pūrvaḥ hi janma paraṃpara aṃśaḥ pūrva antaḥ tam na pratisarati dṛṣṭi prakāraiḥ na ālambate pratītyasamutpādasya yathāvat avasthita tattva darśanāt na anyathā avasthitam vastu anyathā abhiniviśate tatra aṣṭau dṛṣṭayaḥ pūrva antam ālambya anyathā pravṛttāḥ tad yathā abhūmatītam adhvānam na abhūm iti ca dṛṣṭayaḥ yāḥ tāḥ śāśvata loka ādyāḥ pūrva antam samupāśritāḥ tatra iti śabdaḥ ādi arthaḥ athavā dṛṣṭi dvaya upādānam upalakṣaṇa artham catastraḥ tu etāḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ tad yathā kim nu aham abhūvam atītam adhvānam na abhūvam atītam adhvānam abhūvam ca na abhūvam ca na eva abhūvam na na abhūvam iti etāḥ catasraḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ pūrva antam samāśritāḥ aparā api catasra iti āha yāḥ tāḥ śāśvata loka ādyāḥ pūrvam prasaṅgena upavarṇitāḥ tā api pūrva antam samupāśritāḥ tatra yadi api pūrva antāt  dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayāt uttaram dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayam na atibhidyate tathā api tāvat mātra viśeṣam āśritya pṛthak upādīyate tad ca uttaratra vyākhyāsyāmaḥ tatra śāśvataḥ  lokaḥ iti etad  abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti etasmāt na atibhidyate athavā ayam viśeṣaḥ yad śāśvataḥ  lokaḥ iti eṣām dṛṣṭiḥ sāmānyena pūrva antam āśritā abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti eṣā tu ātmana eva pūrva anta parāmarśena pravṛttā na sāmānyena iti evam anyāsu api dṛṣṭiṣu viśeṣaḥ  vaktavyaḥ iti evam tāvat  aṣṭau  etā dṛṣṭayaḥ pūrva antam samupāśritāḥ uktaḥ pūrva antar tad ālambikābhiḥ dṛṣṭibhiḥ sārdham idānīm aparānta ucyate tatra vartamānam ātma bhāvam apekṣya bhāvinaḥ ātma bhāvāḥ aparānta iti ucyate aparaḥ  hi janma paraṃpara aṃśa u apara antaḥ tam na pratisarati dṛṣṭi prakāraiḥ na ālambate pratītyasamutpādasya yathāvat avasthita tattva darśanāt na anyathā avasthitam vastu anyathā abhiniviśate tatra aṣṭau dṛṣṭayaḥ apara antam ālambya anyathā pravṛttāḥ tad yathā dṛṣṭayaḥ  na bhaviṣyāmi kim anyaḥ anāgate adhvani bhaviṣyāmi iti ca antādyā apara antam samāśritāḥ iha api dṛṣṭi dvaya upādānam upalakṣaṇa artham catastraḥ tu etāḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ tad yathā kim nu bhaviṣyāmi anāgatam adhvānam na bhaviṣyāmi bhaviṣyāmi ca na bhaviṣyāmi ca na eva bhaviṣyāmi na ca na bhaviṣyāmi anāgatam adhvānam iti etāḥ catasraḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ apara antam samāśritāḥ kim etā eva catasraḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ apara antam samāśritāḥ na iti āha kim tarhi aparā api catasraḥ  vidyante anta ādyā apara antam samāśritāḥ tatra antādyāḥ catasraḥ  dṛṣṭayaḥ sāmānyena aparāntam āaśritya pravṛttāḥ kim tu bhaviṣyāmi anāgatam adhvānam iti etāḥ tu ātmana eva apara antam āśritya pravṛttāḥ iti evam dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayasya viśeṣa iti boddhavyam tatra ādyasya tāvat  pūrva anta ālambikasya dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayasya yathā na saṃbhavaḥ tathā pratipādayan  āha abhūmatītam adhvānam iti etad na upapadyate yaḥ  hi janmasu pūrveṣu sa eva na bhavati ayam tatra ya eva atīteṣu janmasu babhūva yadi sa eva ayamadhunā syāt  tadā yuktam asya grahītum abhūvam aham atītam adhvānam iti na ca etad evam saṃbhavati nityatva prasaṅgāt  nityasya ca saṃsaraṇa anupapatteḥ eka gati sthasya api nānā gati saṃgṛhītatva prasaṅgāt  iha hi pūrvam yadi naraka ādi gatikaḥ  bhūtvā idānīm karma vaicitryāt  manuṣyeṣu upapannaḥ evaṃkalpayet  aham eva asau nāraka āsam iti tad asya na yuktam katham hi nāma manuṣyaḥ san nāraka ādikaḥ syāt  yad tarhi idam paṭhayate sūtre aham eva sa tena kālena tena samayena māndhātā nāma rājā cakravartī abhūvam iti tad  katham veditavyam iti anyatva pratiṣedha param tad vacanam na ekatva pratipādakam iti vijñeyam ata eva hi na anyaḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena iti paṭhayate yadi punar  sa eva ayam iti pūrvakasya ca adhunātanasya ca eka tvam syāt  kaḥ  doṣaḥ syāt  uktaḥ tāvat atra doṣaḥ nitya tvam syāt iti tathā api bhūya ucyate sa eva ātmā iti tu bhavet upādānam viśiṣyate yadi sa eva pūrvaka ātmā ayam idānīm syāt  tadā upādānasya pañca skandha lakṣaṇasya viśeṣaḥ  na syāt  upāda ātura viśeṣāt pūrva avasthāyām iva na ca evam upādāna aviśeṣaḥ  asya ātmanaḥ kim tarhi viśiṣyata eva upādānam upādātuḥ karma bhedāt  kāraka bhedāt ca tatas ca upādāna viśeṣāt  sa eva ayam ātmā iti na yujyate atha manyase viśiṣyatām upādānam ātmā tu eka eva iti atas  ātmanaḥ  aviśiṣṭa tvāt abhūmatītam adhvānam iti etad  bhaviṣyati eva ucyate upādāna vinirmukta ātmā te katamaḥ punar  yadi hi anyat upādānam anyaḥ ca ātmā syāt  tadā upādāna viśeṣe api ātmanaḥ  aviśeṣāt  syāt etad evam na ca etad  bhedena darśayitum śakyam ayam asau  ātmā idam asya upādānam iti upādāna viśiṣṭa svabhāva tvāt ātmanaḥ  ahetukatva prasaṅgāt  pṛthak grahaṇa prasaṅgāt ca yadā ca evam upādāna vinirmukta ātmā darśayitum na śakyate tadā upādāna viśeṣe api ātma aviśeṣa iti na śakyate kalpayitum atha api kaścid  parikalpayet  satyam upādāna vinirmukta iti evam na saṃbhavati kim upādānam eva ātma tvena parikalpyate iti etad api na yuktam iti pratipādayan  āha upādāna vinirmuktaḥ  na asti ātmā iti kṛte sati syāt upādānam eva ātmā na asti ca ātmā iti vaḥ punar  yathā tāvat upādānam eva ātmā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha na ca upādānam eva ātmā vyeti tad samudeti ca katham hi nāma upādānam upādātā bhaviṣyati tatra yad etad  pañca upādāna skandha ākhyam upādānam tad  pratikṣaṇam utpadyate ca vinaśyati ca na ca evam ātmā pratikṣaṇam utpadyate ca vinaśyati ca ātmā skandhebhyaḥ tattva anyatva ādinā ca nitya anitya tvena api aśakya eva vaktum aneka doṣa prasaṅgāt  nitya tve hi ātmanaḥ śāśvata vādaḥ syāt  anitya tve ca uccheda vāda prasaṅgaḥ tatas ca tad ubhayam śāśvata uccheda ākhyam mahānartha karam iti na upagantavyam atas  upādānam eva ātmā iti tāvat na yujyate api ca katham hi nāma upādānam upādātā bhaviṣyati iha upādīyate iti upādānam karma tasya ca avaśyam upādātrā upārjakena bhavitavyam tasya ca upādānasya yadi ātma tvam iṣyate tatra upādānam eva upādātā iti api vidyate tatas ca kartṛ karmaṇoḥ aikye sati chetṛ  chettavya ghaṭa kumbhakāra agni indhana ādīnām api aikyam syāt  na ca etad  dṛṣṭam yuktam vā iti pratipādayan  āha katham hi nāma upādānam upādātā bhaviṣyati iti api tu atyanta asaṃbhava eva asya pakṣasya iti abhiprāyaḥ atra āha satyam upādāna mātram ātmā na yujyate kim tarhi upādāna vyatirikta eva ātmā bhaviṣyati etad api na yuktam kim kāraṇam yasmāt  anyaḥ punar upādānāt ātmā na eva upapadyate gṛhyate hi anupādānaḥ  yadi anyaḥ  na ca gṛhyate yadi upādānāt ātmā vyatiriktaḥ syāt  gṛhyeta sa upādāna vyatiriktaḥ ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ na ca evam gṛhyate tasmāt upādāna vyatiriktaḥ  api na asti anupādānaḥ upādāna vyatirekeṇa agṛhyamāṇa tvāt  kha puṣpavat  iti abhiprāyaḥ idānīm yathā upapāditam artham nigamayan  āha evam na anya upādānāt na ca upādānam eva saḥ ātmā na asti anupādānaḥ atha syāt  yadi ātmā upādāna svarūpaḥ  na bhavati upādāna upādātroḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt  udaya vyaya prasaṅgāt ca sa hi anyaḥ  api na bhavati upādānam anapekṣya bhedena grahaṇa prasaṅgāt  na ca api anupādānaḥ upādāna nirapekṣasya grahaṇa prasaṅgāt  evam tarhi na asti ātmā iti astu ucyate na api na asti eṣa niścayaḥ yaḥ  hi nāma skandhān upādāya prajñapyate sa katham na asti iti syāt  na hi avidyamānaḥ  vandhyā tanayaḥ skandhān upādāya prajñapyate katham sati upādāne upādātā na asti iti yujyate tasmāt na astitvam api asya na yujyate tasmāt na asti ātmā iti niścayaḥ  api eṣa na upapadyate asya tu ātmanaḥ  vyavasthānam vistareṇa madhyamaka avatārāt avaseyam iha api ca pūrvam eva sthāna sthāneṣu kṛtā vyavasthā iti na punar iha tadvayava sthāne yatna āsthīyate evam tāvat abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti eṣā kalpanā na upapadyate idānīm na abhūvam atītam adhvānam ityet api yathā na upapadyate tathā pratipādayan  āha na abhūm atītam adhvānam iti etad na upapadyate yaḥ  hi janmasu pūrveṣu tatas  anyaḥ  na bhavati ayam yadi pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ asya adhunātanasya ātmanaḥ  anya tvam syāt  tadānīm na abhūm atītam adhvānam iti syāt  na ca etad evam saṃbhavati tasmāt na abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti etad na upapadyate yadi punar  pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ asya anya tvam syāt  kaḥ  doṣa iti ucyate yadi hi ayam bhavet anyaḥ pratyākhyāya api tam bhavet  tathā eva ca sa saṃtiṣṭhet tatra jāyeta vā amṛtaḥ yadi hi ayam adhunā atana ātmā pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ anyaḥ syāt  tadā tam pūrvakam ātmānam pratyākhyāya parityajya tad nirapekṣaḥ atad dhetuka eva syāt  kim ca anyat  tathā eva ca sa saṃtiṣṭhet tatra yadi pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ asya anya tvam syāt  tadā anya tvāt  ghaṭa utpāde paṭa avināśavat  pūrvasya ātmanā uttarasmin  api ātmani samutpadyamāne api anirodhaḥ syāt  aniruddha tvāt ca yatra pūrvam deva manuṣya ādi janmasu upapannaḥ yena varṇa saṃsthāna ādinā pūrvam upalabhyamānaḥ tena eva prakāreṇa tathā eva sa tatra avatiṣṭheta tathā eva avatiṣṭheta iti tasmāt na abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti etad na upapadyate atra āha tatra yad uktam yadi hi ayam bhavet anyaḥ pratyākhyāya api tam bhavet  iti yadi puna pūrvakam ātmānam pratyākhyāya [ayam iha bhavet  kaḥ  doṣaḥ syāt  tatra doṣā bahavaḥ syuḥ katham iti ced  yasmāt evam sati ucchedaḥ karmaṇām nāśaḥ tathā anya kṛta karmaṇām anyena paribhogaḥ syāt evamādi prasajyate yadi pūrvakam ātmānam pratyākhyāya ayam ātmā bhavet  tadā] pūrvakasya ātmanaḥ tatra naṣṭa tvāt  iha ca anyasya eva ca utpādanāt pūrvakasya ātmana ucchedaḥ syāt  tasmin  ca ātmani ucchinne karmaṇā ām adatta phalānām eva āśraya vicchedena vicchedāt  bhoktaḥ ca abhāvāt nāśa eva syāt  atha pūrvakena ātmanā kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ uttareṇa ātmanā phala paribhogaḥ parikalpyate tathā api anyena kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phalasya anyena upabhogaḥ syāt  tatas ca akṛta abhyāgam bhayam syāt karma akṛtakam yadi iti evamādi aniṣṭam āpadyate api ca yadi ayam ātmā pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ anya eva atra upapannaḥ syāt  tadā pūrvam abhūtvā paścāt utpanna iti syāt  na ca etad yuktam iti pratipādayan  āha na api abhūtvā samudbhūtaḥ  doṣaḥ  hi atra prasajyate kṛtakaḥ  vā bhavet ātmā saṃbhūtaḥ  vā api ahetukaḥ iti yadi hi ātmā pūrvam abhūtvā paścāt utpannaḥ syāt  tadā kṛtaka eva ātmā syāt  na ca kṛtaka ātmā iṣyate anityatva prasaṅgāt  vyatiriktasya ca tad niṣpādakasya kartuḥ abhāvāt  kutas  kṛtaka tvam ātmanaḥ  yojyeta kṛtake ca ātmani parikalpyamāne ādimān saṃsāraḥ syāt eva apūrva sattvasya prādurbhāvaḥ ca na ca etad evam tasmāt na kṛtaka ātmā api ca saṃbhūtaḥ  vā api ahetukaḥ abhūtvā prāc ātmā samutpadyamānaḥ  nirhetuka eva upapadyate pūrvam hi ātmā na asti iti akṛta kaḥ nirhetukaḥ syāt  vā śabdaḥ  vikalpe kṛtakaḥ  vā bhavet ātmā yadi vā na abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti etad na abhyupeyam saṃbhūtaḥ  vā api ahetukaḥ yadi vā na abhūm atītam adhvānam iti etad na upapadyate iti abhyupagamyatām idānīm yathā upavarṇitam eva artham nigamayan  āha evam dṛṣṭiḥ atīte yā na abhūm aham abhūmaham ubhayam na ubhayam ca iti na eṣā samupapadyate evam yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena abhūmatītam adhvānam iti yā dṛṣṭiḥ eṣā api na eva upapadyate etad dvayasya abhāvāt ca ubhayam api na upapadyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt  dvayam hi etad samāhatam ubhayam iti kalpyate ekaikasya ca pṛthak pṛthak abhāvāt  kutas tad samāhāra iti ubhayam api na saṃbhavati ubhayasya abhāvāt  kutas tad pratiṣedhena na ubhayam bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt na eva abhūvam na na abhūvam iti etad api na upapadyate tad evam pūrva antam samāśritasya dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayasya asaṃbhavam udbhāvya idānīm aparānta samāśritasya pratiṣedham āha adhvani anāgate kim nu bhaviṣyāmi iti darśanam na bhaviṣyāmi ca iti etad atītena adhvanā samam yathā eva hi atīte adhvani dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayam niṣiddham evam anāgate api adhvani dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayam niṣedhanīya m ukta pāṭha parivartanena tad yathā adhvani anāgate kim nu bhaviṣyāmi iti asaṃgatam aiṣya janmani yaḥ  bhāvaḥ sa eva na bhavati ayam iti evamādinā sarvam samam yojyam ekatva pratiṣedhe evam anyatva pratiṣedhe api samam yojyam na syām anāgate kāle iti etad na upapadyate aiṣya janmani yaḥ  bhāvaḥ tatas  anyaḥ  na bhavati ayam iti evamādinā pūrva śloka pāṭha parivartanena idānīm pūrva antam samāśritasya śāśvata ādi dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayasya pratiṣedha artham āha sa devaḥ sa manuṣyaḥ ced evam bhavati śāśvatam anutpannaḥ ca devaḥ syāt jāyate na hi śāśvatam iha hi kaścid manuṣya gati sthaḥ kuśalam karma kṛtvā deva gatim gacchati tatra yadi sa eva devaḥ sa eva manuṣya iti evam ubhayoḥ aikyam syāt  tadā śāśvatam syāt  na ca etad evam yad eva eva manuṣyaḥ  bhavet iti atas  na asti kiṃcid śāśvatam api ca śāśvata vāde sati asamutpannaḥ ca devaḥ syāt  kim kāraṇam yasmāt jāyate na hi śāśvatam yad hi vastu śāśvatam tad vidyamāna tvāt na eva jāyate tatas ca anutpannaḥ  devaḥ syāt  anutpannaḥ  devaḥ  na yujyate iti evam tāvat śāśvatam na yujyate idānīm aśāśvatam api yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha devāt anyaḥ  manuṣyaḥ ced aśāśvatamatas  bhavet  devāt anyaḥ  manuṣyaḥ ced saṃtatiḥ na upapadyate yadi hi anyaḥ  devaḥ  anyaḥ ca manuṣyaḥ syāt  tadā pūrvakasya manuṣya ātmanaḥ tatra naṣṭa tvāt iha ca anyasya eva utpādāt  sa pūrva kaḥ  manuṣya ātmā tatra vinaṣṭa iti aśāśvatam syāt  tad saṃtāna anuvṛttyā na aśāśvatam iti ced  ucyate devāt anyaḥ  manuṣyaḥ ced saṃtatiḥ na upapadyate yadi devāt anyaḥ  manuṣyaḥ  bhavet  tadā yathā nimbasya na āmra taru saṃtānaḥ  bhavati evam manuṣyasya devaḥ eka saṃtāna patitaḥ  na syāt  tatas ca pūrvakasya vināśādaśāśvatam eva bhavet  athavā yadi devāt anyaḥ  manuṣyaḥ  bhavet  tadā saṃtāna anuvṛttiḥ na syāt  asti ca iyam saṃtāna anuvṛttiḥ devasya manuṣyaḥ eka saṃtāna patita iti tasmāt  saṃtāna abhāva prasaṅgāt  devāt anyaḥ  manuṣyaḥ  na bhavati yatas ca evam atas  aśāśvatam api na asti idānīm śāśvata aśāśvata pratiṣedha artham āha divyaḥ  yadi eka deśaḥ syāt eka deśaḥ ca mānuṣaḥ aśāśvatam śāśvatam ca bhavet tad ca na yujyate yadi ayam manuṣyaḥ aṃśena manuṣya tām vijahyāt  aṃśena vihāya manuṣya tām deva ātma bhāvam upādadyāt  tadā eka deśasya nāśādaśāśvatam syāt  eka deśasya ca avasthānāt śāśvatam syāt  etad ca ayuktam yad ekasya divya gati saṃgṛhītaḥ eka deśaḥ syāt  eka deśaḥ ca manuṣyaḥ syāt  tasmāt śāśvatam ca aśāśvatam ca etad ubhayam na upapadyate idānīm naśāśvatana eva aśāśvata dṛṣṭi pratiṣedha artham āha aśāśvatam śāśvatam ca prasiddham ubhayam yadi siddhe na śāśvatam kāmam na eva aśāśvatam iti api yadi śāśvatam kiṃcid vastu syāt  tadā paścāt aśāśvata darśanāt na eva śāśvatam iti syāt  evam yadi kiṃcid aśāśvatam syāt  tadā tasya paścāt śāśvata upapattitaḥ  na aśāśvatam iti syāt  yadā tu śāśvata aśāśvatam eva aprasiddham tadā kutas tad pratiṣedhena na eva śāśvatam na aśāśvatam syāt iti tasmāt etad api ayuktam atha syāt  anādi janma maraṇa paraṃpara apravṛttam avicchinna kamam saṃsāra prabandham upalabhya śāśvata mā ātmānam parikalpayāmaḥ asti asau śāśvataḥ kaścid  padārthaḥ yaḥ  hi nāma evam anādimati saṃsāre paribhraman  adya api upalabhyate iti ucyate etad api na upapadyate kim kāraṇam yaḥ  hi nāma kutaścid āgataḥ kaścid kiṃcid gacchet punar  kvacid  yadi tasmāt anādiḥ tu saṃsāraḥ syāt na ca asti saḥ yadi hi saṃskārāṇām ātmanaḥ  va kutaścid gati antarāt  gamanam gati antaram āgamanam syāt  tatas ca ganti antarāt  punar  kvacid  gamanam syāt  tadānīm ana ādiḥ saṃsāraḥ syāt  na ca kutaścid  kasyacid āgamanam saṃbhavati nityasya vā anityasya vā āgamana anupapatteḥ na ca api itas  punar  kasyacid  kvacid  gamanam saṃbhavati nityasya vā anityasya gamana anupapatteḥ yadā ca evam na saṃbhavati tadā kutaḥ janma maraṇa paraṃparāyā ati dīrgha tvena ādi anupalambhāt anādimān saṃsāraḥ syāt  saṃsartuḥ abhāvāt  kutas  anādimat tvam ādima tvam vā saṃsārasya saṃbhavet  yadā ca na saṃbhavati tadā yad uktam asti asau śāśvataḥ kaścid padārthaḥ yaḥ  hi nāma evam anādimati saṃsāre paribhraman  adya api upalabhyate iti tad na yuktam atas ca evam yathā udita nyāyena na asti ced śāśvataḥ kaścid  kaḥ  bhaviṣyati aśāśvataḥ śāśvataḥ  aśāśvataḥ ca api dvābhyām ābhyām tiraskṛtaḥ yadā ca evam śāśvata eva padārthaḥ  na saṃbhavati tadā kasya vigama nāt aśāśvataḥ syāt  śāśvata aśāśvatā anupalambhāt ca kutas  ubhayam kutaḥ na ubhayam iti tasmāt evam śāśvata ādi dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayam pūrva ante saṃsārasya na saṃbhavati idānīm anta ananta ādi catuṣṭayam apara ante yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha antavān yadi lokaḥ syāt para lokaḥ katham bhavet  atha api anantavān  lokaḥ para lokaḥ katham bhavet  yadi hi antavān vināśāt ūrdhvam pūrva lokaḥ  na syāt  tadā para lokaḥ  na syāt  asti ca para loke  iti antavān  loke  iti na upapadyate atha api anantavān  lokaḥ syāt  tadānīm api para lokaḥ katham bhavet  na eva para lokaḥ syāt iti abhiprāyaḥ na ca para lokaḥ  na asti atas  para loka sadbhāvā dantavān api lokaḥ  na bhavati idānīm antavat tvam anantava tvam ca ubhayam etad lokasya yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha skandhānām eṣa saṃtānaḥ  yasmāt dīpa arciṣām iva pravartate tasmāt na anta anantavat tvam ca yujyate pūrva uttara hetu phala bhāva saṃbandha nairantarya avicchinnakamavartī yasmāt ayam pradīpavat  pratikṣaṇa vināśī skandha saṃtānaḥ pravartate tasmāt hetu phala pravṛtti darśanāt na antavat tvam na anantavat tvam ca yujyate katham kṛtvā pūrve yadi ca bhajyeran  utpadyeran na ca api amī skandhāḥ skandhān pratītya imān atha lokaḥ  antavān bhavet  yadi pūrve manuṣya skandhā naśyeyuḥ tān  ca pratītya uttare deva gati upapatti saṃgṛhītā na upapadyeran tadā antavān lokaḥ  bhavet  taila varti kṣaya niruddha pradīpavat uttara ātma bhāva utpādāt na asti antavat tvam pūrve yadi na bhajyeran  utpadyeran na ca api amī skandhāḥ skandhān pratītya imān  lokaḥ  anantaḥ  bhavet atha atha yadi pūrvakāḥ skandhā na naśyeṣuḥ tān pratītya uttare phala bhūtāḥ skandhā na utpadyeran tadā anantaḥ  avināśī lokaḥ syāt  sva rūpāt apracyuta tvāt yadā tu pūrvakāḥ skandhā nirudhyante tad hetukāḥ ca apare skandhā uttara kālam jāyante tadā pūrvakānām anavasthānāt kutaḥ anantavat tvam saṃsārasya syāt  idānīm tṛtīyam ubhaya pakṣa bhāvam pratipādayan  āha antavān eka deśaḥ ced eka deśaḥ tu anantavān syāt antavān anantaḥ ca lokaḥ tad ca na yujyate yadi hi kasyacid eka deśasya vināśaḥ syāt  eka deśasya ca gati antara gamanam syāt  yāt tadānīmantavān  ca lokaḥ  anantavān  ca na ca etad evam saṃbhavati yad eka deśaḥ  naśyati eka deśaḥ  na naśyati iti atas  antavān  ca anantavān  ca loka iti na yujyate kasmāt  punar eka deśasya vināśaḥ eka deśasya ca avasthānam na yujyate iti pratipādayan  āha katham tāvat upādātuḥ eka deśaḥ  vinaṅkṣyate na naṅkṣyate ca eka deśa evam ca etad na yujyate iha eka deśasya vināśe eka deśasya ca avasthāne parikalpyamāne yadi vā upādātuḥ eka deśasya vināśaḥ avasthānam vā parikalpyeta yadi vā upādānasya tatra yadi tāvat upādātuḥ eka deśasya vināśaḥ eka deśasya ca avasthānam parikalpyate tad na yujyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt  katham tāvat upādātuḥ eka deśaḥ  vinaṅkṣyate na naṅkṣyate ca eka deśaḥ na eva hi atra kācid upapattiḥ asti yayā eka deśasya vināśam eka deśasya ca avināśam parikalpayiṣyāmaḥ ata eva upapattim apaśyan  ācārya āha evam ca etad na yujyate iti athavā upādātā hi nāma ātmā sa ca skandheṣu pañcadhā mṛgyamāṇaḥ  na saṃbhavati yaḥ ca na saṃbhavati tasya katham eka deśaḥ  vinaṅkṣyate eka deśaḥ ca na naṅkṣyate ata eva āha evam ca etad na yujyate iti athavā yadi upādātuḥ eka deśaḥ  naśyet eka deśaḥ ca na naśyet  tadā ekasya eva upādātuḥ deva tvam aṃśena anyena manuṣya tvam syāt  na ca etad iṣyate iti āha evam ca etad na yujyate iti evam tāvat upādāturantavat tvam anantavat tvam ca na yuktam iti idānīm upādānasya api yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha upādāna eka deśaḥ ca katham nāma vinaṅkṣyate na naṅkṣyate ca eka deśaḥ  na etad api upapadyate upādātṛvat etad api vyākhyeyam tad evam ubhaya darśana asaṃbhavam pratipādya idānīm yathā na ubhayam api na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan  āha antavat ca api anantam ca prasiddham ubhayam yadi siddhe na eva antavat kāmam na eva anantavat iti api pratiṣedhyasya vastunaḥ  asaṃbhavāt  pratiṣedhasya api asaṃbhava iti atas  antavat tve ca anantavat tve ca ubhayasmin  apratīte kasya pratiṣedhena na eva antavān na anantavān lokaḥ iti dṛṣṭi saṃbhavaḥ syāt iti evam tāvat  sāṃvṛtam pratibimba ākāram upādātāram upādānam ca abhyupetya api śāśvata ādi dṛṣṭayasaṃbhavam pratipādya idānīm sarvathā bhāva svabhāva anupalambhena bandhyā putra śyāma gaura ta ādivat  śāśvata ādi dṛṣṭī nāma saṃbhavam pratipipādayiṣuḥ āha athavā sarva bhāvānām śūnya tvāt śāśvata ādayaḥ kva kasya katamāḥ kasmāt saṃbhaviṣyanti dṛṣṭayaḥ iha sarva bhāvānām pratītyasamutpanna tvāt  śūnya tvam sakalena śāstreṇa pratipāditam tatas ca sarva bhāvānām śūnya tvāt  katamāḥ tāḥ sarva bhāva bāhyāḥ śāśvata ādyā dṛṣṭayaḥ  bhaviṣyanti yāḥ kaścid  grahīṣyati yatas tad nirākaraṇam ārapsyāmahe tathā kim vā ālambanam yad  sarva bhāva anantargatam yatra etā dṛṣṭaya utpatsyante yatra etā dṛṣṭīḥ nivārayiṣyāmaḥ katamaḥ ca asau bhāvaḥ pudgalaḥ  vā sarva bhāva bāhyāḥ yasya etā dṛṣṭayaḥ utpatsyante yam dṛṣṭibhyaḥ  nivārayiṣyāmaḥ kim vā dṛṣṭīnām utpatti kāraṇam ālambana nimittam sarva bhāva bāhyam yasmāt nimittāt utpadyamānāḥ śāśvata ādikāḥ dṛṣṭīḥ vārayiṣyāmaḥ sarveṣām eva hi padārthānām sarva bhāva antargata tvāt śūnya tvam śūnya tvāt ca sarve eva hi te padārthā na upalabhyanta iti kva kasya katamāḥ kasmāt saṃbhaviṣyanti dṛṣṭayaḥ na eva kāścid  na eva kvacid  na eva kasyacid  na api kenacid ākāreṇa saṃbhaviṣyanti iti abhiprāyaḥ asaṃbhave ca sati āsām parikalpanā eva na utpadyate iti ayuktā eva etā dṛṣṭayaḥ tad evam sarva dṛṣṭi prahāṇāya yaḥ saddharmam adeśayat  anukampām upādāya tam namasyāmi gautamam tatra saṃsāra nirvāṇa prahāṇa adhigama upalambha prapāta patana saṃdhāraṇāt dharmaḥ satām āryāṇām kṛta kāryāṇām dharmaḥ saddharmaḥ yadi vā śobhanaḥ  dharmaḥ saddharmaḥ sakala saṃsāra duḥkha kṣaya kara tvena praśaṃsanīya tvāt  yaḥ saddharmam anirodham anutpādam anucchedam aśāśvatam aneka artha manāna artham anāgamam anirgamam prapañca upaśamam śivam pratītyasamutpāda saṃjñayā hi deśitavān sarva dṛṣṭi prahāṇa artham jagatām anukampām upādāya mahā karuṇām eva āśritya priya eka putra adhikatara prema pātra sakala tribhuvana janaḥ na lābha satkāra pratyupakāra ādi lipsayā tam namasyāmi niruttaram advitīyam śāstāram kiṃnāmadheyam gautamam parama ṛṣi gotra saṃbhūtam iti arthaḥ yathā uktam ārya śāli stamba sūtre āryamaitreyeṇa mahā bodhisattvena ya imam pratītyasamutpādam evam yathābhūtam samyak prajñayā satata samitam ajīvam nirjīvam yathāvat aviparītam ajātam abhūtam akṛtam asaṃskṛtam apratigham anāvaraṇam śivam abhayam anāhāryam avyayam avyupaśama svabhāvam paśyati asataḥ tucchataḥ rikta taḥ  asārataḥ  rogataḥ  gaṇḍataḥ śalyataḥ  aghataḥ  anityataḥ  duḥkhataḥ śūnyataḥ  anātmataḥ na sa pūrva antam pratisarati kim nu aham abhūvam atīte adhvani āhosvit na abhūvam atīte adhvani kaḥ  nu aham abhūvam atīte adhvani katham nu aham abhūvam atīte adhvani apara antam vā punar na pratisarati kim nu aham bhaviṣyāmi anāgate adhvani āhosvit na bhaviṣyāmi anāgate adhvani kaḥ  nu bhaviṣyāmi anāgate adhvani katham nu bhaviṣyāmi anāgate adhvani pratyutpannam vā punar na pratisarati kim nu idam katham nu idam ke santaḥ ke bhaviṣyāmaḥ ayam sattvaḥ kutam āgataḥ sa itas cyutaḥ kutra gamiṣyati iti yāni ekeṣām śramaṇa brāhmaṇānām pṛthak loke dṛṣṭi gatāni bhaviṣyanti tad yathā ātma vāda pratisaṃyuktāni jīva vāda pratisaṃyuktāni kautuka maṅgala pratisaṃyuktāni tāni asya tasmin samaye prahīṇāni bhavanti parijñātāni samucchinna mūlāni tāla mastaka vadana ābhāsa gatāni āyatyām anutpāda ani rodha dharmāṇi atha khalu āyuṣmān śāriputraḥ  maitreyasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya bhāṣitam abhinandya anupramodya utthāya āsanāt prakrāntaḥ prakrāntāḥ te ca bhikṣava iti iti ācārya candra kīrti pāda upara citāyām prasanna padāyām madhyamaka vṛttau dṛṣṭi parīkṣā nāma saptaviṃśatitamam prakaraṇam samāptam samāptam ca idam madhyamaka śāstram sakala laukika lokottara pravacana nītaneya artha vyākhyāna naipuṇya viśāradam śrāvaka pratyekabuddha anuttara samyaksaṃbuddha bodhimaṇḍāsana dāyakam iti
